




























































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































Hayssafe kaallidi xaafettidayssi Dawite na7a Abrahame na7a gidida Yesuus Kiristtoosa yeletethaa.
Abrahamey Yisaaqa yelis; Yisaaqi Yayqooba yelis; Yayqoobi Yihudanne iya ishata yelis;
Yihudi Ti7imaarippe Faaresenne Zaara yelis; Faaresi Asroome yelis; Asroomey Raame yelis;
Raamey Aminaadabe yelis; Aminaadabey Na7asoona yelis; Na7asooney Salmoona yelis;
Salmooney Ra7abippe Boo7eza yelis; Boo7ezi Uruutippe Iyobeede yelis; Iyobeedi Isseyye yelis;
Isseyyey kawuwa Dawite yelis; Dawitey Ooriyo machcheefe Solomone yelis;
Solomoney Robi7aama yelis; Robi7aamey Abiya yelis; Abiyey Asaafe yelis;
Asaafi Iyosaafexe yelis; Iyosaafixey Iyoraame yelis; Iyoraamey Ooziyane yelis;
Ooziyaney Iyo7ataame yelis; Iyo7ataamey Akkaza yelis; Akkazi Hiziqiyasa yelis;
Hiziqiyasi Minaase yelis; Minaasey Amoona yelis; Amooni Iyosiyaasa yelis;
Isra7eele asay di7ettidi Baabiloone biittaa bida wode Iyosiyaasi Ikoniyaananne iya ishata yelis.
Baabiloone biitta Isra7eele asay di7ettidi bidaappe guye Ikoniyaani Salatiyaale yelis. Salatiyaaley Zerubaabela yelis;
Zerubaabeli Abdiyu yelis; Abdiyuy Eliyaaqeme yelis; Eliyaaqemey Azaara yelis;
Azaari Sadooqe yelis; Sadooqey Akiime yelis; Akiimey Eliyuuda yelis;
Eliyuudi Alaazara yelis; Alaazari Maatane yelis; Maataney Yayqooba yelis;
Yayqoobi Yoosefa yelis; Yoosefi Kiristtoosa giya Yesuusa yelida Mayraami azina.
Hiza, yeletethay Abrahameppe Dawite gakkanaw tammanne oydda. Dawiteppe bidi Baabiloone di7uwa gakkanaw tammanne oydda. Baabiloone di7uwappe bidi Kiristtoosa gakkanaw tammanne oyddu yeletethi gidees.
Yesuus Kiristtoosa yeletethaa taarikey hayssafe kaalleyssa. Iya aaya Mayraama Yoosefas oyshetta de7ashe Yoosefara gahettonna Geeshsha Ayyaanaappe qanthatasu.
Yoosefi Xillo asi gidida gisho iyo asan kessanaw koyibeenna. Yaaniya gisho qosan iyo agganaw qoppis.
I he qofan de7ishin Xoossaa kiitanchchoy amuhon qonccidi, “Dawite na7aw, Yoosefa, Mayraama qanthatiday Geeshsha Ayyaanaappe gidiya gisho iyo ekkanaw yayyofa” yaagis.
Iya adde na7a yelana, I ba deriya entta nagaraappe ashshiya gisho iya sunthaa ne Yesuusa gada xeegana.
Goday nabiya Isayaasa doonan,
“Hekko geela7iya qanthatana; adde na7akka yelana; iya sunthay Ammanu7eela geetettana” goyssi polettana mela ha ubbay hanis. Ammanu7eela geyssas birshshethay “Xoossay nuura de7ees” guussu.
Yoosefi dhiskkofe barkkidi Godaa kiitanchchoy kiittidayssa mela Mayraamo ba soo efis.
Shin ba bayra na7a yelana gakkanaw iyo bochchibeenna; yelettida na7akka Yesuusa gidi xeegis.
Kawuwa Heroodisa woden Yesuusi Yihuda biittan Beeteleme kataman yelettidayssafe guye xoolintto taybiya asati dolohappe Yerusalaame yidi,
“Yelettida Ayhude kawoy awun de7ii? Nuuni doloha baggara keyida iya xoolinttuwa be7idi iyaw goynnanaw yida” yaagidi oychchidosona.
Kawoy Heroodisi hessa si7ida wode dagammis. Yerusalaamen de7iya asay ubbayka dagammidosona.
Heroodisi kahine halaqatanne higge asttamaareta baakko xeegidi, “Kiristtoosi awun yelettanddeshsha?” yaagidi entta oychchis.
Enttika, “Yihuda Beetelemena; nabey,
‘Yihudan de7iya Beeteleme, Yihudan de7iya gooba katamatappe, neeni aybinkka guuxaka. Ta deriya Isra7eele aysanayssi, neeppe keyana’ gidi xaafis” yaagidosona.
Hessafe guye, Heroodisi dolohappe yida asata geeman xeegidi, xoolinttuwa entti be7ida wodiya enttafe geeshshidi eris.
I enttana Beeteleme yeddishe, “Bidi yelettida na7aa minthidi koyite; iya hintte demmida wode takka bada iyaw goynnana mela simmidi yishe taw odite” yaagis.
Enttika kawoy Heroodisi gidayssa si7idi bidosona. Entti doloha baggara be7ida xoolinttoy enttana kaalethishe na7ay de7iyasuwa gakkanaw efis.
Entti he xoolinttuwa be7ida wode gita ufayssi ufayttidosona.
Soo gelidi na7aa ba aaye Mayraamira de7eyssa be7idosona. Iyaw gulbbatidi goynnidosona. Bantta saaxiniya dooyidi worqqa, ixaanenne karbbe iyaw immidosona.
Entti Heroodisakko guye simmona mela Xoossay amuhon enttaw odin, hara ogera bantta biittaa simmidosona.
Doloha baggafe yida asati bidaappe guye, Godaa kiitanchchoy Yoosefas amuhon qonccidi, “Heroodisi na7aa wodhanaw koyaa gisho dendda; ellesada na7aanne na7aa aayiw ekkada Gibxxe biittaa ba. Ne simmana wodiya ta new odana gakkanaw yan gam77a” yaagis.
Hessa gisho, Yoosefi he qamman denddidi, na7aanne na7aa aayiw ekkidi Gibxxe bis.
Nabiya doonan Xoossay, “Taani, ta na7aa, Gibxxe biittafe xeegas” geetettida qaalay polettana mela Heroodisi hayqqana gakkanaw I yan de7is.
Hessafe guye, doloha baggafe yida asati iya cimmidayssa erida wode daro yilotis. I kase enttafe si7idayssada Beetelemeninne he heeran de7iya nam77u laythi kumidayssatanne nam77u laythafe garssan de7iya adde nayta ubbaa ba wotaddareta yeddidi wodhisis.
Nabiya Ermmiyasa doonan, “Yeehoynne zeleelssi, Raama kataman si7ettis. Raahela ba naytas yeekkawusu; entti hayqqida gisho minettanaw dandda7abuukku” gidi odidayssi polettis.
<range>
Heroodisi hayqqidaappe guye Gibxxen Godaa kiitanchchoy Yoosefas amuhon qonccidi,
“Na7aa wodhanaw koyaa asati hayqqida gisho denddada na7aanne na7aa aayiw ekkada Isra7eele biittaa simma” yaagis.
Yoosefi denddidi na7aanne na7aa aayiw ekkidi Isra7eele biittaa simmis.
Shin Arkkeliyoosi Yihudan ba aawa Heroodisa bessan kawotidayssa si7ida wode yaa baanaw yayyis. Xoossay amuhon iyaw qonccisin Galiila biittaa bis.
Nabeta doonan, “Naazirete asi geetettana” gidi odettidayssi polettana mela Naazirete katamaa bidi yan de7is.
He wode Xammaqiya Yohaannisi, “Xoossaa kawotethay matattida gisho hintte nagaraappe simmite” yaagidi sabbakishe Yihuda bazzo biittaa bis.
<range>
Nabiya Isayaasi Yohaannisabaa odidayssa mela, “Bazzo biittan, issoy ba qaala dhoqqu oothidi, ‘Godaa ogiya giigisite. Iya horogaa piddi oothite’ gis” yaagettiday iyassa yaagis.
Yohaannisi gimale ikiseppe oosettida afila ma77ees. Ba xeessan dafo danccees. I miya kathayka boolenne degera eesi.
Asay he wode Yerusalaame katamaappe, Yihuda biitta ubbaafenne Yorddaanose Shaafaa heerappe iyaakko yoosona.
Bantta nagaraa paaxidi Yorddaanose Shaafan Yohaannisa kushen xammaqettosona.
Yohaannisi, daro Farisaawetinne Saduqaaweti xammaqettanaw baakko yeyssata be7idi, enttako, “Ha iita shooshatoo, yaana Xoossaa hanquwafe baqatana mela hinttena oone zoriday?
Hiza, hinttee, hintte nagaraappe simmidayssa erisiyabaa oothite.
Hinttee, hintte wozanan, ‘Abrahamey, nu aaway de7ees’ gidi qoppofite. Loythi si7ite! Xoossay ha shuchchatappe Abrahames na7a kessanaw dandda7ees.
Beexey mithaa xaphuwan giigidi uttis; lo77o ayfe ayfonna mitha ubbay qanxettidi taman yegettana.
“Hinttee, hintte nagaraappe simmidayssa erisanaw taani hinttena haathan xammaqays. Shin taappe guyera yeyssi hinttena Geeshsha Ayyaananinne taman xammaqana. I taappe daro wolqqaamees; taani hari attoshin iya caammaa tookkanawukka bessike.
Kathaa geeshshiya pithey iya kushen de7ees. Kathaa loythi geeshshees; gisttiya ba shaaliyan qolana, shin punuwa to7onna taman xuuggana” yaagis.
He wode Yesuusi Yohaannisa kushen xammaqettanaw Galiilappe Yorddaanose Shaafaa bis.
Shin Yohaannisi iya digganaw koyid, “Taani nenan xammaqettanaw koshshishin neeni taakko yay?” yaagis.
Shin Yesuusi zaaridi, “Xoossay nuuppe koyabaa ubbaa nu polanaw bessiya gisho ha77i taw ero ga” yaagis. Yohaannisi iyaw ero gidi ekkis.
Yesuusi xammaqettida mela haathaafe keyis. Iirakka saloy dooyettin Xoossaa Ayyaanay holleda yishin qassi ba bolla wol77ammidi wodhdhishin be7is.
He wode “Ta dosiya, iyan tana ufayssiya ta na7ay hayssa” yaagiya qaalay saloppe yis.
Hessafe guye, Xalahey Yesuusa paaccana mela Geeshsha Ayyaanay Yesuusa bazzo biittaa efis.
Oytamu qammanne oytamu gallas xoomidaappe guye koshattis.
Xalahey Yesuusakko yidi “Neeni Xoossaa na7a gidikko, ane ha shuchchati uythi gidana mela kiitta” yaagis.
Yesuusi zaaridi, “ ‘Asi Xoossaa doonappe keyaa qaala ubban daanappe attin uytha xalaalan de7enna’ geetettidi Xoossaa qaalan xaafettis” yaagis.
Kaallidikka, Xalahey Yesuusa geeshsha katamaa efidi, Xoossaa keetha huu7iya kessidi,
“Neeni Xoossaa na7a gidikko, ane duge sa7an kundda. Ays giikko, ‘Ne tohoy shuchchan dhubetti deshettonna mela, bantta kushiyan nena denthana mela, Xoossay ba kiitanchchota ne gisho kiittana’ geetettidi Xoossaa qaalan xaafettis” yaagis.
Yesuusi iyaakko, “Qassika, ‘Xoossaa qaalan ne Godaa, ne Xoossaa paaccofa’ yaagettidi xaafettis” gidi zaaris.
Wurssethan Xalahey Yesuusa issi wolqqaama deriya huu7e kessidi alamiya kawotethata entta bonchchuwara issife bessidi,
“Ne taw kunddada goynniko ta new ha ubbaa immana” yaagis.
Yesuusi zaaridi, “Ha Xalahiyaw, taappe haakka! ‘Ne Godaa, ne Xoossaa goynna, iya xalaala haggaaza’ geetettidi Xoossaa qaalan xaafettis” yaagis.
Hessafe guye, Xalahey aggidi bis; kiitanchchoti yidi iya haggaazidosona.
Yesuusi, Yohaannisi qashettoyssa si7ida wode Galiila biittaa bis.
Naazirete katamaa aggidi Zaabiloonaninne Niftaaleme heeran, abbaa matan de7iya Qifirnahoome katamaa bidi yan de7is.
Hessi haniday nabiya Isayaasa doonan,
“Zaabiloone biittan, Niftaaleme biittan, Yorddaanose Shaafappe hefinthan, abbaa ogiya gaxan de7iya, Ayhude gidonna derey de7iya Galiilan,
dhuman de7iya derey, wolqqaama poo7o be7is. Hayqo kuya biittan, de7eyssatas poo7oy keyis” yaagidi odettida qaalay polettana melassa.
He wodeppe doomidi Yesuusi, “Xoossaa kawotethay matattida gisho hintte nagaraappe simmite” yaagidi qaala sabbakees.
Yesuusi Galiila Abbaa matara aadhdhishe nam77u ishata, Phexiroosa geetettiya Simoonanne iya ishaa Inddiriyasa be7is. Entti molo oykkeyssata gidida gisho bantta gitiya abban yeggoosona.
Yesuusi enttana, “Haa yiite; tana kaallite! Molo oythi attoshin, ta hinttena ase oythi tamaarssana” yaagis.
Enttika, ellesidi bantta gitiya yeggi aggidi Yesuusa kaallidosona.
Yesuusi yaappe buroo gede sinthe aadhdhishe hara nam77u ishata, Zabdiyoosa nayta, Yayqoobanne Yohaannisa be7is. Bantta aawa Zabdiyoosara issife wogoluwa giddon bantta gitiya giigiseyssata xeegis.
Enttika, ellesidi bantta wogoluwanne bantta aawa aggidi Yesuusa kaallidosona.
Yesuusi Ayhude Woosa Keethatan tamaarssishe, salo kawotethaa Wonggelaa odishenne dumma dumma harggiyafe asaa pathishe Galiila biitta ubban yuuyis.
Hessafe denddoyssan iya sunthay Sooriya biitta ubban keyis. Dumma dumma harggen oykettidayssatanne waayetteyssata, tuna ayyaanan oykettidayssata, shoci yeggiya harggen oykettidayssatanne, gunddata iyaakko ehidosona; ikka enttana pathis.
Asay Galiilappe, Tammu Katamatappe, Yerusalaameppe, Yihudappenne Yorddaanose Shaafaa hefinthan de7iya biittaafe yida daro asay iya kaallidosona.
Daro derey shiiqidayssa Yesuusi be7ida wode deriya bolla keyidi uttis. Iya tamaareti iyaakko shiiqin,
hayssada yaagidi tamaarssis:
“Bantta ayyaanan manqoti anjjettidayssata, salo kawotethay enttassa.
Yeekkeyssati anjjettidayssata, entti minthetho demmana.
Bantta wozanan ashkketi anjjettidayssata, entti sa7aa laattana.
Xillobaa oothanaw koshatteyssatinne saamotteyssati anjjettidayssata, entti kallana.
Maareyssati anjjettidayssata, entti maarotethi demmana.
Wozana geeshshati anjjettidayssata, entti Xoossaa be7ana.
Sigetheyssati anjjettidayssata, entti Xoossaa nayta geetetti xeegettana.
Xillobaa oothiya gisho gidi, goodetteyssati anjjettidayssata, salo kawotethay enttassa.
“Asay hinttena ta gisho gidi cayaa wode gooddiya wodenne hintte bolla iitabaa ubbaa worddon odisiya wode hintte anjjettidayssata.
Hintte woytoy salon gita gidiya gisho ufayttite, hashshu giite. Hinttefe kase de7iya nabeta hessada goodidosona.
“Hinttee biittaas maxine; maxiney ba maxinetethaa aggiko, ba mal77otethaa waati zaari demmanee? Kare holin asan yedhdhettanaappe attin aybiskka maaddenna.
“Hintte biittaas poo7o; dere bolla de7iya katamiya qosettanaw dandda7ukku.
Xomppe oythidi son de7iya asa ubbaas poo7ana mela dhoqqa son wotheesippe attin daallo gidon wothey baawa.
Hessa mela asay hintte lo77o oosuwa be7idi, salon de7iya hintte aawa bonchchana mela hintte poo7oy asa sinthan poo7o.
“Taani Muse higgiyanne nabeta qaala shaaranaw yida hinttew daanoppo. Taani, entti odidayssi tuma gideyssa qonccisanaw yasippe attin shaaranaw yabiikke.
Ta hinttew tuma odays; saloynne sa7ay aadhdhana gakkanaw higge ubbay polettanaappe attin higgiyafe issi qaalay woykko pidaaley aadhdhenna.
Hessa gisho, ha kiitatappe guuxiya issi kiitaa menthiya oonikka qassi harata hessatho oothana mela tamaarssey oonikka salo kawotethan ubbaafe guutha gidana. Shin ha kiitaa poleysinne haratakka polana mela tamaarssey salo kawotethan gita gidana.
Ta hinttew odays; hintte xillotethay Farisaaweta xillotethaafenne higge asttamaareta xillotethaafe aadhdhonna ixxiko, salo kawotethaa gelekketa.
“Hintte mayzatas, ‘Wodhoppite; shemppo wodhida oonikka pirddettana’ geetettoyssa si7ideta.
Shin ta hinttew odays; ba ishaa hanqettiya ubbay pirddettana. Ba ishaa cayaa oonikka daynna sinthi pirddas shiiqana. Ba ishaakko, ‘Eeyay’ giya oonikka qassi gaanname taman pirddettana.
“Hessa gisho, neeni ne yarshshuwa yarshshiya wode ne ishaa qohidabay new akeeketiko,
ne yarshshuwa he bessan aggada ba; koyrota bada ne ishaara giiga; yaata simmada, ne yarshshuwa Xoossaas yarshsha.
“Nena mooteyssara pirdda keethi bashe oge bolla iyara giiga. Hessi atto giikko I nena daynna sinthi efana. Daynnay nena qachcheyssas aathi immana; I nena woynen yeggana.
Ta tuma odays; ne bolla pirddettida accuwa issi santimey attonna cigga onggana gakkanaw qasho keethafe keyakka.
“Hayssafe kase, ‘Laymatoppite’ geetettoyssa si7ideta.
Shin ta hinttew odays, maccas xeellidi, amottida ubbay ba wozanan iira laymatees.
Ne ushachcha ayfey new nagaras gaaso gidikko, kessa hola. Ne asatethay kumethi gaanname taman wodhdhanaappe ne asatethaafe issoy dhayikko new lo77o.
Ne ushachcha kushey new nagaras gaaso gidikko, iya qanxa hola. Ne asatethay kumethi gaanname taman wodhdhanaappe ne asatethaafe issoy dhayikko, new lo77o.
“ ‘Ba machchiw yeddiya oonikka anjjo warqqatiya immo’ geetettis.
Shin ta hinttew odays; ba machchiya laymatonna de7ishin billiya oonikka iya laymatana mela oothees. Hessadakka, anjjettida maccasiw ekkiya ubbay laymatees.
“Hintte mayzatakko, ‘Worddon caaqqofite; hintte Xoossaa sinthan caaqqidayssa polite’ geetettidayssa si7ideta.
Shin ta hinttew odays; ubbarakka caaqqofite. Xoossay uttiya araata gidiya gisho salon caaqqofite.
Iya tohoy yedhdhiya soo gidiya gisho sa7ankka caaqqofite. Gita kawuwa katama gidiya gisho Yerusalaamenkka caaqqofite.
Hintte binaanappe issuwaka boothi woykko kareethi oothanaw dandda7onna gisho hinttee hintte huu7enkka caaqqofite.
Hessa gisho, hintte qaalay, ‘Ee’ woykko ‘Akkay’ gido. Hessafe kare keyey Xalaheppe yees.
“ ‘Ayfe gisho ayfe; achcha gisho achche’ geetettidayssa si7ideta.
Shin ta hinttew odays; hintte bolla iitabaa oothiya uraara eqettofite. Oonikka ne ushachcha shakalaa baqqiko ne haddirssa shakalaakka bessa.
Issi asi ne shaamiziya ekkanaw nena mootikko, ne kootiya gujjada imma.
Issi asi nena wolqqan babaa toossidi issi saate oge baara baana mela nena un77ethiko, iyara nam77u saate oge ba.
Woossiya ooddeskka imma; neeppe tal77anaw koyaa oonakka diggofa.
“ ‘Nena doseyssa dosa; nena ixxeyssa ixxa’ geetettoyssa si7ideta.
Shin ta hinttew odays; hintte morkketa dosite; hinttena qoheyssatas woossite.
Hessatho hintte oothiko, salon de7iya hintte aawas hintte nayta gidana. I iitatasinne lo77otas awa kessees; xillotasinne nagaranchchotas ba iraa bukisees.
Hinttena dosiya asaa xalaala hintte dosikko, hinttew ay woytoy de7ii? Hari attoshin, qaraxa qanxiseyssatikka hessa oothoosona.
Hinttee, hintte ishata xalaala sarothiko, haratappe ay hara aadhdhiyabaa oothidetii? Hari attoshin, Xoossaa ammanonna asaykka hessa oothoosona.
Hiza, salon de7iya hintte aaway polo gidoyssada hintteka polo gidite.
“Asi be7o gidi hintte lo77o oosuwa asa sinthan oothonnaada naagettite. Hessatho hanonna ixxiko salon de7iya hintte Aawappe woyto demmeketa.
“Hinttee manqotas immiya wode asa sinthan bonchchettanaw gidi cubboti ogiya doonaninne Ayhude Woosa Keethatan ootheyssada asi be7o gidi oothofite. Ta hinttew tuma odays; entti bantta kumetha woytuwa ekkidosona.
Shin hinttee manqotas immiya wode hintte ushachcha kushey ootheyssa hintte haddirssa kushey eroppo;
hintte imoy geeman gido. Geeman ootheyssa be7iya hintte aaway hinttew woytuwa qonccen immana.
“Woosa woossishe cubbotatho hanoppite. Entti, banttana asi be7o gidi Ayhude Woosa Keethaninne ogiya doonan eqqidi woosseyssa dosoosona. Ta hinttew tuma odays; entti bantta kumetha woytuwa ekkidosona.
Shin neeni woossiya wode ne soo gela, wulaa gorddada geeman de7iya ne Aawakko woossa; geeman oosettidayssa be7iya ne aaway new woytuwa immana.
Hintte woossiya wode ammanonna asaatho coo qaala darssidi woossofite. Entti adussi woossin Xoossay si7ees gidi qoppoosona.
Hessa gisho, enttayssada hanoppite. Ays giikko, hintte aaway hinttew ay koshshiyako hintte woossanaappe sinthattidi erees.
“Hiza, hintte yaagidi woossite: ‘Salon de7iya nu aawaw, ne geeshsha sunthay anjjetto.
Ne kawotethay yo, ne sheney salon hanidayssada sa7ankka hano.
Gallasa kathaa hachchi hachchi nuus imma.
Nuuni nuna qohidayssata, atto geyssada, nuuskka nu qohuwa atto ga.
Nuna iitappe ashshafe attin paacen gelssofa. [Kawotethay, wolqqaynne bonchchoy merinaw neessa. Amin77i.]’
“Hintte hinttena qohidayssata atto giikko, salon de7iya hintte Aaway hintte qohuwakka atto gaana.
Shin hintte hara asa nagara atto goonna ixxiko hintte Aaway hintte nagara atto geenna.
“Hintte xoomiya wode cubbotatho kayottofite. Ays giikko, entti xoomeyssa asi erana mela bantta som77uwa qitayoosona. Ta tuma odays; entti bantta woytuwa ekkidosona.
“Shin neeni xoomiya wode ne som77uwa meecca, ne huu7iya tiyetta.
Hessada ne oothiko ne xoomiya xoomay asappe geemmidayssa, shin geeman de7iya ne Aaway eriya xooma gidana. Geeman oosettidayssa be7iya ne Aaway new woytuwa immana.
“Bili miyason, biraati shi7iyason, kaysoy bookkidi ekkiyason, ha sa7an, hinttew shalo shiishoppite.
Shin bili moonason, biraati shi7onnason, kaysoy bookkidi ekkonnason salon hinttew shalo shiishite.
Ne shaloy de7iyasuwan ne wozanay de7ana.
“Ayfey asatethaas xomppe. Hessa gisho, ne ayfey paxa gidikko ne kumetha asatethay poo7o gidees.
Ne ayfey hargganchcho gidikko ne kumetha asatethay dhuma gidees. Hiza, nenan de7iya poo7oy dhuma gidikko, dhumay ay mela aadhdhidi dhumanddeshsha!
“Issi asi nam77u godas haarettanaw dandda7enna. Issuwa dosikko hankkuwa ixxees; woykko issuwa bonchchiko hankkuwa kadhees. Xoossasinne miishes haarettanaw dandda7ekketa.
“Hiza, si7ite! Hinttee de7on daanaw, ‘Ay maanee? Ay uyanee? Ay ma77anee?’ gidi un77ettofite; de7oy kathafe woykko ma7oppe aadhdhenee?
Salo kafota xeellite; entti zerokkona, buuccokona, shaalen yeggokona, shin hintte salo aaway entta muzees. Hintte enttafe keehi aadhdheketii?
Hintte giddofe daro un7ettidi ba laythaa bolla issi gallas gujjanaw dandda7ey de7ii?
“Qassi hintte ma77iyabaas ays un7ettetii? Ane ciishshata be7ite, ooson daaburokkona woykko suqqokona.
Si7ite! Hari attoshin, kawuwa Solomoney ba bonchcho ubban ha ciishshatappe issuwa melakka ma77ibeenna.
Hinttenoo, ammanoy paccidayssato, Xoossay hachchi benttidi wontto taman wodhdhanaw de7iya maata yaatidi mayziyabaa gidikko, hinttena enttafe aathidi waati mayzennee?
Hessa gisho, ‘Ay maanee? Ay uyanee? Ay ma77anee?’ gidi un77ettofite.
He ubbaa Xoossaa ammanonna asay darssidi demmanaw un77ettoosona. Hintte salo aaway he ubbay hinttew koshsheyssa erees.
Shin ubbaafe sinthe Xoossaa kawotethaanne iya xillotethaa koyite; he ubbay hinttew gujji imettana.
Hessa gisho, wonttos qoppishe un77ettofite. Wonttoyssi wonttos aqo; issi issi gallasay baw gidiya metora de7ees.
“Hintte bolla pirddettonna mela harata bolla pirddofite.
Ays giikko, harata bolla hintte pirddeyssada hintte bolla pirddettana; hintte haratas makkidaban hinttew zaari makettana.
Ne ayfen de7iya tuussu daaneyssa be7onna ne ishaa ayfen de7iya buuriya ays be7ay?
Ne ayfen tuussi de7ishin ne ishaa ayfen de7iya buuriya kesso gaanaw waana dandda7ay?
Neno cubbuwaw, koyrottada ne ayfen de7iya tuussi daaneyssa kessa. Iyappe guye, ne ishaa ayfen de7iya buuriya kessanaw ne geeshsha xeellana.
“Guye simmidi hinttena saxxonna mela geeshshabaa kanatas yeggofite. Bantta tohuwan yedhdhidi iissonna mela hintte al77o inquwa gudunthota sinthan yeggofite.
“Woossite hinttew imettana, koyite hintte demmana, kare yidi xeegite hinttew dooyettana.
Woossiya ooddeskka imettana, koyaa ooddeskka benttana, kare yidi xeegiya ooddeskka dooyettana.
“Hintte giddofe ba na7i uythi woossiko shuchchi immey oonee?
Woykko molo woossiko shooshi immey de7ii?
Yaatin hintte iita gidishe hintte naytas lo77obaa imo erikko, hintte salo aaway bana woosseyssatas lo77obaa waati darssidi immenee?
Harati hinttew oothana mela hintte koyabaa ubbaa hintteka haratas oothite. Ays giikko, Muse higgeynne nabeti tamaarssey hayssa.
“Xuuntha wulara gelite; ays giikko, dhayos efiya ogey wogga, wulaykka dalgga. Iyara geliya asaykka daro.
Shin de7uwakko efiya ogeynne wulay xuunthu; yaa geliya asaykka guutha.
“Bolla baggara dorsse daanidi bantta gaathan suudhume gididi hintte giddo geliya worddanchcho nabetappe naagettite.
Hintte entta, entta ayfiyaappe erana; agunthafe woyney, kinchchoteppe laadey maxettenna.
Hessa mela lo77o mithi ubbay lo77o ayfe ayfees; iita mithi iita ayfe ayfees.
Lo77o mithi iita ayfe ayfenna, qassi iita mithi lo77o ayfe ayfanaw dandda7enna.
Lo77o ayfe ayfonna mithi ubbay qanxettidi taman xuugettana.
Hessa gisho, hintte entta, entta ayfiyaan erana.
“Salon de7iya ta aawa sheniya oothiya uray salo kawotethi gelanaappe attin coo tana ‘Godaw, Godaw’ giya ubbay salo kawotethi gelenna.
Pirdda gallas daroti, ‘Godaw, Godaw, ne sunthan tinbbite odibookko? Ne sunthan tuna ayyaanata kessibookko? Ne sunthan malaatata oothibookkoo?’ yaagana.
He wode taani, ‘Ta hinttena ubbarakka erikke, hinttee iita ootheyssati taappe haakkite’ yaagana.
“Hiza, ha ta qaala si7idi oothiya oonikka ba keethaa shuchcha bolla keexida wozanaama asa mela.
Iray bukkis, di7oy di77is, carkkoyka carkkidi he keethaa sugis. Shin keethay shuchcha baaso bolla keexettida gisho kunddibeenna.
Ha ta qaala si7idi oothonna oonikka ba keethaa shafe bolla keexida eeya uraa mela.
Iray bukkidi, di7oy di77idi, carkkoyka carkkidi, he keethaa sugin, he keethay kunddis; iya kunddethaykka wolqqaama” yaagis.
Yesuusi ba oda onggida wode iya timirttey higge asttamaareta mela gidonna maatara gidiya gisho asay iya timirttiyan malaalettidosona.

Yesuusi deriyappe wodhdhiya wode daro asay iya kaallidosona.
Hekko issi baro hargganchchoy iyaakko shiiqidi, iya sinthan gulbbatidi, “Godaw, ne shene gidikko tana geeshshada pathanaw dandda7aasa” yaagis.
Yesuusi ba kushiya yeddidi iya bochchidi, “Ee, ta shene, paxa” yaagis. Uray iirakka geeyi aggis.
Yesuusi iyaakko, “Ne paxuwa ooddeskka odoppa. Shin bada ne geeyada paxoyssa kahine bessa. Ne paxuwas markka gidana mela bada Musey kiittida yarshshuwa yarshsha” yaagis.
Yesuusi Qifirnahoome katama gakkida wode issi mato halaqay iyaakko shiiqidi,
“Godaw, ta aylley asatethay gunddin daro harggettidi, son zin77idi de7ees” yaagidi woossis.
Yesuusi zaaridi, “Taani bada iya pathana” yaagis.
Shin mato halaqay zaaridi, “Godaw, ne ta soo gelanaw bessiya asi gidikke, shin ne han uttada qaala xalaala oda, ta aylley paxana.
Ays giikko, taappe bollara ta kiitettiya asati de7oosona, qassi taappe garssara taw kiitetteyssati de7oosona. Enttafe issuwa, ‘Ba’ giyade bees; hankkuwa qassi ‘Haaya!’ giyade yees. Ta aylliya, ‘Hayssa ootha’ giyade oothees” yaagis.
Yesuusi hessa si7ida wode malaalettidi, bana kaalliya asaakko, “Ta hinttew tuma odays; taani hayssa mela ammano Isra7eele asankka be7abiikke.
Ta hinttew odays; daroti dolohappenne wulohappe yidi, salo kawotethan Abrahamera, Yisaaqaranne Yayqoobara issife imato bolla uttana.
Shin salo kawotethaa laattanaw bessishin attidayssati kare dhuman holettana. Yan enttaw yeehonne achcha garccethi gidana” yaagis.
Yesuusi mato halaqaakko, “Ne soo ba, ne ammanuwatho new hano” yaagis. Iya aylley sohuwara paxi aggis.
Yesuusi Phexiroosa soo geliya wode Phexiroosa machche aayyaa qoxo misha harggen sakettada zin77idaaro be7is.
Yesuusi I kushiya bochchida wode qoxoynne mishay aggi aggis. Paxa denddada iya mokkasu.
He wode omarssi tuna ayyaanan oykettida daro asata, asay Yesuusakko ehidosona. Ikka tuna ayyaanata ba qaalan kessis, hargganchchota ubbaa pathis.
Hessankka nabiya Isayaasi, “I nu harggiya baw ekkis, i nu harggiya tookkis” gida qaalay polettis.
Yesuusi daro asay iya yuushuwan eqqidayssa be7idi, abbaafe hefinthi pinnana mela ba tamaareta kiittis.
Higge asttamaaretappe issoy, “Asttamaariyaw, ne biyaso ubbaa ta kaallana” yaagis.
Yesuusi iyaakko “Workkanatas olli de7ees, salo kafotas keethi de7ees. Shin Asa Na7aas ba huu7iya shemppisiya bessi baawa” yaagis.
Yesuusa kaalliya asatappe issoy, “Godaw, taani sinthata bada ta aawa moogada yaana” yaagis.
Shin Yesuusi, “Hayqqidayssati bantta hayqota moogo; neeni tana kaalla” yaagis.
Yesuusi baanaw wogoluwan gelida wode iya tamaaretikka iyara baanaw gelidosona.
Entti qopponna de7ishin, wolqqaama hobbey haatha bolla denddin wogoloy mitettanaw gakkis. Shin Yesuusi dhiskkis.
Iya tamaareti iyaakko shiiqidi iya barkkethidi, “Godaw, nu dhayos nuna ashsharkkii” yaagidosona.
Yesuusi enttako, “Hinttenoo, ammanoy paccidayssato, ays yayyetii?” yaagis. Denddidi, hobbiyanne gotiya essis. Ellesidi ubbabay si77i gis.
Iya tamaareti malaalettidi, “Hayssi, hari attoshin, hobbeynne gotey kiitetteyssi waanida asee?” yaagidosona.
Yesuusi abbaafe hefinthan de7iya Gerggesoone giya biittaa gakkida wode tuna ayyaanay oykkida nam77u asati duufoppe keyidi iyara gahettidosona. Entti daro iitanne yashshiya asata gidiya gisho asi he bessaara aadhdhanaw dandda7enna.
Enttika, “Xoossaa Na7aw, nunanne nena aybe gathey? Wodey gakkonna de7ishin nuna pirddanaw yadii?” gidi waassidosona.
Enttafe daro haakkonna guduntho wudey heemettes.
Tuna ayyaanati Yesuusa, “Ne nuna kessanabaa gidikko, hini guduntho wudiya giddo yeddarkkii” yaagidi woossidosona.
Yesuusi, “Biite” yaagis. Tuna ayyaanati asatappe keyidi gudunthotan gelidosona. Gudunthoti ubbay aafo doonara dirggidi bidi abban mitettidi hayqqidosona.
Guduntho wudiya heemmeyssati baqatidi katama bidi, hanidabaanne tuna ayyaanay oykkida asata bolla oosettidaba ubbaa odidosona.
Yaatin, kataman de7iya asa ubbay Yesuusa be7anaw keyidosona. Entti Yesuusa be7ida wode bantta biittaafe keyidi baana mela woossidosona.
Hessafe guye, Yesuusi wogoluwan gelidi, abbaa pinnidi ba katamaa bis.
Hanida guutha asati issi gundda uraa alggara tookkidi Yesuusakko ehidosona. Yesuusi entta ammanuwa be7idi, gundda uraa, “Ta na7aw, yayyofa! Ne nagaray atto geetettis” yaagis.
He saatiyan, Ayhude higge asttamaaretappe issoti issoti, “Hayssi Xoossaa cashshe gidennee” yaagidi bantta wozanan qoppidosona.
Yesuusi entta qofaa eridi, “Iitabaa hintte wozanan ays qoppeetii?
Hanoshin, ‘Ne nagaray atto geetettis’ geyssafenne ‘Dendda eqqada ba’ geyssafe awussi kawuyii?
Shin sa7a bolla nagara atto gaanaw Asa Na7aas maati de7eyssa ta hinttena erisana” yaagidi, gundda addiyako, “Dendda eqqa, ne alggaa tookkada, ne soo ba” yaagis.
Gundda uray denddidi ba soo bis.
Derey hessa be7idi malaalettidosona. Hessa mela maata asas immida Xoossaa galatidosona.
Yesuusi yaappe denddidi bishe Maatoosa geyssa qaraxa qanxisiya bessan uttidashin be7idi, “Tana kaalla” yaagis. Ikka denddidi kaallis.
Yesuusi Maatoosa son gayta bolla uttidashin, qaraxa qanxisiya daro asatinne nagaranchchoti yidi iyaranne iya tamaaretara issife maanaw uttidosona.
Issi issi Farisaaweti hessa be7idi, Yesuusa tamaareta, “Hintte asttamaarey qaraxa qanxiseyssataranne nagaranchchotara ays mii?” yaagidosona.
Yesuusi hessa si7idi, “Dhale koshshey haragganchchotassafe attin paxatassa gidenna.
Shin hintte bidi, ‘Taani hintte yarshshuwa gidonnashin hintte harata maarana mela koyays’ geetettidi xaafettidayssi woy guusseeko erite. Ays giikko, taani nagaranchchota xeeganaw yasippe attin xillota xeeganaw yabiikke” yaagis.
He wode Yohaannisa tamaareti Yesuusakko shiiqidi, “Nunne Farisaaweti xoomos, shin ne tamaareti ays xoomokkonaa?” yaagidi oychchidosona.
Yesuusi zaaridi enttako, “Mushuray enttara de7ishin xeegettidi yida asay kayottanaw dandda7oona? Mushuray entta matappe ekettana wodey yaana, entti he wode xoomana.
“Ooratha ma7oppe peedhidi gal77a ma7o bolla sikkey oonikka baawa. Hessatho oothiko oorathay gal77aa peedhees. Peedhethayka gujji dalggees.
Ooratha woyne gal77a ogoron qoliya oonikka baawa. Hessatho oothiko ooratha woyney gal77a ogoruwa dhusees woyneykka gukkees; ogoroykka nam77antho maaddonnabaa gidees. Shin ooratha woyney ooratha ogoron qoletanaw bessees. Hessatho oosettiko nam77ayka iitonna naagettoosona” yaagis.
Yesuusi hessa odo bolla de7ishin, Ayhude halaqatappe issoy iyaakko yidi, iya sinthan gulbbatidi, “Ta na7iya ha77i hayqqasu, shin iya paxana mela neeni yada ne kushiya I bolla wotharkkii” gidi woossis.
Yesuusi denddidi iyara bis; iya tamaaretikka kaallidosona.
I bishin tammanne nam77u laythi kumethi suuthi goggidi waaysiya issi maccasiya guyera shiiqada Yesuusa afilaa macaraa bochchasu.
Iya ba wozanan, “Ta iya afilaa macaraa xalaala bochchiyakko paxana” yaagada qoppasu.
Yesuusi guye simmi iyo xeellidi, “Ta naatte, yayyofa! Nena ne ammanoy pathis” yaagis. Maccasiya sohuwara paxa aggasu.
Yesuusi Ayhude halaqaa soo gakkiya wode zaye punneyssatanne yeekkeyssata be7idi,
“Ane kichchite; guutha na7iya dhiskkasuppe attin hayqqabuukku” yaagis. Shin asay iya bolla miicidosona.
Asaa kare kessidaappe guye soo gelidi, na7ee kushiya oykkis, na7iya dendda eqqasu.
He worey he biitta ubbaa gakkis.
Yesuusi yaappe denddidi gede sinthe biya wode nam77u qooqeti bantta qaala dhoqqu oothidi, “Dawite na7aw, nuna maararkii” yaagishe iya kaallidosona.
Yesuusi soo gelida wode qooqeti iya kaallidi yidosona. Yesuusi enttako, “Taani hessa oothanaw dandda7eyssa hintte ammaneetii?” yaagis. Enttika, “Ee, Godaw” yaagidi zaaridosona.
Hessafe guye, Yesuusi entta ayfiyaa bochchidi enttako, “Hinttew, hintte ammanuwatho hano” yaagis.
Entta ayfeykka dooyettis. Yesuusi enttako, “Hayssa ooddeskka odoppite” yaagidi minthi odis.
Shin asati bidi Yesuusabaa he biitta ubban odidosona.
Entti yaappe keyaa wode asay tuna ayyaanay oykkidi muumisida issi asi Yesuusakko ehidosona.
Tuna ayyaanay keyidaappe guye muume uray odettis. Dereykka malaalettidi, “Hayssa mela oorathabay Isra7eele biittan hanibeenna” yaagidosona.
Shin Farisaaweti, “Tuna ayyaanata halaqan tuna ayyaanata kessees” yaagidosona.
Yesuusi Ayhude Woosa Keethatan tamaarssishe, salo kawotethaa Wonggelaa sabbakishe, asaa hargge ubbaafe pathishe katamataninne guta ubban yuuyis.
Daro derey, heemmiya asi baynna dorssada enttana be7iya asi dhayin un77ettidi de7eyssata be7idi enttaw qadhettis.
Ba tamaaretakko, “Shiiqana kathay daro, shin kathaa shiishiya asay guutha.
Hessa gisho, Goday kathaa shiishiya oosanchchota yeddana mela woossite” yaagis.
Yesuusi tammanne nam77u tamaareta baakko xeegidi, tuna ayyaanata kessana melanne hargge ubbaa pathana mela enttaw maata immis.
Yesuusi kiittida tammanne nam77u hawaareta sunthay: koyroy Phexiroosa giya Simoonanne iya ishaa Inddiriyasa, Zabdiyoosa na7aa Yayqoobanne iya ishaa Yohaannisa,
Filphoosanne Bartolomiyoosa, Toomasanne qaraxa qanxisiya Maatoosa, Ilfiyoosa na7aa Yayqooba, Taadiyosa,
ba biittaas mishettiya Simoonanne Yesuusa aathi immida Asqoroota Yihuda.
He tammanne nam77ata Yesuusi kiittidi yeddishe, “Ayhude gidonna deriyakko booppite, qassi Samaareta katamakka geloppite.
Shin Isra7eele keethaafe gidida hini dhayida dorssatakko biite.
Yaa bidi, ‘Salo kawotethay matattis’ gidi odite.
Hargganchchota pathite, hayqqidayssata hayqoppe denthite, baro hargganchchota geeshshi pathite, tuna ayyaanata kessite. Hintte coo ekkidayssa coo immite.
Hintte kiisen worqqa, woykko bira santime oykkofite.
Hintte ogiyas karxiito, nam77u afila, woykko caamma woykko xam77a oykkofite; oosanchchuwas gallasa kathi koshshees.
“Hintte issi katamaa woykko gutaa geliya wode hinttena mokkidi ekkanaw ufayttiya uraa koyidi iya son shemppite; hintte baana gakkanaw yan gam77ite.
Qassi oodde sookka gelishe sarothite.
He keethay hinttena mokkiko hintte sarothida saroy enttana gakko, shin entti mokkonna ixxiko hintte sarothida saroy hinttew guye simmo.
Oonikka hinttena mokkonnanne hintte odiyabaa si7onna ixxiko he keethaafe woykko he katamaappe keyishe hintte tohuwan de7iya baana pittidi keyite.
Ta hinttew tuma odays; Xoossaa pirdda gallasan he katamaappe Soodomesinne Gamoora katamatas pirdday kawuyana.
“Ta hinttena dorssatada suudhumeta giddo yeddana. Hessa gisho, shooshada cinccata, holleda aadata gidite.
Asay hinttena pirdda daynnatas aathi immana, qassi Ayhude Woosa Keethan hinttena garaafana. Hessa gisho, enttafe naagettite.
Ta gisho gidi hinttena deriya haareyssata sinthenne kawota sinthe efana. Entta sinthaninne Ayhude gidonna deriya sinthan eqqidi hintte tabaa markkattana.
Shin hinttena pirddas aathi immiya wode woygidi zaarino gidi un77ettofite; he saatiyan hintte gaanabaa Xoossay hinttew immana.
Ays giikko, hinttenan haasayey hintte Aawa Geeshsha Ayyaanaappe attin hinttena gidekketa.
“Ishay ba ishaa, aaway ba na7aa, hayqos aathi immana, nayti banttana yelidayssata bolla denddidi enttana wodhisana.
Ta gisho gidi asa ubbay hinttena ixxana, shin wurssethi gakkanaw minniday attana.
Issi heerappe hinttena entti gooddiko hara katama baqatite. Taani hinttew tuma odays; Asa Na7ay yaana gakkanaw, hintte Isra7eele katama ubbaa kantheketa.
“Tamaarey ba asttamaariyappe, aylley ba godaappe aadhdhenna.
Tamaarey ba asttamaariya, aylley ba godaa daanikko iyaw gidana. Keethaawa Bi7elzebuula giikko iya soo asaa waanidi iissidi xeegenne?
“Hiza, asas yayyofite. Kamettidabay qoncconna, qosettidabay geeshshi keyonna attenna.
Taani hinttew dhuman odiyabaa hintte poo7on odite; ta hinttew haythan kalkkashidabaa dabaaban awaajjite.
Ashoppe attin shemppo wodhanaw dandda7onnayssatas yayyofite. Shin shemppuwanne ashuwa gaannamen dhayssanaw dandda7iya Xoossaas yayyite.
Nam77u buubbeti issi santimen bayzettokonaayye? Hanoppe attin, enttafe issinnaka hintte Xoossay goonna de7ishin sa7an wodhdhuku.
Hari attoshin, hintte huu7e binaanaykka paydettidi de7ees.
Hiza, daro buubbetappe hintte aadhdhiya gisho yayyofite.
“Asa sinthan taw markkattiya ubbaas taanikka saluwan de7iya ta aawa sinthan markkattana.
Shin asa sinthan tana kaddeyssa taanikka salon de7iya ta aawa sinthan kaddana.
“Taani sa7an saro ehanaw yida hinttew daanoppo. Taani toorappe attin sarotethi ehanaw yabiikke.
Taani yiday, ‘Na7aa aawappe macca na7iw aayeppe na7aa machchiw azina aayeppe shaakkanaassa.
Asas morkketi iya soo asata gidana.’
“Taappe aathidi ba aawa woykko ba aayiw dosey, tabaa gidanaw bessenna. Ba adde na7a woykko ba macca na7iw taappe aathidi dosey, tabaa gidanaw bessenna.
Ba masqaliya tookkidi tana kaallonna oonikka tabaa gidanaw bessenna.
Ba shemppuwa ashshanaw koyey dhayssana, shin ba shemppuwa ta gisho aathi immey ashshana.
“Hinttena mokkey tana mokkees, tana mokkey qassi tana kiittidayssa mokkees.
Nabiya nabe sunthan mokkey, nabiyatho woytettana; qassi xilluwa xillo sunthan mokkey, xilluwatho woytettana.
Ta hinttew tuma odays; ha ta tamaaretappe guuxiya issuwas tana kaalliya gisho hari attoshin guutha irxxa haathi immiko iya woytoy dhayenna” yaagis.
Yesuusi tammanne nam77u tamaareta kiitaa onggidaappe guye yaappe denddidi tamaarssanawunne sabbakanaw Galiila katamata bis.
Yohaannisi qasho keethan de7ishe Kiristtoosi oothiyabata si7idi, ba tamaaretappe iyaakko kiittidi,
“Yaana geetettiday neneyye? Woykko nuuni haraa naaginoo?” yaagidi oychchis.
Yesuusi enttako zaaridi, “Bidi hintte si7iyabaanne hintte be7iyabaa Yohaannisas odite.
Qooqeti xeellosona, wobbeti hamuttoosona, baro hargganchchoti paxoosona, tulleti si7oosona, hayqqidayssati hayqoppe denddoosona; manqotas Wonggelay sabbakettees.
Tanan dhubettonay anjjettidayssa” yaagis.
Yohaannisa tamaareti guye simmidi bin, Yesuusi deriyas Yohaannisabaa odishe, “Ha bazzuwa ay be7anaw keyidetii? Carkkoy qaathiya maqqaa be7anaw yidetiyye?
Yaatin, ay be7anaw keyidetii? Kitte ma7o ma77ida ase be7anaaseyye? Kitte ma7o ma77idayssati kawota keethan de7oosona.
Yaatin, ay be7anaw keyidetii? Nabe be7anaaseyye? Hekko, hintte nabeppekka aadhdheyssa be7eeta.
“Ne ogiya ne sinthan giigisiya ta kiitanchchuwa neeppe sinthe kiittana” geetettidi xaafettiday iyassa.
Ta hinttew tuma odays; maccasappe yelettidayssata giddofe Yohaannisappe aadhdhey oonikka baawa; salo kawotethan ubbaafe guuxey I, iyappe aadhdhana.
Xammaqiya Yohaannisa wodiyappe doomidi hachchi gakkanaw salo kawotethay daro naaqettees, minnida asati wolqqan yaa gelana.
Nabeti ubbaynne Muse higgey Yohaannisa wode gakkanaw salo kawotethaabaa tinbbite odidosona.
Hiza, hintte entta kiitaa ammanana gidikko, yaana geetettida Eliyaasi, I Yohaannisa.
Hiza, si7iya haythi de7ey si7o.
“Hiza, ha wodiya yeletethaa aybira daaniso? Giya giddon uttidi woli xeegidi,
‘Nu hinttew suusul77e punnin; hintte yexxeketa. Nu sabbidi zeleelin; hintte yeekkeketa’ yaagiya nayta daanosona.
Xammaqiya Yohaannisi moonnanne uyonna yin, ‘Tuna ayyaani de7ees’ yaagideta.
Asa Na7ay mishenne uyishe yin, ‘Yarambbanne ushshanchcho, qaraxa qanxiseyssatanne nagaaranchchota dabbo’ yaagideta. Hiza, cinccatethaa tumatethay iya oosuwan qonccees” yaagis.
Hessafe guye, Yesuusi daro malaatata oothida katamatan de7iya asati bantta nagaraappe simmidi maarotan gelonna ixxida gisho enttana,
“Ayye Koraaziine katamaw, ayye Beetesayda katamaw, ays giikko, hintte giddon oosettida malaatati Xiroosaninne Sidoonan oosettida gidiyakko, entti beni bido tiyettidi, kalle ma77idi bantta nagaraappe simmi aggana.
Shin ta hinttew odays; pirdda gallas hinttefe aathidi Xiroosasinne Sidoonas pirdday kawuyana.
Qassi, Qifirnahoome, neeni pude salo keyanaw koyay? Hanenna! Neeni Si7oolen yegettana. Ays giikko, ne giddon oosettida malaatati Soodomen oosettidabaa gidiyakko, Soodomey hachchi gakkanaw de7anashin.
Shin ta new odays; pirdda gallas neeppe aathidi Soodomes pirdday kawuyana” yaagidi hanqettis.
He wode Yesuusi, “Aawaw, saluwanne sa7aa Godaw, neeni hayssa eranchchotappenne cinccatappe genthada naytas qonccisida gisho nena galatays.
Ee, ta Aawaw, hayssi ne lo77o sheniyada hanis.
“Ubbay taw ta Aawappe imettis. Aawappe hari Na7aa erey baawa, Na7aappenne I enttaw qonccisanaw koyeyssatappe hari Aawa eranaw dandda7ey baawa.
“Hinttenoo, daaburanchchoto, toohoy deexida ubbay taakko haa yiite; taani hinttena shemppisana.
Taani ta wozanan ashkkenne aada gidiya gisho ta qambbaran gelite, taappe tamaarite; hinttee, hintte shemppuwas shemppo demmana.
Ta qambbaray liiqo, qassi ta toohoykka kawushshe” yaagis.
Hessafe guye, Sambbaata gallas, Yesuusi gade giddora aadhdhees. Yesuusa tamaareti koshattida gisho tiya bangga shirikidi moosona.
Shin Farisaaweti hessa be7idi Yesuusakko, “Hekko, ne tamaareti Sambbaata gallas oothanaw bessonnabaa oothoosona” yaagidosona.
Yesuusi enttako zaaridi, “Dawitey koshattida wode Iyara de7eyssatara ay oothidaakko nabbabibeekketii?
Dawitey Xoossaa keethi gelidi kahineta xalaalappe attin inne iyara de7eyssatas bessonna geeshsha daabbuwa mis.
Woykko kahineti Sambbaata wogaa shaaridi Xoossa Keethan Sambbaata gallas ooso oothiko enttaw bala gidonnayssa Muse higgiyan nabbabibeekketii?
Shin si7ite! Xoossa Keethaafe aadhdhey hayssan de7ees.
‘Taani hintte yarshshuwa gidonnashin hintte harata maarana mela koyays’ giya qaalay woy guusseeko hintte eridaakko xillo asa bolla pirddeketa.
Asa Na7ay Sambbaata Godaa” yaagis.
Yesuusi yaappe bidi Ayhude Woosa Keethi gelis.
Yan kushey gunddida issi uray de7ees. Yesuusa mootanaw gaaso koyaa asati, “Sambbaata gallas pathanaw bessi bessennee?” yaagidi oychchidosona.
I enttako, “Hintte giddofe issuwas dorssi Sambbaata gallas aafon wulliko, goochchidi kessonnay oonee?
Yaatin asi dorssafe waanidi daro aadhdhenee? Hessa gisho, Sambbaata gallas lo77obaa oosoy bessees” yaagis.
Hessafe guye, Yesuusi addiyako, “Ne kushiya piddi ootha” yaagin, uray piddi oothis. Iya kushey paxidi hankko kushiyada hanis.
Shin Farisaaweti yaappe kare keyidi, Yesuusa waati wodhaneekko maqettidosona.
Yesuusi entta qofaa eridi he bessaa aggidi hara soo bis. Daro asay iya kaallidi bidosona, hargganchchota ubbaa pathis.
Yesuusi, “Tabaa hara ooddeskka odoppite” yaagidi minthi odis.
Hessika nabiya Isayaasi,
“Hekko ta doorida aylley, ta doseyssi, tana ufaysseyssi, taani ta ayyaanaa, iya bolla shemppisana; I, Ayhude gidonna deriyas suure pirddabaa awaajjana.
I palamenna woykko kaccenna; ba qaalakka denbban coo sissenna.
Suure pirddan xoono demmana gakkanaw, dinccettida maqqaa menthenna, cuyiya muqaadaa toysenna.
Ayhude gidonna derey ubbay iyan ufayssi wothana” yaagidi xaafidayssi polettana melassa.
Hessafe guye, tuna ayyaanan oykettida qooqenne muume ase de7eyssa iyaakko ehidosona. Yesuusi uraa pathin, uray be7isinne odettis.
Asa ubbay malaalettidi, “Hayssi Dawite Na7aa gidanddeshshaa?” yaagidosona.
Shin Farisaaweti hessa si7idi, “Ha uray tuna ayyaanata kessey tuna ayyaanata halaqaa Bi7elzebuula wolqqaana” yaagidosona.
Yesuusi entta qofaa eridi, “Woli giddon shaakettiya kawotetha ubbay kunddana; qassi woli giddon shaakettiya katamay woykko keethay minnidi eqqenna.
Xalahey Xalahe kessiyabaa gidikko ba giddon shaakettis guussu. Hessatho haniyabaa gidikko iya kawotethay waanidi minnidi eqqanaw dandda7ii?
Taani tuna ayyaanaa kessey Bi7elzebuula wolqqan gidikko hinttena kaalliya asati oodde wolqqan kessannee? Hessa gisho, hinttena kaalliya asati hinttena pirddana.
Shin taani tuna ayyaanata kessey Xoossaa Ayyaanan gidikko, Xoossaa kawotethay hintteko yis.
“Woykko issi asi wolqqaama asa soo gelidi iya shaluwa bonqanaw koykko koyrottidi he uraa qachchonna ixxiko waattidi dandda7ii? Yaatikko iya shaluwa bonqanaw dandda7ees.
“Taara gidonnay oonikka taara eqettees; qassi taara issife shiishonna ubbay laallees.
Hessa gisho, si7ite; asay oothiya ay nagarinne cashsha qaali ubbay atto geetettana, shin Geeshsha Ayyaana cayaa ooddeskka iya nagaray atto geetettenna.
Oonikka Asa Na7a bolla iitabaa odettiko iyaw atto geetettana, shin Geeshsha Ayyaana bolla iitabaa odettiya ooddeskka ha sa7an gidin yaana alamiyan iya nagaray atto geetettenna.
“Lo77o mithay lo77o ayfe ayfees; qassi iita mithay iita ayfees. Hiza, mithay erettey ba ayfiyaana.
Hinttenoo, shoosha nayto, hintte iita gidishe waanidi lo77obaa odettanaw dandda7etii? Asi ba wozanan kumidabaappe doonan odettees.
Lo77o asi ba wozanan wothida lo77obaappe, lo77obaa kessees; iita asi ba wozanan wothida iitabaappe, iitabaa kessees.
Shin si7ite, asay odettiya coo oda ubbaas pirdda gallas zaaro immana.
Ays giikko, ne odettiya ne qaalan xillana; ne odettiya ne qaalay ne bolla pirddana” yaagis.
Hessafe guye, issi issi Farisaawetinne higge asttamaareti Yesuusakko, “Asttamaariyaw, neeni malaata oothada nuna bessa” yaagidosona.
Shin Yesuusi zaaridi, “Ammanettonnanne iita yeletethay malaata koyees. Shin nabiya Yoonasa malaatappe hara malaati iyaw imettena.
Yoonasi gita molo ulon heedzu gallasinne heedzu qamma gam77idayssa mela Asa Na7ay heedzu gallasinne heedzu qamma biitta garssan gam77ana.
Nanawe asay pirdda gallas denddidi ha yeletethaa bolla pirddana; ays giikko, entti Yoonasa sibkkatiya si7idi bantta nagaraappe simmidosona. Hekko, Yoonasappe aadhdheyssi hayssan de7ees.
Pirdda gallas dugeha kawiya denddada ha yeletethaa bolla pirddana; ays giikko, iya Solomone cinccatethaa si7anaw biittaa gaxappe yasu. Hekko, Solomoneppe aadhdhey hayssan de7ees.
“Tuna ayyaanay asappe keyidaappe guye baw shemppiyaso koyidi haathi baynna mela bessan daaburees, shin ba koyaa shemppuwa demmenna.
Yaanin, ‘Ta agga keyida keetha simmada baana’ yaagees. I simmiya wode keethay kaysi gideyssanne pitettidi giigi uttidayssa demmees.
Hiza, simmi bidi, baappe iitiya hara laappun iita ayyaanata ekkidi yees; enttika uraa giddo gelidi de7oosona. He uraas kaseyssafe guyeyssi daro iitees. Ha iita yeletethaa bolla hessa mela hanana” yaagis.
Yesuusi deriyas oda bolla de7ishin iya aayyaanne iya ishati iya odisanaw koyidi karen eqqidosona.
Issi asi iyaakko, “Ne aayyaanne ne ishati nena odisanaw koyidi karen eqqidosona” yaagis.
Yesuusi zaaridi, “Ta aayyaa oonee? Ta ishatikka oonantee?” yaagis.
Ba kushiyara tamaareta mallishe, “Be7ite, ta aayanne ta ishati hayssata.
Salon de7iya ta Aawa sheniya oothiya ubbay ta isha, ta michchonne ta aayo” yaagis.
He gallas Yesuusi sooppe keyidi abbaa gaxan uttis.
Daro derey iya yuushuwan shiiqin asaa abbaa gaxan aggaagidi wogolon gelidi uttis.
Asaas darobaa leemison yaagidi odis: “Issi goshshanchchoy zerethi zeranaw keyis.
I zeriya wode issi issi zerethati oge gaxan wodhdhidosona; enttaka kafoti yidi maxi midosona.
Issi issi zerethati garssan shaalloy de7iya biitta bolla wodhdhidosona. Daro biitti baynna gisho ellesidi dolis.
Shin away keyin shullis; xaphoy baynna gisho melis.
Issi issi zerethay aguntha giddon wodhdhis; agunthay diccidi he dolaa cuullis.
Harati qassi aradda biitta bolla wodhdhis; dolidi ayfe ayfis. Issoy xeeta, issoy usuppun tamma, issoy qassi hasttama ayfis.
Si7iya haythi de7iya uray si7o” yaagis.
Yesuusa tamaareti iyaakko shiiqidi, “Ays neeni deriyas leemison oday?” yaagidi oychchidosona.
I zaaridi, “Hinttew salo kawotethaa xuuraa eray imettis, shin enttaw imettibeenna.
De7iya ubbaas guzhettana, iyaw darana, shin baynnayssafe hari attoshin iyaw de7iyarakka ekettana.
Hessa gisho, taani entti, xeellishe demmonna mela, si7ishe si7onna mela woykko akeekonna mela enttaw leemison odays.
“Isayaasi ba maxaafan odidayssi entta bolla polettis. I odishe, ‘Hintte sissaa si7eeta, shin akeekekketa; hintte xeelleta, shin be7ekketa.
Ays giikko, ha asaa wozanay zel77umis; bantta haythaa erishe tullisidosona, bantta ayfiyaa goozidosona. Hessi baynneeko entti bantta ayfiyaan be7idi, bantta haythan si7idi, bantta wozanan akeekidi, taakko simmana, takka entta pathanashin’ yaagis.
“Shin hintte ayfeti be7iya gishonne hintte haythati si7iya gisho hintte anjjettidayssata.
Ta hinttew tuma odays; daro nabetinne xillo asati hintte be7eyssa be7anawunne hintte si7eyssa si7anaw amottidosona, shin enttaw hanibeenna.
“Hiza, ha zerethaa zeriya uraa leemisuwa si7ite.
Oge gaxan wodhdhida zerethaa leemisoy hayssa: salo kawotethaa qaala si7idi akeekonna uraa wozanappe Xalahey yidi iya wozanan de7iya zerethaa maxi digees.
Shaalloy garssan de7iya biitta bolla zerettidayssi qaala si7idi ellesidi ufaysan ekkeyssata.
Shin xapho yeddanaw dandda7onna gisho daro gam77okona. Qaala gaason metoy woykko goodetethi yaa wode ellesi dhubettoosona.
Aguntha gaathan zerettidayssi qaala si7is, shin ha alamiya duussaa hirggaynne duretetha qofay qaala cuulliya gisho ayfe ayfonna attees.
Shin aradda biittan zerettida zerethay akeekan qaala si7iya uraa. I ayfe ayfees; issoy xeeta, issoy usuppun tamma issoy qassi hasttama ayfees” yaagis.
Yesuusi enttaw hara leemiso odis, “Xoossaa kawotethay ba goshshan lo77o zerethi zerida uraa daanees.
Shin asi ubbay dhiskkin iya morkkey yidi gisttiya giddon leeshsho zeridi bis.
Gisttey diccidi ayfiyaa wode leeshshoy iya giddon benttis.
“Gadiya godaa aylleti godaakko bidi, ‘Godaw, ne goshshan ne lo77o zerethi zerabikkishsho? Yaatin, leeshshoy awuppe yidee?’ yaagidosona.
“I enttako, ‘Hessa morkkey oothis’ yaagis. “Aylleti godaakko, ‘Nu bidi leeshshuwa shoddana mela koyay?’ yaagidosona.
“Shin I, ‘Atto bochchofite; hintte leeshshuwa shoddays gishin gisttey shodettana.
Bochchofite; caka wodey gakkanaw issife dicco. He wode cakkiya asata leeshshuwa sinthattidi maxidi taman xuugganaw mirqen mirqen qachchite. Shin gisttiya shiishidi ta shaaliyan qolite’ yaagana” yaagis.
Qassi hara leemiso yaagidi odis; “Salo kawotethay issi asi ba goshshan bakkida guutha mithee ayfe daanees.
He mithee ayfey hara mitha ayfetappe guutha, shin iya dolaa diccida hara mithata ubbaafe aadhdha gitatawusu. I tashiyan kafoti keexidi uttana gakkanaw wolqqaama mithi gidawusu” yaagis.
Kaallidikka, Yesuusi hara leemiso odis; “Salo kawotethay issi maccasi heedzu gabate dhiille ekka munuqada, munuqay denddana mela iyan gujjida irshsho daanees” yaagis.
Yesuusi deriyas he leemisuwa ubbaa odis. Leemisoy baynna issibaakka odibeenna.
Nabey ba maxaafan, “Taani ta doona, leemison dooyana; saloynne sa7ay medhettosappe, geemmidayssa odays” yaagidi odidayssi hessan polettis.
Yesuusi deriya moyzidi soo gelis. Iya tamaareti iyaakko shiiqidi, “Goshshan de7iya leeshshuwa birshshethaa nuus oda” yaagidosona.
I zaaridi, “Lo77o zerethaa zeriday Asa Na7a.
Goshshay ha alamiya. Lo77o zerethay salo kawotethaa nayta. Leeshshoy Xalahe nayta.
Leeshshuwa zeriday morkkiya Xalahe. Caka wodey, wodiya wurssethaa. Cakkeyssati kiitanchchota.
“Leeshshoy maxettidi taman xuugetteyssa mela wodiya wurssethan hessada hanana.
Asa Na7ay ba kiitanchchota kiittana. Entti nagaras gaaso gideyssatanne iita oothiya ubbaa maxidi iya kawotethaafe kessana.
Maxi shiishidi yeehoynne achcha garccethi de7iya to7onna taman yeggana.
He wode xilloti bantta Aawa kawotethan awada poo7ana. Si7iya haythi de7ey si7o!
“Xoossaa kawotethay goshshan moogettida miishe daanees. Issi asi he miishiya demmidi zaari moogis. Daro ufayttidi bidi baw de7iyaba ubbaa bayzidi he goshsha gadiya shammis.
“Hessadakka, qassi salo kawotethay inqo giya al77o shuchchata koyaa zal77anchcho daanees.
Daro al77o inquwa demmidi bidi baw de7iyaba ubbaa bayzidi iya shammis.
“Qassi Xoossaa kawotethay abban yegettida dumma dumma qommo molo oykkiya gitiya daanees.
Molo oykkiya asati moloy gitiyan kumin abbaafe gaxa kessidosona. Yan uttidi lo77uwa qori qori daachchon yeggidosona, shin iita molota wora holidosona.
Wodiya wurssethan hessatho hanana. Kiitanchchoti yidi nagaranchchota xillotappe shaakkidi,
yeehoynne achcha garccethi de7iya to7onna taman yeggana.
“Ha ubbay hinttew gelidee?” yaagidi entta oychchis. Entti zaaridi, “Ee” yaagidosona.
Yesuusi, “Hiza, salo kawotethaa eraa ekkidi higgiya tamaarssiya ubbay, ba minjjida shaluwappe oorathaanne gal77a kessiya ase daanees” yaagis.
Yesuusi ha leemisuwa odi wurssidaappe guye yaappe denddidi bis.
Ba yelettida biittaa bidi Ayhude Woosa Keethan deriya tamaarssis. Entti malaalettidi, “Ha uray ha cinccatethaanne ha malaatata oothiya wolqqaa awuppe ekkidee?
Hayssi anaaxiya na7aa gidenneyye? Iya aaye sunthay Mayraamo gidennee? Iya ishati Yayqooba, Yoosefa, Simoonanne Yihuda gidokkonaayye?
Iya michcheti nuura de7oosona gidokkonaa? Yaatin, ha uray ha ubbaa awuppe ekkidee?” yaagidosona.
Hessa gisho, I giyabaa ekkonna ixxidosona. Shin Yesuusi, “Nabey ba yelettida biittaninne ba soo asaa matan bonchchettenna” yaagis.
Entti ammanonna ixxida gisho daro malaatata he bessan oothibeenna.
He wode Galiila aysiya Heroodisi Yesuusabaa si7is.
Ba aylletakko, “Hayssi Xammaqiya Yohaannisa; I hayqoppe denddis. Yaanida gisho ha ubbaa malaatata I oothees” yaagis.
I hessa giday Heroodisi ba ishaa Filphoosa machche Heroodiyadi gaason Yohaannisa qasho keethi gelssida gishossa.
Yohaannisi Heroodisa, “Ne iyo ekkanaw woga gidenna” yaagis.
Heroodisi Yohaannisa wodhanaw koyis, shin derey Yohaannisa nabe oothidi be7iya gisho yashettis.
Heroodisi ba yelettida gallasa bonchchiya wode Heroodiyada na7iya asaa sinthan yethan durada iya ufayssasu.
Yaatin, I, “Iya koyaba ubbaa immana gidi” caaqqis.
Na7iya ba aaye zoriya si7ada Heroodisakko, “Xammaqiya Yohaannisa huu7iya keren wothada taw imma” yaagasu.
Iya yaagin kawoy qiirottis, shin ba caaquwa gishonne baara de7iya imathata gisho gidi I oyshay polettana mela kiittis.
Kawoy ase kiittidi Yohaannisi qasho keethan de7ishin iya qoodhiya goyrisis.
Huu7iya keren wothi ehidi na7ees immidosona; na7iyakka ekkada ba aayes efasu.
Yohaannisa tamaareti yidi iya ahaa efidi moogidosona. Iyappe guye hanidabaa ubbaa bidi Yesuusas odidosona.
Yesuusi hanidabaa si7ida wode wogoluwan gelidi he bessaafe issi geemmiya soo barkka bis. Asay hessa si7idi katamatappe denddidi tohon iya kaallidosona.
Yesuusi wogoluwappe wodhdhidi daro asaa be7idi enttaw qadhettis. Entta giddon de7iya hargganchchota pathis.
Sa7ay omarssishe biya wode Yesuusa tamaareti iyaakko shiiqidi, “Ha bessay asi baynna bessi, sa7aykka qammis. Yaaniya gisho, heeran de7iya gutata bidi banttaw shammidi maana mela deriya yedda” yaagidosona.
Shin Yesuusi enttako, “Derey moonna baanaw koshshenna; entti maanabaa hintte immite” yaagis.
Entti zaaridi, “Nuus hayssan ichchashu uythaafenne nam77u moloppe hari baawa” yaagidosona.
Ikka, “Ane entta haa ehite” yaagis.
Kaallidikka, derey maatan uttana mela odis. Ichchashu uythaanne nam77u molota ekkidi, salo xeellidi galati simmidi, uythaa menthidi ba tamaaretas immis; entti qassi deriyas immidosona.
Ubbay midi kallidosona. Yesuusa tamaareti mishin attidayssa tammanne nam77u gayta denthidosona.
Kathaa mida asay maccasaynne nayti attin ichchashu mukulu gidees.
Yesuusi ba tamaareti wogoluwan gelidi baappe sinthattidi abbaafe he finthi pinnana mela kiittidi baw deriya moyzanaw guye attis.
Deriya moyzi simmidi barkka woossanaw issi deriya bolla keyis. Sa7ay qamminkka I barkka yan gam77is.
He wode wogoloy abbaa bolla bishin sintha baggara carkkoy denddin hobbey wogoluwa un77ethis.
Wontimaatha bolla Yesuusi abbaa bolla hamuttishe ba tamaaretakko yis.
Iya tamaareti, I abbaa bolla hamuttishe banttako yeyssa be7idi yayyidosona. Enttika, “Hayssi moytille” gidi yayyidi waassidosona.
Shin Yesuusi ellessidi, “Aykkoy baawa! Yayyofite! Tanabay” yaagis.
Phexiroosi iyaakko, “Godaw, nena gidikko, taani haatha bollara hamuttada neekko baana mela tana kiitta” yaagis.
Yesuusi Phexiroosakko, “Haaya” yaagis. Phexiroosi wogoluwappe wodhdhidi haatha bollara hamuttishe Yesuusakko buussu oykkis.
Shin wolqqaama carkkuwa be7idi yayyis. Haathan mitetethi oykkida wode “Godaw, tana ashsharkkii” yaagidi waassis.
Yesuusi ellesidi ba kushiya yeddi iya oykkidi, “Neno, ammanoy paccidaysso ays sidhay” yaagis.
Yesuusaranne Phexiroosara wogoluwan gelida wode carkkoy si77i gis.
Wogoluwa giddon de7iya iya tamaareti, “Neeni tumakka Xoossaa Na7a” gidi goynnidosona.
Entti abbaa pinnidi Gensareexe biittaa gakkidosona.
He biittan de7iya asay Yesuusa erida wode bantta heeran de7iya guta ubbaa kiita yedidosona. Asay hargganchchota ubbaa iyaakko ehidosona.
Hargganchchoti iya afila macaraa xalaala bochchana mela woossidosona. Bochchida ubbayka paxidosona.
Hessafe guye, issi issi Farisaawetinne higge asttamaareti Yerusalaameppe Yesuusakko yidi,
“Ne tamaareti ays nu aawata wogaa menthonaa? Entti kathi maanappe sinthe bantta kushiya meecettokona” yaagidi oychchidosona.
Yesuusi zaaridi, “Hinttee, hintte wogaa gisho Xoossaa kiitaa poleyssa ays ixxeeti?
Ays giikko, Xoossay, ‘Ne aawanne ne aayiw bonchcha. I ba aawa woykko ba aayiw cayeyssi hayqo gibeennee?’ yaagis.
Shin hintte, issi asi ba aawa woykko ba aayiw maaddanabay de7ishin, ‘Hayssa ta Xoossas yarshshas giikko,
ba aawa woykko ba aayiw bonchchanaw bessenna’ yaageeta. Yaatidi hinttee, hintte wogaa polanaw Xoossaa qaala mentheeta.
Hinttenoo, cubboto, Isayaasi hinttebaa likke odis,
“ ‘Ha asay tana bantta doonan bonchchees, shin entta wozanay taappe haahon de7ees.
Asay tana coo goynnosona; entti asi medhdhida kiitaa Xoossaa higge daanisidi tamaarssoosona’ gis” yaagis.
Yesuusi daro asaa baakko xeegidi, “Si7ite! Akeekite!
Ase tunisiyabay doonara geliyaba gidonnashin doonappe keyaabaa” yaagis.
Hessafe guye, Yesuusa tamaareti iyaakko yidi, “Farisaaweti neeni gidayssa si7idi dhubettidayssa akeekay?” yaagidosona.
Shin Yesuusi enttaw zaaridi, “Saluwan de7iya ta aaway tokkiboonna mithay ubbay shodettana.
Enttabaa hirggofite; entti qooqe kaalethiya qooqeta. Qooqey qooqe kaalethiko, nam77ayka ollan kunddana” yaagis.
Phexiroosi zaaridi, “Ha leemisuwa birshshethaa nuus odarkkii” yaagis.
Yesuusi enttako, “Hinttewuka ha77i gakkanaw gelibeennee?
Doonara geliyabaa ubbay ulo gelidi kare keyeyssa erekketii?
Shin doonara keyaabay wozanappe keyees. Ase tunisiyabati hessata.
Enttika asa wozana giddofe keyaa iita qofa, wodho, laymatethi, iita ooso, kayso, worddo markkatethi, cashshe.
Hessa daaniyabati ase tuniseesippe attin meecettonna kushera meyssi tunisenna” yaagis.
Hessafe guye, Yesuusi yaappe keyidi Xiroosanne Sidoona katamati de7iya biittaa bis.
Issi Kanaane biitta maccas Yesuusakko yada, ba qaalaa dhoqqu oothada, “Godaw, Dawite na7aw, taw qadhettarkii; ta na7iw tuna ayyaanay oykkidi iita waayses” yaagasu.
Shin Yesuusi issi qaalakka zaaronna si77i gis. Yesuusa tamaareti iyaakko yidi, “Ha maccasiya nu geedo kaalla kaallada, woossawusu. Hessa gisho, neeni iyo moyzarkkii” yaagidi woossidosona.
Yesuusi zaaridi, “Taani wudeppe dhayida dorssada Isra7eele keethaafe dhayida asata xalaalas kiitettas” yaagis.
Shin iya, iya sinthan kunddada, “Godaw, tana maaddarkii?” yaagasu.
I zaaridi, “Nayta kathi ekkidi kanatas yeggeyssi lo77o gidenna” yaagis.
Maccasiyakka, “Godaw, hessi tuma, shin hari attoshin kanati bantta godati mishin, gaytappe wodhdhiya tiifiya moosona” yaagasu.
Yesuusi zaaridi, “Ha maccasete, ne ammanoy gita; ne koyidayssada new hano” yaagis. I na7iya iirakka paxa aggasu.
Yesuusi yaappe denddidi Galiila Abbaa mati bis. Issi dere bolla keyidi, yan uttis.
Daro asay banttara, wobbeta, qooqeta, kuunata, doona muumetanne, hara daro hargganchchota ekkidi, iyaakko ehidi iya sinthan wothidosona. Yesuusi enttana pathis.
Hessa gisho, muumeti odettishin, kuunati piddi gishin, wobbeti hamuttishin, qooqeti xeellishin asay be7idi malaalettidi, Isra7eele Xoossaa galatidosona.
Yesuusi ba tamaareta baakko xeegidi, “Ha daro asay taara heedzu gallas gam77ida gishonne enttaw ha77i miyabay baynna gisho taani enttaw qadhettays. Entti ogen daaburidi kunddonna mela aykko muzonna entta mela yeddanaw koyikke” yaagis.
Iya tamaareti zaaridi, “Nuuni ha bazzuwan hayssa keena asaas gidiya kathi awuppe demmanee?” yaagidosona.
Yesuusi enttako, “Hinttew aappun uythi de7ii?” yaagidi oychchis. Entti zaaridi, “Laappun uythinne laafa molotappe guuthi de7ees” yaagidosona.
Yesuusi deriya sa7an uttite yaagidi kiittis.
Hessafe guye, he laappun uythaanne moluwa ekkidi Xoossaa galatis. Menthidi ba tamaaretas immis. Iya tamaareti asaas gishidosona.
Asay ubbay midi kallidosona. Iya tamaareti, mishin attida tiifiya laappun gita gayta kumethi denthidosona.
Mida asay maccasinne na7a paydonna adde xalaali oyddu mukulu.
Yesuusi deriya yeddidaappe guye wogoluwan gelidi Magedoona giya biittaa bis.
Farisaawetinne Saduqaaweti Yesuusakko yidosona. Iya paaccanaw koyidi, banttana saloppe malaata besso gidi oychchidosona.
Shin I enttako, “Sa7i omarssiya wode ‘Saloy zo77ida gisho wontto booqallana’ yaageta.
Wonttiya wode, ‘Saloy zo77idi shaaratida gisho iray bukkana’ yaageta. Yaatin hintte salo mallaa be7idi ereeta, shin wodiya malla eranaw dandda7ibeekketa.
Iitanne ammanonna yeletethay malaata koyees. Shin iyaw Yoonasa malaatappe hara malaati imettenna” yaagis. Hessafe guye, enttana yan aggidi hara soo bis.
Entti abbaafe hefinthi pinnida wode daabbo ekkidi yaanayssa dogidosona.
Yesuusi enttako, “Farisaawetappenne Saduqaaweta irshshuwaafe naagettite” yaagis.
Enttika bantta garssan, “I hessa giday nu daabbo ekkidi yoonna gishossa gidana” yaagidosona.
Yesuus entta qofaa eridi, “Hinttenoo, ammanoy paccidayssato! Daabbo ekkonna yida gisho woli gidon ays odetteetii?
Ha77ika hintte akeeketii? Ichchashu mukulu asaas ichchashu uythaa gishidayssanne entti midi kallin hintte aappun gayta kumethi denthidaakko dogidetii?
Hessadakka, laappun uythaa oyddu mukulu asaas gishidayssanne entti midi kallin, hintte aappun gita gayta kumethi denthidaakko akeekekketii?
Hiza, taani Farisaawetanne Saduqaaweta irshshuwaafe naagettite gada odeyssi daabbobaa gidonnayssa akeekekketii?” yaagis.
Yaatin, iya tamaareti Yesuusi odey munuqa denthanaw yegettiya irshshobaa gidonnashin Farisaawetanne Saduqaaweta timirttiyafe naagettanayssa gideyssa akeekidosona.
Yesuusi Qisaariya Filphoosa biittaa gakkida wode ba tamaaretakko, “Asay, Asa Na7aa oona goonaa?” yaagidi oychchis.
Enttika, “Issoti issoti Xammaqiya Yohaannisa, harati Eliyaasa qassi hankkoti Ermmiyasa woykko nabetappe issuwa goosona” yaagidosona.
Yesuusi zaaridi, “Yaatin, hintte tana oona geeti” gidi entta oychchis.
Simoona Phexiroosi zaaridi, “Neeni Kiristtoosa, de7o Xoossaa na7a” yaagis.
Yesuusi Phexiroosakko, “Yoona na7aa Simoona, neeni anjjettidayssa! Hayssa new qonccisiday saluwan de7iya ta aawappe attin ase gidenna.
Ta new odays Phexiroosa, neeni zaalla! Taani ha zaalla bolla ta woosa keethaa keexana. Hayqo wolqqatikka iyo xoonokkona.
Salo kawotethaa qulppeta ta new immana. Sa7an neeni diggiyabay ubbay salon Xoossaa matan digettidabaa gidana. Sa7an neeni hano giyabay ubbay salon Xoossaa matan hanidabaa gidana” yaagis.
Hessafe guye, I, Kiristtoosa gideyssa ooddeskka odonna mela ba tamaareta minthidi kiittis.
He wodiyappe doomidi Yesuusi ba tamaaretas, “Taani Yerusalaame baanaw bessees. Yan deriya cimatan, kahine halaqatanne higge asttamaareta kushen waaye ekkanaw bessees. Entti tana wodhana, shin taani heedzantho gallas hayqoppe denddana” yaagidi qonccisis.
Phexiroosi Yesuusa gaxa kessidi, “Godaw, hessi hanenna! Hessa melabay nena ubbarakka gakkofo!” yaagidi hanqettis.
Yesuusi Phexiroosakko guye simmidi, “Ha Xalahiyaw, taappe haakka! Neeni asa qofa qoppasappe attin Xoossaa qofa qopponna gisho taw dhube gidaasa” yaagis.
Hessafe guye, Yesuusi ba tamaaretakko, “Oonikka tana kaallanaw koyabaa gidikko bana kaddo, ba masqaliya tookkidi tana kaallo.
Ba de7uwa ashshanaw koyaa ubbay dhayssees. Shin ba de7uwa ta gisho gidi aathi immeyssi ashshees.
Asi alame kumethaa babaa oothidi, gidoshin ba shemppuwa dhayssikko iya ay maaddii? Woykko asi ba shemppuwa laame ay immanaw dandda7ii?
Asa na7ay ba aawa bonchchuwan ba kiitanchchotara yaana. He wode issi issi uraas iya oosuwada immana.
Ta tuma odays; asa Na7ay kawo gididi simmeyssa be7ana gakkanaw hayssan eqqida asaappe hayqqonnayssati de7oosona” yaagis.
Usuppun gallasappe guye Yesuusi, Phexiroosa, Yayqoobanne iya ishaa Yohaannisa baara ekkidi banttarkka gidanaw deriya bolla keyis.
Yan entta sinthan Yesuusa malay kumethi laamettis; iya som77oyka awada xolqqis. Iya ma7oykka daro booxis.
Hekko, Museynne Eliyaasi iyara odettishin be7idosona.
Phexiroosi Yesuusakko, “Nuuni hayssa hashshu yida. Ne koykko issino new, issino Muses, issino Eliyaasas hayssan heedzu shaqara shaqarana” yaagis.
Phexiroosi hessa buroo odishin bootha shaaray enttana kammis. Shaara giddora, “Tana ufayssiya, ta dosiya na7ay hayssa, iya si7ite!” yaagiya qaalay yis.
Yesuusa tamaareti hessa si7ida wode dagammidi bantta som77uwara sa7an kunddidosona.
Shin Yesuusi enttako shiiqidi entta bochchidi, “Denddite, yayyofite!” yaagis.
Entti dhoqqu gidi be7iya wode Yesuusappe hara oonakka be7ibookkona.
Entti deriyappe wodhdhishin Yesuusi enttako, “Asa Na7ay hayqoppe denddana gakkanaw ha hintte be7idabaa ooddeskka odoppite” gidi kiittis.
Yesuusa tamaareti, “Yaatin, higge asttamaareti Eliyaasi Kiristtoosappe kasetidi yaana giday aybisse?” yaagidi oychchidosona.
Yesuusi zaaridi, “Ee! Eliyaasi kaseti yidi ubbabaa giigisana.
Shin ta hinttew tuma odays; Eliyaasi kasetidi yis. Enttika iya bolla koyidabaa oothidosonappe attin iya shaakki eribookkona. Hessada Asa Na7ay entta kushen waayettana” yaagis.
He wode Yesuusi giday Xammaqiya Yohaannisabaa gideyssa akeekidosona.
Entti deriyappe asaakko simmiya wode issi asi Yesuusa sinthan gulbbatidi,
“Godaw, hayyana ta na7as qadhettarkii; iya shocidi yeggiya harggey daro un77ethidi tamaninne haathan yeggees.
Ne tamaaretakko ehas, shin entti pathanaw dandda7ibookkona” yaagis.
Yesuusi zaaridi, “Hinttenoo, ammanonna geella yeletethaw awude gakkanaw ta hinttera daane? Awude gakkanaw ta hinttena dandda7anee? Ane na7aa haa ekki yiite” yaagis.
Yesuusi tuna ayyaanaa hanqqin, tuna ayyaanay na7aappe keyis; he saatenkka na7ay paxis.
Hessafe guye, Yesuusa tamaareti banttarkka iyaakko shiiqidi, “Nuuni tuna ayyaanaa kessanaw dandda7iboonnay aybisse?” yaagidi oychchidosona.
I enttako, “Hinttew ammanoy laafida gishossa. Ta hinttew tuma odays; gaashe ayfe mela ammanoy hinttew de7ikko ‘Ha deriya hayssafe denddada gede aadhdha’ giikko hinttew kiitettana. Hinttew dandda7ettonabay deenna.
[Shin hessa melay woosappenne xoomappe attin haran keyenna]” yaagis.
Yesuusa tamaareti Galiilan shiiqidi de7ishin Yesuusi enttako, “Asa Na7ay asa kushen aadhdhidi imettana.
Entti iya wodhana, shin I heedzantho gallas hayqoppe denddana” yaagis. Iya tamaaretikka daro qiirottidosona.
Yesuusaranne iya tamaaretara Qifirnahoome katama gakkida wode Xoossa Keetha giira qanxiseyssati Phexiroosakko yidi, “Hintte asttamaarey Xoossa Keetha giira giirii?” yaagidi oychchidosona.
Phexiroosi zaaridi, “Giirees” yaagis. Phexiroosi soo geliya wode Yesuusi kasetidi, “Phexiroosa, new ay daanii? Ha sa7aa kawotethati qaraxanne giira ooppe ekkonaa? Gade asappeyye woykko asa gade asappe?” yaagidi oychchis.
Phexiroosi “Asa gade asappe” gidi zaaris. Yesuusi zaaridi, “Gade asay giira giirokkona guussu.
Shin entti dhubettonna mela abbaa bada moluwa oykkiya manxxaqo yegga. Koyro ne oykkiya moluwa doona dooyada giiras gidiya miishiya ne gishonne ta gisho efada giira” yaagis.
He wode Yesuusa tamaareti yidi, “Salo kawotethan ubbaafe aadhdhey oonee?” yaagidi oychchidosona.
Yesuusi issi guutha na7a xeegidi entta giddon essidi hayssada yaagis.
“Taani hinttew tuma odays; hintte laamettonanne guutha naytada hanonna ixxiko salo kawotethaa ubbarakka gelanaw dandda7ekketa.
Hiza, ha guutha na7aada bana kawushshiya oonikka salo kawotethan ubbaafe aadhdheyssa gidana.
Hayssa mela na7a ta sunthan mokkiya oonikka tana mokkees.
“Shin tanan ammaniyaa ha guuthatappe issuwa naagara oothana mela dhube gidiya oonikka gita gaachcha woxa ba qodhen qachchidi ciimmo abban mitettiko iyaw lo77o.
Alamen asay nagara oothana mela oothiyabati de7iya gisho alamiya ayye. Hessa melabati yoonna attenna, shin dhubey iya gaason yaa uraa ayye.
“Ne kushey woykko ne tohoy nena balethikko neeppe qanxa yegga. Neeni nam77u kushera woykko nam77u tohora merinaa taman yeggettanayssafe kushe woykko toho duuxa gidada merinaa de7o demmeyssi new lo77o.
Qassi ne ayfey nena balethikko iyo wooca kessada wora hola. Neeni nam77u ayfera gaanname taman yeggetteyssafe issi ayfera merinaa de7uwa geleyssi new lo77o.
“Ta hinttew odays; salon de7iya entta naagiya kiitanchchoti ubba wode salon de7iya ta Aawa sinthan de7iya gisho hintte ha guuthatappe issuwaka kadhonna mela naagettite.
Asa Na7ay dhaydayssata ashshanaw yis” yaagis.
Qassi Yesuusi, “Hinttew ay daanii? Issi uraas xeetu dorssati de7eyssatappe issoy dhayikko uddufun tammanne uddufunata deriya bolla yeggi aggidi he dhayidayssa koyanaw beenne?
Ta tuma odays; I demmida wode uddufun tammanne uddufunatappe aathidi dhayidi benttida issi dorssan ufayttees.
Hessadakka, salon de7iya hintte aaway ha guuthatappe issoy dhayana mela koyenna.
“Ne ishay nena qohikko nerkka iyaakko bada iya balaa iyaw oda. I nena si7ikko ne ishaa new isha ootha.
Shin I nena si7onna ixxiko, nam77u woykko heedzu asa markkan mootoy lasettiya gisho issi woykko nam77u asi ekkada iyaakko ba.
I enttana si7onna ixxiko, woosa keethas oda. Woosa keethi giyabaa si7onna ixxiko ammanonna asada woykko qaraxa qanxisiya asada iya payda.
“Ta hinttew tuma odays; sa7an hintte diggiyabati ubbay salon Xoossaa matan digettidaba gidana. Sa7an hintte hano giyabati ubbay salon Xoossaa matan hanidabaa gidana.
“Qassika ta hinttew odays; sa7an hinttefe nam77ay bantta woossiyabas issi wozanan gididi Xoossaa woossiyabaa gidikko salon de7iya ta Aaway hinttew oothana.
Tana kaalleyssatappe nam77a woykko heedza gididi shiiqiya bessan taani entta giddon benttana” yaagis.
He wode Phexiroosi Yesuusakko yidi, “Godaw, ta ishay tana qohikko aappun toho taani atto gaanaw bessii? Laappun toho gakkanaaseyye?” gidi oychchis.
Yesuusi zaaridi, “Gidenna, laappun tammu toho laappunappe attin laappun toho gidenna.
“Hessa gisho, Xoossaa kawotethay ba oosanchchotara ba miishey paccidaakkonne palahidaakko be7anaw qoppida kawuwa daanees.
He kawoy miishey paccidaakkonne palahidaakko be7iya wode daro ginddigindda acoy de7iya issi uraa iyaakko ehidosona.
Shin he aylley acuwa qanxanaw xoonettin iyara, iya machcheera, iya naytinne iyaw de7iyabay ubbay bayzettidi acoy cigettana mela iya goday kiittis.
Yaatin aylley ba godaa tohuwa bolla gulbbatidi, ‘Ta godaw, hayyana guutha wode takkarkki, ta acuwa ubbaa ta ciggana’ yaagidi woossis.
Kawoy iyaw qadhettidi, yeddi aggis; iya acuwa maaris.
“Shin he aylley keyi bidi ba lagge oosanchchotappe issoy baappe daro guutha miishe tal77idayssa, ‘Ne bolla de7iya ta miishiya taw cigga’ gidi qoodhe oykkis.
“He iya lagge aylley iya sinthan gulbbatidi, ‘Hayyana guutha wode takkarkki taani ta acuwa ubbaa ciggana’ yaagidi woossis.
“Shin ixxidi ekki efidi ba laggey acuwa qanxana gakkanaw qasho keethi gelssis.
Hessa gisho, hara lagge oosanchchoti hessa be7ida wode daro yilotidi, bidi bantta godaas I oothidabaa ubbaa odidosona.
“Yaatin kawoy he aylliya xeegisidi, ‘Ha iita aylliyaw, neeni tana woossida gisho ta ne acuwa ubbaa new maaras.
Yaatin, taani ne acuwa maaridayssada neeni ne lagge aylliya acuwa maaranaw new bessennee?’ yaagis.
Hessa gisho, kawoy daro yilotidi, I ba acuwa ubbaa ciggana gakkanaw paxa kaa7ettana mela qasho keethan yeggis.
“Hessadakka, hintte issoy issoy hintte ishaa wozanappe maaronna ixxiko salon de7iya ta Aaway hinttena hessada oothana” yaagis.
Yesuusi hessa odi onggidaappe guye Galiilappe denddidi Yorddaanose Shaafappe hefinthan de7iya Yihuda biittaa bis.
Daro asay iya kaallidi bin entta giddofe hargganchchota pathis.
Farisaaweti iya paaccanaw koyidi iyaakko yidi, “Issi asi ay gaasonkka ba machchiw yeddanaw bessii?” yaagidi oychchidosona.
Yesuusi zaaridi, “Xoossay koyro addenne maccas oothi medhdhidayssa hintte nabbabibeekketii?
‘Hessa gisho, Issi asi ba aawanne ba aayiw aggidi ba machcheera issino gidees, nam77ayka issi asho gidoosona.’
Hessa gisho, entti issi asho gidoosonappe attin nam77a gidokkona. Hiza, Xoossi qachchidayssa asi shaakkofo” yaagis.
Farisaaweti, “Yaatin, Musey issi asi anjjo worqqate immidi yeddana mela ays kiittidee?” yaagidi oychchidosona.
Yesuusi zaaridi, “Hinttee, hintte machcheta yeddana mela Musey hinttena kiittiday, hintte wozanaa minotethaa gishoppe attin koyroppe hessa mela gidenna.
Ta hinttew odays; ba machchiya laymatonna de7ishin yeddidi hara ekkiya oonikka laammees” yaagis.
Iya tamaareti iyaakko, “Azinabaynne machchibay hessa mela gidikko ekko geloy attiko lo77o” yaagidosona.
Yesuusi zaaridi, “Hessa mela timirttey Xoossay dandda7a immidayssatassafe attin asa ubbaassa gidenna.
Hiza, yelettishe shuufa gididi yelettidayssati de7oosona, qassi asi qaaratidayssati de7oosona, qassi salo kawotethaa gisho gidi banttana shuufaydayssati de7oosona. Hessa gisho, hayssa ekkanaw dandda7iya oonikka ekko” yaagis.
Yesuusi ba kushiya guutha nayta bolla wothidi enttaw woossana mela issi issi asay nayta iyaakko ehidosona. Shin iya tamaareti asaa hanqettidosona.
Shin Yesuusi, “Xoossaa kawotethay hayssata melassa gidiya gisho guutha nayti taakko yeyssa diggofite; yo giite” yaagis.
Ba kushiya entta bolla wothidaappe guye he bessaafe aggidi bis.
Issi gallas issi uray Yesuusakko yidi, “Asttamaariyaw, taani merinaa de7o demmanaw ay lo77obaa ootho?” yaagis.
Yesuusi iyaakko, “Lo77obaa ne tana ays oychchay? Issi Xoossaafe attin hari lo77oy baawa. Shin neeni merinaa de7uwa ekkanaw koykko kiitata naaga” yaagis.
Uray zaaridi, “Awussa kiitata” yaagidi oychchis. Yesuusi zaaridi, “Wodhoppa, laymatoppa, kaysotoppa, worddo markkattofa,
ne aawanne ne aayiw bonchcha, ne shooruwa ne huu7iyatho dosa” yaagis.
He na7atethay, “Taani hayssata ubbaa na7atethafe doomada naagas. Yaatin, hari taw pacciyabay aybee?” yaagidi oychchis.
Yesuusi zaaridi, “Neeni polo gidanaw koykko bada new de7iyabaa bayzada manqotas imma; neeni salon duretana. Yaata simma yada tana kaalla” yaagis.
Shin he naatetha uray daro dure gidiya gisho hessa si7ida wode azzanishe aggidi bis.
Hessafe guye, Yesuusi ba tamaareta, “Taani hinttew tuma odays; durey salo kawotethi gelanayssi daro meto.
Dure asi Xoossaa kawotethaa gelanayssafe gimaley marppe luhora aadhdheyssi kawuyees” yaagis.
Yesuusa tamaareti hessa si7idi malaalettidi, “Yaatin, ooni attanaw dandda7ii?” yaagidi oychchidosona.
Yesuusi entta caddi xeellidi, “Hayssi asas dandda7ettenna, shin Xoossas ubbay dandda7ettees” yaagis.
Phexiroosi zaaridi, “Nuuni ubbabaa aggidi nena kaallida. Yaatin, nuuni ay demmanee?” yaagis.
Yesuusi enttako hayssada yaagis: “Taani hinttew tuma odays; Asa Na7ay yaana alamiyan ba bonchcho araatan uttiya wode hintte tammanne nam77ati, tana kaallidayssati, tammanne nam77u araatan uttidi tammanne nam77u Isra7eele zerethata bolla pirddana.
Ta sunthaa gisho keethe woykko ishata woykko michcheta woykko aawa woykko aayiw woykko nayta woykko gadiya aggiday oonikka xeetu kushe ekkana. Qassi merinaa de7uwakka ekkana.
Shin daroti ha77i dethan sinthe gididayssati guye gidana, qassi guye gididayssati sinthe gidana” yaagis.
“Xoossaa kawotethay ba woyniya giddon oosanchchota kera oosisanaw wontta guura keyida keethaawa daanees.
I he oosanchchotas hachchi hachchi issi dinaare qanxanaw enttara giigidi, entta ba woyniya giddo yeddis.
“Qassi wonttafe heedzu saate gidishin keyidi ooso dhayidi giya bolla eqida hara asata demmis.
I enttako, ‘Hintteka ta woyniya giddo bidi oothite, taani hinttew bessiya gatiya qanxana’ yaagis.
Enttika bidosona. Qassika I usuppun saateninne uddufun saaten keyidi hessada oothis.
Tammanne issi saate gidishin I keyaa wode harati yan eqqidayssata demmidi, ‘Hintte ooso oothonna gallas kumethi hayssan ays eqqidi pee7idetii?’ yaagis.
“Entti zaaridi, ‘Nuna kera oosisiya asi dhayida gishossa’ yaagidosona. “Ikka, ‘Hintteka ta woyniya giddo bidi oothite’ yaagis.
“Sa7i omarssin, woyniya goday oosanchchota halaqaakko, ‘Oosanchchota xeegada wurssethan ooso gelidayssatappe doomada koyro gelidayssata gakkanaw entta gatiya qanxa’ yaagis.
Tammanne issi saaten ooso oykkidayssati yidi, huu7en huu7en issi issi dinaare ekkidosona.
Koyro ooso oykkidayssati yidi, banttaw daro imettana gidi qoppidosona. Shin enttika huu7en huu7en issi issi dinaare ekkidosona.
Bantta miishiya ekki simmidi keethaawa bolla zuuzummidosona.
‘Hayssati guyeppe yidi issi saate xalaala oothidosona. Shin gallas kumethi awa suulan daaburidi pee7ida nuura entti waanidi issino gidoona’ yaagidosona.
“Woyniya keethaaway oosanchchotappe issuwako, ‘Ta ishaw, taani nena qohabikke; ne taara giigiday issi dinaaressa gidennee?
Ne miishiya ekkada ne soo ba. Ta omarssi yidayssaskka neyssa mela immanaw koyays.
Taani ta miishiyan koyidabaa oothanaw taw maati baawe? Woykko taani keeha gidida gisho neeni qanaatay?’ yaagis.
“Hessada ha77i dethan guye gididayssati sinthatana, sinthattidayssati qassi guyetana” yaagis.
Yesuusi Yerusalaame bishe, tammanne nam77u tamaareta dumma gaxa kessidi enttako yaagis:
“Hekko, nuuni ha77i Yerusalaame buussa bolla de7oos. Yan Asa Na7ay kahine halaqatasinne higge asttamaaretas aadhdhi imettana. Enttika iya bolla hayqo pirdda pirddana.
Iya Ayhude gidonna deriyas aathi immana. Entti iya kawushshana, garaafana, yaatidi iya masqaliya bolla kaqqana. Shin I heedzantho gallas hayqoppe denddana” yaagis.
He wode Zabdiyoosa machchiya ba nam77u adde naytara Yesuusakko yada, iya sinthan gulbbatada issibaa iya woossasu.
Yesuusi iikko, “Ne ay koyay?” yaagis. Iya zaarada, “Ne kawotethan ha ta nam77u nayti issoy ne ushachchan issoy ne haddirssan utto garkkii!” yaagasu.
Shin Yesuusi naytakko zaaridi, “Hintte ay woossiyako erekketa; taani uyanaw de7iya waaye xuu7aa uyanaw dandda7etii?” yaagis. Enttika, “Ee dandda7os” yaagidosona.
Yesuusi, “Tumakka taani uyanaw de7iya xuu7appe hintte uyana. Shin ta ushachchaninne haddirssan uttanayssata doorey tana gidikke. He bessay imetey, ta aaway immanaw giigisida asatassa” yaagis.
Attida tammu iya tamaareti hessa si7ida wode nam77u ishata bolla hanqettidosona.
Shin Yesuusi entta ubbaa xeegidi hayssada yaagis. “Ayhude gidonna asaa haareyssati bantta asaa bolla godateyssanne entta kaaletheyssati wolqqan haareyssa hintte ereeta.
Shin hintte giddon hessada gidoppo. Hinttefe gitatanaw koyaa oonikka hinttew aylle gido.
Hintte giddon ubbaafe bolla gidanaw koyaa oonikka hinttew aylle gidanaw bessees.
Hessadakka, Asa Na7ay ase haggaazanawunne daro asaa wozanaw ba shemppuwa immanaw yisippe attin asan haggaazetanaw yibeenna” yaagis.
Hessafe guye, Yesuusi ba tamaaretara Iyaarkkofe keyidi bishin, daro asay enttana kaallidosona.
Oge gaxan uttida nam77u qooqeti Yesuusi yaara aadhdheyssa si7idi, “Godaw, Dawite Na7aw, nuus qadhettarkii” yaagidi waassidosona.
Daro asay enttana, “Hayzite” yaagidi kaccidosona. Shin entti, “Godaw, Dawite na7aw, nuus qadhettarkii” gidi gujji waassidosona.
Yesuusi eqqidi, entta xeegidi, “Ta hinttew ay oothana mela koyeetii?” yaagidi oychchis.
Enttika, “Godaw, nu ayfey xeellana mela koyoos” yaagidosona.
Yesuusi enttaw qadhettidi, entta ayfiyaa bochchis. Ellesidi entta ayfey xeellis; entti iya kaallidi bidosona.
Yesuusaranne iya tamaaretara Yerusalaame matidi, Shamaho Deriya bolla de7iya Beetefaage giya gutaa gakkishe, Yesuusi ba tamaaretappe nam77ata baappe sinthe yaagidi kiittis:
“Hinttefe sinthan de7iya guta biite. Yan issi harey qashon de7iyaro I maarara hintte sohuwara demmana. Entta billidi haa ekki yiite.
Oonikka hinttena oychchiko, ‘Goday enttana koyees’ yaagite. I enttana iirakka yeddi aggana” yaagis.
Hessika nabey,
“Xiyoone katamaas, ‘Hekko, ne kawoy ashkke gididi, hare bollanne hare mara bolla uttidi, neekko yees’ yaagite” yaagidi xaafidayssi polettana mela hessi hanis.
Iya tamaareti bidi Yesuusi entta kiittidayssada oothidosona.
Hariwunne hare maraa ehidi bollara ma77ida bantta ma7uwa entta zokkon yeggidosona. Yesuusi ma7ota bolla uttis.
Daro asay bantta ma7uwa ogiyan hiixidosona. Harati boncco tashidi ogiya bolla yeggidosona.
Yesuusappe sinthara hamutteyssatinne iyappe guyera kaalliya daro asay, “Hosaana! Dawite na7ay galatetto! Godaa sunthan yeyssi anjjettidayssa! Bonchchoy Ubbaafe Dhoqqa Saluwan Xoossaas gido!” yaagidi waassidosona.
Yesuusi Yerusalaame katamaa gelida wode he kataman de7iya asa ubbay, “Hayssi oonee?” yaagidi yarkkidosona.
Asay, “Hayssi Galiilan de7iya Naazirete katamaappe yida nabiya Yesuusa” yaagidosona.
Yesuusi Xoossa Keethi gelidi, yan bayzeyssatanne shammeyssata ubbaa kare goodis. Miishe laammeyssata xarpheezatanne holleta bayziya oydeta shiri yeggis.
Ikka enttako, “Xoossaa qaalan, ‘Ta keethay Xoossaa woossiya keethi geetettana’ geetetti xaafettis. Shin hintte panggati qosettiya gonggolo oothideta” yaagis.
Yesuusi Xoossa Keethan de7ishin qooqetinne gunddati iyaakko yin entta pathis.
Shin kahine halaqatinne higge asttamaareti Yesuusi oothida malaalisiyabata be7idayssasinne guutha nayti Xoossa Keethan, “Dawite na7ay, galatetto” yaagidi waasseyssa si7idi hanqettidosona.
Entti Yesuusakko, “Hayssati geyssa ne si7ay?” yaagidosona. Yesuusi, “Ee si7ays, Xoossaa qaalan, ‘Guutha nayta doonaninne dhammiya nayta doonan galata wothadasa’ geetettidi xaafettidayssa hintte nabbabibeekketii?” yaagis.
Enttana yan aggidi Bitaaniya katamaa bidi aqis.
Yesuusi wontta guura katama simmidi yishe koshattis.
Oge gaxan issi balase mithi be7idi iikko bis. Shin haythafe attin hara aykkoka demmibeenna. Hessa gisho, iyo, “Hizappe nam77antho ayfe ayfoppa!” yaagis. He balase mithiya ellesada mela aggasu.
Iya tamaareti hessa be7idi, “Ha balasiya waanada ellesa meladee?” yaagidi malaalettidosona.
Yesuusi zaaridi, “Taani hinttew tuma odays; hinttew ammanoy de7ikko, qassi hintte sidhonna ixxiko balase bolla taani oothidayssa mela xalaala ootheketa, shin ‘Ha deriya shodettada abban wodhdha’ yaagikko hanana.
Ammanidi hintte woossiyabaa aybibaa gidikkoka hintte ekkana” yaagis.
