Entti he bessaafe denddidi, Galiilara aadhdhidi bidosona; Yesuusi ba de7iyasuwa oonikka erana mela koyibeenna.
I ba tamaaretakko, “Asa Na7aa, asi asas aathi immananne wodhana; I heedzu gallasappe guye, hayqoppe denddana” yaagidi tamaarssees.
Shin enttaw I geyssi gelibeenna; qassi iya oychchanawukka yayyidosona.
Entti Qifirnahoome katamaa bidi soo gelidayssafe guye Yesuusi enttako, “Ogen ay odetteetii?” yaagidi oychchis.
Shin entti, “Nu giddon ubbaafe aadhdhanay oonee?” yaagidi palamida gisho si77i gidosona.
Yesuusi uttidi, tammanne nam77u tamaareta xeegidi, “Oonikka sinthe aadhdhanaw koykko, ubbaafe guye aadhdhidi, ubbaas aylle gidanaw bessees” yaagis.
Issi guutha na7aa ekkidi, entta giddon essis; he guutha na7aa idimmidi enttako,
“Hayssa mela guutha naytappe issuwa ta sunthan mokkiya oonikka tana mokkees; qassi tana mokkiya oonikka tana kiittidaysaka mokkeesippe attin ta xalaala mokkenna” yaagis.
Yohaannisi, “Asttamaariyaw, issi asi ne sunthan tuna Ayyaanata kessishin nuuni be7idi, nu bagga gidonna gisho iya diggida” yaagis.
Shin Yesuusi, “Oonikka ta sunthan Xoossay oothiya malaatata oothidi, ellesidi ta bolla iitabaa odettanaw dandda7ey baynna gisho diggofite.
Nubaa ixxonna uray nu bagga.
Taani hinttew tuma odays; hintte tayssata gidiya gisho oonikka hinttew ta sunthan halo haathi uyanaw immikokka, ba woytuwa ekkana.
“Tana ammaniyaa ha guuthatappe issuwa balethiya oonikka, gaachcha wogga woxa ba qodhen qachchidi, abban wulliyako iyaw lo77o.
Ne kushey nena balethikko, qanxa hola. Neeni nam77u kushera to7onna gaanname taman yegetteyssafe, duuxa kushera de7uwa geloy new lo77o.
<range>
Ne tohoy nena balethikko, qanxa hola. Neeni nam77u tohuwara gaanname taman yegetteyssafe, wobbe gidada de7uwa geleyssi new lo77o.
<range>
Ne ayfey nena balethikko, wooca kessa hola. Neeni nam77u ayfiyaara gaanname taman yegetteyssafe, issi ayfiyaara Xoossaa kawotethaa geleyssi new lo77o.
Yan entta miya guxuney hayqqenna, tamaykka to7enna.
“Yarshshoy maxinen geeyeyssa mela asi ubbay taman harqettana.
Maxiney lo77o, shin I mal77onna ixxiko, zaaridi waati mal77ethanee? Hinttenan maxiney de7o. Yaanidi issoy issuwara sarotethaan de7ite” yaagis.
Yesuusi hessafe denddidi, Yihuda biittaa bidi Yorddaanose Shaafaa pinnis. Daro asay zaaridi iyaakko shiiqin, kaseyssadakka he asaa tamaarssis.
Issi issi Farisaaweti paaccanaw koyidi Yesuusa, “Issi asi ba machchiw yeddana mela Muse higgey kiitii?” yaagidi iya oychchidosona.
I zaaridi, “Musey hinttena woygidi kiittidee?” yaagis.
Entti, “Musey, ‘Issi asi ba machchees anjjo worqqate immidi yeddo’ gis” yaagidosona.
Yesuusi zaaridi, entta “Hintte odin si7onnayssata gidiya gisho Musey ha kiitaa hinttew xaafis.
Shin Xoossay koyro medhdhiya wode addenne macca oothidi, entta medhdhis.
Hessa gisho, issi asi ba aawanne ba aayiw aggidi, ba machcheera issife de7ees.
Entti nam77ay issi ase gidoosona; hizappe, entti issi ase gidoosonappe attin nam77u asi gidokkona.
Hessa gisho, Xoossay issife qachchidayssa asi shaakkofo” yaagis.
Entti soo simmida wode iya tamaareti ha odabaa Yesuusa nam77antho oychchidosona.
Yesuusi enttako, “Ba machchiw yeddidi hara ekkiya oonikka laymatees.
Qassi maccasiyakka ba azinaappe keyada hara azina gelikko laymatawusu” yaagis.
Yesuusi guutha nayta bochchana mela, issi issi asay nayta iyaakko ehoosona, shin iya tamaareti he asa hanqettidosona.
Yesuusi hessa be7idi, ba tamaareta hanqettidi; enttako, “Guutha nayti taakko yeyssa diggofite; Xoossaa kawotethay hayssata melassa.
Taani hinttew tuma odays; Xoossaa kawotethaa guutha na7ada ekkonna uray oonikka he kawotethaa ubbarakka gelenna” yaagis.
Guutha nayta idimmidi, ba kushiya entta issuwa issuwa bolla wothidi anjjis.
Yesuusi baanaw keyida wode issi uray woxxi yidi, iya sinthan gulbbatidi, “Keeha asttamaariyaw, merinaa de7uwa laattanaw taani ay ootho?” yaagidi oychchis.
Yesuusi, “Ays tana keehaw gada xeegay? Xoossaa xalaalappe attin hari keehi oonikka baawa.
Xoossaa kiitaa, wodhoppa; laymatoppa; kaysotoppa; worddo markkattofa; inxarssan cimmofa; ne aawanne ne aayiw bonchcha yaageyssa eraasa” yaagis.
Uray, “Asttamaariyaw, taani hessa ubbaa na7atethafe doomada ha77i gakkanaw naagays” yaagis.
Yesuusi uraa tishshi oothi xeellidi dosis; “New issibay paccees; bada new de7iyaba ubbaa bayzada, he miishiya manqotas imma; neeni salon duretana. Yaata simmada tana kaalla” yaagis.
Shin uray hessa si7idi, I daro dure gidiya gisho ba som77uwa kaarethis, ufayttonna aggidi bis.
Yesuusi ba tamaareta yuushshi aathi xeellidi, “Dure asi Xoossaa kawotethaa gelanayssi waanidi metanddeeshsha!” yaagis.
Iya tamaareti iya timirttiya si7idi malaalettidosona. Shin Yesuusi qassika enttako, “Nayto, Xoossaa kawotethaa gelanayssi waanidi metanddeeshsha!
Dure asi Xoossaa kawotethaa gelanayssafe, gimaley narppe luhora aadhdheyssi kawuyees” yaagis.
Iya tamaareti malaalettidi, “Yaatin, ooni attanee?” yaagidi, issoy issuwa oychchidosona.
Yesuusi entta tishshi oothi xeellidi, “Hayssi Xoossas dandda7eteesppe attin asas dandda7ettenna; Xoossas ubbabay dandda7ettees” yaagis.
Phexiroosi Yesuusakko, “Hekko; nuuni nubaa ubbaa aggidi, nena kaallida” yaagis.
Yesuusi “Taani hinttew tuma odays; ta gishonne Wonggelaa gisho keetha woykko ishata woykko michcheta woykko aawa woykko aayiw woykko machchiw woykko nayta woykko gadiya aggiday oonikka,
ha77i ha wodiyan xeetu kushe keetha, ishata, michcheta, aayeta, nayta, gadiya, goodetethara issife ekkana. Sinthafe yaana wodiyankka merinaa de7uwa ekkana.
Shin daroti ha77i dethan sinthe gididayssati guye gidana, qassi daroti ha77i guye gididayssati sinthe gidana” yaagis.
Yesuusaranne iya tamaaretara Yerusalaame bishin, Yesuusi ba tamaareta sinthan hamuttees. Entti malaalettidosona. Iya kaalleyssatikka yayyidosona. Nam77antho, tammanne nam77u tamaareta gaxa kessidi, bana gakkanabaa dumma enttaw hayssada yaagidi odis.
“Hekko, nuuni Yerusalaame ha77i keyoos. Yan Asa Na7ay, kahine halaqatasinne higge asttamaaretas aathi imettana. Entti iya bolla hayqo pirddaa pirddana; qassi Ayhude gidonna deriyas iya aathi immana.
He Ayhude gidonna derey iya toochchana, iya bolla cuttana, lisson garaafananne wodhana. I heedzu gallasappe guye, hayqoppe denddana” yaagis.
Zabdiyoosa nayti Yayqoobinne Yohaannisi Yesuusakko yidi, “Asttamaariyaw, nuuni nena woossiya issibaa nuus ootharkkii” yaagidosona.
Yesuusi enttako, “Taani hinttew ay ootho?” yaagis.
Entti, “Neeni ne bonchcho kawotethan uttiya wode nuuppe issuwa ushachcha baggara qassi issuwa haddirssa baggara uttisarkkii” yaagidosona.
Shin Yesuusi enttako, “Hintte ay woossiyako erekketa, ta uyanaw de7iya xuu7aa uyanaw dandda7etii? Qassi taani xammaqettanaw de7iya xinqqatiya xammaqettanaw dandda7etii?” yaagis.
Entti zaaridi, “Ee dandda7os” yaagidosona. Yesuusi qassi, “Tumakka ta uyanaw de7iya xuu7aa hintte uyana, taani xammaqettanaw de7iya xinqqatiya hintte xammaqettana.
Shin taappe ushachcha baggaranne haddirssa baggara uttanayssata dooranaw taw maati baawa, shin he bessay Xoossay immanaw giigisi wothidayssatassa” yaagis.
Hankko tammu tamaareti hessa si7ida wode Yayqoobanne Yohaannisa hanqettidosona.
Yesuusi entta ubbaa baakko xeegidi, “Ayhude gidonna asaa halaqati deriya haareyssata geetettidi xeegetteyssanne haareyssatas deriya bolla maati de7eyssa hintte ereeta.
Shin hintte giddon hessa mela gidenna; hintte giddon gitatanaw koyey oonikka hinttew aylle gidanaw bessees.
Qassi hintte giddon ubbaafe bolla gidanaw koyey oonikka hintte ubbaas aylle gidanaw bessees.
Hari attoshin, Asa Na7aykka, asaas oothanawunne darota wozanaw ba shemppuwa aathi immanaw yisippe attin asi iyaw oothana mela yibeenna” yaagis.
Entti Iyaarkko katama bidosona. Yesuusi ba tamaaretaranne daro asaara Iyaarkkofe keyishin, Ximoosa na7ay, qooqey, Barximoosa geetetteyssi, oge gaxan woossishe uttis.
Barximoosi, yaara aadhdhey Naazirete Yesuusa gididayssa si7ida wode ba qaala dhoqqu oothidi, “Dawite na7aa Yesuusa, tana maararkii!” yaagusu oykkis.
Daro asay iya, “Hayza!” gidi hanqettidosona. Shin, I ba qaala kaseyssafe daro dhoqqu oothidi, “Dawite na7aw, tana maararkii!” yaagis.
Yesuusi eqqidi, “Iya haa xeegite” yaagis. Entti qooqiyakko, “Aykkoy baawa, dendda eqqa, nena xeegees” yaagidosona.
Qooqey ba ma7uwa holi yeggidi, guppi denddi eqqidi, Yesuusakko bis.
Yesuusi, “Taani new ay oothana mela koyay?” yaagis. Qooqey, “Asttamaariyaw, ta xeellanaw koyays” yaagis.
Yesuusi iya, “Ba, ne ammanoy nena pathis” yaagis. Sohuwarakka iya ayfey xeellin, Yesuusa kaallis.
Entti Yerusalaame matishe, Shamaho Deriya matan de7iya Beetefaagenne Bitaaniya katamata gakkidosona. Yesuusi ba tamaaretappe nam77ata sinthe kiittidi,
“Hinttefe sinthan de7iya gutaa biite; yaa gelida mela oonikka toggiboonna qashon de7iya hare mari hintte demmana, iya billidi, haa ekki yiite.
Oonikka hinttena, ‘Hayssa ays ootheetii?’ yaagidi oychchiko, ‘Goday iya koyees, ellesidi haa yeddana’ yaagite” yaagis.
Entti bidi, hare mari kare bolla oge matan qashettidi de7eyssa demmidi billidosona.
He bessan eqqida issi issi asati enttako, “Hare maraa waatanaw billeeti?” yaagidosona.
Iya tamaareti Yesuusi banttana kiittidayssa odin, asati yeddi aggidosona.
Entti hare maraa Yesuusakko ehidi, bantta ma7uwa iya zokkon hiixin Yesuusi he hare maraa toggis.
Daro asay bantta ma7uwa ogiyan hiixidosona; qassi harati mitha tashe tashidi, ogen hiixidosona.
Yesuusappe sinthara hamuttiya asaynne iya kaalliya asay bantta qaala dhoqqu oothidi, “Hosaana! Xoossay galatetto! Godaa sunthan yeyssi anjjettidayssa.
Godaa sunthan yaa nu aawa Dawite kawotethay anjjettidayssa. Ubbaafe Bolla Saluwan de7iya Xoossay galatetto” yaagidosona.
Yesuusi Yerusalaame bidi, Xoossaa Keetha gelis. Qassi ubbabaa yuuyi xeellidaappe guye, sa7ay qammiya gisho tammanne nam77u tamaaretara Bitaaniya katama bis.
Wonttetha gallas entti Bitaaniyappe keyidi bishin, Yesuusi koshattis.
Haahon issi balase mithiw haytha xalaala ma77a uttidaaro be7idi, I bolla ayfey beettiko gidi, be7anaw iikko bis, shin iikko I biya wode haytha xalaalappe attin issi ayfekka demmibeenna; ays giikko, balasey ayfiyaa wodey gakkibeenna.
Yesuusi he balasiw, “Hiza, neeppe merinaw asi ayfe mooppo” yaagis. Iya tamaareti I geyssa si7idosona.
Entti Yerusalaame bidosona; Yesuusi Xoossa Keetha gelidi, yan bayzeyssatanne shammeyssata kare goodo oykkis; qassi miishe laammeyssata xarpheezanne holle bayzeyssata oydiya aathi yeggidi,
asi aybibaakka tookkidi, Xoossa Keetha giddora aadhdhonna mela diggis.
Yesuusi asaa hayssada yaagidi tamaarssis: “Geeshsha Maxaafan, ‘Ta keethay asi ubbay Xoossaa woossiya keethi gidana’ geetettidi xaafettis. Shin hintte iya panggati qosettiya gonggolo oothideta” yaagis.
Kahine halaqatinne higge asttamaareti hessa si7idi, iya wodhanaw oge koshshi oykkidosona. Shin daro asay iya timirttiyan malaalettiya gisho iyaw yayyidosona.
Sa7ay omarssiya wode Yesuusinne iya tamaareti katamaappe gaxa keyidosona.
Entti wonttetha gallas he ogiyara aadhdhishe, he balasiya xaphora melidaaro be7idosona.
Phexiroosi akeekidi, “Asttamaariyaw, hekko, neeni qanggida balasiya melasu” yaagis.
Yesuusi zaaridi, “Xoossaa ammanite.
Taani hinttew tuma odays; oonikka ba wozanan sidhonna gidabay hananayssa ammanidi, ha deriya, ‘Denddada abban kundda’ yaagikko iyaw hanana.
Hessa gisho, taani hinttew odays; Xoossaa hintte woossiyabaanne oychchiyabaa aybaa gidikkoka ekkidaada ammanite, hintte ekkana.
Xoossaa woossanaw hintte eqqiya wode salon de7iya hintte Aaway hintte nagara atto gaana mela, oonikka hinttena naaqidabay de7ikko, iyaw atto giite.
Shin asa nagara hintte atto goonna ixxiko, salon de7iya hintte Aawaykka hintte nagaraa hinttew atto geenna” yaagis.
Entti zaaridi Yerusalaame bidosona. Yesuusi Xoossa Keethan hamuttishin, kahine halaqati, higge asttamaaretinne cimati iyaakko yidi,
“Neeni hayssa oothanaw new ay maati de7ii? Woykko new ha maata immiday oonee?” yaagidosona.
Yesuusi zaaridi enttako, “Ta hinttena issibaa oychchana, taw odite. Ta qassi hayssa ay maatan oothiyako, hinttew odana.
Yohaannisa xinqqatey Xoossafeyye woykko asappe? Taw odite” yaagis.
Entti bantta giddon palama doomidi, “Nuuni, ‘Xoossafe’ giikko, I nuukko, ‘Yaatin, Yohaannisi odidayssa ays ammanibeekketii?’ yaagana.
‘Asappe giikko’ asa ubbay Yohaannisi nabe gideyssa eroosona.” Yaaniya gisho asaas yayyidosona.
Hessa gisho, entti Yesuusakko, “Nuuni erokko” yaagidi zaaridosona; Yesuusi, “Taanikka hayssa ay maatan oothiyako, hinttew odikke” yaagis.
Yesuusi enttaw leemison yaagidi odis; “Issi uray woyne atakiltte tokkidi, yuushshi aathidi dirssi diris. Qassi he woyniya gum77iya olaaka bookkis. Iya naaganaw adussa shakko shakkis. Hessafe guye, kothe oothiya asaas immidi, hara biitta bis.
Woyne ayfiyaa maxiya wodey gakkin, bana gakkeyssa ekkidi yaana mela, issi ba aylliya kothe aawatakko kiittis.
Kothe aawati iya aylliya oykkidi wadhdhidi, mela kushe yeddidosona.
Nam77antho hara aylle enttako kiittin, entti he aylliyas huu7iya qoo7idi kawushshidi yeddidosona.
Woyne atakilttiya goday qassika hara aylle kiittis. He aylliya wodhidosona, qassi hara darota hessada oothidosona, issota issota wadhdhidi, harata wodhidosona.
“Woyne atakilttiya godaas kiittanaw ubbaafe wurssethan I daro dosiya ba na7aa xalaali attis. I, “Entti ta na7aa bonchchonna aggokona” gidi, ba na7aa enttako kiittis.
“Shin kothe aawati bantta giddon, ‘Laattanayssi hayssa; yedhdhite iya wodhoos; iya laatay nubaa gidana!’ yaagidosona.
Na7aa oykkidi wodhidi, iya ahaa woyne atakilttiya giddofe gaxa kessi holidosona.
“Hiza, woyne atakilttiya goday waatanee? Yidi he kothe aawata wodhi onggidi, woyniya kothe oothiya hara asas immana.
‘Gimbbeyssati boridi ixxida shuchchay godaa xaphuwa minthiya, ubbaafe aadhdhiya shuchchu gidis. Hayssi Goday oothidabaa; qassi nu ayfiyaaskka malaalisiyabaa’ yaageyssa Geeshsha Maxaafaappe nabbabibeekketii?” yaagis.
<range>
Kahine halaqati, higge asttamaaretinne cimati Yesuusi he leemisuwa bantta bolla leemisidayssa erida gisho iya oykkanaw koyidosona, shin asaas yayyidi, aggi bidosona.
Qassi iya odaappe bala demmidi, iya oykkana mela, Farisaawetappenne Heroodisa baggatappe guutha asata iyaakko kiittidosona.
Entti iyaakko yidi, “Asttamaariyaw, neeni tuma odetteyssanne asappe ase shaakkonnayssa nuuni eroos. Neeni ase dummayakka; qassi Xoossaa ogiya tumatethan tamaarssaasa. Nuuni Roome biittaa Kawuwa Qeesares giira giireyssi wogeyye woga gidennee? Giira giiranee agganee?” yaagidosona.
Shin entta cubbotethaa Yesuusi eridi, “Tana ays paacetii? Ane issi santime tana bessite” yaagis.
Entti iyaw ehidosona, “Ha malaynne sunthay ooddeysee?” yaagidi entta oychchis. Entti, “Roome Kawuwa Qeesareyssa” yaagidosona.
Yesuusi zaaridi, “Yaatikko, Qeesareyssa Qeesares, Xoossayssa Xoossaas immite” yaagin entti iyabaa malaalettidosona.
Hayqqida asi denddenna giya Saduqaawetappe issi issi asati Yesuusakko yidi, hayssada yaagidi, iya oychchidosona.
“Asttamaariyaw, Musey nuus higgiya xaafishe, ‘Machcho ekkida asi na7a yelonna hayqqiko, he hayqqidayssa ishay iya machchiw ekkidi, ba ishaas na7a yelanaw bessees’ yaageyssa xaafis.
Beni wode laappun ishati de7eyssatappe bayray machcho ekkidi, na7a yelonna hayqqis.
Nam77anthoy iyo ekkis, ikka na7a yelonna hayqqis. Heedzanthoyka hessada hanis.
Laappunatikka hessatho iyo ekkidi, na7a yelonna hayqqidosona. Ubbaafe guye, qassi he maccasiya hayqqasu.
Yaatin, laappunati iyo ekkida gisho hayqqida asay hayqoppe denddiya gallas, iya enttafe awussas machcho gidanee?” yaagidosona.
Yesuusi zaaridi, “Hintte baley, Geeshsha Maxaafata woykko Xoossaa wolqqaa eronna gishossa!
Hayqqida asay hayqoppe denddiya gallas, salon de7iya kiitanchchota mela gidanaappe attin adde asay ekkokona; macca asay gelekkona.
Shin hayqqidayssata dendduwabaa gidikko, Muse maxaafan xaafettida xuugettiya buuriyabaa odiya bessan, Xoossay Musekko, ‘Taani, Abrahame Xoossaa, Yisaaqa Xoossaa, Yayqooba Xoossaa’ gidayssa nabbabibeekketii?
Hessa gisho, I, paxa de7eyssata Xoossaafe attin hayqqidayssata Xoosse gidenna. Hintte daro balideta” yaagis.
Higge asttamaaretappe issoy entti palameyssa shiiqidi si7is. Qassi Yesuusi enttaw loythi zaaridayssa si7idi, “Kiita ubbaafe aadhdhiya kiitay awussee?” yaagidi Yesuusa oychchis.
Yesuusi zaaridi, iya hayssada yaagis: “Kiita ubbaafe aadhdhiya kiitaa si7ite; ‘Isra7eele asaw, Goday nu Xoossay issi Godaa.
Ne Godaa ne Xoossaa ne kumetha wozanappe, ne kumetha shemppuwafe, ne kumetha qofaappe, ne kumetha wolqqaafe dosa’ yaagees.
Qassi kiita ubbaafe aadhdhiya nam77antho kiitay hayssa; ‘Ase ubbaa ne huu7iyada dosa’ yaageyssa; hayssatappe aadhdhiya hara kiiti baawa” yaagis.
Higge asttamaarey Yesuusakko, “Asttamaariyaw, tuma gadasa; neeni ‘Xoossay issi Xoossaa xalaala. Iyappe attin hari baawa’ gidayssi tuma.
Xoossaa kumetha wozanappe, kumetha qofaappenne kumetha wolqqaafe doseysinne qassi ase ubbaa ba huu7iyada doseyssi, xuuggiya yarshshuwafenne hara yarshsho ubbaafe aadhdhees” yaagis.
Yesuusi higge asttamaariya zaaroy aadhdhida eranchcho asa zaaro gididayssa be7idi, “Neeni Xoossaa kawotethaafe haakkabaakka” yaagis; hessafe guye, Yesuusa harabaa oychchanaw oonikka minnibeenna.
Yesuusi Xoossa Keethan tamaarssishe, hayssada yaagis: “Higge asttamaareti Kiristtoosa woygidi Dawite na7a goonaa?
Dawitey Geeshsha Ayyaanan kumidi, ‘Goday, ta Godaa, “Taani ne morkketa ne tohoy yedhdhiyaso oothana gakkanaw, hayssan taappe ushachcha baggara utta” gis’ yaagis.
Dawitey ba huu7en Kiristtoosa, ‘Godaa’ gidi xeegikko, yaatin, Kiristtoosi waanidi, Dawite na7a gidii” yaagis. Daro asay Yesuusi geyssa ufayssan si7idosona.
Yesuusi tamaarssishe, hayssada yaagis: “Higge asttamaaretappe naagettite; entti adussa ma7o ma77idi yuuyeyssanne giyankka asay entta bonchchidi sarotheyssa dosoosona.
Entti Ayhude Woosa Keethatan daro lo77o oyde dosoosona; qassi asi banttana mokkiya bessan bonchcho bessi dosoosona.
Entti am77eta keethaa bonqidi, banttaw lo77o daananaw woosa adussoosona; entti ubbaafe aadhdhiya pirddaa ekkana” yaagis.
Yesuusi Xoossa Keethan muxaata yeggiya saaxiniya matan uttidi, asay ba miishiya he saaxiniyan yeggeyssa be7is; daro dure asay daro miishiya he saaxiniyan yeggoosona.
Issi manqo am77iya yada, nam77u bakkannata he saaxiniyan yeggasu.
Yesuusi ba tamaareta xeegidi, “Taani hinttew tuma odays; muxaata saaxiniyan yeggida asa ubbaafe ha manqo am77iya darssada yeggasu.
Ays giikko, harati ubbay banttaw palahida miishiyappe yeggidosona. Shin iya ba pacciyaafe, baw de7iya aquwaa kumethi immasu” yaagis.
Yesuusi Xoossa Keethafe keyishin, iya tamaaretappe issoy, “Asttamaariyaw, ha lo77o shuchchaanne ha lo77o shuchcha keethaa be7ay!” yaagis.
Yesuusi zaaridi, “Ha gita shuchcha keethaa be7ay? Ha keethay shuchchi shuchcha bolla gimbbettida mela laalettonna attenna; issi shuchchika attonna ubbay laalettana” yaagis.
Yesuusi Xoossa keethafe hini baggara Shamaho Deriya bolla uttidashin, Phexiroosi, Yayqoobi, Yohaannisinne Inddiriyasi banttarkka iyaakko yidi,
“Hayssi awude hananeekko, nuus oda; ha ubbay polettana wodiya erisiya malaatay aybee?” yaagidi oychchidosona.
Yesuusi qassi enttaw hayssada yaagidi odis: “Hinttena oonikka balethonna mela naagettite.
Daro asati ta sunthan, ‘Taani Kiristtoosa’ yaagidi tamaarssishe yidi, daro asaa balethana.
Matan de7iya olaanne haahon de7iya ola wore hintte si7iya wode hirggofite. Hessa melabay hananaw bessees, shin wurssethay buroona.
Issi biittaa asay hara biitta asaara olettana; qassi issi kawotethay hara kawotethatara olettana; biittaa qaaxoy ubba bessan hanana; koshay daana, shin hessi ubbay yelo iqethas zooke mela.
“Shin hinttee, hintte huu7en naagettite. Ays giikko, asi hinttena oykkidi, pirdda keethas aathi immana; qassi Ayhude Woosa Keethatankka hinttena lisson garaafana; deriya haareyssata sinthaninne kawota sinthan ta gisho hintte markkattanaw eqqana.
Wurssethay gakkanaappe sinthe Wonggelay koyro dere ubbaas odettanaw bessees.
Entti hinttena pirdda keethi ehiya wodenne aathi immiya wode woygidi odaneekko koyro hirggofite; he saatiyan Xoossay hinttew immiyabaa odite. Hinttenan Geeshsha Ayyaanay odetteesippe attin hinttena gidekketa.
“Ishay ba ishaa, aaway ba na7aa wodhisana. Nayti banttana yelidayssata bolla denddidi, entta wodhisana.
Asay ubbay hinttena ta sunthaa gisho ixxana, shin wurssethi gakkanaw minniday attana.
“Shin bashshaa tunatethay eqqanaw bessonna bessan eqqidashin hintte be7ana.” (Akeekiso: Hessi woy guusseeko nabbabeyssi akeeko!) “Yihuda biittan he wode de7eyssati deriyakko baqato.
Keetha huu7en de7iya uraykka issibaa ekkanaw duge wodhdhidi, ba soo geloppo.
Gaden de7eyssi ba ma7uwa ekkanaw guye simmofo.
He wode qanthatida maccasatasinne dhanthiya maccasatas daro un77a gidana.
Shin hayssi ubbay haniya wodey balggo gidonna mela, Xoossaa woossite.
Ays giikko, Xoossay alamiya medhdhida wodiyappe doomidi, ha77i gakkanaw haniboonna metoynne sinthafekka hanonna metoy asa bolla he wode hanana.
Goday he gallasata taybuwa guuthonaako, ase gididay oonikka attenna. Shin I ba doorida asa gisho he gallasata taybuwa guuthees.
“He wode oonikka hinttena, ‘Hekko, Kiristtoosi hayssan de7ees woykko Kiristtoosi hinin de7ees’ yaagikko, hessa ammanoppite.
Worddanchcho Kiristtoosatinne worddo nabeti denddidi banttaw dandda7ettiko, hari attoshin Xoossay dooridayssatakka balethanaw malaatatanne malaalisiyabata bessana.
Shin hintte naagettite; taani hinttew ubbabaa kasetada odas.
“Shin he wode he waayappe guye, away dhumana; ageenay poo7uwa aggana;
xoolinttoti saloppe kunddana; qassi salon de7iya wolqqatikka qaaxxana.
He wode Asa Na7ay, gita wolqqaranne bonchchuwara shaara giddora yishin entti be7ana.
He wode taani kiitanchchota sa7a oyddu bagga kiittana; sa7a gaxappe saluwa gaxa gakkanaw, Xoossay doorida asaa shiishana.
“Leemisuwa balase mithaafe akeekite; balasiya aaciya wodenne I haythay cil77iya wode torchchey matattidayssa hintte ereeta.
Hessadakka, hintte he ubbabay haneyssa be7iya wode I matidi pengge gakkidayssa erite.
Taani hinttew tuma odays; ha ubbabay hanana gakkanaw hayssan de7iya asa ubbay hayqqenna.
Saloynne sa7ay aadhdhana, shin ta qaalay ubbarakka aadhdhenna.
“Shin he gallasaanne he saatiya Aawa xalaalappe attin hari attoshin salon de7iya kiitanchchota gidin woykko Na7aa gidin oonikka erey baawa.
He wodey awude gidaneekko, hintte eronna gisho naagettitenne minnite.
Ta yuussay ba keetha aggidi, oge biya uraa mela. Uray ba aylleta huu7en huu7en oosuwa immidi entta ba oosuwas aawa oothis; qassi naageysika minthidi naagana mela kiittis.
“Hessa gisho, minnite. Ays giikko, keethaaway omarssi gidin woykko giddi bilahe gidin woykko kutto waaso gidin woykko wontta guura gidin awude yaanekko, hintte erekketa.
Hintte akeekonna I yidi hinttena dhiskkidi de7ishin demmonna mela minnite.
Taani hinttew odeyssa asa ubbaas odays; minnite” yaagis.
Paasika Baale bonchchiya gallasaynne Uytha Baale bonchchiya gallasay gakkanaw nam77u gallasi attis. Kahine halaqatinne higge asttamaareti asi eronna Yesuusa oykkidi wodhdhiya oge koyoosona.
“Asay ooshshi kessonna mela Paasika bonchchiya gallasan hessa oothoko” yaagidosona.
Yesuusi Bitaaniya kataman baro hargganchchuwa Simoona son gibira bolla uttidashin, issi maccasiya albasxiroose giya shuchchafe oosettida philqqaaxe kumetha narddoose giya daro al77o shitto ekkada yasu. He philqqaaxiya menthada shittuwa Yesuusa huu7iyan tigasu.
He bessan de7iya asappe issoy issoy hanqettidi, “Ha shittoy mela coo iitey aybisse?
Ha shittuwa heedzu xeetu dinaaren bayzidi, miishiya manqotas immanaw dandda7ettees” yaagidi bantta giddon odettidosona. Yaatidi, he maccasiw daro boridosona.
Shin Yesuusi “Ha maccasiw aykkoka gooppite; iyo ays waaysetii? Iya taw lo77obaa oothasu.
Manqoti ubba wode hinttera de7oosona. Hintte koyida wode awudekka hintte entta maaddanaw dandda7eeta, shin taani ubba wode hinttera de7ikke.
Iya ba dandda7idayssa oothasu; qassi tana moogos giigisanaw kasetada shitto tiyasu.
Taani hinttew tuma odays; sa7a ubban Wonggelaa odiyason awunkka, asay iyo akeekana mela ha iya oothidayssi odettana” yaagis.
Tammanne nam77u tamaaretappe issoy Asqoroota Yihuda geetetteyssi Yesuusa kahine halaqatas aathi immanaw enttako bis.
Entti hessa si7ida wode ufayttidi, “Nuuni new miishe immana” yaagidosona; Yihudi Yesuusa aathi immanaw injje wode koyees.
Uythaa Baaley bonchchettiya koyro gallas, Paasika kathaa maanaw maraze shukkiya wode Yesuusa tamaareti iyakko, “Paasika bonchchiya gallas neeni maana kathaa nuuni aw bidi giigisino?” gidi oychchidosona.
Yesuusi ba tamaaretappe nam77ata hayssada yaagidi kiittis: “Katamaa biite; hintte bishin, otora haathe tookkida issi uray hinttera gahettana; iya kaallite.
I bidi geliya keethaawa, ‘Asttamaarey neekko, “Taani ta tamaaretara Paasika maanaw imatha kifiley awunee?” yaagees’ yaagite.
Keethaaway hinttena pooqiya bolla de7iya giigi uttida dalgga kifile bessana; hessan giigisite” yaagis.
He nam77u tamaareti keyidi, katama bidosona; Yesuusi enttaw odidayssada demmidi, Paasika kathaa giigisidosona.
Sa7ay omarssiya wode Yesuusi tammanne nam77u tamaaretara yaa bis.
Entti uttidi kathi mishin, Yesuusi enttako, “Taani hinttew tuma odays; hinttefe issoy taara meyssi, tana aathi immana” yaagis.
Iya tamaareti dagammidi, bantta huu7en huu7en, “Tuma taneshsha?” yaagidi iya oychchidosona.
Yesuusi zaaridi, “He uray hintte tammanne nam77atappe issuwa; I taara issife tushanaw ba uythaa shaatiyan yeddeyssa.
Asa Na7ay, Geeshsha Maxaafay hayqqana gidayssada hayqqana, shin Asa Na7aa, aathi immiya uraa ayye. He uray yelettonna attidaakko iyaw lo77oshin” yaagis.
Entti miishin, Yesuusi uythaa ekkidi, Xoossaa galatis; he uythaa menthidi, ba tamaaretas immishe, “He7ite, hayssi ta ashuwa” yaagis.
Xuu7aa ekkidi, Xoossaa galatidi, enttaw immin ubbayka he xuu7appe uyidosona.
Yesuusi, “Hayssi ooratha caaquwan daro asaa gisho gukkiya ta suuthaa.
Taani hinttew tuma odays; taani Xoossaa kawotethan ooratha woyniya uyana gallasay gakkanaw zaarada ha woyniyappe uyikke” yaagis.
Mazmure yexxidaappe guye Shamaho Deriya bolla bidosona.
Yesuusi enttako, “Hintte ubbay tana yeggi aggidi baqatana; Geeshsha Maxaafay, ‘Xoossay dorssa heemmeyssa wodhana, dorssati ubbay laalettana’ yaagees.
Shin taani hayqoppe denddidaappe guye hinttefe kasetada Galiila baana” yaagis.
Phexiroosi zaaridi, “Entti ubbay nena yeggi aggidi baqatikkoka, ta nena aggike” yaagis.
Yesuusi Phexiroosakko, “Taani new tuma odays; hachchi qamma kuttoy nam77u toho waassanaappe sinthe neeni tana heedzu toho kaddana” yaagis.
Shin Phexiroosi kaseyssafe minthidi, “Taani hari attoshin, neera issife hayqqiyakokka, nena kaddike” yaagis. Qassi harati ubbatikka hessada gidosona.
Geetesemaane giya bessaa bidosona; Yesuusi ba tamaaretakko, “Taani Xoossaa woossada simmana gakkanaw hintte hayssan uttishite” yaagis.
Yesuusi Phexiroosa, Yayqoobanne Yohaannisa baara ekkidi bis; daro waayettisinne un77ettis.
Qassi enttako, “Taani hayqqana gakkanaw azzanas, hayssan gam77ishite; dhiskkofite” yaagis.
Guuthi sinthe shiiqidi, sa7an gufannidi, dandda7ettiyabaa gidikko, he waaya saatey baappe aadhdhana mela, Xoossaa woossis.
Qassi, “Abbaa, ta Aawaw, ubbabay new dandda7ettees, ha waaye xuu7aa taappe digga. Shin ne sheney hanoppe attin ta sheney hanoppo” yaagis.
Yesuusi ba tamaaretakko simmi yidi, entti dhiskkidashin demmidi, Phexiroosakko, “Simoonaa, dhiskkadii? Neeni issi saatekka barkkada naaganaw dandda7abiikkii?
Paacen hintte gelonna mela barkkidi naagitenne Xoossaa woossite. Hinttew lo77o amoy de7ees, shin hintte daaburanchcho asi” yaagis.
Qassika bidi kaseyssadakka Xoossaa woossis.
Ba tamaaretakko guye simmidi yaa wode dhiskkidashin demmis. Entta ayfiyaa dhiskkoy goozi wothida gisho iyaakko ay odettiyakokka erokkona.
Heedzantho enttako yidi, “Ha77i gakkanawukka dhiskkeetinne shemppetii? Hiza, gidana; saatey gakkis; be7ite! Asa Na7ay, nagaranchcho asatas aadhdhi imettana wodey gakkis.
Denddidi yedhdhite; be7ite, tana aathi immanayssi gakkis” yaagis.
Yesuusi hessa buroo odishin, tammanne nam77u iya tamaaretappe issoy, Yihudi, ellesidi gakki wodhdhis. Qassi kahine halaqati, higge asttamaaretinne cimati kiittin, mashshenne xam77a oykkida daro asay iyara issife yidosona.
Yesuusa aathi immanayssi he daro asaas, “Taani yeerey iya; iya oykkidi, loythi naagidi, ekki efite” yaagidi malla odi wothis.
Yihudi gakki wodhdhida mela Yesuusakko shiiqidi, “Asttamaariyaw” yaagidi Yesuusa yeeri ekkis.
He daro asay Yesuusa oykkidosona.
Shin matan eqqidayssatappe issoy ba mashshaa shoddidi kahine halaqaa aylliya shocidi, iya haytha qanxidi holis.
Yesuusi zaaridi, he shiiqida daro asaakko, “Tana pangga kessidi, pangga oykkeyssada oykkanaw mashshenne xam77a oykkidi yidetii?
Taani Xoossa Keethan tamaarssashe, gallas gallas hinttera de7iya wode tana oykkibeekketa, shin Geeshsha Maxaafay gidayssi polettanaw bessees” yaagis.
Iya tamaareti ubbay iya yeggi aggidi baqatidosona.
Laxana xalaala ma77ida issi naatetha uray Yesuusa kaalleyssa asay oykkis.
Shin he uray laxana yeggi aggidi, xire kallo baqatis.
Asay Yesuusa kahine halaqaa soo efidosona. Yan kahine halaqati, cimatinne higge asttamaareti shiiqidi de7oosona.
Phexiroosi kahine halaqaa zabbaa gakkanaw haahon iya kaalli bidi yan naageyssatara uttidi tama kayees.
Kahine halaqatinne shiiqida asa ubbay Yesuusa wodhanaw iya bolla markka koyidosona, shin aykkoka demmibookkona.
Daro asati iya bolla worddo markkattidosona, shin entta markkatethay issino gidenna.
Issi issi asati denddi eqqidi Yesuusa bolla, “I, ‘Taani asi keexida ha Xoossa Keetha laallada, asa kushen keexettiboonna hara Xoossa Keetha heedzu gallasa giddon keexana’ gishin nuuni si7ida” yaagidi worddo markkattidosona.
<range>
Gidoshin, entta markkatethay hessankka issino gidenna.
Kahine halaqay asa ubbaa sinthan denddi eqqidi, “Hayssati nena mootiya mootuwas ne zaariyabay baawe?” yaagidi Yesuusa oychchis.
Shin Yesuusi si77i gis; aykkoka zaaribeenna. Kahine halaqay, “Anjjettida Xoossaa Na7ay, Kiristtoosi neneyye?” yaagidi zaari oychchis.
Yesuusi zaaridi, “Ee tana, hintte Asa Na7ay, wolqqaama Xoossaafe ushachcha baggara uttidashin qassi saluwa shaarara yishin be7ana” yaagis.
Kahine halaqay ba ma7uwa peedhidi, “Nuna hara markka ay koshshii?
Hintte iya cashshaa si7ideta; hintte qofay aybee?” yaagis. Entti ubbay, “I hayqqanaw bessees” yaagidi iya bolla pirddidosona.
Enttafe issoti issoti iya bolla cutethi oykkidosona. Iya ayfiyaa goozidi baqqishe, “Nena dechchiday oonee? Ane nuus oda!” yaagidosona. Naageyssati iya ekki efidi garaafidosona.
Phexiroosi kahine halaqaa zabban garssa baggara de7ishin, kahine halaqaa macca aylletappe issinniya yaa yasu.
Phexiroosi tama kayeyssa be7ada, tishshi ootha xeellada, “Neenikka Naazirete Yesuusara de7aasa” yaagasu.
Shin Phexiroosi, “Ne geyssi aybeekko ta erikke, taw akeekettenna” yaagidi kaddis. Yaagi simmidi zago keyaa wode sohuwara kuttoy waassis.
He aylliya Phexiroosa be7ada, iya matan eqqida asatakko, “Ha uraykka enttara de7ees” gada zaara odasu.
Shin Phexiroosi qassika kaddis. Guuthi gam77ishin, matan eqqida asati nam77antho Phexiroosakko, “Neeni Galiila biitta asi gidiya gisho tuma enttara de7aasa” yaagidosona.
Shin Phexiroosi, “Taani hintte giya uraa erikke!” yaagidi bana qanggethinne caaqo oykkis.
Sohuwara kuttoy nam77antho waassi aggis. Phexiroosi Yesuusi iyaakko, “Neeni kuttoy nam77u toho waassanaappe sinthe heedzu toho tana kaddana” iyaakko gidayssa akeekidi daro yeekkis.
Wontta guura ellesidi kahine halaqati, cimati, higge asttamaaretinne Ayhude shanggoti ubbay shiiqidi maqettidosona. Entti Yesuusa qachchi efidi Philaaxoosas aathi immidosona.
Philaaxoosi iyakko, “Neeni Ayhudeta kawo?” yaagidi oychchis. Yesuusi zaaridi, “Ne gadasa” yaagis.
Kahine halaqati Yesuusa daroban mootidosona.
Shin Philaaxoosi zaaridi Yesuusakko, “New zaariyabay baawe? Entti ne bolla ay mela mootuwa ehiyakko be7ikki?” yaagis.
Shin Yesuusi harabaa zaaronna ixxin, Philaaxoosi malaalettis.
Philaaxoosas Paasika Baale bonchchiya gallasan asay koyaa issi uraa qashoppe billiya meezey de7ees.
He wode issi Barbbaana giya uray ooshshu kessidi shemppo wodhida asatara issife qasho keethan de7ees.
Shiiqida daro asay Philaaxoosi kaseyssada oothana mela iya oychchidosona.
Philaaxoosi asa zaaridi, “Taani hinttew Ayhudeta kawuwa billanayssa koyeetii?” yaagidi oychchis.
Hessa I giday, kahine halaqati Yesuusa qanaattidi aathi immidayssa eriya gishossa.
Shin kahine halaqati Yesuusa gisho Barbbaana billanaada, he shiiqida asay Philaaxoosa woossana mela asa maqqidosona.
Philaaxoosi zaaridi, “Yaatin, ha hintte Ayhude kawo geyssa waato?” yaagis.
Asay Philaaxoosa bolla waassidi, “Masqaliya bolla iya kaqqa” yaagidosona.
Philaaxoosi asaakko, “Ays? I ay iitabaa oothidee?” yaagis. Shin asay kaseyssafe gujji waassidi, “Masqaliya bolla iya kaqqa” yaagidosona.
Philaaxoosi asaa ufayssanaw koyidi, Barbbaana asaas billis; yaatidi lisson Yesuusa garaafidi, masqaliya bolla kaqqana mela enttaw aathi immis.
Hessafe guye, wotaaddareti Yesuusa deriya haareyssa ooso keetha ekki efidi, hara wotaaddareta ubbaa issife xeegidosona.
Qassi zo7o afilaa iya mayzidosona; aguntha kalachcha giigisidi, iya huu7en wothidosona.
Hessafe guye, iyakko, “Ayhudeta kawuwaw mirinaw kawota” yaagidi, iyaw ziggidosona.
Iya huu7iya xam77an shoccidosona; qassi iya bolla cuttidosona; gulbbatidi iyaw goynnidosona.
Iya toochchidayssafe guye zo7o afilaa iyappe qaari ekkidi, iya afilaa iya mayzidi masqaliya bolla iya kaqqanaw ekki efidosona.
Entti bishe, Iskkinddirenne Rufoosa aawa, Simoona giya Qereena biitta asi, gaxareppe katama yeyssara gahettidi, Yesuusa masqaliya wolqqan toossidosona.
Yaatidi Golggotta giya bessaa Yesuusa efidosona. “Golggotta” guussay “Huu7e guugge” guussu.
Sakoy si7ettonna mela karbbe giya dhaley walakettida woyne uyo gidi iyaw immidosona. Shin I uyonna ixxis.
Entti masqaliya bolla iya kaqqidosona. Oona aybi gakkaneekko gidi iya afilaa shaakkidi saama yeggidosona.
Entti masqaliya bolla iya kaqqiya wode wonttafe heedzu saate.
Entti, “Ayhudeta kawuwa” yaagidi iya mootiya xuufe xaafidi wothidosona.
Yesuusara nam77u panggata issuwa iyappe ushachcha baggara hankkuwa iyappe haddirssa baggara masqaliya bolla kaqqidosona.
Geeshsha Maxaafay, “Iitabaa oothida asatara I paydettis” geetettidayssi polettis.
Ogiyara aadhdhiya asay Yesuusa kadhidi, bantta huu7iya qaathiddi cayidosona; “Hekko! Xoossa Keetha laallada heedzu gallasa giddon keexeysso, ne huu7iya ashsha;
ane masqaliya bollafe wodhdha” yaagidosona.
Hessadakka, kahine halaqati higgiya tamaarsseyssatara issife Yesuusa toochchidi, “Harata ashshis, shin bana ashshanaw dandda7enna;
nuuni be7idi ammanana mela Kiristtoosi, Isra7eele Kawoy, ane masqaliya bollafe ha77i wodhdho” yaagidosona. Qassi hari attoshin, iyara masqaliya bolla kaqettidayssatikka iya toochchidosona.
Usuppun saateppe doomidi, uddufun saate gakkanaw biitta ubbay dhumis.
Uddufun saatiyan Yesuusi ba qaala dhoqqu oothidi, “Elohee, Elohee, laama sabaqitani?” yaagis. Hessa guussay, “Ta Xoossaw, ta Xoossaw, tana ays aggadi?” guussu.
Hessan eqqida asappe issoy issoy hessa si7idi, “Hekko, Eliyaasa xeegees” yaagis.
He asappe issoy woxxidi, ispponjjen caala woyne kunthis; hessa xam77a xeeran wothidi, “Naagite; Eliyaasi masqaliyappe iya wodhisanaw yaanekko ane be7oos” yaagidi Yesuusa doonaakko ushshanaw shiishis.
Yesuusi ba qaala dhoqqu oothi waassidi, hayqqis.
Xoossa Keethan kaqettida magaraajjoy qommofe duge gakkanaw, nam77u keyidi daaketi wodhdhis.
Masqaliyappe sintha baggara yan eqqida issi mato halaqay, Yesuusi waanidi hayqqidaakko be7ida wode “Ha uray tuma Xoossaa Na7a” yaagis.
Hessa haahon eqqidi be7iya guutha maccasati de7oosona. Entta giddon Magdela Mayraama, kaaluwa Yayqoobanne Yoosa aayyaa Mayraamanne Salooma de7oosona.
He macca asati Yesuusi Galiilan de7iya wode iya kaallidayssatanne iya mokkidayssata qassi Yesuusara issife Yerusalaame bida hara daro macca asati yan de7oosona.
Sa7ay omarssida wode shiiqida asan bonchchettida Ayhude shanggotappe issoy, Yoosefa giya uray, Xoossaa kawotethay yaanayssa naagishe de7eyssi, Armmatiyasa katama asi de7eyssi yis. Wonttethe Sambbaatas giigettiya gallas gidida gisho Yoosefi minnidi Philaaxoosakko bidi, Yesuusa ahaa ekkanaw woossis.
<range>
Philaaxoosi Yesuusi hayqqidayssa si7ida wode malaalettis; mato halaqaa xeegidi, “I hayqqidi gam77idee?” yaagidi oychchis.
Philaaxoosi Yesuusi hayqqidayssa mato halaqaappe si7idi iya ahaa Yoosefas immis.
Yoosefi moogo afila shammis; Yesuusa ahaa masqaliyappe wothidi, afilan xaaxidi, shuchchafe woocettida duufo giddon iya aha moogis. Qassi he duufuwa doonan gita shuchchu gonddorssidi wothis.
Magdela Mayraamanne Yoosa aayyaa Mayraama Yesuusa ahaa entti awun wothiyako be7oosona.
Sambbaatay aadhdhidaappe guye Magdela Mayraama, Yayqooba aayyaa Mayraamanne Salooma bidi, Yesuusa ahaa tiyanaw shitto shammidosona.
Wogga wode wontta daro guura xalqey caarshin, duufuwa bidosona.
Entti bantta giddon issoy issuwara, “Duufuwa doonappe nuus shuchchaa oonee gonddorssidi digganay?” yaagidi odettidosona.
Entti xeelliya wode he daro gita shuchchay gonddorettidi kichchidayssa be7idosona.
Yesuusi moogettida duufuwa giddo geliya wode issi pantha addey bootha ma7o ma77idi, ushachcha baggara uttidayssa be7idi dagammidosona.
Shin I enttako, “Dagammofite; masqaliya bolla kaqettida, Naazirete Yesuusa hintte koyeyssa taani erays. I hayssan deenna, hayqoppe denddis. Entti iya moogida bessaa hayssa be7ite.
Ha77i bidi Yesuusa tamaaretasinne Phexiroosas, ‘Yesuusi hinttefe sinthattidi Galiila bees. I hinttew odidayssada hintte iya yan be7ana’ yaagidi odite” yaagis.
Maccasati yashshan kokkorishe duufuwappe keyidi baqatidosona. Qassi entti yayyida gisho hessa ooddeskka aykkoka odibookkona.
Yesuusi hayqoppe denddidaappe guye wogga gallas wontta, laappun tuna ayyaanata kessida Magdela Mayraamis koyrottidi benttis.
Iya bada kase iyara de7eyssatas, entti azzanishenne yeekkishe de7ishin odasu.
Shin Yesuusi paxa de7eyssanne iw benttidayssa entti si7ida wode iya geyssa ammanibookkona.
Hessafe guye, enttafe nam77ati katamaappe keyidi bishin, oge bolla Yesuusi kaseyssafe dummattidi enttaw benttis.
Entti guye simmidi, haratas odidosona, shin haratikka entta odaa tuma gibookkona.
Guyeppe tammanne issi iya tamaareti kathi miishin, Yesuusi enttaw benttis. Enttaw ammanoy baynna gishonne hayqoppe I denddidayssa be7ida asay odin entti ammanonna ixxida gisho I entta boris.
I enttako, “Biitta ubbaa bidi asa ubbaas Wonggelaa odite.
Ammaneynne xammaqetey attana, shin ammanonnay pirddettana.
Ammaneyssatas ha malaatati imettana. Entti ta sunthan tuna ayyaanata kessana, ooratha doonan odettana.
Entti shooshu oykkikokka woykko wodhiyabaa uyikkoka entta qohenna. Qassi entti bantta kushiya hargganchchota bolla wothidi entta pathana” yaagis.
Goday Yesuusi tamaaretara odettidaappe guye pude salo keyis; Xoossaafe ushachcha baggara uttis.
Iya tamaareti bidaso ubban qaala odidosona. Godaykka enttara issife oothees. Entti odiya qaalay tuma gididayssa Xoossay enttaw immiya malaatatan erisis.
Bonchcho Tewofiloosa, nu giddon polettidabas daroti, banttaw dandda7ettida mela xaafidosona.
He taarikiya entti xaafiday koyroppe doomidi ayfe markkatinne qaala haggaazeyssati nuus odidayssa.
Takka ta baggara koyroppe akeeka xeellidaappe guye he taarikiya hanotaa maarayada new xaafoy taw lo77o gidi benttis.
Hessika, ne tamaaridabay tuma gideyssa erisanaassa.
Yihuda kawuwa Heroodisa wode Abiya yaraappe gidida Zakkariyaasa giya Ayhude kahiney de7ees. Iya machchiyaka Aarona sheeshaappe. I sunthaykka Elssabeexo.
Nam77ayka Godaa wogaanne kiita ubbaa naagidi borey baynna Xoossaa sinthan xillotethan de7idosona.
Hanoppe attin Elssabeexa maynthi gidida gisho enttaw na7i baawa. Nam77ayka qassi cimidosona.
Issi gallas Zakkariyaasi ba gishuwa maaran Xoossaa sinthan kahinetethan haggaazees.
Kahinetetha wogan Xoossa Keethi gelidi ixaane cuyisanaw iya saami gakkis.
Ixaaney cuya wode asay karen woossees.
Godaa kiitanchchoy yarshshuwa yarshshiya bessaafe ushachcha baggara eqqidi benttis.
Zakkariyaasi iya be7ida wode dagammidi daro yayyis.
Shin kiitanchchoy iyaakko, “Zakkariyaasa yayyofa; ne woosay si7ettis. Ne machchiya Elssabeexa adde na7a yelana, iya Yohaannisa gada ne sunthana.
I new injjenne ufayssi gidana; daroti iya yeletethan ufayttana.
Godaa sinthan I gita gidana; woyne ushshaa gidin hara mathoya ushshaa uyenna. Ba aaye ulon de7ishe Geeshsha Ayyaanan kumana.
Isra7eele asatappe darota bantta Godaa, Xoossaakko zaarana.
Aawata wozana naytakko zaarana, kiitettonayssata xillota cinccatethaako zaarana mela, Godaas bessiya dere giigisanaw Eliyaasa ayyaananinne wolqqan Godaa sinthan baana” yaagis.
Zakkariyaasi kiitanchchuwako, “Ta hessa aybin eranee? Taaranne ta machcheera cimida” yaagis.
Kiitanchchoy zaaridi, “Taani Xoossaa sinthan eqqiya Gabreele. Ha mishirachchuwa new odanaw Xoossaafe kiitetas.
Hekko, wodiya naagidi polettiya ta qaala ne ammanonna ixxida gisho hayssi polettana gakkanaw neeni muume gidana, odettanawukka dandda7akka” yaagis.
He wode Zakkariyaasi Xoossa Keethi gelidi gam77ida gisho aybi hanide gidi asay karen naagishe gam77is.
I kare keyidi enttana odisanaw dandda7ibeenna. Malli besoppe attin odettanaw dandda7onayssa be7ida wode qonccethi be7idayssa eridosona.
Zakkariyaasi haggazo wodiya polidi ba soo simmis.
Hessafe guye, iya machchiya Elssabeexa qanthatasu. Ichchashu ageena kumethi bana geenthada gam77asu.
Iya, “Goday ba maarotan ta boriya asaa giddofe digganaw be7idi ha wodiyan hayssa oothis” yaagasu.
Elssabeexa qanthatin usuppuntha ageenan, Xoossay kiitanchchuwa Gabreele Galiila biittan de7iya Naazirete katamaa kiittis.
Kawuwa Dawite sheeshaappe gidida Yoosefa giya uraas oyshettida geela7eekko kiittis. He geela7iya Mayraamo geetettawusu.
Kiitanchchoy iikko bidi, “Daro dosettidare, saroy new gido, Xoossay neera de7ees” yaagis.
Mayraama iya odan daro dagammada, “Hayssi aybi sarotho” gada heetasu.
Kiitanchchoy zaaridi, “Mayraame, babbofa; neeni Xoossaa sinthan saba demmadasa.
Hekko neeni qanthatana adde na7a yelana, iya sunthaaka Yesuusa gada sunthana.
I gita gidana, Ubbaafe Bolla Xoossaa na7aa geetetti xeegettana. Godaa Xoossay iya aawa Dawite araata iyaw immana.
I Yayqooba sheeshaa bolla merinaw kawotana; iya kawotethaas zawi baawa” yaagis.
Mayraama kiitanchchuwako, “Hessi waanidi hananee? Ta adde erikke” yaagasu.
Kiitanchchoy zaaridi, “Geeshsha Ayyaanay ne bolla wodhdhana, Ubbaafe Bolla Xoossaa wolqqay ne bolla kuyattana. Hessa gisho, yelettiya geeshsha na7ay Xoossaa Na7aa geetettana.
Hekko, ne dabbiya Elssabeexa ba cimatetha laythan adde na7a qanthatasu. Iya maynthi geetettidaaro, shin ha77i usuppuntha ageena oykkasu.
Xoossaa xooniyabay baawa” yaagis.
Mayraama, “Hekko, taani Godaa aylliw, ne qaalada taw hano” yaagasu. Hessafe guye, kiitanchchoy iippe shaakettis.
Mayraama he saaminttan denddada Yihuda biittan de7iya issi geze katama basu.
Zakkariyaasa soo gelada Elssabeexo sarothasu.
Elssabeexa Mayraami sarothuwa si7ida wode I uluwan de7iya na7ay ufayssan guppis. Elssabeexa Geeshsha Ayyaanan kumada,
ba qaala dhoqqu oothada, “Neeni maccasaa giddofe anjjettidaaro, ne qanthatida na7aykka anjjettidayssa.
Hanoshin, ta Godaa aaye, neeni taakko yaana mela taani oonee?
Hekko ne sarothuwa ta si7ida wode ta uluwan de7iya na7ay ufayssan guppis.
Goday polana gidi immida qaala ammanidaara, iya anjjettidaaro” yaagasu.
Mayraama hayssada yaagasu: “Ta shemppiya Godaa bonchchawusu,
ta Ayyaanay dhaliya Xoossan ufayttees.
I ba aylle kawushshatethaa be7is. Hachchife doomidi yeletethi ubbay tana anjjettidaaro gaana.
Ays giikko, wolqqaama gidida I, taw gitabaa oothis. Iya sunthay Geeshshaa.
Iya bonchcheyssata bolla, iya maarotethay merinaappe merinaa gakkanaassa.
Ba qesiyan minobaa oothis, bantta wozanan otortteyssata laallis.
Wolqqaama kawota araataappe kawushshis; banttana kawushshidayssata kabboys.
Koshattidayssata lo77oban kalssis, shin dureta mela kushe yeddis.
Ba maarota qoppidi, Ba aylliya Isra7eele maaddis.
Hessika nu aawatas odida qaalaa, Abrahamesinne iya sheeshas gidayssa merinaw polanaassa” yaagasu.
Mayraama Elssabeexi matan heedzu ageena mela gam77ada ba soo simmasu.
Elssabeexis yelo qammay gakkin adde na7a yelasu.
I shoorotinne I dabboti Goday gita maarota oothidayssa si7idi, iira issife ufayttidosona.
Hosppuntha gallasan yooga na7aa qaxxaranaw yidosona. Iya aawa sunthan Zakkariyaasa gidi sunthanaw koyidosona.
Shin aayyaa, “Akkay, Yohaannisa geetettanaw bessees” yaagasu.
Enttika, “Ne dabbotappe ha sunthan xeegettiday oonikka baawa” yaagidosona.
Iya aaway oona gidi sunthaneekko eranaw koyidi iya malla oychchidosona.
I xaafiyabaa oychchi ekkidi, “Iya sunthay Yohaannisa” gidi xaafis. Ubbay I xaafidayssa be7idi malaalettidosona.
Iira Zakkariyaasa inxarssay bilettis, Xoossaa galatishe odetethi oykkis.
Shooroti ubbay yashshan kumidosona. Ha hanidabay geze Yihuda biittan odettis.
Hessa si7ida ubbay, “Ha na7ay ay hananddeshsha” gidi bantta giddon odettidosona. Godaa kushey iyara de7ees.
Yohaannisa aaway Zakkariyaasi Geeshsha Ayyaanan kumidi hayssada yaagidi tinbbite odis.
“Isra7eeliya Goday galatetto, yidi ba asaa wozis.
Ba aylliya Dawite keethan atotethaa kaciya denthis.
Hessika beni wode geeshsha nabeta doonan odettidayssa mela,
Iya ashoy nu morkketappenne nuura eqettiya ubbaa kushiyappe.
Hessa I oothiday nu aawatas ba maarota bessanaasinne, ba geeshsha caaquwa naaganaassa.
Nu aawa Abrahames caaqqida caaquwa qoppanasinne
nu morkketa kusheppe kessidi yashshi baynna iya haggaazana melassa.
Nu laytha ubban geeshshatethaninne xillotethan ba sinthan nuna essanaassa.
Qassi laa na7aw, neeni Ubbaafe Bolla Xoossaa nabe geetettana. Godaa ogiya loythanaw ne iya sinthan baana.
Entta nagaray qushettin, entti atotethi demmanayssa ne Godaa deriyas odana.
Nu Xoossaa lo77o maarotethaafe denddoyssan wontta xalqey nuus saluwappe keyis.
Hessika dhumaninne, hayqo kuya garssan de7eyssatas poo7isanaassa, nu tohuwakka saro ogiyakko zaaranaassa” yaagis.
Na7ay diccis, Ayyaanan minnis, Isra7eele asaas qonccana gakkanaw bazzo biittan de7is.
He wode Roome biittan de7iya asa ubbay taybettana melanne sunthay xaafettana mela kawoy Awugisxoosi kiittis.
Hessika Qerenoosi Soore biittaa aysiya wode oosettida koyro taybuwa.
Hessa gisho, issi issi asi ba sunthaa xaafettanaw ba yelettida biittaa bis.
Yoosefikka Dawite keethaafenne yaraappe gidida gisho Galiila Naazirete katamaappe denddidi Dawite katama gidida Yihuda Beeteleme bis.
Bishe, yelanaw wodey wurida I oychchi wothida, Mayraamira wolla xaafettanaw bis.
Entti yan de7ishin iw yelo wodey gakkis.
Ba bayra na7aa yelasu. Curqqara xaaxada imathi aqiyason bessi dhayida gisho daran mehe muziya gonggen zin77isasu.
He gadiyan qamma dorssa wudiya naagishe karen aqiya henthanchchoti de7oosona.
Godaa kiitanchchoy hassayonna yidi entta matan eqqis. Godaa bonchchoy entta yuushuwan poo7is; enttika wolqqaama yashshi yayyidosona.
Shin kiitanchchoy, “Yayyofite! Hekko, asaa ubbaas gidiya gita ufayssaa mishirachchuwa ekkada yas.
Hessika, Dawite kataman ashsheyssi hinttew hachchi yelettis. I Godaa Kiristtoosa.
Zoqale na7ay curqqara xaaxettidi gonggen zin77idayssa hintte demmana; hessika hinttew malla gido” yaagis.
Qopponna daro salo kiitanchchoti kiitanchchuwura issife qonccidi,
“Bonchchoy Xoossaas dhoqqa saluwan, saroy biitta bolla Xoossay dosiya asaas gido” yaagidi galatidosona.
Kiitanchchoti enttafe shaakettidi saluwa keyidaappe guye henthanchchoti, “Ane Goday nuus qonccisidabaanne hanidabaa be7anaw Beeteleme boos” yaagidosona.
Enttika ellesidi bidosona. Mayraamo, Yoosefanne zoqale na7aa gonggen zin77idayssa be7idosona.
Be7i simmidi na7abaa enttaw odettoyssa, qonccisidi he bessan de7iya asaas markkattidosona.
Hessa si7ida ubbay henthanchchoti odidayssan malaalettidosona.
Mayraama hanidabaa ubbaa ba wozanan qoppashe de7asu.
Henthanchchoti enttaw odettidayssada hanin be7idosona. Hessa gisho, bantta si7idabaasinne be7idaba ubbaas Xoossaa bonchchishenne galatishe simmidosona.
Hosppuntha qamman, qaxxaro wodey gakkin, I qanthatanaappe sinthe kiitanchchoy wothida sunthan Yesuusa geetettis.
Muse woga mela entta geeshshatetha wodey polettidaappe guye Yoosefaranne Mayraamira yooga na7aa bantta Godaas immanaw Yerusalaame bidosona.
Hessika, Godaa wogan, “Adde gidida bayra na7i ubbay Godaas dummattidayssa gido” geetettidi xaafettidayssa polanaassa.
Qassi Godaa wogan, nam77u kuraachcho woykko holle yarshshanaw efidosona.
He wode geeshshinne ammanora mino gidida Simoona geetettiya asi Yerusalaamen de7ees. I Isra7eeleta atotethaa naagishe de7ees. Geeshsha Ayyaanaykka iya bolla de7ees.
Qassi Kiristtoosa be7onna hayqqonnayssa Geeshsha Ayyaanay iyaw qonccisin eridi de7ees.
I he gallas Ayyaanay kaalethin Xoossa Keethi bis. Na7aa aayeranne aawara wogaa polanaw yooga na7aa Yesuusa ekkidi gelida wode
Simooni mokki ekkidi na7aa idimmidi,
“Godaw ne taw gelida qaala mela, ha77i ne aylliya saron moyza.
Ta ayfey asaa ubbaa sinthan ne giigisida,
ne ashuwa be7is.
Hessika kawotethata ubbaas, Xoossaa ogiya qonccisiya poo7o, ne asaa Isra7eeleskka bonchcho” yaagidi Xoossaa galatis.
Yoosefaranne Mayraamira iyaw odettidaban malaalettidosona.
Simooni entta anjjis. Aaye Mayraamikko, “Hekko daro asaa wozanaa qofay qonccana mela, Isra7eelen de7iya darotas entta kunddethaasinne dendduwas Xoossan doorettis.
Qassi eqetteyssatas malla gidana. Ne shemppuwarakka qassi mashshi aadhdhana” yaagis.
Qassi Aseere yaraappe gidida Faanu7ela na7iya Haanna geetettiya nabey de7awusu. Iya daro cimasu; iya ba koyro azinaara laappun laythi de7asu.
I azinay hayqqin hosppun tammanne oyddu laythi gidana gakkanaw qammanne gallas pacey baynna woosaninne xooman Xoossa Keethan haggaazasu.
Iya he saatiyan bada Xoossaa galatasu; Yerusalaame wozetethaa naagiya ubbaas yooga na7abaa markkattasu.
Yoosefaranne Mayraamira Godaa higgiyan kiitettida woga ubbaa polidaappe guye Galiila biittan de7iya bantta katama Naazirete simmidosona.
Na7ay diccishenne minnishe bis. Cinccatethan kumis; Xoossaa aadho keehatethay iya bolla de7ees.
Yoosefaranne Mayraamira Faasikka Baale bonchchanaw laythan laythan Yerusalaame boosona.
Yesuusas tammanne nam77u laythi gidiya wode kase meezetidayssada baaliya bonchchanaw bidosona.
Baaliya bonchchidaappe guye soo simmiya wode na7ay Yesuusi Yerusalaamen attis. Shin Yoosefaranne Mayraamira I Yerusalaamen attoyssa eribookkona.
I soo simmiya asaara wolla de7iya daanin entti issi gallasa oge bidosona. I baynnayssa eridaappe guye bantta dabbotanne laggeta matan koyidosona.
I yan dhayin koyishe guye Yerusalaame gakkanaw bidosona.
Heedzu gallasappe guye Xoossa Keethan asttamaareta giddon uttidi enttabaa si7ishenne entta oychchishe de7ishin demmidosona.
Iya si7iya ubbay iya akeekaninne zaaruwan malaalettidosona.
Soo asay iya demmida wode malaalettidosona. Iya aayyaakka, “Ta na7aw, ays nuna hayssada oothadii? Ne aawaranne taara nena koyishe un77ettida” yaagasu.
Yesuusi enttako, “Tana ays koyeetii? Ta, ta aawa keethan daanaw besseyssa erekketii” yaagis.
Shin I enttako gidabaa entti akeekibookkona.
Hessafe guye, enttara issife Naazirete katama bis. Enttaw kiitettishe de7is. Iya aayyaa he ubbaa ba wozanan wothada naagasu.
Yesuusi, cinccatethan, geesaninne teeman Xoossaa sinthaninne asa sinthan diccis.
Kawoy Xibaaryoosi Roome biittan kawotin, tammanne ichchashantho laythan, Phenxe Philaaxoosi Yihuda haariya wode Heroodisi Galiila haariya wode iya ishaa Filphoosi Ixuuriyasanne Xirakkonddoosa haariya wode Lisaniyoosi Ablaanisa haariya wode
Haannaranne Qayyaafara kahine halaqa gidi de7ishin, Xoossaa qaalay Zakkariyaasa na7aa Yohaannisakko bazzo biittaa yis.
Yohaannisi, “Hintte nagaraappe simmitenne xammaqetite. Xoossay hintte nagaraa atto gaana” yaagidi tamaarssishe Yorddaanose Shaafaa heeran de7iya biitta ubbaa bis.
Hessika nabey Isayaasi ba maxaafan, “Bazzo giddon ba qaala dhoqqu oothidi, waassiya uraa qaalay, ‘Godaa ogiya giigisite, horogaakka piddi oothite.
Aafo ubbay kumana, zumaynne derey ziqqi gaana. Wobbe ogey luulana, giigonna horogay qinxi gaana.
Asho ma77ida ubbay, Xoossaa ashuwa be7ana’ ” gidi xaafidayssada hanis.
Yohaannisi, ba kushen xammaqettanaw yida asaakko, “Hinttenoo, shoosha nayto yaanaw de7iya hanquwafe attana mela hinttena zoriday oonee?
Hiza, hintte simuwa qonccisiya lo77o ooso oothite, hintte wozanan, ‘Nuus, nu aaway Abrahamey de7ees gidi ceeqettofite.’ Haa si7ite, ha shuchchatappe Xoossay Abrahames na7a kessanaw dandda7ees.
Hekko, beexey mithaa xaphon de7ees. Hiza, lo77o ayfe ayfonna mitha ubbay qanxettidi taman yegettana” yaagis.
Asay, “Yaatin nuuni ay oothinoo?” yaagidi oychchidosona.
Yohaannisi zaaridi, “Nam77u afili de7iya asi baynnayssas immo. Kathi de7eyssi baynnayssas immo” yaagis.
Qaraxa qanxiseyssati xammaqettanaw yidi, “Asttamaariyaw, nuuni ay oothinoo?” yaagidosona.
I zaaridi, “Hintte qanxisanaw kiitettoyssafe aathidi ekkofite” yaagis.
Qassi wotaaddareti yidi, “Nuuni ay oothinoo” yaagidi oychchidosona. Yohaannisi, “Ooddebaakka wolqqan dafidi ekkofite, oonakka worddon mootoppite, hintte damoozey hinttew gido; ufayttidi de7ite” yaagis.
Asay Kiristtoosa naagishe de7iya gisho Yohaannisa, “I Kiristtoosa gidanddeshshaa?” gidi qoppidosona.
Yohaannisi ubbaas zaaridi, “Taani hinttena haathan xammaqays, shin taappe aadhdhidi wolqqaameyssi yaana. Taani iya caammaa wodoruwa billanaw bessonna asi. I hinttena Geeshsha Ayyaananinne taman xammaqana.
Wudumman de7iya kathaa polo geeshshanaw pithey iya kushen de7ees. Geeshsha kathaa ba shaaliyan qolana; kaliya dhayonna taman xuuggana” yaagis.
Qassi Yohaannisi asaa daro zore zoridi Wonggelaa odis.
Shin Yohaannisi Heroodisi ba ishaa machchiw, Heroodiyada, ekkida gishonne haraa iita oosota gisho kaccida wode
Heroodisi kaseyssa bolla haraba ubbaa gujjidi Yohaannisa woyne gelssis.
Yohaannisi qashettanaappe sinthe asaa ubbaa xammaqidi simmin, Yesuusikka qassi xammaqettis. I woossishin saloy dooyettis.
Geeshsha Ayyaanay holleda benttishe iya bolla uttis. Saloppe “Taani dosiya na7ay nena; ne tana ufayssaasa yaagiya” qaalay yis.
Yesuusi tamaarsso oykkiya wode iyaw hasttamu laythi gidishin, asay iya Yoosefa na7a gidi qoppis. Yoosefi Eele na7a,
Eeley Maate na7a, Maatey Leewe na7a, Leewey Malkka na7a, Malkkey Yoona na7a, Yooni Yoosefa na7a,
Yoosefi Mataate na7a, Mataatey Amoxe na7a, Amoxey Nahoome na7a, Nahoomey Asiliime na7a, Asiliimey Naage na7a,
Naagey Ma7aate na7a, Ma7aatey Mataatiye na7a, Mataatiyey Samaye na7a,
Samayey Yihuda na7a, Yihudi Yoonane na7a, Yoonaney Rase na7a, Rasey Zerubaabela na7a, Zerubaabeley Salatiyaale na7a, Salatiyaaley Neere na7a,
Neerey Malkka na7a, Malkkey Haade na7a, Haadey Qoosame na7a, Qoosamey Elmodaane na7a, Elmodaaney Eere na7a,
Eerey Yoose7e na7a, Yoose7ey Alaazara na7a, Alaazari Yoorame na7a, Yooramey Maate na7a, Maatey Leewe na7a,
Leewey Simoona na7a, Simooni Yihuda na7a, Yihudi Yoosefa na7a, Yoosefi Yoonane na7a, Yoonaney Eliyaaqeme na7a,
Eliyaaqemey Maliyye na7a, Maliyyey Maynaane na7a, Maynaaney Maate na7a, Maatey Naatane na7a, Naataney Dawite na7a,
Dawitey Isseyye na7a, Isseyyey Iyobeede na7a, Iyobeedey Boo7eza na7a, Boo7ezi Salmoona na7a, Salmooney Na7asoona na7a,
Na7asooney Aminaadabe na7a, Aminaadabey Raame na7a, Raamey Arnne na7a, Arnney Asroome na7a,
Asroomey Faarese na7a, Faaresey Yihuda na7a, Yihudi Yayqooba na7a, Yayqoobi Yisaaqa na7a, Yisaaqi Abrahame na7a, Abrahamey Taara na7a,
Taari Naakkore na7a, Naakkorey Saruuge na7a, Saruugey Rehu na7a, Rehuy Faaleqe na7a, Faaleqey Ebeera na7a, Ebeeroy Seela na7a,
Seeli Qaynaame na7a, Qaynaamey Arfakisaada na7a, Arfakisaadey Seeme na7a, Seemey Nohe na7a, Nohey Laamehe na7a,
Laamehey Matusaala na7a, Matusaali Heenoke na7a, Heenokey Yaarede na7a, Yaaredey Malaal77ela na7a, Malaal77eli Qaynaane na7a,
Qaynaaney Heenosa na7a, Heenosey Seeta na7a, Seetey Addaame na7a, Addaamey Xoossaa na7a.
Yesuusi Geeshsha Ayyaanan kumidi Yorddaanose Shaafappe simmida mela Ayyaanay iya bazzo efis.
Yan oytamu gallasinne qamma xalahen paacettis. He gallasatan aykkoka moonna gam77ida gisho wurssethan koshattis.
Xalahey iyaakko, “Neeni Xoossaa na7a gidikko ane hayssi shuchchay uythu gido gada kiitta” yaagis.
Yesuusi zaaridi, “Asi uytha xalaalan deenna geetettidi xaafettis” yaagis.
Hessafe guye, Xalahey Yesuusa adussa dere bolla kessidi ha alamiya kawotethata ayfe qiphi zaaranaw bessis.
Xalahey, “Ha ubbaas maataynne bonchchoy taw imettis. Taani dosida ooddeskka immiya gisho new immana.
Hessa gisho, neeni taw goynniko ubbay new gidana” yaagis.
Yesuusi zaaridi, “Ne Godaa, ne Xoossaa, iya xalaala goynna geetettidi xaafettis” yaagis.
Wurssethan Xalahey Yesuusa Yerusalaame efidi Xoossa Keethas huu7iya bolla essidi, “Neeni Xoossaa na7a gidikko ane duge sa7an nena yegga.
Ays giikko, ‘Nena naagiya Kiitanchchota Xoossay ne gisho kiittana.
Entti ne tohoy shuchchan dhubettonna mela, bantta kushiyan dhoqqu oothidi nena denthana’ geetettidi xaafettis” yaagis.
Yesuusi zaaridi, “Ne Godaa Xoossaa paaccofa geetettidi xaafettis” yaagis.
Xalahey Yesuusa paaciya wurssidaappe guye hara injje wode demmana gakkanaw iyappe shaakettis.
Yesuusi Ayyaana wolqqan kumidi Galiila simmis. Iya sunthay heeran de7iya biitta ubban keyis.
I Ayhude Woosa Keethi gelidi tamaarssis; asa ubbay iya galatidosona.
Yaappe I diccida katamaa Naazirete yis. Kase meezetidayssada Sambbaata gallas Ayhude Woosa Keethi gelis. Nabbabanawukka denddi eqqis.
Nabiya Isayaasa maxaafay iyaw imettin, dooyidi, hayssada yaagidi xaafettidayssa demmis:
“Godaa Ayyaanay ta bolla de7ees, manqotas Wonggelaa odana mela Xoossay tana dooris. Qashettidayssatas biletethi, qooqidayssata xeelisanaasinne un77ettidayssata birshshana mela,
Xoossay keehanaw qoppida laythaa odana mela tana kiittis” yaagis.
Hessafe guye, maxaafaa xaaxidi haggaazeyssas immidi tamaarssanaw uttis. Ayhude Woosa Keethan de7iya asati ubbay caddi xeellosona.
I, “Hayssi hintte haythan hintte si7iya ha maxaafaa qaalay hachchi polettis” yaagis.
Ubbay iyabaa darssidi odettoosona. Qassi iya doonappe keyaa aadho keehatethan kumida qaalan malaalettishe, “Hayssi Yoosefa na7aa gidenneyye?” yaagidosona.
I, “ ‘Neno dhale aawaw nena ashsha, Qifirnahoomen ne oothidabaa nu si77oyssa qassi hayssan ne kataman ootha’ yaagiya leemisuwan hintte tana gaanayssas sidhey baawa” yaagis.
Qassi, “Tuma odays; nabey ba yelettida biittan bonchchettena.
“Ta hinttew tuma odays; saloy heedzu laythinne bagga gorddettin mino koshi biitta ubban de7iya Eliyaasa wode daro am77eti Isra7eelen de7oosona.
Eliyaasi enttafe issinnekokka kiitettibeenna. Shin Sarapttan de7iya am77eeko kiitettis.
Nabiya Elssa7e wode Isra7eelen daro baro hargganchchoti de7oosona. Shin Soore uraa Ni7imaaneppe attin oonikka paxibeenna” yaagis.
Ayhude Woosa Keethan de7iya asa ubbay hessa si7ida wode daro yilotidosona.
Bantta uttida bessaafe denddidi zuma bolla keexettida katamaappe gaxa kessidi sugi yeddanaw aafo doona efidosona.
Shin I entta giddora kanthidi aadhdhis.
Yaappe Galiila biittan de7iya Qifirnahoome katamaa bis. Yan Sambbaata gallas asaa tamaarssis.
I tamaarssey maatara gidiya gisho ubbay iya timirttiyan malaalettidosona.
Ayhude Woosa Keethan tuna ayyaanay oykkida uray de7ees.
I, “Naazirete Yesuusa nuna ays waaysay nuuppe haakka; neeni yiday nuna dhayssanaaseyye? Neeni ooneekko taani erays. Neeni Xoossaafe yida Geeshsha” yaagidi waassis.
Yesuusi tuna ayyaanaakko, “Si7i gada ha uraappe keya” yaagidi hanqis. Tuna ayyaanay uraa asaa ubbaa sinthan holi yeggidi aykkoka qohonna yeddidi keyis.
Asa ubbay malaalettidosona. Wolikko, “Hanos, hayssi aybi timirtte? Tuna ayyaanata maataninne wolqqan kiittees; enttika keyosona” yaagidosona.
Iya sunthay heera ubban keyis.
Hessafe guye, Yesuusi Ayhude Woosa Keethafe keyidi Simoona soo gelis. Simoona machche aayyaa mino qoxo misha harggen sakettasu. Iyo pathana mela Yesuusa woossidosona.
I hiixaakko shiiqi hokkidi I harggiya hanqis. Mishay aggin ellesa denddada entta mokkasu.
Away wullana hanishin dumma dumma harggiyan oykettida asaa iyaakko ehidosona. I issuwa issuwa bolla ba kushiya wothidi pathis.
Tuna ayyaanati qassi, “Neeni, Xoossaa na7aa” gidi waassishe daro asaappe keyidosona. Shin I enttana hanqis. I Kiristtoosa gideyssa entti eriya gisho issibaakka odettonna mela diggis.
Buroo wonttiya wode Yesuusi issi geema bessi bis. Asay koyishe I de7iya bessaa yidosona. Enttafe I shaakettidi boonna mela butetidosona.
Shin I, “Taani hara katamata bada Xoossaa kawotethaa Wonggelaa markkattanaw bessees. Ta kiitettiday hessassa” yaagis.
Yihuda biittan de7iya Ayhude Woosa Keethan sabbakis.
Issi gallas Yesuusi Gensareexe Abbaa matan eqqidashin daro asay iya yuushuwa un77ethidi, I tamaarssiya Xoossaa qaala si7oosona.
Yan haatha gaxan de7iya nam77u wogolota be7is. Molo oykkiya asati wogolotappe wodhdhidi bantta gitiya meeccosona.
He wogolotappe Simoonayssan gelidi biittaafe guuthi giddo shiishana mela oychchis. Yaatidi, he wogoluwa bolla uttidi asaa tamaarssis.
Ba tamaarssuwa onggidaappe guye Simoonakko, “Gede ciimmuwako shiishada moluwa oykkanaw hintte gitiya yeggite” yaagis.
Simooni zaaridi, “Asttamaariyaw, qamma kumethaa daaburishe aqidi aykkoka oykkibookko, shin ne giikko gitiya yeggana” yaagis.
Entti gitiya yeggida wode gitey daakettana gakkanaw daro molo oykkidosona.
Hara wogoluwan de7iya bantta laggeti yidi, banttana maaddana mela wuttidi xeegidosona. Entti yidi nam77u wogolota, haathan mitettana gakkanaw molon kunthidosona.
Simoon Phexiroosi hessa be7ida wode Yesuusa sinthan kunddidi, “Godaw, taani nagaranchcho asi gidiya gisho taappe shaaketta” yaagis.
Hessa I giday inne iyara de7eyssati oykkida moluwa darotethan malaalettida gishossa.
Qassi Simoona lagge gidida Zabdiyoosa nayti Yayqoobaranne Yohaannisara malaalettidosona. Yesuusi Simoonakko, “Babbofa! Hizappe neeni ase oykkiya asi gidana” yaagis.
Entti wogolota gaxa shiishidaappe guye ubbaa aggidi Yesuusa kaallidosona.
Yesuusi katamatappe issuwan de7ishin issi baro harggen oykettida asi he kataman de7ees. He uray Yesuusa be7idi iya sinthan gufannidi, “Godaw, ne shene gidikko tana geeshshanaw dandda7aasa” gidi woossis.
Yesuusi ba kushiya yeddi bochchidi, “Ee, ta shene; geeya” yaagis. Iira baro harggey uraappe kichchis.
Yesuusi, “Hayssa ooddeskka odoppa, shin bada nenatethaa Ayhude kahiniya bessa. Ne geeyidayssas markka gidana mela Musey kiittida yarshshuwa yarshsha” gidi kiittis.
Gidoshin, iya sunthay kaseppe aadhdhidi dalggishe bis. Daro asay I odiyabaa si7anawunne bantta harggiyafe paxanaw yoosona.
Shin Yesuusi daro wode geema bessi bidi woossees.
Issi gallas Yesuusi tamaarssishin Galiilappenne Yihuda heera ubbaafe qassi Yerusalaameppekka yida Farisaawetinne higge asttamaareti yan uttidosona. Asaa pathiya Godaa wolqqayka iyara de7ees.
He wode asay issi gundda asi halara tookkidi ehidosona. Soo gelssidi iya sinthan wothanaw qoppidosona.
Shin asaa darotethaafe denddoyssan soo gelssanaw xoonettidi keethaa bolla keyidi, kaara qawuxidi, hargganchchuwa halara asaa shaakkidi Yesuusa sinthan yeggidosona.
Yesuusi entta ammanuwa be7idi, “La addiyaw, ne nagaray qushettis” yaagis.
Higge asttamaaretinne Farisaaweti, “Hayssi Xoossaa bolla yaagidi odettey oonee? Issi Xoossaafe attin hari nagara quchchanaw dandda7ey oonee?” yaagidi qoppidosona.
Yesuusi entta qofaa erida gisho enttako, “Hintte wozanan hessatho ays qoppeetii?
‘Ne nagaray qushettis geyssafenne denddada ba geyssafe awussi kawuyii?’
Shin ta hessa giday Asa Na7ay sa7a bolla nagara quchchanaw maati de7eyssa hintte erana melassa.” Hessafe kaallidi, gundda uraakko, “Dendda; ne alggaa tookkada ne soo ba” yaagis.
I ellesi denddidi entta sinthan eqqis; I tookettidi yida alggaa tookkidi Xoossaa galatishe ba soo bis.
He wode ubbayka malaalettidosona. Xoossaa galatishe, “Hachchi gita malaata be7ida” yaagidi yashettidosona.
Hessafe guye, Yesuusi yaappe keyidi bis. Leewe geetettiya issi qaraxa qanxiseyssi qaraxa qanxisiya bessan uttidayssa be7idi, “Tana kaalla” yaagis.
I ubbabaa aggi denddidi iya kaallis.
He Leewey ba son gita gibira giigisis. Daro qaraxa qanxiseyssatinne hara asati kathaa maanaw uttidosona.
Farisaawetinne higge asttamaareti, “Qaraxa qanxeyssataranne nagaranchchotara ays meetinne uyeetii?” yaagidi Yesuusa tamaareta bolla zuuzummidosona.
Yesuusi enttako, “Hargganchchotassafe attin paxatas aakime koshshenna.
Taani nagaranchchota maarotaakko zaaranaassafe attin geeshshata xeeganaw yabiikke” yaagidi zaaris.
Entti Yesuusakko, “Yohaannisa tamaareti daro wode xoomosona, woossosona; qassi Farisaaweta tamaaretikka hessatho oothoosona. Shin neyssati ubba wode moosonanne uyoosona” yaagidosona.
Yesuusi enttako, “Mushuray enttara de7ishin xeegettida asay xoomana mela oothanaw dandda7etii?
Shin mushuray enttafe shaakettana gallasay yaana, he wode entti xoomana.”
Qassi yaagidi leemiso odis; “Ooratha ma7oppe peedhidi gal77a ma7o bolla sikkey oonikka baawa. Hessatho oothiko ooratha ma7uwa peedhees, oorathay gal77aas giigenna.
Mal77antto woyniya gal77a ogoron qoliya oonikka baawa. Hessa oothiko, ooratha woyney gal77a ogoruwa dhusees; woyney gukkees ogoroykka maaddonabaa gidees.
Hessa gisho, ooratha woyney ooratha ogoron qolettanaw bessees.
Hiza, caalay lo77o giya gisho caala woyne uyi simmidi mal77antto koyey oonikka baawa” yaagis.
Issi Sambbaata gallas Yesuusi gistte gade giddora aadhdhees. Yesuusa tamaareti tiya bangga duuthidi bantta kushen shirkkidi moosona.
Shin Farisaaweta giddofe issoti issoti, “Sambbaata gallas oothanaw bessonnabaa ays ootheetii?” yaagidosona.
Yesuusi enttako zaaridi, “Dawitey koshattida wode baara de7eyssatara issife oothoyssa nabbabibeekketii?
Xoossa Keethi gelidi Ayhude kahineta xalaalas bessiya daabbuwa mis; baara de7eyssataskka immis” yaagis.
Qassi Yesuusi, “Asa Na7ay Sambbaata Goda” yaagis.
Hara Sambbaata gallas Yesuusi Ayhude Woosa Keethi gelidi tamaarssees. He bessan ushachcha kushey gunddida issi asi de7ees.
Higge asttamaaretinne Farisaaweti iya mootanaw gaaso koyidi Sambbaata gallas pathiko be7ana gidi naagoosona.
Shin Yesuusi entta qofaa eridi kushey gunddida uraakko, “Denddada asaa gidduwan eqqa” yaagis. Uraykka denddi eqqis.
Yesuusi, “Ane ta hinttena issibaa oychchays; Sambbaata gallas oothanaw bessey lo77obayeyye iitabaye? Shemppo ashoyye woykko dhaysso?” yaagis.
Qassi Yesuusi iya yuushuwan de7iya asaa yuushshi xeellidi uraakko, “Ne kushiya piddi ootha” yaagis. Uraykka I gidayssada oothin kushey paxis.
Shin higge asttamaaretinne Farisaaweti daro yilotidosona. Yesuusa bolla ay oothinoo gidi bantta giddon maqettidosona.
He wode gallasatappe issuwan Yesuusi woossanaw deriya bolla keyis. Qamma kumethaa Xoossaa woossishe aqis.
Wonttethe ba tamaareta xeegidi entta giddofe tammanne nam77ata dooridi, enttana, “Hawaareta” gidi sunthis.
Enttika, Phexiroosa gidi sunthida Simoona, iya ishaa Inddiriyasa, Yayqooba, Yohaannisa, Filphoosa, Bartolomiyoosa,
Maatoosa, Toomasa, Ilfiyoosa na7aa Yayqooba, ba biittaas mishettiya Simoona,
Yayqooba na7aa Yihudanne Yesuusa aathi immida Asqoroota Yihuda.
Yesuusi enttara issife deriyappe wodhdhidi denbba bessan eqqis. Iya tamaaretappe daroti he bessan de7oosona Yihuda biitta ubbaafe Yerusalaameppe, Xiroosappenne Sidoona abbaa gaxappe yida daro asay de7ees.
Entti yiday I tamaarssiyabaa si7anawunne bantta harggiyafe paxanaassa. Tuna ayyaanan waayettiya asatikka paxidosona.
Wolqqay iyappe keyidi asa ubbaa pathiya gisho asay iya bochchanaw koyoosona.
Ba tamaaretakko xeellidi hayssada yaagis: “Hinttenoo, manqoto, hintte anjjettidayssata; Xoossaa kawotethay hinttessa.
Hintte ha77i koshatteyssati anjjettidayssata, hintte kallana. Hintte ha77i yeekkeyssati anjjettidayssata hintte miicana.
Asay hinttena Asa Na7aa gisho ixxiya wode hinttena hiliya wode hinttena entti toochchiya wodenne, iita sunthi entti hinttew immiya wode hintte anjjettidayssata.
“Hekko, hintte woytoy salon gita gidiya gisho he wode ufayssan guppite. Ays giikko, beni entta aawati nabeta bolla hessada oothidosona.”
“Shin dureto hinttena ayye; hintte ha77i lo77o duussaa ekkideta.
Ha77i kallidayssato hinttena ayye; hintte koshattana. Ha77i miiceyssato hinttenoshsho hintte kayottananne yeekkana.
Asi ubbay hintte lo77otethaa xalaala odiya wode hinttena ayye. Entta aawati beni worddanchcho nabeta bolla hessada oothidosona.
“Shin tana si7iya hinttes ta odays; hintte morkketa siiqite; hinttena ixxeyssatas lo77obaa oothite.
Hinttena qanggeyssata anjjite, hinttena naaqqeyssatas woossite.
Issi bagga shakalaa baqqeyssas hankko baggaaka bessa. Ne laxana ekkana geyssas ne shaamiziyakka gujjada imma.
Nena woossiya ubbaas imma; neeppe ekkida oonakka zaaro gada oychchofa.
Asay hinttew oothana mela hintte koyabaa ubbaa hintteka asaas oothite.
“Hintte hinttena dosiya asata xalaala dosikko, ay galati hinttew de7ii? Hari attoshin, nagaranchchotikka banttana siiqeyssata siiqoosona.
Hinttew lo77obaa ootheyssata xalaalas lo77obaa oothiko hinttew ay galati de7ii? Nagaranchchotikka hessada oothoosona.
Tal77e zaarana asa xalaalas hintte tal77iko ay dumma galatetteetii? Nagaranchchotikka guye zaarana asi be7idi tal77osona.”
“Shin hintte morkketa siiqite; enttaw lo77obaa oothite. Guye ekkanaw qopponna tal77ite. Hessan hintte ekkana woytoy gita gidana. Hintte Ubbaafe Bolla Xoossaa nayta gidana. I bana galatonnayssatasinne iitatas keeha.
Hintte aaway keeha gidoyssada hintteka keeha gidite.
“Asa bolla pirddofite; hintte bolla pirddettenna. Hintte borettonna mela oonakka boroppite. Atto giite; Xoossay hinttew atto gaana.
Immite; hinttew imettana. Hintte makkidaban hinttew zaari makettana, ubbarakka lo77o makkiyaban baqqidi, suuddi kunthidi, laalettana gakkanaw hinttew maketi imettana” yaagis.
Qassika Yesuusi yaagidi enttaw leemiso odis; “Qooqey qooqe kaalethanaw dandda7ii? Kaalethiko nam77ayka woli ekkidi aafon wullokonayye?
Tamaarey asttamaareppe aadhdhenna. Shin loythi tamaarida uray ba asttamaariyatho hanees.
“Ne ishaa ayfiyaan de7iya buuriya ays be7ay? Ne ayfiyaan de7iya tuussi daaneyssa ays be7ikki?
Ne ayfiyaan de7iya tuussi daaneyssa be7onna ne ishaakko, ‘Ta ishaw ne ayfiyaan de7iya buuriya kesso’ gaanaw waana dandda7ay? Neno cubbuwaw, koyrottada ne ayfiyaan de7iya tuussi daaneyssa kessa. Hessafe guye, ne ishaa ayfiyaan de7iya buuriya kessanaw geeshshada xeellana.
“Lo77o mithi iita ayfe ayfenna; hessadakka iita mithi lo77o ayfe ayfena.
Ayfe ayfiyaa mithi ubbay ba ayfiyaan erettees. Agunthafe balase mitha ayfey maxettenna qassi laadeppe woyne ayfey maxettenna.
Lo77o asi ba wozanan kumida lo77obaappe lo77obaa kessees. Iita asi ba wozanan kumida iitabaappe iitabaa kessees. Asi ba wozanan kumidi palahidabaappe ba doonan haasayees.
“Ta geyssa ootheketa, shin yaatin ays tana, ‘Godaw, Godaw, geeti?’
Taakko yeynne ta qaala si7idi poliya ubbay oona daaniyakko ta hinttena bessana.
I keethe keexanaw ziqqi oothi, olla bookkidi, garssan de7iya zaalla bolla keethaa essida cincca uraa daanees. Di7oy di77idi he keethaa sugis, shin minthidi keexida gisho qaaxxanaw dandda7ibeenna.
Shin ta qaala si7idi oothonay ba keethaa shafe biitta bolla keexida uraa daanees. Di7oy di77idi he keethaa sugida wode ellesidi kunddis. He keethay wolqqaama kunddethi kunddis” yaagis.
Yesuusi hessa ubbaa asaa sinthan tamaarssidi onggidaappe guye, Qifirnahoome katamaa bis.
He bessan issi mato halaqay de7ees. I daro dosiya aylley harggettidi hayqos gakkis.
I Yesuusabaa si7ida wode ba aylliya pathana mela iya woosso gidi issi issi Ayhude cimata Yesuusakko kiittis.
Kiitettidayssati, Yesuusakko bidi, “Ne iyaw hayssa oothanaw bessees.
Ays giikko, ha uray nu asaa dosees, Ayhude Woosa Keethaka keexxis” gidi minthi woossidosona
Yesuusikka enttara bis. Mato halaqaa sookko matiya wode ba laggeta iyaakko kiittidi, “Godaw, ta kaarappe garssan ne gelanaw ta bessonna gisho daaburoppa.
Takka tana ne sinthe shiiqanaw bessiya asi gada qoppike. Shin ne issi qaala oda; ta aylley paxana.
Taw taappe bollara halaqay de7ees, taappe garssan ta kiittiya wotaaddareti de7oosona. Issuwa, ‘Ba’ giikko bees, hankkuwa, ‘Haaya’ giikko yees. Ta aylliyakko, ‘Hanno ootha’ giikko oothees” yaagis.
Yesuusi hessa si7ida wode malaalettis. Guye simmidi baara yaa asaakko, “Taani hinttew tuma odays; hari attoshin Isra7eelenkka hayssa mela gita ammano demmabiikke” yaagis.
Kiitettidayssati soo simmiya wode aylley paxin demmidosona.
Guutha wodeppe guye Yesuusi Nayne katamaa bis. Iya tamaaretaranne hara daro asati iyara bidosona.
I katamaa gelana haniya wode aha tookkida daro asati katamaappe keyosona. Hayqqida na7ay ba aayes issuwa, iyakka am77o gidada da7awusu. Katama asaappe daroti iira de7oosona.
Goday iyo be7ida wode qadhettidi, “Yeekkofa” yaagis.
Shiiqidi halaa bochchin tookkida asati eqqidosona. Yesuusi, “La, yalagaw dendda” yaagis.
Hayqqidayssi denddi uttidi oda oykkis. Yesuusi na7aa ekkidi aayes immis.
Asa ubbay yashettidi, “Gita nabey nu giddon denddis; Xoossay ba asaa be7is” yaagidi Xoossaa galatidosona.
Iya sunthay Yihudaninne he heeran de7iya biitta ubban si7ettis.
Xammaqiya Yohaannisa tamaareti hessa ubbaa Yohaannisas odidosona. I entta giddofe nam77ata xeegidi,
“Yaana geetettiday neneyye? Woykko haraa naaginoo?” yaagidi oychchite gidi Godaakko kiittis.
Asati Yesuusakko bidi, Xammaqiya Yohaannisi, “Yaana geetettiday neneyye? Woykko haraa naaginoo?” giite gidi nuna neekko kiittis yaagidosona.
He saatenkka Yesuusi daro asaa harggiyafe pathis. Tuna ayyaanata kessis, qooqida ayfiyakka xeelisis.
Yohaannisa matappe kiitettidi yidayssatakko, “Bidi hintte be7idayssanne si7idayssa Yohaannisas odite. Ayfe qooqeti xeellosona, gunddati birshshettidi hamuttoosona, baro hargganchchoti geeyosona, tulleti si7oosona, hayqqidayssati hayqoppe denddoosona, manqotas Wonggelay sabbakettees.
Tanan dhubettonna oonikka anjjettidayssa.”
Yohaannisi kiittidayssati bidaappe guye Yesuusi asaas Yohaannisabaa yaagidi odis: “Hintte ay be7anaw bazzo biitta keyidetii? Carkkoy qaathiya maata be7anaaseye?
Yaatin, ay be7anaw keyidetii? Koyse ma7o ma77ida asaa be7anaaseyye? Koyse ma7o ma77idayssatinne sa7i injjetida asay kawo keethan de7oosona.
Yaatin, ay be7anaw keyidetii? Nabiya be7anaaseye? Ee, ta yaagays: hintte be7anaw keyiday nabeppe aadhdheyssa.
‘Ne ogiya ne sinthan giigisiya ta kiitanchchuwa neeppe sinthe ta kiittana’ geetettidi xaafettiday iyassa.
Ta hinttew odays; maccasappe yelettidayssata giddofe Yohaannisappe aadhdhey baawa. Xoossaa kawotethan ubbaafe guuxeyssi, I ubbaafe gita gidana” yaagis.
Hari attoshin, Yesuusa qaala si7ida qaraxa qanxiseyssati ubbay Yohaannisa kushen xammaqettidi Xoossay xillo gideyssa qonccisidosona.
Shin Farisaawetinne higge asttamaareti Yohaannisa kushen xammaqettonna ixxidi Xoossaa zoriya leqisidosona.
Yesuusi kaallidi hayssada yaagis: “Hiza, ha wodiya yeletethaa aybira daaniso? Enttika oona daanoona?
Giya giddon uttidi woli xeegidi, ‘Nu hinttew suusul77e punnin, hintte yexxeketa. Nu sabbidi zeleelin, hintte yeekkeketa’ yaagiya nayta daanosona.
Xammaqiya Yohaannisi moonnanne uyonna yin, ‘Iita ayyaanara de7ees gideta.’
Asa Na7ay mishenne uyishe yin, ‘Yarambbanne ushshanchcho, qaraxa qanxiseyssatanne nagaranchchota dabbo’ gideta.
Hiza, cinccatethaa tumatethay iya nayta ubbaa matan erettis” yaagis.
Issi Farisaawey Yesuusa kathi muzanaw ba soo xeegis. I Farisaawiya soo bidi gayta bolla uttis.
He kataman issi nagaranchcho maccasi de7iyara Yesuusi Farisaawiya son gibira bolla de7eyssa si7ida wode daro al77o philqqaaxe shitto ekkada yasu.
Yesuusas guye baggara, iya tohuwa matan eqqada yeekkashe iya tohuwa ba afuthaara laakethawsu. Ba binaanara iya tohuwa quchchashenne yeerashe shitto tiyasu.
Gibira giigisida Farisaawey hessa be7ida wode ba wozanan, “Hayssi nabe gidiyakko ha maccasiya iya bochchiyara ooneekko qassi iya nagaranchcho gideyssakka I eranashin” yaagis.
Yesuusi, “Simoona, ta new odiyabay de7ees” yaagis. I, “Asttamaariyaw, taw oda” yaagis.
Yesuusi iyaakko, “Nam77u asati issi uraappe miishe tal77idosona. Issoy ichchashu xeetu bira hankkoy qassi ishatamu bira tal77idosona.
Nam77ayka tal77iya cigganaw xoonettin, nam77ataskka tal77iya maaris. Hiza, ha nam77atappe he uraa daro dosanay new awussa daanii” yaagis.
Simooni, “Daro acoy maarettida uray daro dosana daanees” yaagis. Yesuusi, “Ne tuma pirddadasa” yaagis.
Hessafe guye, Yesuusi maccaseekko simmi xeellidi, Simoonakko, “Hanno maccasiw be7ay? Taani ne soo gelin hari attin ne taw toho haathe immabaakka, shin iya ta tohuwa ba afuthan laakothada ba binaanan quchchasu.
Neeni tana yeera ekkabaakka, shin iya ta ne soo geloodeppe doomada ta tohuwa yeero aggabukku.
Neeni ta huu7iyan zayte tiyabaka, shin iya ta tohuwa shitto tiyawusu.
Iya tana daro dosida gisho I daro nagaray atto geetettis. Iya guutha nagaray atto geetettiday guuthara dosees.”
Yesuusi maccaseekko, “Ne nagaray atto geetettis” yaagis.
Iyara issife gaytan uttidi miya imathati, “Nagara atto yaagey, I hayssi oonee?” yaagidi bantta wozanan qoppidosona.
Yesuusi maccaseekko, “Ne ammanoy nena ashshis; saro ba” yaagis.
Hessafe guye, Yesuusi Xoossaa kawotethaa Wonggelaa sabbakishe katamaaranne gutaara aadhdhis. He wode tammanne nam77u hawaareti iyara de7oosona.
Qassi tuna ayyaanaappenne dumma dumma harggiyafe paxida issi issi maccasati iyara de7oosona. Enttika, laappun tuna ayyaanati keyida Magdela Mayraamo,
Heroodisa shuumaa Kuuza machchiw Yohaanna, Soosinnaranne qassi hara daroti enttana miishen maaddeyssati de7oosona.
Daro asay dumma dumma katamaappe iyaakko shiiqin leemison enttaw odis.
“Issi goshshanchchoy zerethi zeranaw keyis. I zerishin issi issi zerethay oge gaxan wodhdhidi yedhdhettis, salo kafoti maxidosona.
Harati shaalloy garssan de7iya biitta bolla wodhdhidosona. Buroo dolida mela biittan laahoy baynna gisho miccidosona.
Hara zerethay qassi aguntha giddon wodhdhis. Agunthaara wolla diccida gisho agunthay cuullidi bessan ashshis.
Harati lo77o biitta bolla wodhdhidosona. Dolida wode xeetu kushe ayfidosona.” Hessa odi onggidi, ba qaala dhoqqu oothidi, “Si7iya haythi de7iya ubbay si7o” yaagis.
Iya tamaareti, “Ha leemisuwa birshshethay aybee?” yaagidi oychchidosona
I, “Xoossaa kawotethaa xuuraa erana mela hinttew imettis. Shin harati be7ishe demmonna mela, si7ishe akeekonna mela leemison odays.
“Hiza, ha leemisuwa birshshethay hayssa: zerethi yaagettiday Xoossaa qaala.
Oge gaxan wodhdhida zerethay qaala si7eyssata. Gidoshin, entti ammanidi attonna mela Xalahey qaala entta wozanaappe maxi digees.
Shaalloy garssan de7iya biitta bolla wodhdhida zerethay qaala si7idi ufayssan ekkeyssata. Entti ha77is ammanoosonappe attin xaphoy baynna gisho paacey gakkiya wode ellesidi kaddoosona.
Aguntha giddon zerettidayssati qaala si7eyssata. Enttika alamiya qofan, duretethaaninne sa7aa duussaa miikkotethan cuulettidi besseyssada ayfibookkona.
Lo77o biittan wodhdhida zerethay lo77o wozanan qaala si7idi naageyssatanne dandda7an minnidi ayfe ayfeyssata.
“Xomppe xomppidi, daachcho kammey woykko arssafe garssan wothey deenna. Geliya asi be7ana mela dhoqqa bessan wothees.
“Hessa gisho, qoncce keyonna qosettidi attiyaabay, erettonna geemmidi attiyaabay deenna.
“Hiza, hintte qaala waati si7iyakko akeekite. De7iya ubbaas guzhetidi imettana, baynnayssas hari attoshin iyaw de7iya guuthiyaka iyappe ekettana” yaagis.
Yesuusa aayeranne ishatara iyaakko yidosona. Shin asaa darotethaafe denddoyssan iya demmanaw dandda7ibookkona.
Issi asi Yesuusakko, “Ne aayeranne ne ishatara nena koyidi karen naagoosona” yaagis.
Yesuusi zaaridi, “Xoossaa qaala si7idi ooson peeshsheyssati ubbay taw aayonne taw isha” yaagis.
Issi gallas Yesuusaranne iya tamaaretara issife wogolon gelidi, “Abbaa pinnoos” yaagis. Enttika baanaw denddidosona.
Abbaa bollara entti pinnanaw bishin Yesuusi dhiskkis. Qopponna mino carkkoy abbaa bolla denddis. Haathay wogoluwan gelin wogoloy mitetethi oykkiya wode ubbay babbidosona.
Iya tamaareti iyaakko shiiqidi, “Nu Godaw, nu Godaw, nu dhayos yaagidi” Yesuusa denthidosona. Yesuusi denddidi carkkuwanne gotiya seeris. Ellesidi carkkoynne gotey woppu gis. Sarotethayka simmis.
Yesuusi ba tamaaretakko, “Hintte ammanoy awunee” yaagis. Enttika, yayyishenne malaalettishe issoy issuwako, “Carkkoynne haathay kiitetteyssi, I hayssi oonee” yaagidosona.
Abbaa pinnidi Galiila baggara de7iya Gerggesoone biittaa gakkidosona.
Yesuusi wogoluwappe keyidi sa7an wodhdhishin tuna ayyaanan oykettida uray katamaappe keyidi iyara gahettis. Daro laythi afili ma77onna kallo duufon de7eesippe attin soo gelenna.
Yesuusa be7ida wode iya sinthan gufannidi, ba qaala dhoqqu oothidi, “Ubbaafe Bolla Xoossaa na7aw Yesuusa neera taw aybi issifetethi de7ii? Hayyana tana ha77i un77ethofarkkii” yaagis.
Hessa I giday, tuna ayyaanay uraappe keyana mela Yesuusi hanqettida gishossa. Daro wode tuna ayyaanay iya haarida gisho santhalaataninne toho qachchiya biraatan qashettidi naagettees. Shin qashuwa duuthidi tuna ayyaanan laagettidi bazzo gelis.
Yesuusi, “Ne sunthay oonee” yaagidi oychchis. I, daro tuna ayyaanati iya oykkidi gisho bana, “Leegiyona” gis.
Tuna ayyaanati banttana Si7oole kiittonna mela woossidosona.
He bessan zooze bolla miya guduntho wudey hamuttees. Hini gudunthotan gelino gidi woossidosona, ikka “Gelite” gis.
