Tuna ayyaanati uraappe keyidi gudunthotan gelidosona. Wudey deriyappe duge gurgguxidi abban gelis.
Henthanchchoti hanidayssa be7ida wode woxxi bidi, katamaninne guta ubban odidosona.
Asay hanidabaa be7anaw keyidi Yesuusakko yidosona. Tuna ayyaanay keyida uray ma7o ma77idi, iya wozanay simmin, Yesuusa toho matan uttidayssa demmidi yayyidosona.
Iya be7ida asay tuna ayyaanan oykettida uray waanidi paxidaakko odidosona.
Gerggesoone yuushuwan de7iya asay gita yashshi yashettidi Yesuusi bantta matappe baana mela woossidosona. I wogoluwan gelidi guye simmis.
Tuna ayyaanay keyida uray Yesuusara daanaw woossis.
Shin Yesuusi iyaakko, “Ne soo simma, Xoossay ay mela gitabaa new oothidaakko oda” yaagidi mooyzis. Uraykka Yesuusi ay mela gitabaa iyaw oothidaakko katama ubban markkattishe bis.
Asay naagidi gam77ida gisho Yesuusi simmiya wode mokki ekkidosona.
Ayhude Woosa Keetha halaqa gidida Iyaroosa giya uray ba soo yaana mela Yesuusa tohuwa bolla wodhdhidi woossis.
Iyaw tammanne nam77u laythi gidida macca na7a de7iyara sakettada hayqos gakkada de7awusu. Yesuusi biya wode asay iya un77ethees.
Tammanne nam77u laythi suuthi goggishe gam77ida maccasi de7iyara de7awusu. Iya baw de7iya miishiya aakimetas immada onggasu. Shin paxanaw dandda7abukku.
Iya Yesuusas guye baggara shiiqada, iya afilaa macaraa bochchasu, sohuwara goggiya suuthay eqqi aggis.
Yesuusi, “Tana bochchiday oonee?” yaagis. Ubbay “Nu bochchibookko” yaagin, Phexiroosi, “Asttamaariyaw, daro asay kaallishininne un77ethishin be7ashe waanada, ‘Tana bochchiday oonee?’ gay” yaagis.
Shin Yesuusi, “Issi asi tana bochchis; ays giikko, wolqqi taappe keyoyssi taw erettis” yaagis.
Maccasiya, ibay qonccidayssa erida wode kokkorashe yada Yesuusa tohuwa bolla kunddasu. Ays bochchidaakkonne waanada ellesada paxidaakko asaa ubbaa sinthan markkattasu.
I, “Ta naatte, ne ammanoy nena pathis; saron ba” yaagis.
Yesuusi oda onggonna de7ishin, Ayhude Woosa Keetha halaqaa, Iyaroosa sooppe issi asi yidi, “Iyaroosa, ne na7iya hayqqasu; asttamaariya mela daaburissofa” yaagis.
Shin Yesuusi hessa si7idi Iyaroosakko, “Babbofa! Ammana, ne na7iya paxana” yaagis.
Yesuusi Iyaroosa soo gakkida wode Phexiroosappe, Yohaannisappe, Yayqoobappe, na7ee aawappenne aayeppe attin hari gelana mela koyibeenna.
He bessan de7iya asa ubbay na7ees mishettidi yeekkishin, Yesuusi, “Yeekkofite! Na7iya dhiskkasuppe attin hayqqabuukku” yaagis.
Asay na7iya hayqqidayssa eriya gisho iya oda leqqidi miicidosona.
Shin Yesuusi na7ee kushiya oykkidi, “Naatte dendda” yaagis.
Na7ees shemppoy simmin dendda eqqasu. Yesuusi enttako, “Iwu miyabaa immite” yaagis.
Na7ee aawaranne aayera malaalettidosona. Shin Yesuusi hayssa, “Ooddeskka odoppite” yaagis.
Yesuusi tammanne nam77u hawaareta baakko xeegidi, tuna ayyaanata kessana melanne hargge ubbaa pathana mela wolqqanne maata immis.
Xoossaa kawotethaabaa markkattanaadanne hargganchchota pathanaada kiittis.
I enttako, “Xam77a gidin ogoro gidin kathi gidin miishe gidin laammi ma77iya afila gidin oges gidi aykkoka oykkofite.
He katamaappe hintte keyana gakkanaw imathatethan hintte gelidasuwan gam77ite.
Oonikka hinttena mokkonna ixxiko he katamaappe keyishe enttaw markka gidana mela hintte tohuwan de7iya baana pittidi keyite.”
Enttika kiitettidayssada keyidi Wonggelaa odishenne dumma dumma gutatan hargganchchota pathishe aadhdhidosona.
Galiila biittaa haariya Heroodisi Yesuusi oothidabaa ubbaa si7ida wode dagammis. Ays giikko, issi issi asati Yohaannisi hayqoppe denddonna aggenna yaagosona.
Baggati, “Eeliyaasi qonccis” goosona; harati qassi, “Beni nabetappe issoy hayqoppe denddis” yaagidi odettoosona.
Shin Heroodisi, “Yohaannisa qoodhiya ta qanxisada wodhas. Yaatin, hayssatho yaagettidi iyabaa odettey, I oonee?” yaagidi ba ayfen be7anaw koyees.
Tammanne nam77u hawaareti guye simmi yidi, entti oothidabaa ubbaa Yesuusas odidosona. I enttana ekkidi Beetesayda katamaappe gaxa efis.
Shin daro asay Yesuusa gideyssa eridi iya kaallidosona. I entta mokki ekkidi Xoossaa kawotethaabaa tamaarssis; paxanaw koyeyssatakka pathis.
Sa7i omarssiya wode tammanne nam77u hawaareti iyaakko shiiqidi, “Nu de7ey bazzo biitta gidiya gisho asay dumma dumma gutatanne katamata bidi, kathinne aqiyaso koyana mela asaa moyza” yaagidosona.
Shin I, “Enttaw miyabaa hintte immite” yaagis. Entti, “Nuus de7ey ichchashu uythinne nam77u molo gidiya gisho ha asaas gidiya kathi nuuni bidi shammonna ixxiko gidenna” yaagidosona.
He bessan ichchashu mukulu gidiya addeti de7oosona. Yesuusi ba tamaaretakko, “Ishataman ishataman shaakki shaakki asaa utisite” yaagis.
Iya tamaareti, I kiittidayssada asaa utisidosona.
I ichchashu uythaanne nam77u molota ekkidi, salo xeellidi, Xoossaa galatidi, meenthidi asaa ubbaa gathana mela ba tamaaretas immis.
Ubbay midi kallidosona. Enttafe attida tiifey tammanne nam77u gayta kumethi gidis.
Yesuusi ba xalaala woossishin, iya tamaareti iyaakko yidosona. I, “Asay tana oona goonaa?” gidi oychchis.
Entti zaaridi “Issoti issoti, ‘Xammaqiya Yohaannisa, baggati Eliyaasa, harati qassi, beni nabetappe issoy hayqoppe denddis’ yaagosona” yaagidosona.
I zaaridi, “Yaatin hintte tana oona geeti” yaagis. Phexiroosi, “Neeni Xoossaafe kiitettida Kiristtoosa” yaagidi zaaris.
Yesuusi hayssa ooddeskka odoppite gidi minthidi odis.
Qassika Yesuusi, “Asa Na7ay daro metuwa ekkana. Biitta cimatan, kahine halaqatan, higge asttamaaretan aadhdhi imettana. Entti iya wodhana, shin I heedzantho gallas hayqoppe denddana” yaagis.
Yesuusi asaa ubbaako, “Tana kaallanaw koyey oonikka de7ikko bana kaddo, ba masqaliya gallas gallas tookkidi tana kaallo.
Ba shemppiw ashshanaw koya ubbay iyo dhayssees, ba shemppiw ta gisho gidi dhayssiya oonikka iyo ashshees.
Asi alame ubbaa haaridi, gidoshin ba shemppiw dhayssiyabaa woykko qohiyabaa gidikko iya ay maaddii?
Oonikka tananinne ta qaalan yeellatikko Asa Na7ay ba bonchchuwara hessadakka aawa bonchchuwaranne Geeshsha kiitanchchota bonchchuwara yaa wode iyan yeellatana.
Ta hinttew tuma odays; hayssan eqqidayssata giddofe Xoossaa kawotethaa be7onnashin hayqqonna asati de7oosona” yaagis.
Yesuusi he oda odin, hosppun gallasappe guye Phexiroosa, Yayqoobanne Yohaannisa baara ekkidi woossanaw deriya bolla keyis.
I woosa bolla de7ishin iya ayfe karey laamettis; afilaykka awa mela phoolidi booxis.
Nam77u asati, enttika Museranne Eliyaasara bonchchon qonccidi,
Yerusalaamen polettanaw de7iyabaa, hessika, I ha alamiyappe shaakettanabaa iyara odettoosona.
Phexiroosanne iyara de7eyssata dhiskkoy efin, entti dhiskkofe barkkiya wode iya bonchchuwanne iyara eqqida nam77u asata be7idosona.
Asati Yesuusappe shaakettidi baana hanishin, Phexiroosi Yesuusakko, “Godaw, hayssan gideyssi nuus ay mela lo77o! Issino new, issino Muses, issino Eliyaasas oothidi heedzu shaqara shaqaroos” yaagis. Shin I ay gidaakko erenna.
I yaagidi odettishin shaaray yidi enttana kammis. Entti he shaara giddo gelishe babbidosona.
Shaara giddofe, “Ta doorida na7ay hayssa iya si7ite” yaagiya qaalay si7ettis.
He qaalay si7ettidaappe guye Yesuusi barkka de7ishe benttis. He wode entti be7idabaa ooddeskka odonna, bantta wozanan oykkidi si77i gidosona.
Wonttethe entti deriyappe wodhdhiya wode daro asay yidi iyara gahettidosona.
He wode asaa giddofe issi asi, “Asttamaariyaw, ta issi na7aa yada be7arkki.
Tuna ayyaanay qopponna oykkidi waasises; goppontto yegisidi qakerethees, asatethaa qohidi un77ethidi yeddees.
Ne tamaareti kessana mela woossas, shin entti dandda7ibookkona” yaagidi woossis.
Yesuusi, “Ammanoy baynna geella yeletethato, awude gakkanaw ta hinttera daane, hinttena dandda7anee? Ne na7aa bada haa ekkaya” yaagis.
Na7aa ekkidi yaa wode tuna ayyaanay sa7an holi yeggidi kokkorssis. Shin Yesuusi tuna ayyaanaa hanqidi na7aappe kessis. Na7aakka na7aa aawas immis.
Asay ubbay Xoossaa gita wolqqan malaalettidosona. Entti I oothidaban malaalettishin, Yesuusi ba tamaaretakko,
“Hayssa ta hinttew odeyssa loythi si7ite; Asa Na7ay morkketa kushen aadhdhi imettana” yaagis.
Shin I gidabay enttafe geemmida gisho akeekibookkona. Hessa gisho, zaaridi oychchanaw babbidosona.
Yesuusa tamaareti, “Nu giddon gita gidanay oonee?” gidi palama oykkidosona.
Yesuusi entta wozanaa qofaa eridi yooga na7aa ba matan essidi,
“Ha yooga na7aa ta sunthan mokkiya oonikka tana mokkees, tana mokkey tana kiittidayssa mokkees, hintte ubbaafe guuxeyssi, I gita gidana” yaagis.
Yohaannisi, “Godaw, issi asi ne sunthan tuna ayyaanata kessishin be7idi I nuura gidonna gisho diggida” yaagis.
Yesuusi zaaridi, “Hinttera eqettonnayssi, I hintte bagga. Hessa gisho, iya diggofite” yaagis.
Yesuusi salo biya wodey matattida gisho Yerusalaame baanaw qanxidi denddis.
Samaare biittan de7iya issi gutaa bidi, ubbabaa iyaw giigisana mela ase yaa kiittis.
Shin I bey Yerusalaame gidiya gisho entti iya mokki ekkibookkona.
Yesuusa tamaareti Yayqoobaranne Yohaannisara hessa be7idi, “Godaw, saloppe tami wodhdhidi entta mo gaana mela ne koyay” yaagidosona.
Shin Yesuusi guye simmi entta hanqettidi, “Hintte garssan aybi ayyaani de7iyakko hintte erekketa. Asa Na7ay ase ashshanaw yisippe attin dhayssanaassa gidenna” yaagis.
Yaappe denddidi hara guta bidosona.
Entti ogiyara bishin, issi asi, “Ne biyaso ubbaa ta kaallana” yaagis.
Yesuusi zaaridi, “Workkanatas olli, salo kafotas keethi de7ees, shin Asa Na7ay ba huu7iya shemppisiyasoy baawa” yaagis.
Hankkuwako, “Neeni tana kaalla” yaagis. Shin uray, “Godaw, koyrottada ta aawa moogada yaana” yaagis.
Shin Yesuusi, “Hayqqidayssati hayqqidayssata moogana mela enttaw aggaaga; neeni bada Xoossaa kawotethaa sabbaka” yaagis.
Qassi hara asi, “Godaw, ta nena kaallana, shin koyrottada ta soo asa sarothada yaana” yaagis.
Yesuusi zaaridi, “Koxe oykkidi guye xeelliya oonikka Xoossaa kawotethaas bessenna” yaagis.
Hessafe guye, Goday haraa laappun tammanne nam77u asata dooris. I baanaw qoppida katamaanne guta ubbaa sinthattidi baanada nam77a nam77a oothidi kiittis.
Yesuusi enttako, “Hekko shiiqana kathay daro shin oosanchchoti guutha. Yaaniya gisho, kathaa goday oosanchchota kiittana mela woossite.
Hiza, biite, dorssatada suudhumeta giddo hinttena taani yeddana.
Hintte biya ogiyas aykkoka oykkofite, miishe gidin kathi gidin caamma oykkofite. Oge bolla oonakka sarothofite
Hintte geliya keethaa ubbaa koyrottidi, ‘Saroy ha keethaas gido’ yaagite.
Saro dosiya asi he bessan de7ikko, hintte saroy yan shemppana; ixxas giikko hintte saroy hinttew simmana.
Oosanchchos damooze bessiya gisho hintte gelida keethan hinttew shiishidaba ubbaa mishenne uyishe yan gam77ite. Issuwa sooppe issuwa soo yuuyoppite.
Ay katamakka hintte geliya wode asay hinttena mokkidi, hinttew shiishidaba ubbaa miite.
He kataman de7iya hargganchchota pathishe, ‘Xoossaa kawotethay hintteko matis’ yaagidi odite.
Shin issi katamaa geliya wode asay hinttena mokkonna ixxiko dabaaba keyidi hayssada giite:
‘Nu tohuwa bolla de7iya hintte katamaa baana pittoos, shin Xoossaa kawotethay hintteko matattidayssa erite.’
Pirdda gallasan ha katamaappe Soodome katamaas pirdday kawushshe gidanayssa ta hinttew odays” yaagis.
Kaallidikka, Yesuusi, “Neno Koraaziine, neno Beetesayda, ayye, hinttenan oosettida malaatati Xiroosaninne Sidoonan oosettidaakko yan de7iya asay kalle ma77idi, bidintha bolla uttidi beni maarotan geli agganashin.
Hessa gisho, hinttefe aathidi Xiroosasinne Sidoonas Xoossaa pirdday kawuyana.
Nekka Qifirnahoome, salo gakkanaw nena dhoqqu oothanaw koyay? Ne duge Si7oole holettana” yaagis.
Qassika Yesuusi ba tamaaretakko, “Hinttena si7ey tana si7ees, hinttena ekkonnay tana ekkena, tana ekkonnay tana kiittidayssa ekkenna” yaagis.
Laappun tammanne nam77u tamaareti kiitettida bessaafe keehi ufayttishe simmidosona. Yesuusakko shiiqidi, “Godaw, ne sunthan tuna ayyaanatikka nuus kiitettidosona” yaagidosona.
Yesuusi enttako, “Xalahey saloppe wol77anthada wodhdhishin ta be7as.
Hekko, shooshaanne kornne yedhdhana melanne morkkiya wolqqaa zaarana mela maata hinttew immas. Hinttena qohanabay aykkoyka deenna.
Gidoshin, hintte sunthay salo mazggaban xaafettida gisho ufayttiteppe attin tuna ayyaanati kiitettida gisho ufayttofite” yaagis.
He wode Yesuusi Geeshsha Ayyaanan ufayttidi, “Saluwa sa7aa Godaw, hayssa cinccatappenne eranchchotappe geenthada yalagatas qonccisida gisho galatetta. Ee ta aawaw, hessa ne oothanaw lo77o shene gidis.
“Ubbabay ta aawappe taw imettis. Na7ay ooneekko aawappe attin hari woykko na7ay qonccisanaw koyeyssafe hari oonikka aawa erey baawa” yaagis.
Kaallidikka, Yesuusi dumma ba tamaaretakko, “Hintte be7eyssa be7eyssati anjjettidayssata.
Tuma daro nabetinne kawoti hintte be7eyssanne si7eyssa be7anawunne si7anaw amottidosona, shin be7ibookkona, si7ibookkona” yaagis.
Hekko, issi gallas Muse wogaa eriya issi uray denddidi Yesuusa yaagidi paace oysho oychchis. “Asttamaariyaw, merinaa de7uwa laattanaw taani ay ootho?” yaagis.
Yesuusi, “Muse maxaafan xaafettiday woygii? Ne waata nabbabay?” yaagis.
Addey zaaridi, “ ‘Ne Godaa ne Xoossaa, ne kumetha wozanappe, ne kumetha shemppuwafe, ne kumetha wolqqaafenne ne kumetha qofaappe dosa. Qassi ase ne shooruwa ne huu7iyada dosa’ yaagees” yaagis.
Yesuusi iyaakko, “Neeni likke zaaradasa, nekka hessada ootha. Neeni merinaw de7on daana” yaagis.
Shin uray bana xillo oothanaw koyidi, “Hanos I ta shooroy oonee?” yaagis.
Iya oyshaas Yesuusi yaagidi zaaro immis, “Issi ase de7eyssi Yerusalaame katamaappe duge Iyaarkko katamaa bishin oge bolla panggati keyidi shocidosona. Iya ma7uwa qaari ekkidi hayqoppenne paxappe giddon yeggidi bidosona.
Guyeppe, Ayhude kahine issoy he ogiyara ba buussu bishe uraa be7idi deshshi gidi aadhdhis.
Qassi issi Leewe de7eyssi he bessaa gakkishe uraa be7idi harasoora aadhdhidi bis.
Shin, issi Samaare biitta ase de7eyssi he ogiyara yishe uraa be7idi iyaw qadhettis
Iyaakko shiiqidi, iya madunthaa bolla zaytenne woyne tigidi qachchis. Ba hariya bolla utisidi imathi aqiya keethi efis. He bessan iyaw koshshiyaba ubbaa oothis.
Wonttethe nam77u dinaare kessidi imatha keethaawas immidi, ‘Hayyana ha uraa loytha xeella. Taani new immidayssafe bollara ne kessiyabaa ubbaa ta new ciggana’ yaagis.
“Hiza, ha heedzu asatappe panggati shocida uraas shoorotey new oona daanii?”
Uray zaaridi, “Iyaw qadhettidayssaka” yaagis. Yesuusi, “Nekka bada hessada ootha” yaagis.
Yesuusi ba tamaaretara oge bishe issi guta gakkis. Yan Martta geetettiya issi maccasiya iya ba son mokkasu.
Iwukka Mayraamo giya michchiya de7awusu, Mayraama qaala si7ashe Godaa tohuwa matan uttasu.
Shin Martta daro ooson un77ettada Yesuusakko shiiqada, “Godaw, ta michchiya oosuwa ta xalaalas yeggada utta aggin ta daaburiya wode neeni be7ashe si77i gay? Iya tana maaddana mela odikkii” yaagasu.
Shin Goday hayssada gidi zaaris, “Martta, Martta, neeni daroban un77ettasaanne metootasa.
Gidoshin, koyettey issibaa xalaala. Mayraama lo77obaa doorasu, hessika iippe ekettenna” yaagis.
Issi gallas Yesuusi issi bessan woossees. Woosaa wurssida wode iya tamaaretappe issoy, “Godaw, Yohaannisi ba tamaareta woosa tamaarssida mela nekka nuna woosa tamaarssa” yaagis.
Yesuusi, “Hayssada yaagidi woossite: ‘Saluwan de7iya nu aawaw ne geeshsha sunthay anjjetto; ne kawotethay yo.
Nu gallasa kathaa hachchi hachchi nuus imma.
Nuna qoheyssata nuuni atto geyssada, nu nagara atto ga; paacen nuna gelssofa’ yaagite” yaagis.
Kaallidikka, Yesuusi ba tamaaretakko yaagis: “Leemisos hinttefe issuwas laggey de7ees. I giddi bilahe ba laggiya soo bidi, ‘Ta laggiyaw, heedzu soollo taw tal77arkki.
Taw lagge gidida issi asi ogeppe yin, iyaw aathiyabaa dhayas’ yaagikko,
“Iya laggey keethaa giddon gididi, ‘Hayyana tana waaysoppa, wulay gorddettis. Ta naytikka taara arssa bolla zin77idosona. Yaaniya gisho, denddada ne koyabaa immanaw dandda7ikke’ yaagiyye?
Ta hinttew odays; laggetethaa gisho denddidi immanaw koyonna ixxikokka woosan salethida gisho denddidi koshshiyaba ubbaa immees.
“Hessa gisho, taani hinttew odays; woossite hinttew imettana; koyite hintte demmana; kare yidi xeegite hinttew dooyettana.
Gaasoykka woossiya ubbay ekkees; koyey demmees; kare yidi xeegeyssas dooyettees.
“Hinttenoo, aawato hintte giddofe na7i uythi woossin shuchchu immey oonee? Molo woossin shooshi immey oonee?
Woykko phuuphphulle woossiko kornne immi?
Hintte iitata gidishe hintte naytas lo77obaa immo erikko, salon de7iya hintte aaway woosseyssatas Geeshsha Ayyaana waati aathi immenne?” yaagis.
Issi gallas Yesuusi doona muumisida tuna ayyaanaa issi uraappe kessis. Tuna ayyaanay keyida mela muume uray odettis. Asaykka malaalettis.
Shin issoti issoti, “Tuna ayyaanaa halaqaa, Bi7elzebuula wolqqan tuna ayyaanata kessees” yaagidosona.
Harati qassi paaces saloppe malla bessana mela koyidosona.
Shin Yesuusi entta qofaa eridi enttako, “Woli giddon shaakettiya kawotethi ubbay dhayees; woli giddon shaakettiya keethi kunddees.
Xalahey woli giddon shaakettiko iya kawotethay waanidi minnidi eqqanee? Hintte tana, ‘I tuna ayyaanata Bi7elzebuula wolqqan kessees’ yaageta.
Hiza, taani tuna ayyaanaa Bi7elzebuula wolqqan kessiyabaa gidikko hintte nayti oodde wolqqan kessonashsha? Hessa gisho, entti hintte bolla pirddeyssata gidana.
Shin taani tuna ayyaanata Xoossaa biradhdhen kessiyabaa gidikko hiza Xoossaa kawotethay hintteko matidayssa erite.
“Mino asi danccettidi ba keethaa naagiyabaa gidikko, iya shaloy boshettenna.
Hanoshin, iyappe aadhdhi mino gidida asi yidi, iya qohidi xoonikko ammanettidi danccida danccuwa bilisidi, iya shaluwa bonqqidi haraas shaakkees.
“Taara gidonnayssi tana ixxees; taara shiishonnaysika laallees.
“Tuna ayyaanay asappe keyida wode shemppiyaso koyidi haathi baynnasoora yuuyees. Shemppiyaso dhayida wode ‘Ta keyidasuwa simmana’ yaagees.
I simmiya wode keethay pitettidi lo77idi de7ishin demmis.
Hessafe guye, bidi iyappe aadhdhidi iitida haraa laappun tuna ayyaanata ekkidi yees. Iyan gelidi duussu oykkees. He uraas koyroyssafe guyeyssi aadhdhidi iita gidees” yaagis.
Yesuusi hessa oda bolla de7ishin issi maccasi asaa gaathafe denddada, ba qaala dhoqqu oothada, “Nena tookkida uloynne neeni dhammida dhanthati anjjettidosona” yaagasu.
Shin I, “Anjjettidayssati Xoossaa qaala si7idi kiitetteyssata” yaagis.
Daro asay shiiqida wode Yesuusi, “Ha yeletethay iita; ooratha malla koyees. Shin Yoonasa malaatappe attin hari enttaw imettena.
Yoonasi Nanawe asaas malla gidida mela Asa Na7aykka ha yeletethaas malla gidana.
Dugeha kawiya pirdda gallas ha yeletethaara denddada pirddana. Gaasoykka, iya Solomone cinccatethaa si7anaw biitta gaxappe denddada yasu. Hekko Solomoneppe aadhdheyssi hayssan de7ees
Nanawe asati pirdda gallas ha yeletethaara denddidi entta bolla pirddana. Gaasoykka Yoonasa sibkkatiyan maarota gelidosona. Hekko, Yoonasappe aadhdhey hayssan de7ees” yaagis.
“Xomppe xomppidi qosa bessan woykko oto giddon wothiya asi deenna. Asi poo7uwa be7ana mela dhoqqa bessan wothees.
Ne asatethaas poo7oy ne ayfiyaa. Ne ayfey lo77o gidikko, ne kumetha asatethay poo7ees. Nena ayfey sakkiko ne asatethay ubbay dhumees.
Hessa gisho, ne garssan de7iya poo7oy dhumonna mela naageeta.
Hiza, ne kumetha asatethay poo7o gidikko, ne asatethankka hari dhuma bessi dhayikko, ne asatetha kumethay wolile poo7o mela gidees” yaagis.
Yesuusi ba oda onggida mela issi Farisaawey baara kathi maana mela xeegis. I iyara issife gelidi gibira bolla uttis.
Farisaawey Yesuusi kathi maanappe sinthe kushe meecconayssa be7idi malaalettis.
Goday iyaakko, “Hintte Farisaaweti quuliyanne shaatiya bolla bagga meecetta. Shin hintte gaathay uuzetethaninne iitatethan kumis.
Hinttenoo, eeyato, kare baggaa medhdhidayssi gaatha medhdhiday iya gidenneyye?
Shin quuliyaninne shaatiyan de7eyssa manqotas immite. He wode hinttew ubbabay geeshshi gidana.
“Farisaaweto hinttena ayye, sawoppe, xalooteppe, hessa melabaappe asraata kesseta. Shin xillotethinne Xoossaa dosoy hinttenan baawa. Harata aggonna hayssatakka oothanaw bessees, shin aggideta.
“Farisaaweto hinttena ayye, Ayhude Woosa Keethan bonchcho oyde, giya giddon bonchcho sarotho doseeta.
“Malay dhayin asay eronna bollara biya duufo daaneyssato hinttena ayye” yaagis.
Higge asttamaarey zaaridi, “Asttamaariyaw, ne hessa gashe nuna cayaasa” yaagis.
Yesuusi, “Hinttenoo, higge asttamaareto, hinttenakka ayye, asay tookkanaw dandda7onna deexo tooho toosseeta, shin hinttee hintte huu7es hari attoshin biradhdhe xeerankka bochcheketa.
“Hintte aawati wodhida nabeta duufuwa hintte giigisiya gisho hinttena ayye.
Hiza, hintte aawata oosuwa minthanaw entti wodhida nabeta duufuwa hintte loythiya gisho entta iita oosuwas hintte markka.
Hessa gisho, Xoossay ba cinccatethan, ‘Nabetanne hawaareta ta hinttew kiittana, shin hintte baggata wodhana; harata gooddana’ yaagis.
Hessa gisho, ha yeletethay alamey medhettoosappe hanno gakkanaw gukkida nabeta ubbaa suuthas oyshettana.
Aabelappe doomidi yarshsho bessaasinne Xoossa Keethaafe gidduwan gukkida Zakkariyaasa suutha gisho ha yeletethay oyshettana.
“Higge asttamaareto, hinttena ayye, eratetha qulppiya hintte kushen oykkideta, shin hinttew gelekketa haratakka gelsseketa.” yaagis.
Yesuusi yaappe baanaw keyaa wode higge asttamaaretinne Farisaaweti iyara eqettidi oyshon waaysosona.
Iya doonappe keyaa qaalan iya oykkanaw koyidi hessa oothidosona.
He wode daro mukulun taybettiya asay woli bolla yedhdhettana gakkanaw asi asa bolla shiiqidi de7ishin, Yesuusi ba tamaaretakko, “Farisaaweta irshshuwaafe naagettite. Hessika entta cubbotethaa.
Qoncconna qosettidi, erettonna geemmidi attiyaabay aykkoyka baawa.
Hiza, hintte dhuman odidabay ubbay poo7on si7ettana, qol77a gaathan kalkkashidabay dabaaban odettana.
“Ta baggato, ta odeyssa si7ite; ashuwa wodhoosonappe attin haraa aykkoka oothanaw dandda7onnayssatas babbofite.
Hanoshin, hintte babbanaw besseyssa ta hinttew qonccisana. Hessika wodhidaappe guye Gaannamen yegganaw wolqqay de7eyssas iyaw babbite. Ee, tuma gays; iyaw babbite.
Ichchashu buubbeti issi santimes bayzettokonaayye? Hanoppe attin enttafe issinnaka Xoossaa sinthan dogetuku.
Hari attoshin, hintte huu7e binaanaykka paydettidi de7ees. Hiza, babbofite; daro buubbetappe hintte aadhdheeta.
“Ta odeyssa si7ite; asa sinthan taw markkattiya ubbaas Asa Na7ay Xoossaa kiitanchchota sinthan markkattana.
Asa sinthan tana kaddeyssas Xoossaa kiitanchchota sinthan ta iya kaddana.
Asa Na7a bolla kadhe qaala haasayaa ubbay maarota demmana, shin Geeshsha Ayyaana bolla kadhe qaala odetteyssi maaretenna.
“Asi hinttena oykkidi Ayhude Woosa Keethan, daynnata sinthaninne kawota sinthan gooshechchiya wode ay odaneekkonne woygi zaaraneekko hirggofite.
He wode hintte odanabaa Geeshsha Ayyaanay hinttena tamaarssana” yaagis.
Asaa giddofe issi asi Yesuusakko yidi, “Ta ishay taw nu aawa laatappe shaakkana mela iyaw oda” yaagis.
Yesuusi zaaridi, “La addiyaw, hintte bolla tana daynnanne laata shaakkiya cima oothiday oonee?” yaagis.
Qassika Yesuusi, “Asa de7oy shalo darotethan gidonna gisho yaare aggidi minthidi hinttena naagite” yaagis.
Kaallidikka leemison, “Gadey daro kathi immiya issi dure uray de7ees.
He uray, ‘Ta kathaa taani shiishanaw bessi guuxida gisho ay ootho?’ yaagidi ba wozanan qoppis.
Hizappe yaatana; kase de7iya shaaleta laallada haraa dalgga shaaleta keexana. Kathaanne taw de7iyaba ubbaa iyan yeggana.
Ba shemppeeko, ‘Ta shemppete, daro laythas new gidiya shalo shiishas. Hiza, shemppada ma, uya, ufaytta’ yaagana.
“Shin Xoossay, ‘La, eeya addiyaw, hachchi qamma ne shemppiya neeppe ekettawusu. Hiza, ne shiishidabay ooddees gidanee?’ yaagis.
“Hessa gisho, baw duretethi sa7an shiishiya asas, Xoossaa matan dure gidonna asaas wurssethay ha urayssa mela” yaagis.
Hessafe guye, Yesuusi ba tamaaretakko, “Hiza, ta odiyabaa si7ite, hintte shemppuwas ay mino hintte bollaas ay ma77ino yaagidi un77ettofite.
Shemppoy kathafe bolli afilappe aadhdhees.
Kafota be7ite zerokkona, kiishokkona, eleykka shaaleykka baawa. Shin Xoossay enttana muzees. Hintte kafotappe daro aadhdheeta.
Hanoshin, hinttefe un77ettidi ba laythaa bolla issi qamma gujjanaw dandda7ey oonee?
Hiza, ha guuthabaa oothanaw dandda7onna hintte harabaas ays un77etteetii?
Ane cishshati waanidi dicciyakko be7ite. Waayokkonanne suqqokona. Hari attoshin, Solomoney ba de7iya bonchcho ubban enttafe issuwa melakka ma77ibeena.
Hinttenoo, ammanoy paccidayssato, hiza, Xoossay hachchi benttidi wontto taman yegettana cishshata hayssada mayzikko, hinttena waati aathi mayzennee?
Hessa gisho, ay miino woykko ay uyino gidi un77ettofite.
He ubbaas Xoossaa ammanonna asati un77ettoosona. Shin hintte aaway Xoossay hessi ubbay hinttew koshsheyssa erees.
Ubbaafe aathidi Xoossaa kawotethaa koyite hessi ubbay hinttew gujji imettana.
“Hinttenoo, guutha deretoo, yayyofite; hintte aawa Xoossay kawotethaa hinttew immanaw ufayttees.
Hinttew de7iyabaa bayzidi manqotas immite. Kaysoy ekkonnason, bili moonnason, cimonna karxiitan, wuronna shaluwa saluwan shiishite.
Hintte wozanay hintte shaloy de7iyasuwan gidana.
“Qanthan danccidi giigettite; hintte xomppey poo7idayssa gido.
Bantta goday yaaganoppe simmana gakkanaw barkkidi naageyssatada, goday yidi xeegiya wode ellesidi dooyanaw giigida asata daanite.
Bantta goday simmiya wode dhiskkonna de7ishe naageyssati anjjettidayssata. Tuma gays; goday qanthan danccidi gayta yuushuwan utisidi mokkees.
Goday laade gidin giddi bilahe gidin woykko wonttimaathe gidin yidi, hessa mela dhiskkonna naagishin demmiya he aylleti anjjettidayssata.
Shin hayssa erite; kaysoy awude yaanekko keethaaway eriyakko keethay boketiya wode si77i gidi be7enna.
Hintteka giigidi naagite; Asa Na7ay hintte qopponna wode yaana” yaagis.
Phexiroosikka, “Godaw ha leemisuwa nu xalaalas odayye woykko asa ubbaasee?” yaagis.
Goday zaaridi, “Hiza, kathaa muzanaw bessiya wodiyan immana mela goday ba aylleta bolla shuumida ammantheysinne wozanaama halaqay oonee?
Goday simmiya wode hessa mela oothishe benttiya aylley I anjjettidayssa
Ta hinttew tuma odays; ba godaas de7iya shalo ubbaa bolla I shuumettana.
Shin he aylley, ‘Ta goday elle yeenna’ yaagidi ba wozanan qoppidi, macca aylletanne adde aylleta wadhdhiko, qassi baw koyida mela mishenne uyishe mathottiko,
he aylliya goday I qopponna gallasaninne hirggonna wode yaana. Yidi iya qanxerethidi, iya qaada ammanonna asatara oothana.
“Godaa sheniyada giigonnayssinne iya goday ay dosiyakko erishe oothonna aylley daro garaafettana.
Shin ba godaa sheniya eronna attidi garaafettanaw besseyssa oothiday guuthara garaafettana. Gaasoykka daro imettidayssafe daro koyettees, daro hadara ekkidayssafekka daro immana gidi naagettees.
“Taani yiday biitta bolla tama oythanaassa. Ha77i tamay oykkiyako tana waati ufayssanddeshsha!
Hanoshin, ta ha77i xammaqettiya xinqqatey de7ees. I polettana gakkanaw ta daro un77ettays.
Sa7a bolla sarotethi ehanaw yida hinttew daanii? Gidenna, ta yiday shaakkanaassa.
Ha77ife doomidi woli giddon shaakettida ichchashu keethaa asati issife de7oosona. Nam77ati heedzata bolla, heedzatikka nam77ata bolla, denddidi shaakettoosona.
Aaway na7aa bolla, na7aykka aawa bolla, aayyaa na7ee bolla, na7iya aaye bolla, azinaa aayyaa na7aa machche bolla, na7aa machchiya azinaa aaye bolla, denddidi shaakettana.”
Qassika asaakko, “Wuloha baggara saloy shaaratiya wode be7idi, ellesidi, ‘Iri yaana’ yaageta, hessadakka hanees.
Dugeha carkkoy carkkiya wode ‘Sa7ay awana’ yaageta, hessadakka hanees” yaagis.
Hinttenoo, cubboto, Salobaanne sa7abaa shaakki ereetashin ha wodiya shaakki eroy hinttena waanidi xoonidee?
“Yaatin, hintte huu7es ays tuma pirddeketii?
Ne morkkiyara wolla daynna sinthan eqqanaw bashe oge bolla giiganaw koya. Ne giigonna ixxiko gooshechchidi daynna sinthi nena efana. Daynnay nena poolisees aathi immana. I nena woynen yeggana.
Si7ite, issi bakkani attonna cigga onggana gakkanaw ne yaappe keyonnayssa era” yaagis.
He wode Yesuusakko asay yidi Philaaxoosi wodhidi entta suuthaara entta yarshshuwa walakkida Galiila asaabaa odida asati he bessan de7oosona.
I hayssada yaagidi zaaris; “Yaatin he Galiila asati he iita hayqo hayqqida gisho Galiilan de7iya asa ubbaafe aadhdhida nagaranchcho daanoona?
Gidenna! Gidoshin, hintteka maarotan simmona ixxiko, ubbay hessada dhayana.
Woykko qassi Salihoome giya bessan gimbbey woddidi wodhida tammanne hosppun asay Yerusalaamen de7iya asa ubbaafe aadhdhida nagaranchcho daanoona?
Gidenna! Shin hintteka maarotan simmona ixxiko ubbay hessada dhayana.”
Qassika Yesuusi hayssada gidi leemiso odis: “Issi uraas woyne gaden tokettida balase mithiya de7awusu. I iippe ayfe koyii yidi aykkoka demmibeenna.
Gadiya goday woyne oosanchchuwakko, ‘Ayfe demmanaw koyada heedzu laythi simerettada aykkoka demmabiikke. Hessa gisho, qanxa digga; ays biittaa melisay?’ yaagis.
“Shin oosanchchoy, ‘Godaw, I yuushuwa oothada osha yeggana gakkanaw ha laythas aggarkii.
Ha laythi ayfikko lo77o, ixxiko qanxa agga’ ” yaagidi zaaris.
Yesuusi Sambbaata gallas Ayhude Woosa Keethan tamaarssees.
He bessan tammanne hosppun laythi tuna ayyaani zokko kuunisida issi maccasiya de7awusu. Iya kuunappe denddoyssan suure eqqanaw dandda7ukku.
Yesuusi iyo be7ida wode xeegidi, “Ha maccasete, ne harggiyafe paxadasa” yaagis.
Ba kushiya I bolla wothin, iya sohuwara suurada eqqasu. Xoossaaka galatasu.
Shin Ayhude Woosa Keetha halaqay yilotidi asaakko, “Ooso oothiya usuppun gallasati de7oosona. Hessa gisho, he gallasatan yidi paxiteppe attin Sambbaata gallas gidenna” yaagis.
Goday, “Cubboto, hintte giddofe boori woykko hare Sambbaata gallas zadalope billidi haathe ushshanaw efonnay oonee?
Yaatin, ha maccasiya Abrahame na7aa gidashe xalahen qashettada tammanne hosppun laythi kumethi de7idaaris Sambbaata gallas birshshetethi koshshennee?” yaagidi oychchis.
I hessa odida wode eqetteyssati ubbay yeellatidosona. Shin asa ubbay I oothida malaalisiya ooso ubban ufayttidosona.
Hessafe guye, Yesuusi hayssada yaagis, “Xoossaa kawotethay ay daanii? Iya aybira daaniso?
Xoossaa kawotethay issi asi ba goshshan tokkida wola ayfe mela. I diccidi mithi gidis. Salo kafoti iya tashiya bolla shemppidosona.
Qassi, “Xoossaa kawotethaa aybira daaniso?
Issi maccasiya daro dhiillera walakkada munuqida guutha irshsho daanees” yaagis.
Hessafe guye, Yesuusi Yerusalaame bishe I kanthiya ogiyan de7iya katamataninne gutatan tamaarssishe aadhdhis.
Issi asi Yesuusakko, “Godaw, attanay guutha asa xalaalee?” yaagidi oychchis. Yesuusi enttako,
“Si7ite, xuuntha wulaara gelanaw baaxetite. Daroti gelanaw koyoosona shin enttaw hanenna.
Keethaaway denddidi wulaa gorddidaappe guye ‘Nuus dooyarkii’ yaagishe karen eqqidi xeessi oykkeeta. Shin I, ‘Hintte ooneekkonne awuppe yidaakko ta erikke’ gidi zaarana.
He wode hintte, ‘Neera wolla mida, uyida, nu dabaabankka tamaarssadasa’ yaagana.
“I zaaridi, ‘Hintte ooneekkonne awuppe yidaakko erikke. Hinttenoo, geellato taappe haakkite’ yaagana.
Abrahame, Yisaaqa, Yayqoobanne nabeta ubbaa Xoossaa kawotethan be7ana, shin hintte karen wodhdhidi attiyaa wode hinttew yeehonne achche garccethi gidana.
Asay dolohappe, wulohappe, pudehappenne dugehappe yidi Xoossaa kawotethan gibira bolla uttana.
Hessa gisho, ha77i dethan guye gididayssatappe sinthe gidanayssati, sinthe gididayssatappe guye gidanayssati de7oosona” yaagis.
He wode Farisaawetappe issoti issoti yidi, “Heroodisi nena wodhanaw koyaa gisho ha bessafe denddada ba gidosona.
I zaaridi, “Bidi, he workkanaas hekko, ‘Hachchinne wontto tuna ayyaanata kessana, hargganchchota pathana, heedzantho gallasan kuushsha bolla gakkana’ yaagis giite.
Hanoppe attin, nabey Yerusalaameppe karen hayqqanaw bessenna. Hessa gisho, hachchi, wonttonne wontti pee7in he bessaa baanaw denddas.
“Yerusalaame, Yerusalaame, nabeta wodhiyare, neekko kiitettidayssata shuchchan caddiyare, kuttoy ba nayta ba qefiyappe garssan shiishiyada ne nayta ta qesiyappe garssan aappun toho shiishanaw koyadina, shin hintte ixxas gideta.
Ta hinttew odays; hintte keethay kaysattana. Godaa sunthan yeyssi anjjettidayssa hintte gaana gakkanaw tana demmeketa” yaagis.
Issi Sambbaata gallas Yesuusi issi Farisaaweta halaqaa soo kathi maanaw geliya wode asay caddi xeellosona.
He bessan shawuhe harggen waayettiya issi asi iyaw sintha baggara zin77is.
Yesuusi Farisaawetakkonne higge asttamaaretakko, “Sambbaata gallas hargganchcho pasoy wogeyye woga gidennee?” yaagidi oychchis.
Entti si77i gidosona. Yesuusi harggettiya uraa bochchi pathidi moyzis.
“Qassika hinttefe issuwas na7i woykko boori Sambbaata gallas aafon wulliko ellesidi kessonnay oonee?” yaagidi oychchis.
Entti issibaakka zaaranaw dandda7ibookkona.
Yesuusi imatuwas xeegettidayssati bonchcho bessi doorishin be7idi, ha leemisuwa odis:
“Issi asi nena yaagano xeegikko bonchcho bessan uttofa. Neeppe aadhdhi bonchchettiya asi xeegettanaw dandda7ees.
Hinttena nam77atakka xeegidayssi yidi, ‘Ne bessaa ha imathaas yedda’ yaagiya wode neeni yeellatashe ziqqa bessi wodhdhaasa.
Gidoshin, ne xeegettida wode koyrottada ziqqa bessi be7ada utta. Xeegoyssi yidi, ‘Ta laggiyaw, ha bonchcho bessan utta’ yaagana. He wode neera issife xeegettida asa ubbaa sinthan ne bonchchettana.
Bana dhoqqu dhoqqu oothiya ubbay kawuyana; bana ziqqi ziqqi oothiya ubbay dhoqqu dhoqqu gaana.”
Qassi Yesuusi iya mokkida keethaa aawakko, “Quma woykko kaho imato xeegiya wode neeni kushe zaaro xeegonna mela ne laggeta woykko ne ishata woykko ne dabbota woykko ne dure shoorota imato xeegoppa.
Gidoshin, ne imato giigisida wode manqota, wobbeta, gunddatanne qooqeta xeega; neeni anjjettana.
Hayssati kushe zaaranaw dandda7onna gisho kushe zaaroy geeshshata denddo gallasan new simmana” yaagis.
Yesuusara wolla imato bolla uttoyssata giddofe issoy hessa si7idi, “Xoossaa kawotethan imato bolla utteyssi anjjettidayssa” yaagis.
Yesuusi, “Issi asi gita imato giigisidi daro asata xeegis.
Imatoy mokettiya saatey gakkiya wode xeegettida imathata, ‘Hekko ubbabay giigis, haa yiite’ yaagidi xeeganaada ba aylliya kiittis.
“Shin ubbayka bantta gaaso gaaso medhdhidosona. Issoy, ‘Ha77i buroo gade shammida gisho bada be7anaw koshshees hayyana tana aggarkii yaaga’ yaagis.
Hankkoy, ‘Ichchashu waatha boori shammas enttana waaxa be7ana gisho hayyana tana lanccofa’ yaagis.
Qassi haray, ‘Taani buroo meddan de7iya gisho yaanaw dandda7ikke’ yaagis.
“Aylley simmi yidi he ubbaa ba godaas odis. He wode yaagano aaway hanqettidi aylliyako, ‘Ellesada kataman de7iya wogga ogetanne daggalata bada, manqota, wobbeta, qooqetanne gunddata haa eha’ yaagis.
“Aylley, ‘Ta godaw, ne kiittidayssi ubbay polettis, shin ha77ika bessi de7ees’ yaagis.
“Goday aylliyako, ‘Horogata bollanne, gade giddo ogeta keya, ta keethay kumana gakkanaw demmida ubbaa yaana mela ootha.
Ta hinttew odays; imatotidayssatappe oonikka ta gibiraappe moonnayssa erite’ gis” yaagis.
Daro asay iyara wolla bishin Yesuusi enttako guye simmidi,
“Taakko yaa ubbay ba aawanne ba aayiw, ba machchiwunne ba nayta, ba ishatanne ba michcheta, hari attoshin ba de7uwa ixxonnay ta tamaare gidanaw dandda7enna.
Ba masqaliya tookkidi tana kaallonnay ta tamaare gidanaw dandda7enna.
“Hinttefe issi asi shuchcha keethi keexanaw koykko, keethaa keexidi ongganaw ay mela miishe koshshiyako koyrottidi eranaw qoppi be7onnay oonee?
Hessa gidonna ixxiko, ha uray baaso shuchchaa hiixin qusttethi xoonikko,
be7iya ubbay, ‘Ha uray gimbbethi oykkin qusttanaw iya xoonis’ yaagidi boroosona.
“Woykko issi kawoy hara kawora olettanaw denddishe laatamu mukulu olanchchota ekki yaa kawuwara tammu mukulu olanchchotara eqettanaw dandda7anayssanne dandda7onayssa uttidi zorettonnay oonee?
Eqettanaw dandda7ettonaba gidikko, he hara kawuwara haahon de7ishin giiganaw koyrottidi cima yeddidi oychchees.
Hessadakka, hinttefe oonikka baw de7iyaba ubbaa aggonna ixxiko ta tamaare gidanaw dandda7enna.
“Maxiney lo77o, shin maxiney ba mal77uwa aggiko, waanidi maxine geetettanaw dandda7ii?
Biittatethaaskka araddatethaaskka maaddonabaa gidiya gisho wora yegettees. Hiza, si7iya haythi de7iya asi si7o” yaagis.
Issi gallas qaraxa qanxeyssatinne nagaranchchoti Yesuusa timirttiya si7anaw iya yuushuwan shiiqidosona.
Shin Farisaawetinne higge asttamaareti, “Hayssi uray nagaranchchota shiishidi ekkees, enttara issife mees” yaagidi zuuzummidosona.
Yesuusi yaagidi hayssa leemiso enttaw odis:
“Hintte giddofe issuwas xeetu dorssati de7iyabaa gidikko enttafe issoy dhayikko uddufun tammanne uddufunata bazzon aggidi dhayoyssa demmana gakkanaw koyonnay oonee?
Demmida wode ufayttidi ba gannan tookkidi,
ba soo simmees. Ba laggettanne shoorota issife xeegidi, ‘Dhayida ta dorssaa demmas, taara issife ufayttite’ yaagees.
Hessadakka, maaroti koshshonna uddufun tammanne uddufun xillotappe aathidi maarotan geliya issi nagaranchchuwa gaason salon gita ufayssi gidees.
“Woykko tammu biri de7iya issi maccasiya tammaafe issiya dhayikko demmana gakkanaw xomppe oythada keethaa pittada mintha koyonnara oonee?
Demmida wode ba laggettanne ba shoorota xeegada ‘Dhayida ta issi bira demmida gisho taara ufayttite’ yaagawusu.
Si7ite, hessa mela issi maarotethan geliya nagaranchchuwan Xoossaa kiitanchchota sinthan ufayssi gidees” yaagis.
Zaaridi Yesuusi, “Issi uraas nam77u nayti de7oosona.
Enttafe kaalo na7ay ba aawakko, ‘Ta aawaw, ne shaluwappe ta gishuwa taw imma’ yaagis. Aaway ba shaluwa ba naytas shaakkis.
Guutha gallasappe guye kaalo na7ay ba gishuwa ubbaa qachchi ekkidi haaho biitta bis. Yan alttacan shaluwa toochchidi onggis.
I baw de7iyaba ubbaa wurssidaappe guye he biitta ubban mino koshi keyin metootis.
Hessa gisho, he biittaa asaappe issuwa soo gaata gelis. Uray iya guduntho heemmana mela ba moothaa yeddis.
Gudunthoti miya harquwafe maanaw amottis, shin iyokka iyaw immiya asi benttibeenna.
Wozani simmin, ‘Aappun ta aawa aylletas kathi wora wodhdhin ta hayssan koshara hayqqanaw gakkadina?’
Denddada ta aawakko bada, ‘Ta aawaw, salon Xoossaa, sa7an nena qohas.
Hizappe ne na7a geetettada xeegettanaw taw bessonna gisho ne son de7iya aylletappe issuwada tana payda’ yaagana” yaagis.
Hessa gisho, denddidi ba aawakko bis. “Hanoshin, I buroo haahon de7ishin aaway qadhettidi, iyaakko woxxi bidi idimmidi yeeris.
Na7aykka, ‘Ta aawaw salon Xoossaa, sa7an nena ta qohas. Hizappe ne na7a geetettada xeegettanaw bessike’ yaagis.
“Iya aaway aylleta xeegidi, ‘Ellesidi ubbaafe lo77o gidida ma7o ehidi iya mayzite; iya biradhdhen sagaayo, iya tohuwan caamma aathite.
Modhdho gatarmentho ehidi shukkite, moos, ufayttoos.
Ta na7ay hayssi hayqqis, shin ha77i paxis; dhays, shin benttis’ yaagis. Hessafe guye, ufayetethi oykkidosona.
“He wode bayra na7ay goshsha gaden de7ees. Yaappe yishe soo matishin yethinne gufa girssi si7is.
I, aylletappe issuwa xeegidi haniyabay aybeekko eranaw oychchis.
Aylley, ‘Ne ishay saro yida gisho ne aaway modhdho gatarmentho iyaw shukkis’ yaagis.
“Bayra ishay yilotidi soo gelanawukka koyibeenna. Aaway kare keyidi soo gelana mela iya woossis.
Shin I ba aawakko, ‘Hekko, hayssa mela laythi ta new aylletada ne kiitaappe issuwaka pacisonna new kiitettin ta ta laggetara ufayttana mela hari attoshin issi laaqa deeshe immabaakka.
Hanoshin, hayssi ne na7ay ne shaluwa laymatara doomisidi yin modhdho gatarmentho shukkadasa’ ” yaagis.
“Aawaykka, ‘Ta na7aw, neeni ubba wode taara de7aasa, tabay ubbay neessa.
Hayssi ne ishay hayqqis, shin paxis; dhays, shin benttis. Hessa gisho, daro ufayttanaw bessees’ yaagana” yaagis.
Yesuusi ba tamaaretakko, “Issi dure uraas iyappe garssara issi shuumay de7ees. He shuumay ba godaa shaluwa toochchees yaagiya worey keethaawa gakkis.
Keethaaway shuumaa xeegisidi, ‘Taani woygiyabaa si7adinaa? Hizappe neeni ta keethas shuuma gidada oothanaw dandda7onna gisho ta shaluwa taw sheedhdha’ yaagis.
“He shuumaykka ba wozanan hayssada yaagidi qoppis. ‘Ta goday tana shuumatethaafe wothana hanees, goya aqanaw wolqqi baawa, woossa maanaw yeellayees; yaatin ta waano?
Shuumatethaafe ta wodhdhiya wode asay tana mokkana mela oothanabaa ta erays’ yaagis.
“Hessa gisho, iya godaa acoy de7iya asaa issuwa issuwa xeegi ehidi koyro uraakko, ‘Ne bolla ta godaa acoy ay meli de7ii?’ yaagidi oychchis.
“I, ‘Laatamu barmeele zayte acoy de7ees’ yaagis. “Shuumay, ‘Wule warqattiya he7e, ellesada, tammu barmeele zayte acoy de7ees gada xaafa’ yaagis.
“Hessafe kaallidi nam77anthuwako, ‘New aappuni de7ii?’ yaagis. “I, ‘370 kunttaale gistte acoy de7ees’ yaagis. “Shuumay, ‘Ne wule warqattiya he7e, ellesada, 296 kunttaale yaagada xaafa’ yaagis.
Keethaaway ammanettiboonna shuumaa iya bilaamatethaas nashshis. Ha alamiya nayti ase oythan poo7o naytappe aadhdhida wozanaamata.
“Hessa gisho, ta hinttew odays; ha alamiya miishey wuriya wode merinaa keethan mokettana mela ha miishiyara hinttew laggeta shammite.
Ubbaafe guuthaban ammanettiday daroban ammanettidayssa gidees. Qassi ubbaafe guuthaban ammanettonnayssi daroban ammanettenna.
Hiza, ha alamiya miishen hintte ammanettonna ixxiko tuma miishe hinttew ooni hadara immanee?
Hintte hara asa miishen ammanettonna ixxiko, hintte buzo miishe hinttew ooni immanee?
“Issi aylley nam77u godatas haarettanaw dandda7enna. Issuwa ixxiko hankkuwa dosees woykko issuwako shiiqikko hankkuwa kadhees. Hessadakka, hintte Xoossasinne miishes haarettanaw dandda7ekketa.”
Miishe dosiya Farisaaweti hessa si7ida wode Yesuusa qelqisidosona.
I, “Hinttee hinttena asa sinthan xilliseeta, shin Xoossay hintte wozanaa erees. Asa sinthan bonchchettidayssi Xoossaa sinthan borettidayssa.
“Muse higgeynne nabeta kiitay Yohaannisa gakkanaw hinttew odettishe gam77is. Hessafe guye, Xoossaa kawotethaa Wonggelay sabbakettishe gam77is. Asi ubbay yaa gelanaw dafettees.
Gidoshin, higgiyafe issi laafa pidaaley attanaappe saloynne sa7ay aadhdheyssi kawuyees.
“Ba machchiw yeddidi haraa ekkiya ubbay laammees. Ba azinaappe anjjettidaaro ekkeysika laammees” yaagis.
“Al77onne alleeqo afila ma77iya, sa7i injjetin gallas gallas ufayssan de7iya issi dure asi de7ees.
Hari qassi asatethay kumethi madunxida issi Alaazara geetettiya manqoy he dure uraa karen yegetidi attidayssi de7ees.
Koshappe denddoyssan dure uraa gaytappe wodhdhiya tiifiya maanaw amottishe de7ees. Hari attoshin, kanati yidi iya madunthaa laaccosona.
“He manqoy hayqqis; kiitanchchoti iya Abrahame ki7uwa efidosona. Qassi dure uraykka hayqqidi moogettis.
Si7oolen un77ettidi de7ishe dhoqqu gidi haahon Abrahamenne iya ki7on de7iya Alaazara be7is.
I, ‘Aawaw Abrahame, taw qadhettarkii; ha laco taman un77ettada de7iya gisho Alaazari ba biradhdhiya haathan yeddidi ta inxarssaa laakothana mela hayyana iya yeddarkki’ yaagidi waassis.
“Shin Abrahamey iyaakko, ‘Ta na7aw, ne sa7an de7iya wode lo77obaata ekkidayssa, qassi Alaazari iitabata ekkidayssa akeeka. Shin ha77i I hayssan ufayttees, qassi neeni waayettashe de7aasa’ yaagis.
Ha ubbaafe aadhdhidi, ‘Haappe hintteko, hinippe haa nuukko aadhdhanaw koyeyssati pinnonna mela nuusinne hinttes giddon gita aafoy de7ees’ yaagis.
“Dure uray, ‘Aawaw, yaakko Alaazara ta aawa soo kiittana mela ta nena woossays.
Taw ichchashu ishati de7idosona, enttika ha waaye bessaa yoonna mela enttaw bidi markkatto’ yaagis.
“Shin Abrahamey, ‘Enttaw Museranne nabetara de7oosona; entti odiyabaa si7ona’ yaagis.
“Dure uray, ‘Aawaw Abrahame, hessatho gidenna; issi asi hayqoppe denddidi biikko entti maarotan gelana’ yaagis.
“Abrahamey, ‘Musenne nabeta si7onna ixxiko, hari attoshin hayqoppe issi asi denddi odikkoka ammanokkona’ yaagis.”
Yesuusi ba tamaaretakko, “Ase dhubethidi nagaran gelssiyabay yoonna aggenna. Gidoshin, nagaran gelana mela oothiya uraa ayye” yaagis.
He uray kaalotappe issuwa balethanaappe woxa ba qoodhen qachchidi abban wulliko iyaw lo77o.
Hessa gisho naagettite. “Ne ishay nagara oothiko hanqetta; qiirottidi maarotethan simmiko, iyaw atto yaaga.
Issi gallasan laappun toho qohidi, laappun toho, ‘Taani ta balaa eras tana maara’ yaagidi neekko yiikko iyaw atto ga.”
Hawaareti Godaakko, “Ammano nuus gujjarkkii” yaagidosona.
Goday, “Gaashe ayfe mela ammanoy hinttew de7ikko ‘Hayssa wolaa shodettada abbaa giddon toketta’ yaagikko hinttew kiitettana” yaagis.
Gujjidikka Yesuusi, “Hintte giddofe issuwas goshshanchchoy woykko dorsse heemmiya aylley de7ikko ooso gadeppe woykko wudeppe soo simmiya wode ‘Elle haayada kathi maanaw utta’ yaagey de7ii?
Deenna, ‘Taw kaho giigisa; taani mada, uyada aggana gakkanaw eqqada muza. Hessafe guye, neeni qassi maasanne uyaasa’ yaagenneyye?
Hiza, goday, aylley kiitaa polida gisho anjjiyye?
Hessa gisho, hintteka kiitettoyssa ubbaa polida wode ‘Nu pathonna aylleta; oothanaw bessiya oosuwa polida’ yaagite” yaagis.
Yesuusi Yerusalaame bishe Samaarisinne Galiila biittaas giddora kanthidi aadhdhis.
Issi gutaa geliya wode baro harggen oykettida tammu asati iya demmidosona. Enttika haahon eqqidi,
“Godaa Yesuusa, nuus qadhettarkii” yaagidi waassidosona.
I entta be7ida wode “Bidi hinttenatethaa Ayhude kahine bessite” yaagis. Entti ogiya bolla bishe paxidosona.
Enttafe issoy ba paxuwa be7ida wode dhoqqu gida qaalan Xoossaa bonchchishe Yesuusakko simmis.
I Samaare biitta asi, shin Yesuusa tohuwa bolla gufannidi iya galatis.
Yesuusi, “Paxiday tammu asata gidokkonaayye? Yaatin, uddufunati aw bidonaa?
Ha allaga uraappe attin hari simmidi Xoossaa galatey deenna guusseyye?” yaagidi oychchis.
Uraakko, “Ne ammanoy nena pathis; denddada ba” yaagis.
Farisaaweti, “Xoossaa kawotethay awude yaanee?” gidi Yesuusa oychchidosona. I, “Xoossaa kawotethay benttiya mallan yeenna.
Qassika iyo, ‘Hannina woykko hinina yaaganaw dandda7enna. Ays giikko, Xoossaa kawotethay hintte giddon de7ees’ ” yaagidi zaaris.
Yesuusi ba tamaaretakko, “Asa Na7aa gallasatappe issuwa be7anaw hintte amottiya wodey yaana, shin hintte be7ekketa.
Asay, ‘I yan de7ees’ woykko, ‘Hayssan de7ees’ yaagana, shin enttana kaallidi booppite.
Wol77anthi wol77ammidi saluwa gaxappe gaxa poo7isiya mela Asa Na7aa yuussaa gallasay hessada hanana.
Shin hessi hananaappe sinthe Asa Na7ay daro waayanawunne ha yeletethan ixettanaw bessees.
Nohe wode hanidayssa mela Asa Na7aa wodiyankka hessada hanana.
Nohey Markkabiyan gelida qammaa gakkanaw asay mishenne uyishe, ekkishenne gelishe de7ishin dhayo haathay yidi ubbaa dhayssis.
Looxe laythankka hessatho hanis. Asay mishenne uyishe, shammishenne bayzishe, tokkishenne keexishe, gam77idosona.
Looxey Soodomeppe keyida gallas diinne geetettiya xuuggiyabay saloppe bukkidi ubbaa dhayssis.
Asa Na7ay qoncciya wodekka hessada hanana.
“He gallasan oonikka karen de7ey keethaa giddon de7iyabaa ekkanaw soo geloppo. Hessadakka, gaden de7iya asi aykkoskka soo simmofo.
Looxe machchiw akeekite;
ba shemppiw ashshanaw koyaa asi oonikka dhayssana; ba shemppiw aathi immiya oonikka I ashshana.
Ta hinttew odays; he gallasan nam77u asati issi arssan zin77ana. Issoy ekettana, hankkoy attana.
Nam77u maccasati wolla gaaccishin issiya ekettana, hankkiya attana.
Nam77u asati wolla gaden goyeyssatappe issoy ekettana, hankkoy attana” yaagis.
Entti, “Godaw aw ekettanee?” yaagidi oychchidosona. I, “Bawuti de7iya bessan ankkoti shiiqoosona” yaagis.
Yesuusi ba tamaareta azalonna ubba wode woossana mela tamaarssanaw koyidi yaagidi leemiso odis:
“Issi kataman Xoossaas yashettonna asaskka yeellatonna issi daynni de7ees
He kataman issi am77iya da7awusu. Iyakka, ‘Tawunne ta morkkiyas giddon de7iya mootuwa pirdda’ yaagada ubba wode he daynnaako simerettawusu.
Daynnay guutha wodes I odaa si7onna ixxis, shin guyeppe ba wozanan, ‘Taani Xoossaas yayyonna, asas yeellatonna ixxikokka,
ha am77iya tana waaysiya gisho iw pirddana; yaatonna ixxiko ubba wode yada tana salethana’ yaagidi qoppis” yaagis.
Godaykka, “Geella daynnay gidayssa si7ideta;
Xoossay qammanne gallas iyaakko waassiya ba dooridayssatas pirddeneyye? Enttana maaddanaw gam77iyye?
Ta hinttew odeyssa si7ite, ellesidi pirddana. Gidoshin, Asa Na7ay yaa wode sa7a bolla ammano demmanddeshsha?” yaagis.
Qassi zaaridi, Yesuusi, banttana xillo asada oothidi ceeqetteyssatasinne harata kadheyssatas hayssada yaagidi leemiso odis:
“Nam77u asati woossanaw Xoossa Keethi bidosona. Issoy Farisaawe hankkoy qassi qaraxa qanxisiya asi.
Farisaawey eqqidi baw woossishe, ‘Xoossaw taani harata mela bonqanchcho, geellanne laymatiya asi, aadhdhida qassi ha qaraxa qanxisiya uraa mela gidonna gisho nena galatays.
Saaminttafe nam77u toho xoomays, ta demmiyaba ubbaafe asiraata kessays’ yaagis.
“Shin qaraxa qanxiseyssi qassi haahon eqqidi hari attoshin salo dhoqqu gidi xeellanawukka yayyidi ba tiraa iccishe ‘Xoossaw, tana nagaranchchuwa maararkii’ gidi woossis.
Ta hinttew odeyssa si7ite; Farisaawiyappe hayssi qaraxa qanxiseyssi Xoossaa sinthan xillo gididi ba soo simmis. Ays giikko, bana dhoqqu dhoqqu oothiya asi kawuyana, bana kawushshiya asi dhoqqu dhoqqu gaana” yaagis.
Yesuusi yooga nayta bolla ba kushiya wothidi anjjana mela asay iyaakko ehoosona. Yesuusa tamaareti hessa be7idi ays Yesuusakko eheeti yaagidi kaccidosona.
Shin Yesuusi nayta baakko xeegidi, “Yooga nayti taakko yaanayssa diggofite; yo giite. Ays giikko, Xoossaa kawotethay enttada hanidayssatassa.
Taani hinttew tuma odays; Xoossaa kawotethaa yooga naytatho ekkonnay oonikka yaa gelenna” yaagis.
Ayhude halaqatappe issoy, “Keeha asttamaariyaw, merinaa de7uwa demmanaw ay ootho?” yaagidi oychchis.
Yesuusi iyaakko, “Ays tana keehaw yaagada xeegay? Issi Xoossaafe attin hari keehi baawa.
Laammofa, wodhoppa, kaysotoppa, worddo markkattofa, ne aawanne ne aayiw bonchcha yaagiya kiitaa eray” yaagidi oychchis.
Uraykka, “Hessata ubbaa taani na7atethafe doomada naagashe gam77as” yaagis.
Yesuusi hessa si7ida wode “Hiza, new issibay paccees; new de7iyaba ubbaa bayzada manqotas imma; salon nena shaloy naagees. Yaata simmada tana kaalla” yaagis.
Shin uray hessa si7ida wode iyaw daro shaloy de7iya gisho daro qiirottis.
Yesuusi uraa be7idi, “Dure asas Xoossaa kawotethaa geloy waanidi un77anddeshsha?
Durey Xoossaa kawotethaa gelanayssafe gimaley narppe luhora kantheyssi kawuyees” yaagis.
Hessa si7ida asay, “Hessa gidikko ooni attanee?” yaagidosona.
Yesuusi, “Asas dandda7ettonabay Xoossaas dandda7ettees” yaagis.
Phexiroosi, “Hekko nuuni nubaa ubbaa aggidi nena kaallida” yaagis.
“Yesuusi tuma ta hinttew odays; Xoossaa kawotethaas gidi ba keethaa woykko ba machchiw woykko ba ishata woykko ba aawanne ba aayiw woykko ba nayta aggiday;
ha wodiyan dakko daro, yaana alamiyan merinaa de7uwa ekkonnay oonikka baawa” yaagis.
Yesuusi tammanne nam77ata baakko xeegidi, “Ane Yerusalaame boos, nabeti Asa Na7aabaa xaafidaba ubbay yan polettana.
I Ayhude gidonna asaas aadhdhidi imettana. Entti iya toochchana, cayananne iya bolla cuttana.
Iya garaafidaappe guye wodhana, shin heedzantho gallasan I hayqoppe denddana” yaagis.
Shin iya tamaareti hessa ubbaafe issibaakka akeekibookkona. Iya xuuray enttaw qosettida gisho I woygidaakko eribookkona.
Yesuusi Iyaarkko matattiya wode issi qooqe uray oge gaxan uttidi woossees.
Qooqe uray asay he bessaara aadhdhishin si7idi, “I aybe?” gidi oychchis.
Entti, “Naazirete Yesuusi hayssara aadhdhees” yaagidosona.
I, “Dawite na7aw, Yesuusa, tana maararkii” yaagidi waassis.
Sinthe sinthe biya asati, “Si7i ga” gidi hanqettidosona. Shin I, “Dawite na7aw, tana maara” yaagidi darssi waassis.
Yesuusi eqqidi uraa baakko ehana mela kiittis. Uraykka, iyaakko shiiqin,
“Ta new ay oothana mela koyay?” yaagidi oychchis. Qooqey, “Godaw ta xeellanaw koyays” yaagis.
Yesuusi, “Xeella, ne ammanoy nena pathis” yaagis.
Uray sohuwara xeelli aggis. Xoossaa bonchchishe Yesuusa kaallis. Asa ubbay hessa be7idi Xoossaa galatidosona.
Yesuusi Iyaarkko gelidi aadhdhees.
Yan Zakkiyoosa geetettiya qaraxa qanxiseyssata halaqay de7ees. I daro dure.
I Yesuusi ooneekko be7anaw koyis. I qanthi gidiya gisho asaa darotethaafe denddoyssan Yesuusa be7anaw dandda7ibeenna.
Yesuusa be7anaw koyidi I biya ogiyas sinthe woxxi bidi issi boobba mitha bolla keyis.
Yesuusi he bessaa gakkishe dhoqqu gidi be7idi, “Zakkiyoosa, hachchi ta ne son pee7anaw bessiya gisho elle wodhdha” yaagis.
I ellesi wodhdhidi ufayssan Yesuusa mokkis.
He bessan de7iya asaa ubbay hessa be7idi, “Nagaranchchuwa soo gelidi mokettanw hanees” yaagidi zuuzummidosona.
Gidoshin, Zakkiyoosi eqqidi Godaakko, “Godaw, hekko taw de7iya shalo ubbaafe baggaa manqotas immana. Asappe aybaakka worddon balethada ekkidabaa gidikko oyddu kushe zaarana” yaagis.
Yesuusi qassi, “Ha uray Abrahame na7a gidida gisho hachchi atotethay ha soo yis.
Asa Na7ay yiday dhayidayssa koyanasaanne ashshanaassa” yaagis.
Asay hessa si7iya wode Yesuusi Yerusalaame matattida gishonne Xoossaa kawotethay ha77i matara qonccana daanida gisho enttaw leemiso odis.
Hessa gisho, Yesuusi, “Issi gita asi de7eyssi baw kawotethi ekkidi yaanaw hara biitta bis.
Iyaw oothiya aylletappe tammata xeegidi issuwas issuwas tammu minaane immidi ‘Ta simmada yaana gakkanaw ha miishiyara zal77ite’ yaagis.
“He biittaa asay iya ixxiya gisho ha uray nu bolla kawotana mela nu koyokko yaagidi ase iya guyera kiittidosona.
“Gidoshin, he uray kawo gididi ba biittaa simmis. He tammu aylleti I immida miishiyan ay mela zal77idi wodhisidaakko eranaw koyidi enttana xeegisis.
“Koyroyssi yidi, ‘Godaw, ne taw immida miishey haraa tamma wodhdhis’ yaagis.
“Iya Goday, ‘Neno ammanettida aylliyaw lo77o oothadasa. Neeni guuthaban ammanettida gisho new tammu katamata bolla maata immas’ yaagis.
“Nam77anthoyka yidi, ‘Godaw, ne taw immida miishey haraa ichchasha wodhdhis’ yaagis.
“Goday iyaakko, ‘Newukka qassi ichchashu katamata bolla maata immas’ yaagis.
“Hekko heedzanthoy yidi, ‘Godaw, ta curqqan xaaxada naagida ne miishiya hannashu.
Ays giikko, neeni nebaa gidonnabaa ekkeyssanne ne zeronnabaa buucciya iita asi gidiya gisho new yayyas’ yaagis.
“Iya goday zaaridi, ‘Neno iita aylliyaw ne doonatho ta nena pirddana. Ta wothonnabaa ekkeyssanne zeronnabaa buucciya asi gideyssa ne erikko,
ta yada ta miishiya wodhera ekkana mela zal77iya asaas ays immabiikkii?’
“Iya goday he bessan eqqidayssatakko, ‘Iyara de7iya miishiya ekkidi tamma wodhisidayssas immite’ yaagis.
“Entti, ‘Godaw, iyaw kasekka tammu minaaney de7ees’ yaagidosona.
“Goday, ta hinttew odays; ‘De7iya ubbaas hari guzhettana, shin baynnayssafe haray atto iyaw de7iyarakka ekettana.
Gidoshin, ta entta bolla kawotonna mela koyidayssata he ta morkketa ha ta sinthe ehidi goyrite’ gis” yaagis.
Yesuusi hessa odidayssafe guye enttafe sinthe aadhdhi hamuttidi Yerusalaame bis.
Shamaho Deriya bolla de7iya Beetefaagenne Bitaaniya matattida wode ba tamaaretappe nam77ata yaagidi kiittis:
“Hintte sinthan de7iya gutaa biite, hintte yaa gakkiya wode oonikka toggonna qashettidi de7iya hare mari demmana. Iya billidi haa ekki yiite.
Oonikka, ‘Ays billeeti?’ gidi oychchiko, ‘Goday iya koyees’ yaagite” yaagis.
Kiitettidayssati bidi I gidayssada hanin be7idosona.
Entti hare maraa billishin godati be7idi, “Hare maraa ays billeeti?” yaagidosona.
Entti zaaridi, “Goday iya koyees” yaagidosona.
Yaappe hare maraa Yesuusakko ehidosona. Bantta ma7uwa hare maraa zokkon yeggidi Yesuusa hare maraa bolla utisidosona.
Asaykka I biya ogiya bolla bantta ma7uwa hiixidosona.
Shamaho Deriya dugethaa wodhisiya ogiyakko matiya wode taybon keehi daro asay entti be7ida malaalisiyaban ufayttidi bantta qaala dhoqqu oothidi,
“Godaa sunthan yaa kawoy anjjettidayssa saluwan saroy ubbaafe dhoqqa saluwan bonchchoy Xoossaas gido.” yaagidi Xoossaa galatidosona.
Asaa giddofe issi issi Farisaaweti Yesuusakko, “Asttamaariyaw, ne tamaareta hayzite gada hanqetta” yaagidosona.
I enttako, “Entti si77i giikko shuchchati waassana” yaagis.
Yesuusi Yerusalaame matishe katamaa be7idi iyaw yeekkis.
“New saro gidanayssa hachchi ne eridabaa gidiyakkoshin, ha77i ne ayfiyaappe geemmis.
Ne morkketi ne yuushuwa diridi dumma dumma ogiyara nena teqqidi un77ethiya wodey yaana.
Nenanne ne dirssaa garssan de7iya ne nayta dhayssana. Issi issi shuchchu denthidi laallana, ays giikko Xoossay nena ashshanaw yaa wodiya erabaakka” yaagidi iw yeekkis.
Hessafe guye, Yesuusi Xoossa Keethi gelidi zal77eyssata yaappe goodis.
Qassi, “ ‘Ta keethay Xoossaa woossiya keethi gidana’ gidi xaafettis, shin hintte ta keethaa panggata gonggolo oothideta” yaagis.
Gallas gallas Xoossa Keethan tamaarssees. Kahineta halaqati, higge asttamaaretinne deriya cimati iya wodhanaw oge koyoosona.
Gidoshin, asa ubbay iya timirttiya bantta wozana yeggidi si7iya gisho enttaw oothanabay dhays.
Issi gallas Yesuusi Xoossa Keethan asaa tamaarssishininne Wonggelaa markkattishin, kahine halaqati, higge asttamaaretinne deriya cimati issife iyaakko yidi,
“Neeni hayssata aybi maatan oothiyako nuus oda. Ha maata new immiday oonee?” yaagidi oychchidosona.
I enttako, “Takka hinttena issibaa oychchana, ane taw zaarite.
Xammaqiya Yohaannisa xinqqatey Xoossafeyye asappe?” yaagis.
Entti woli giddon yaagidi zorettidosona: “Xoossafe giikko yaatin, ays ammanibeekketii?” yaagana.
“Asappe giikko, asa ubbay Yohaannisi nabe gideyssa ammaniyaa gisho nuna shuchchan caddana.”
Yaaniya gisho, “Awuppeeko nu erokko” yaagidi zaaridosona.
Yesuusi zaaridi, “Hiza, takka ay maatan hayssata oothiyako hinttew odikke” yaagis.
Hessafe guye, Yesuusi yaagidi ha leemisuwa asaas odis: “Issi asi woyne tokkis. Goshshanchchotas kera immidi daro wode gam77idi yaanaw hara biitta bis.
Woyne ayfiyaa maxiya wodey gakkin woyniya ayfiyaappe iyaw yeddana mela goshshanchchotakko ba aylliya kiittis. Shin goshshanchchoti he aylliya oykkidi wadhdhidi mela kushe yeddidosona.
Kaallidikka hara aylliya kiittis. Qassi goshshanchchoti iya wadhdhidi, kawushshidi mela kushe yeddidosona.
Ha77ika zaaridi heedzantho aylliya kiittis. Goshshanchchoti iyakka madunxisidi woyniya giddofe gaxa kessidi yeggidosona.
“Woyniya goday, ‘Yaatin ta ay ootho? Ane qassi ta dosiya ta na7aa yeddana; ooni eri entti iya bonchchonna aggokona’ yaagis.
“Shin goshshanchchoti uraa na7aa be7ida wode ‘Hayssi iya laatteyssa, haa yiite iya wodhana, yaatikko laatay nuus gidana’ yaagidi zorettidosona.
Woyniya giddofe gaxa kessidi wodhidosona. “Yaatin, woyniya goday he asata waatanee?
Yidi he goshshanchchota dhayssana, woyniya bessaa hara asatas immana. Asay hessa si7ida wode ‘Shinchchalle hessa melabaa ehoppo’ yaagidosona.
Yesuusi entta caddi xeellidi, “Yaatin ‘Gimbbe keexiya asati borida shuchchay, keethaas malanne minotethi immiya ubbaafe aadhdhiya shuchchi gidis’ geetettidi xaafettidayssa birshshethay aybe?
He shuchchaa bolla kunddiya ubbay qoxettana, shuchchay iya bolla wodhdhiya ubbay liiqana” yaagis.
Higge asttamaaretinne kahine halaqati ha leemisoy odettiday entta bolla gideyssa eridi he wode iya oykkanaw koyidosona, shin asaas babbidosona.
Hessa gisho, Yesuusa deriya haariya Roome kawuwa maatas aathi immanaw koyidi iya doonappe bala qaala naagoosona. Hessa polisanaw xillo daanidi cimmiya asata iyaakko kiittidosona.
Kiitettidi bida asati, “Asttamaariyaw, neeni odeysinne tamaarsseyssi likke gideyssa, qassi Xoossaa ogiya tumatethan tamaarsseyssanne oonakka shaakkonnayssa nu eroos.
Hanoshin, Roome kawuwas giira giiranaw bessi bessennee?” yaagidi iya oychchidosona.
Shin I entta wozanaa iitatethaa erida gisho
“Ane tana issi santime bessite, Iya bolla de7iya misileynne sunthay ooddebaye?” yaagis. Entti zaaridi, “Roome Kawuwa Qeesareyssa” yaagidosona.
I zaaridi, “Yaatikko, Qeesareyssa Qeesares, Xoossayssa Xoossaas immite” yaagis.
Hessa gisho, I zaarida zaaruwan asaa sinthan bala demmanaw dandda7ibookkona. Iya zaaruwan malaalettidi si77i gidosona.
Hayqoppe denddoy baawa yaagiya Saduqaawetappe issoti issoti Yesuusakko yidi,
“Asttamaariyaw, issi asi machcho ekkidi na7a yelonna hayqqiko, iya ishay he maccasiw ekkidi nayta yelidi ba ishaas zerethi ashshana mela Musey xaafis.
Hekko laappun ishati de7oosona. Koyroyssi machcho ekkidi na7a yelonna hayqqis.
Nam77anthoy iyo ekkidi na7a yelonna hayqqis.
Heedzanthoyka hessatho hanis. Laappunati ubbay hessada hanidi iyo ekkidosona, shin na7a yelonna hayqqidosona.
Wurssethan maccasiya hayqqasu.
Hiza, laappun addey iyo ekkida gisho hayqoppe denddiya wode iya oodde machcho gidanee?” yaagidi oychchidosona.
Yesuusi zaaridi, “Asay ha wodiyan ekkoosonanne geloosona.
Shin hayqoppe denddidi yaana alamiyan daanaw besseyssati ekkokonanne gelokkona.
Entti kiitanchcho mela gidiya gisho sinthafe hayqqokona. Hayqoppe denddida gisho entti Xoossaa nayta.
Musey Godaa, ‘Abrahame Godaa, Yisaaqa Godaa, Yayqooba Godaa’ gidi tushiya giddon xuugettiya tama taarikiya xaafidayssan hayqqida asay denddeyssa bessees.
Ubbay iyaw de7on de7eyssata gidiya gisho I de7on de7eyssata Godaappe attin hayqqidayssata Goda gidenna” yaagidi zaaris.
Higge asttamaaretappe issoti issoti, “Asttamaariyaw, lo77obaa odadasa” yaagidosona.
Hessafe guye, hara oysho oychchanaw yayyidosona.
Iyappe kaallidi Yesuusi enttako, “Asay Kiristtoosa waattidi Dawite na7a yaagonaa?
Ays giikko, Dawitey ba huu7en ba maxaafan, ‘Xoossay ta Godaakko “Ta ne morkketa ne tohoy yedhdhiyaso oothana gakkanaw taappe ushachcha baggan utta” gis’ yaagis.
<range>
“Hiza, Dawitey Kiristtoosa, ‘Godaa gidi xeegishe iyaw na7a waanidi gidi?’ ” yaagis.
Derey ubbay si7ishin ba tamaaretakko,
“Adussa ma7o ma77idi yuushshe doseyssatappe, giyan bonchcho sarotho, Ayhude Woosa Keethan bonchcho oyde, mokettiya sonkka bonchcho bessi koyaa higge asttamaaretappe naagettite.
Entti am77eta keethaa kalloyoosona, xillo asi daanidi woosa adussoosona. Entti iita pirdda ekkana” yaagis.
Dure asay Xoossa Keethan muxaata saaxiniyan yeggishin Yesuusi dhoqqu gidi asaa be7is.
Qassi issi manqo am77iya nam77u sikkina yeggishin be7idi,
“Ta hinttew tuma odays; ha manqo am77iya ubbaafe aathada immasu.
Ays giikko, ha asa ubbay banttaw de7iyabaappe immidosona, shin iya ba pacciyaappe, baw de7iya aquwaa ubbaa immasu” yaagis.
Yesuusa tamaaretappe issoti issoti Xoossa Keethay daro lo77iya shuchchaninne asay Xoossaas immida imotan lo77idayssa odettoosona.
Shin Yesuusi, “Ha hintte be7iyabay ubbay laalettonna, shuchchi shuchcha bolla gimbbettida mela attonna wodey yaana” yaagis.
Enttika, “Asttamaariyaw, ha ubbay hananay awude? Qassi hayssi hananayssas malaatay aybee?” yaagidi oychchidosona.
Yesuusi yaagidi enttaw zaaro immis: “Balettonna mela naagettite. Daroti, ‘Taani Kiristtoosa, wodey matattis’ yaagishe ta sunthan yaana, shin hintte entta kaallofite.
Hintte olabaanne asaa geellatethaa si7iya wode dagammofite. Hessi sinthattidi hananayssi attonnabaa gidiya gisho wodiya wurssethay ellesidi yeenna” yaagis.
Kaallidikka, “Derey deriya bolla, kawotethay kawotethaa bolla denddana.
Gita biitta qaaxoy hanana, koshaynne gadoy dumma dumma bessan darana, yashshiyabaynne gita malaatati saloppe qonccana.
Shin ha ubbay hananaappe sinthe ta sunthaa gisho gidi asay hinttena gooddananne oykkana. Ayhude Woosa Keethaninne qasho keethan hinttena yeggana. Kawota sinthenne deriya haareyssata sinthe hinttena efana.
Hessika tabaa hintte enttaw markkattanaw lo77o oge gidana.
Hessa gisho, hintte oyshettiya wode woygidi zaaro immanee gidi hintte wozanan un77ettonna mela akeekite.
Ays giikko, hintte morkketi hinttera eqettanawunne palamanaw dandda7onna doonanne cinccatethi ta hinttew immana.
Hari attoshin, hinttena yelidayssati, hintte ishati, hintte dabbotinne laggeti hinttena aathi immana. Hintte giddofe issota issota wodhana.
Ta sunthaa gisho asa ubbaa sinthan hintte ixettidayssata gidana.
Shin hari attoshin, hintte binaanappe issoykka dhayenna.
Polo dandda7an hintte, hintte shemppuwa ashshana.”
“Yerusalaame katamay wotaaddaren direttidi uttidashin hintte be7ikko iyaw dhayoy matattidayssa erite.
He wode Yihudan de7iya ubbay deriyakko baqato, kataman de7eyssati yaappe keyo, gaxariyan de7eyssati katama geloppo.
Ays giikko, ha xaafettidabay polettana mela hessi Xoossay kushe zaariya wode.
Sa7a bolla gita metoy yaana, hessankka asaa bolla Xoossaa hanqoy yaana. Hessa gisho, qanthatidayssatanne dhantheyssata ayye.
Entti mashshan hayqqana, asa ubbay allaga biitta di7ettana. Ayhude gidonna asaa wodey polettana gakkanaw Yerusalaamey enttanan yedhettidayssa gidana.
“Awan, ageenaninne, xoolinttota bolla malaatati hanidi benttana. Abbaafenne zuliya deshuwappe denddoyssan biittan de7iya asay un77ettananne yarkkana.
Saluwa wolqqati buqettana gisho asay yashshaninne biitta bolla aybi hananddeshsha gidi naagon banttana balettana.
He wode Asa Na7ay wolqqaninne gita bonchchuwan shaarara yishin entti be7ana.
Hintte atotethay matattida gisho ha hanoti poletethi oykkiya wode giigeti eqqite, hintte huu7iya dhoqqu oothidi xeellite” yaagis.
Kaallidikka, hayssada gidi leemiso odis: “Balase mithaanne hara mithata ubbaa be7ite.
Entti aaciya wode torchchey matattidayssa hintte ereeta.
Hessada ha hanoti polettishin hintte be7ikko Xoossaa kawotethay matattidayssa erite.
“Ta hinttew tuma odays; ha ubbay polettana gakkanaw ha yeletethay aadhdhenna.
Saloynne sa7ay aadhdhana, shin ta qaalay aadhdhenna.
“Hiza, dhassi baynna de7on, ushsha daroninne duussabaas un77etethan hintte wozanay oykettonna melanne he qammay akeekonna xiheda hintte bolla gakkonna mela naagettite.
He qammay biitta kumethan de7iya ubbaa bolla gakkana.
Hessa gisho, yaa iitaappe attanawunne Asa Na7a sinthan eqqanaw dandda7ana mela ubba wode minnidi woossite” yaagis.
Gallas gallas Yesuusi Xoossa Keethan tamaarssishe, qamma qamma Shamaho Deriya bolla keyidi aqees.
Asay ubbay iya si7anaw wontta guura iyaakko Xoossaa Keethi yoosona.
He wode ‘Faasikka’ yaagiya Uytha Baaley matis.
Kahine halaqatinne higge asttamaareti asaas yayyida gisho waattidi Yesuusa bantta giddofe dhayssaneekko oge koyoosona.
Xalahey tammanne nam77atappe issuwa gidida Asqoroota Yihuda geetetteyssa gido gelis.
Yihudi kahine halaqatakkonne Xoossa Keetha naageyssata halaqatakko bidi Yesuusa waati aathi immaneekko enttara maqettis.
Enttika hessan ufayttidi miishe immanaw iyara zorettidosona.
Ikka zoretethan giigis. Aathi enttaw immanaw asi baynna injje wode naagishe de7ees.
Hessafe guye, Faasikka dorssay shukettiya Uytha Baaley gakkis.
Yesuusi, “Faasikka kahuwa maana mela bidi nuus giigisite” yaagidi Phexiroosanne Yohaannisa kiittis.
Entti, “Nu awun giigisana mela ne koyay” yaagidi oychchidosona.
I enttako, “Hekko hintte katama gelishin haatha oto tookkida addey hinttera gahettana. I bidi geliya keethaa iya kaallidi gelite.
Keethaawakko asttamaarey, ‘Ta ta tamaaretara wolla Faasikka kahuwa maanaw imatha keethi awunee? yaagis’ giite.
I pooqiya bolla hiixettidi giigidi de7iya dalgga kifile hinttena bessana, yan giigisite” yaagis.
Entti bidi Yesuusi gidayssada hanin demmidosona. Faasikka baale kahuwa yan giigisidosona.
Saateykka gakkida wode Yesuusi hawaaretara wolla kahuwa bolla uttis.
I enttako, “Ta waaye ekkanaappe sinthe ha kahuwa hinttera maanaw daro amottas.
Hiza, si7ite! Xoossaa kawotethan hayssas birshshethay polettana gakkanaw ha kahuwa zaarada miikke” yaagis.
Ushshaa ekkidi galati simmidi, “He7ite hayssa hintte giddon shaakettite.
Si7ite! Xoossaa kawotethay yaana gakkanaw hachchife doomada ha woyne ushshaafe zaarada uyikke” yaagis.
Uythaa ekkidi, galati simmidi, “Hayssi hinttew imettiya ta ashuwa. Hayssa oothishe tana qoppite” yaagidi meenthidi enttaw immis.
Hessadakka, kahuwappe guye ushshaa ekkidi, “Ha ushshay hinttew gukkida ta suuthan gidiya ooratha caaquwa.
Gidoshin, tana aathi immana uraa kushey taara issife gaytaana.
Asa Na7ay iyaw geetettoyssa mela hayqqanaw de7ees, shin iya aathi immiya uraa ayye” yaagis.
Entti bantta giddon, “Hayssa ooni oothanee” gidi woli oychchidosona.
Qassi entta giddon gita gidanay oone giya palami medhettis.
Yesuusi enttako, “Deriya kawoti bantta asaa wolqqan haarosona; bantta deriya bolla godateyssataskka banttana, ‘Lo77o ootheyssata’ yaagidi xeegosona.
Shin hintte giddon hessa mela gidoppo. Hintte giddon bayratey kaaloda hano; kaaletheyssi kaalleyssada hano.
Hanoshin, mokkeyssafenne Moketteyssafe awussi aadhdhi? Moketteyssa gidenneyye? Shin taani hintte giddon mokkeyssa mela.
“Hintteka ta metuwan taappe shaakettonna taara minnidi eqqidayssata.
Hintte ta gaytappe maana mela, uyana melanne araatata bolla uttidi tammanne nam77u Isra7eele sheeshata bolla pirddana mela ta aaway tana shuumidayssada takka hinttena ta kawotethan shuumana” yaagis.
<range>
Kaallidikka Yesuusi, “Simoona, Simoona, Xalahey hinttena gistteda harqqanaw woossis.
Shin taani ne ammanoy dhayonna mela new gaannatas. Nekka simmida wode ne ishata mintha” yaagis.
Simooni, “Godaw, taani neera qashettanawunne hayqqanaw giigettas” yaagis.
Yesuusi Phexiroosakko, “Ta new odays; hachchi kuttoy waassanaappe sinthe ne tana heedzu toho kaddana” yaagis.
Kaallidikka, Yesuusi enttako, “Taani hinttena korojjoy, karxiiteynne caammi baynna kiittida wode hinttew paccidabay de7ii?” yaagidi oychchis. Entti zaaridi, “Aykkoyka paccibeenna” yaagidosona.
I enttako, “Ha77i korojjoynne karxiitey de7ey oykko; mashshi baynnay ba afilaa bayzidi mashsha shammo.
Haa si7ite! ‘Geellatara taybettis’ geetettidi xaafettidayssi tanan polettanaw bessees. Ee, ta gisho xaafettidabay poletteyssi tumattis” yaagis.
Iya tamaareti, “Godaw hayssan nam77u mashshi de7ees” yaagidosona. I, “Gidana” yaagis.
Yesuusi kase meezetidayssada denddidi Shamaho Deriya bolla keyis. Iya tamaareti iya kaallidosona.
He bessaa gakkida wode “Paacen gelonna mela woossite” yaagis.
Enttafe shuchchi holin gakkiya soo mela haakkidi gulbbatidi woossis.
“Ta aawaw, ne shene gidikko ha metuwa taappe aatha. Shin ta shene gidoppo ne sheney hano” yaagidi woossis.
Kiitanchchoy saloppe qonccidi minthis.
Daro un77ettidi minthidi woossees. Iya cawaykka suuthi xokkiyada sa7an xokkees.
Yesuusi woosaa wurssidi ba tamaaretakko yis. Entti, azzaniyappe denddoyssan daaburidi dhiskkidashin demmidi,
“Ays dhiskkeetii? Paacen gelonna mela denddidi woossite” yaagis.
I buroo oda bolla de7ishin daro asati yidosona. Tammanne nam77atappe issoy Yihuda geetetteyssi enttana kaalethees. I Yesuusa yeeranaw mati shiiqis.
Shin Yesuusi, “Yihuda, Asa Na7aa yeerada aatha immanee?” yaagis.
Yesuusa tamaareti he hanuwa be7idi, “Godaw mashshan shocino?” yaagidosona.
Entta giddofe issoy kahine halaqaa oosanchchuwa shocidi ushachcha haytha qanxidi yeggis.
Shin Yesuusi, “Agga! Diggofite” yaagis. Uraa haythaa bochchidi pathis.
Hessafe guye, Yesuusi bana oykkanaw yida kahine halaqatakko, Xoossa Keetha naageyssata shuumatakkonne cimatakko, “Paanno oykkiya asada mashshenne xam77a oykkidi yidetii?
Ubba gallas Xoossa Keethan ta hinttera de7iya wode ta bolla kushe wothibeeketa. Shin hayssi dhuma kawotethay haarida wodenne hintte wode” yaagis.
Hessafe guye, Yesuusa oykkidi kahine halaqaa zabbaa efidosona. Phexiroosi haahon Yesuusa kaallees.
Asati kahine halaqaa zabban tama eethidi wolla uttidashin Phexiroosi enttara issife uttis.
Issi aylliya Phexiroosi tama matan uttidayssa cadda xeellada, “Ha uray iyara de7ees” yaagasu.
Shin Phexiroosi, “Ha maccasete ta he uraa erikke” yaagidi kaddis.
Guutha wodeppe guye issi hara addey iya be7idi, “Nekka enttafe issuwa” yaagis. Shin Phexiroosi, “Ha addiyaw tana gidikke” yaagis.
Issi saate mela gam77idaappe guye issi hara addey tillisidi, “Ha uray Galiilappe gidiya gisho sidhey baynna iyara de7ees” yaagis.
Shin Phexiroosi, “Ha addiyaw, ne geyssa ta erikke” yaagis. I he oda onggonna de7ishin kuttoy waassis.
Goday guye simmidi Phexiroosa xeellis. Phexiroosi, “Hachchi kuttoy waassanaappe sinthe ne tana heedzu toho kaddana” yaagidi, Goday odida qaala akeekis.
Phexiroosi kare keyidi daro kokkoridi yeekkis.
Yesuusa naagiya asati iya leqisonne deshethi oykkidosona.
Iya ayfiyaa goozidi “Ane tinbbite oda; nena dechchiday oonee?” yaagidi oychchosona.
Hara daro cashshe cayidi kawushshosona.
Sa7i wonttiya wode Ayhude biitta cimati, kahine halaqatinne higge asttamaareti shiiqidi, Yesuusa bantta sinthe shiishidosona.
Entti, “Neeni Kiristtoosee? Ane nuus oda?” yaagidi oychchidosona. Yesuusi, “Ta odiyakko ammanekketa.
Ta oychchiyako zaarekketa.
Shin Asa Na7ay hayssafe gede baggan wolqqaama Xoossaa ushachcha baggan uttana” yaagis.
He wode ubbay, “Yaatin, neeni Xoossaa na7ee?” yaagidosona. I, “Ta Xoossaa na7a gideyssa hintte gideta” yaagis.
Entti, “Hiza, hara markka ay koshshii? I ba inxarssan odishin nu si7ida” yaagidosona.
He bessan shiiqida shanggoti ubbay denddidi Yesuusa Philaaxoosakko efidosona.
“Ha uray nu asaa balethishin, kawuwas giira giironna mela diggishininne qassi, ‘Taani Kiristtoosa hintte kawuwa’ yaagishin demmida” yaagidi mootidosona.
Philaaxoosi Yesuusa, “Neeni Ayhudeta kawoyye?” yaagidi oychchis. Yesuusi, “Ee, ne gidayssa mela” yaagis.
Philaaxoosi kahine halaqatakkonne asaakko, “Ha uraa bolla taani issi balakka demmabiikke” yaagis.
Shin entti, “Ha uray Galiilappe doomidi hayssa gakkanaw Yihuda kumethaa iitabaas denthethees” yaagidi minthi odidosona.
Philaaxoosi hessa si7ida wode Yesuusi Galiila aseekko eranaw koyidi iya oychchis.
Yesuusi Heroodisa biittaafe yida asi gideyssa Philaaxoosi erida wode Heroodisi he wode Yerusalaamen de7iya gisho iyaakko yeddis.
Heroodisi Yesuusa be7anaw daro wodeppe koyishe de7iya gisho iya be7ida wode daro ufayttis. Ays giikko, iyabaa si7ida gisho malaalisiyabaa oothin be7anaw amottishe de7ees.
Heroodisi Yesuusa daro oyshota oychchis, shin I aykkoka zaaribeenna.
Kahineta halaqatinne higge asttamaareti yan eqqidi minthidi iya mootosona.
Heroodisaranne iya wotaaddaretara Yesuusa kadhidosonanne leqisidosona. Bonchcho afilaa mayzidi Philaaxoosakko zaaridi yeddidosona.
Heroodisaranne Philaaxoosara kase morkkeshin he gallas wolla giigidosona.
Philaaxoosi kahine halaqata, asaa haareyssatanne asaa xeegidi,
“ ‘Ha uray asaa geellatethas denthethees’ gidi taakko ehideta. Takka hintte sinthan pilggada hintte shiishida mootuwas aybi balakka demmabiikke.
Heroodisi, hessatho aybi balakka iya bolla demmiboonna gisho nuukko yeddis. Tumakka ha uray hayqos gathiya aybi balakka oothibeenna.
Hessa gisho, iya garaafada billa yeddana” yaagis.
Hessa I giday Faasikka Baale wode issi asi enttaw billanayssi iyaw attonnabaa gidiya gishossa.
Derey ubbay issi bolla, “Ha uraa gede digga, nuus Barbbaana billa” yaagidi waassidosona.
Barbbaani katamaa giddon asaa iitabaas denthethidi ase wodhdhidi qashettida asi.
Philaaxoosi Yesuusa billanaw koyidi asaas zaari odis.
Gidoshin, asay, “Kaqqa! Kaqqa!” yaagidi waassidosona.
Philaaxoosi heedzantho, “Ha uray qohidabay aybe? Wodhos gathiya bala ta demmabiikke. Hessa gisho, garaafada yedda aggana” yaagis.
Entti bantta qaala dhoqqu oothidi, “Kaqettanaw bessees” gidi minthi waassidosona. Entta waasoykka xoonis.
Entta oyshaa gisho gidi Philaaxoosi iya bolla pirddis.
Asaa iitabaas denthetheyssanne ase wodhdhidi qashettidayssa billana mela woossida, he uraa enttaw billis. Shin Yesuusa entti koyidabaa oothana mela enttaw aathi immis.
Yesuusa oykkidi efishin Simoona giya Qereena biitta addey gaxareppe yishin, demmidi masqaliya toossidi Yesuusa kaallidi baana mela un77ethidosona.
Daro asaynne bantta tiraa iccishe yeekkiya maccasati iya guyiyara kaalloosona.
Shin Yesuusi enttako guye simmidi, “Hinttenoo, Yerusalaame maccasato, hintte huu7esinne hintte naytas yeekkiteppe attin taw yeekkofite.
‘Hekko maynthati, yelonna ulotinne dhanthonna dhanthati anjjettidosona’ hintte yaagana gallasay yaana.
He wode dereta, ‘Nu bolla kunddite’, zumatakka, ‘Nuna kammite’ yaagana.
Hiza, qaye mithaa hessatho oothiko mela mithaa waatanddeshsha?” yaagis.
Iyara wodhanaw hara nam77u worandzota efidosona.
Qeeraniyo geetettiya bessaa gathidi kaqqidosona. Worandzotappe issuwa ushachcha baggara hankkuwa haddirssa baggara kaqqidosona.
Yesuusi, “Ta aawaw, entti ay oothiyako eronna gisho neeni enttaw atto yaaga” yaagis. Entti iya afilaa bolla saama yeggidi shaakettidi ekkidosona.
Asay eqqidi xeellosona, shin deriya haareyssati, “Harata ashshis; Xoossay doorida Kiristtoosi iya gidikko ane bana ashsho” yaagidi leqisidosona.
Wotaaddareti iyaakko shiiqidi, caala woyne ushshaa immidosona.
Yaatidi, “Neeni Ayhudeta kawo gidikko ne huu7iya ashsha” yaagidi leqisidosona.
Iyaw huu7e baggara, “Hayssi Ayhudeta kawo” yaagiya xuufey de7ees.
Kaqettida worandzotappe issoy cashshe sa7ara goochchishe, “Ane neeni Kiristtoosa gidikko, nenakka nunakka ashsha” yaagis.
Shin hankko worandzoy, “Neeni hayssa mela pirddan de7ashe hari attoshin, Xoossaas yayyikii?
Nuuni nu balaas bessiya pirdda ekkoos, shin ha uray issi iitabaakka oothibeenna” yaagidi hanqettis.
Qassika, “Yesuusa, ne ne kawotethaara yaa wode tana qoppa” yaagis.
Yesuusi, “Ta new tuma odays; hachchi neeni taara gannaten gidana” yaagis.
He gallas usuppun saateppe bidi uddufun saate gakkanaw away poo7uwa diggida gisho biitta ubbaa bolla dhuma gidis. Xoossa Keetha magaraajjoy daakettidi nam77an shaakettis.
<range>
Yesuusi, qaala dhoqqu oothidi, “Ta aawaw, ta ta shemppiw ne kushen sheedhdhays” yaagidi hayqqis.
Mato halaqay, hanidayssa be7idi, “Hayssi uray tumakka xillo” yaagidi Xoossaa galatis.
Ha haniyabaa be7anaw he bessaa shiiqida asa ubbay hanidabaa be7ida wode bantta tiraa iccishe bantta soo simmidosona.
Gidoshin, Yesuusa matan eriya asa ubbay, hessadakka Galiilappe kaallidi yida maccasati hessa be7ishe haahon eqqidosona.
Ayhude shanggotappe issoy, Yoosefa geetettiya uray de7ees. I Armmatiyasa geetettiya Yihuda katamaappe yis. I lo77onne Xillo asi gidiya gisho Xoossaa kawotethaa yuussaa naagees. Shanggotappe issuwa gidishe entta zoretethaaninne oosuwan deenna.
<range>
He uray Philaaxoosakko bidi, Yesuusa ahaa mooganaw taw imma gidi woossis.
Philaaxoosi ekka yaagin, Yesuusa ahaa wodhisidi afilara xaaxis. Zaallafe woocidi kessida hara asi moogettonna ooratha duufon wothis.
Sambbaati gelana haniya gisho he gallasay giigetetha qamma.
Galiilappe denddidi Yesuusa kaallidi yida maccasati Yoosefara bidi iya ahaa waati moogiyakko duufuwa akeekidi be7idosona.
Yaappe simmidi shittonne qibaatiya giigisidosona. Higgey kiitteyssa mela Sambbaata gallas shemppi pee7idosona.
Saaminttafe koyro gallas, wogga wode wontta daro guura, maccasati bantta giigisida shittuwa ekkidi duufuwa bidosona.
Entti yaa gakkiya wode duufuwa doonan de7iya shuchchay gondderettidi kichchoyssa demmidosona.
Entti duufuwa gaathi gelidosona, shin Godaa Yesuusa ahaa demmibookkona.
Entti yan eqqidi aybi hanidee gidi qoppishin akeekonna daro phooliya afila ma77ida nam77u asati entta matan eqqidosona.
Maccasati yashettidi bantta huu7iya sa7an ziqqi oothidi de7ishin, asati enttako, “De7on de7eyssa hayqota giddon ays koyeetii?
I hayssan deenna; hayqoppe denddis, ‘Asa Na7ay nagaranchchota kushen aadhdhi imettana; enttika iya kaqqana. I heedzantho qamman hayqoppe denddana’ yaagidi, I hinttera Galiilan de7ishe hinttew odida qaala qoppite” yaagis.
<range>
Maccasati he wode iya qaala qoppidosona.
Maccasati duufuwappe simmidi hanidabaa ubbaa tammanne issotasinne haratasikka odidosona.
Hessa hawaaretas odiday Magdela Mayraamo, Yohaanna, Yayqooba aayiw Mayraamonne enttara de7iya hara maccasata.
Shin enttaw maccasati odidayssi elmmo daanin ammanibookkona.
Shin Phexiroosi denddi woxxidi duufo bis. He bessaa gakkidi hokki gaathi xeelliya wode moogo afilaa xalaala be7is. Hanidaban malaalettishe ba soo simmis.
He gallas kaalliya tamaaretappe nam77ati Yerusalaameppe tammanne issi kilo mitire haakkiya Emmahuuse gutaa boosona.
Entti wolla hanidabaa ubbaa odettoosona.
Entti he hanotabaa qoppishenne odettishe biya wode Yesuusi ba huu7en shiiqidi enttara bees.
Hanoshin, entti iya eronna mela entta ayfey oykettis.
I, “Hintte wolla oge bolla de7ishe odetteyssi aybe?” yaagis. Entti azzanidi si77i gidi eqqidosona.
Enttafe issoy Qeliyoopha geetetteyssi, “Ha qammata giddon Yerusalaamen hanidabaa eronnayssi, ne biittaas imatheyye?” yaagis.
I zaaridi, “I hanidayssi aybee?” yaagidi oychchis. Entti, “Xoossaa sinthaninne asa sinthan oosoninne odan mino nabe gidida Naazirete Yesuusabaa.
Iya kahine halaqatinne nuna haareyssati hayqo pirddas aathi immidi, kaqqidosona.
Nuuni Isra7eele asaa wozande gidi ufayttidi naagidashin hayssi hanin hachchi heedzantho qamma.
Qassi nu giddofe issi issi maccasati nuna malaalisidosona. Entti hachchi wontta guura duufuwa bidosona.
Iya ahaa dhayida wode simmi yidi, ‘I paxa de7ees’ yaagiya kiitanchchoti qonccin be7ida yaagidi odidosona.
Nu giddofekka issoti issoti duufuwa bidi maccasati odidayssatho hanin be7idosona, shin iya be7ibookkona” yaagis.
I enttako, “Hinttenoo, akeekonna asaw, hintte wozanay nabeti odidabaa ubbaa ammananaw gam77eyssato,
Kiristtoosi ha metuwa ekkanawunne ba bonchchuwan gelanaw bessennee?” yaagis.
Museppenne nabeta ubbaafe denddidi Geeshsha Maxaafan iyabay xaafettidayssa ubbaa enttaw qonccisis.
Entti biya gutaakko matattida wode Yesuusi aadhdhidi haaho soo biya daanin,
Entti, “Sa7ay qammida gisho nuura aqa” yaagidi minthidi woossidosona. Hessa gisho, enttara aqanaw gelis.
Enttara issife gayta bolla uttidi, uythaa denthidi, meenthi anjjidi enttaw immis.
He wode entti erana mela entta ayfey dooyettis. Enttika eridosona. Shin I enttafe geemmis.
Entti, “Nu ogiya bolla de7ishin I nuus Geeshsha Maxaafaa birshshishininne nuna haasayisishin nu wozanay xuugettibeenne?” yaagidosona.
He wode denddidi guye Yerusalaame yidosona. Tammanne issotinne harati issi bolla shiiqidi de7ishin demmidosona.
Entti, “Goday tuma denddis; Simoonas qonccis” yaagidosona.
He nam77u tamaareti Emmahuuse ogiya bolla de7ishin hanidayssanne uythaa meenthida wode waati iya eridaakko enttaw odidosona.
