Hessa gisho, Yihudi paanose, xomppe, tooranne gonddalle oykkida daro wotaaddareta, kahine halaqatinne Farisaaweti kiittida Xoossa Keetha naagiya pooliseta kaalethi ekkidi, he bessaa bis.
Yesuusi bana gakkana haniyabaa ubbaa eridi, gaxa keyidi, “Oona koyeetii?” yaagis.
Entti zaaridi, “Naazirete Yesuusa koyoos” yaagidosona. I zaaridi, “Taani Yesuusa” yaagis. Yesuusa aathi immida Yihudi yan enttara eqqis.
I, “Taani Yesuusa” gida wode entti guye shiiqidi, sa7an kunddidosona.
Yesuusi qassika, “Oona koyeetii?” yaagidi oychchis. Entti, “Naazirete Yesuusa koyoos” yaagidosona.
I zaaridi, “Taani Yesuusa gideyssa hinttew odas. Hiza, hintte tana koyabaa gidikko hayssata yeddite” yaagis.
I hessa giday, “Aawaw, neeni taw immidayssatappe hari attoshin issuwaka dhayssabiikke” gidayssi polettana melassa.
Simoon Phexiroosas mashshi de7ees. I he mashshaa shoddidi kahine halaqaa aylliyas ushachcha haytha shocidi, qanxi yeggis. He aylliya sunthay Malkkoosa.
Yesuusi Phexiroosakko, “Ne mashshaa shoohuwan zaara. Ta Aaway taw immida xuu7appe taani uyonnabaa new daanii?” yaagis.
Roome wotaaddaretinne entta halaqay Xoossa Keetha naagiya poolisetara issife Yesuusa oykkidi qachchidosona.
Koyro Yesuusa Haannako efidosona. Haanni he laythi kahine halaqa gidiya Qayyaafa bollo.
Qayyaafi, “Asa ubbaa gisho issi asi hayqqiko lo77o” gidi kase Ayhudeta zoridayssa.
Simoon Phexiroosinne hara issi tamaarey Yesuusa kaallidi bidosona. Kahine halaqay he hara tamaariya loythi erees. Hessa gisho, I Yesuusara kahine halaqaa zabbaa gelis.
Shin Phexiroosi karera dirssaa penggen eqqis. Kahine halaqay eriya hara tamaarey kare keyidi, penggiya naagiya na7ees odidi, Phexiroosa gaathi gelssis.
Penggiya naagiya na7iya Phexiroosakko, “Neeni, he addiya tamaaretappe issuwa gidikkii?” yaagasu. Phexiroosi zaaridi, “Akkay, taani gidikke” yaagis.
Sa7ay meeggiya gisho aylletinne naageyssati xiifa tama eethidi, yuuyi aadhdhi eqqidi kayosona. Phexiroosikka enttara eqqidi tama kayees.
Kahine halaqay Yesuusa, iya tamaaretabaanne iya timirttiyabaa oychchis.
Yesuusi zaaridi, “Taani asa ubbaas qonccen odas. Taani Ayhude ubbay shiiqiya Ayhude Woosa Keethaninne Xoossa Keethan ubba wode tamaarssas. Geeman aykkoka odabiikke.
Yaatin, neeni tana ays oychchay? Ta odishin si7ida asaa oychcha. He asay taani odididayssa eroosona” yaagis.
Yesuusi hessa gida wode he bessan eqqida wotaaddaretappe issoy Yesuusa baqqidi, “Kahine halaqaas hayssada zaaray?” yaagis.
Yesuusi zaaridi, “Taani iitabaa odidabaa gidikko hayssan de7iya asa ubbaa sinthan oda. Shin taani tuma odidabaa gidikko tana ays baqqay?” yaagis.
Hessa gisho, Haanni, Yesuusi qashettida mela kahine halaqaa Qayyaafakko yeddis.
Phexiroosi yan eqqidi, tama kayishin, harati iyaakko, “Neeni ha addiya tamaaretappe issuwa gidikkii?” yaagis. Phexiroosi zaaridi, “Akkay, taani gidikke” yaagidi kaddis.
Kahine halaqaa aylletappe issoy, Phexiroosi haythaa qanxida addiya dabboy, Phexiroosakko, “Taani nena iyara atakilttiya giddon be7abiikkina?” yaagidi oychchis.
Phexiroosi qassika kaddis. Sohuwara kuttoy waassi aggis.
Wontta guura, entti Yesuusa Qayyaafa sooppe deriya haareyssa ooso keethi efidosona. Ayhudeti Paasika Baale kathaa maanaw banttana tunisonna mela deriya haareyssa ooso keethaa gelibookkona.
Hessa gisho, Philaaxoosi enttako kare keyidi, “Ha addiya ays mooteetii?” yaagis.
Entti, “I iita oothonnabaa gidiyakko nuuni iya neekko ehokko” yaagidosona.
Philaaxoosi zaaridi, “Hintte iya ekki efidi, hintte higgey geyssada iya bolla pirddite” yaagis. Ayhudeti, “Oonakka wodhiya maati nuus baawa” yaagidosona;
Hessi haniday Yesuusi ay mela hayqo hayqqaneekko erisanaw odidayssi polettanaassa.
Philaaxoosi ba ooso keetha zaari gelidi, Yesuusa xeegidi, “Neeni Ayhude kawo?” yaagidi oychchis.
Yesuusi Philaaxoosa, “Ha oysha neeni neeppe oychchayye woykko hara asi new tabaa odidee?” yaagis.
Philaaxoosi zaaridi, “Ta Ayhude asee? Ne asaynne kahine halaqati nena taw aathi immidosona. Ne ay oothadii?” yaagis.
Yesuusi, “Ta kawotethay ha alamiyana gidenna. I hayssan gidiyakko ta Ayhudeta halaqatas aadhdha imettonna mela ta aylleti taw olettana. Shin ta kawotethay ha alamiyana gidenna” yaagis.
Hessa gisho, Philaaxoosi Yesuusakko, “Yaatin, neeni kawoyye?” yaagidi oychchis. Yesuusi zaaridi, “Tuma ta kawo gideyssa ne gadasa. Taani yelettidaynne ha alamiya yiday tumatethaas markkattanassa. Tumaa bagga gidida oonikka taani geyssa si7ees” yaagis.
Philaaxoosi, “Tumi aybee?” yaagis. Philaaxoosi hessa gidaappe guye Ayhudetakko kare keyidi, “Taani iyappe ay iitakka demmabiikke.
Shin Paasika Baale gallas, issi ase hinttew qashoppe billiya meezey de7ees. Taani hinttew Ayhudeta kawuwa billana mela koyeetii?” yaagis.
Entti zaaridi, bantta qaalaa dhoqqu oothidi, “Barbbaana billafe attin iya gidenna” yaagidosona. Shin Barbbaani pangga.
Hessafe guye, Philaaxoosi Yesuusa garaafisis.
Wotaaddareti aguntha kallachcha medhdhidi iya huu7en wothidosona. Qassi zo7o ma7o iya mayzidosona.
Iyaakko shiiqidi, “Ayhude kawuwaw, merinaw kawota” yaagidi iya baqqidosona.
Philaaxoosi qassika kare keyidi, Ayhudetakko, “Hekko, taani iyappe ay iitakka demmaboonnayssa hintte erana mela iya hintteko kare kessana” yaagis.
Hessafe guye, Yesuusi aguntha kallachcha ba huu7en wothidi, zo7o ma7o ma77idi, kare keyis. Philaaxoosi Ayhudetakko, “Uraa hayssa be7ite” yaagis.
Kahine halaqatinne Xoossa Keetha naageyssati iya be7ida wode bantta qaala dhoqqu oothidi, “Masqaliya bolla kaqqa! Kaqqa!” yaagidosona. Philaaxoosi enttako, “Hintte iya efidi, masqaliya bolla kaqqite. Taani iyappe ay iitakka demmabiikke” yaagis.
Ayhudeti zaaridi, “Nuus higgey de7ees. I bana Xoossaa na7a oothida gisho nu higgiyatho I hayqqanaw bessees” yaagidosona.
Philaaxoosi hessa si7ida wode kaseyssafe daro yayyis.
Qassika Philaaxoosi ba ooso keethi simmi gelidi Yesuusakko, “Neeni awuppe yadi?” yaagidi oychchis. Shin Yesuusi iyaw aykkoka zaaribeenna.
Hessa gisho, Philaaxoosi, “Taw odikkii? Nena billanaw woykko masqaliya bolla kaqqanaw taw maati de7eyssa erikkii?” yaagis.
Yesuusi, “Xoossay new maata immiboonnabaa gidiyakko ta bolla maati new deennashin. Hessa gisho, tana new aathi immidays aadhdhiya nagara oothis” yaagis.
Philaaxoosi hessa si7ida wode Yesuusa billanaw oge koyis. Shin Ayhudeti bantta qaala dhoqqu oothidi, “Neeni iya billiyabaa gidikko Kawuwa Qeesare bagga gidakka. Bana kawo giya oonikka Qeesare morkke” yaagidosona.
Philaaxoosi hessa si7idi Yesuusa kare kessis. Yaatidi, “Lochche Shuchchi” giyason pirdda oydiyan uttis. Ibraysxe qaalan he bessay “Gabata” guussu.
He gallasay Paasika Baale bonchchanaw giigetetha gallas. He wode sa7i usuppun saate heera. Philaaxoosi Ayhudetakko, “Hintte kawuwa hayssa be7ite” yaagis.
Ayhudeti bantta qaala dhoqqu oothidi, “Digga! Digga! Masqaliya bolla kaqqa” yaagidosona. Philaaxoosi zaaridi, “Hintte kawuwa taani masqaliya bolla kaqqanayssa koyeetii?” yaagidi oychchis. Kahine halaqati, “Qeesareppe hara kawoy nuus baawa” yaagidosona.
Hessafe guye, entti Yesuusa masqaliya bolla kaqqana mela Philaaxoosi enttaw aathi immis. Entti Yesuusa oykkidi efidosona.
Yesuusi ba masqaliya tookkidi, “Huu7e guugge” giya bessaa bis. “Huu7e guugge” guussay Ibraysxe qaalan “Golggotta” guussu.
Entti he bessan masqaliya bolla Yesuusa kaqqidosona. Qassi iyara hara nam77u asata, issuwa ya baggara hankkuwa ha baggara masqaliya bolla kaqqidosona.
Philaaxoosi, “Ayhudeta Kawuwa, Naazirete Yesuusa” yaagiya xuufe xaafidi masqaliya bolla wothis.
Yesuusi masqaliya bolla kaqettida bessay katamaas matan de7iya gisho daro Ayhudeti he xuufiya nabbabidosona. Xuufey xaafettiday Ibraysxe doonan, Laatine doonaninne Girike doonana.
Hessa gisho, kahine halaqati Philaaxoosakko, “ ‘Ha addey bana Ayhude kawo yaagis’ gada xaafappe attin ‘Ayhude kawo’ gada xaafoppa” yaagidosona.
Yaatin, Philaaxoosi, “Ta xaafidayssa xaafas” yaagidi zaaris.
Wotaaddareti masqaliya bolla iya kaqqidaappe guye iya ma7uwa ekkidi, oyddu bessan shaakkidi, isso isso ekkidosona. Yeda ma7ettiya iya adussa ma7uwa ekkidosona.
Wotaaddareti, “Oona gakkaneekko, saama yegganaappe attin ma7uwa peedhokko” yaagidosona. Hessi haniday Geeshsha Maxaafan, “Ta ma7uwa shaakki ekkidosona; ta adussa ma7uwa bollaka saama yeggidosona” geetettidayssi polettana melassa. Hessa gisho, wotaaddareti hessa oothidosona.
Shin Yesuusa masqaliya matan iya aayyaa, iya aaye michchiya, Qeliyophe machchiya Mayraamanne Magdela Mayraama eqqidosona.
Yesuusi ba aayiwunne I dosiya tamaarey yan eqqidayssata be7idi, ba aayeko, “Ta aaye, ne na7aa hayssa be7a” yaagis.
Hessafe guye, he tamaariyakko, “Ne aayiw hanno be7a” yaagis. He tamaarey iyo he wodeppe doomidi baara daana mela soo efis.
Hessafe guye, Yesuusi ubbay ha77i polettidayssa eridi, Geeshsha Maxaafan xaafettidayssi polettana mela “Tana saamees” yaagis.
He bessan issi xugga kumetha caala woyney de7ees. Entti ispponjje he woyniyan yeggidi, hisophe mitha xeeran wothidi, Yesuusa doonaakko shiishidosona.
Yesuusi woyniya ganxi be7idi, “Polettis” yaagis. Hessafe guye, ba huu7iya ziqqi oothidi ba shemppuwa immis.
He gallasay giigetetha gallas gidiya gishonne wonttetha gallasay bonchcho Sambbaata gidiya gisho asata ahay masqaliya bolla Sambbaata gallas pee7onna mela entta tohuwa menthidi, masqaliyappe wodhisana mela Ayhudeti Philaaxoosa woossidosona.
Hessa gisho, wotaaddareti bidi, Yesuusara kaqettida nam77u asata tohuwa menthidosona.
Shin Yesuusakko yida wode I hayqqidayssa be7idi, iya tohuwa menthibookkona.
Shin wotaaddaretappe issoy iya miya tooran caddin sohuwara suuthinne haathi goggis.
Hintte ammanana mela hessa be7idayssi markkattis. Iya markkatethayka tuma. Qassi I odeyssi tuma gideyssa erees.
Hessi haniday Geeshsha Maxaafay, “Iya meqethatappe issoykka meqqenna” gidayssi polettana melassa.
Qassika Geeshsha Maxaafay hara bessan, “Entti bantta caddidayssa be7ana” yaagees.
Hessafe guye, Armmatiyasa katamaappe yida Yoosefi Yesuusa ahaa ekkanaw Philaaxoosa woossis. Yoosefi Ayhudetas yayyida gisho qosan Yesuusa kaalleyssa. Philaaxoosi, “Ekka” yaagis. Hessa gisho, Yoosefi bidi Yesuusa ahaa ekkis.
Qassi Niqodimoosi, hayssafe kase Yesuusakko qamma yidayssi, karbbenne godare uuthara walakettida hasttamanne issi kilo giraame gidiya shitto ekkidi Yoosefara yis.
He nam77u asati Yesuusa ahaa ekkidi, Ayhudeti aha xaaxiya maaran, shittora, moogo afilan xaaxidosona.
Yesuusi masqaliya bolla kaqettida bessan daro atakilttey de7ees. He atakilttiya giddon shuchchafe woocettidi oosettida buroo oonikka moogettibonna ooratha duufoy de7ees.
He gonggoloy matan de7iya gishonne Ayhudeti Sambbaatas giigettiya gallas gidiya gisho Yesuusa ahaa yan moogidosona.
Wogga wode wontta buroo geeyonna de7ishin, Magdela Mayraama, Yesuusi moogettida duufuwa bada shuchchay he duufuwa doonappe denddidayssa be7asu.
Simoon Phexiroosakkonne Yesuusi dosiya hankko tamaariyakko woxxa bada, “Duufuwappe Godaa efidosona; iya awun wothidaakko nu erokko” yaagasu.
Hessa gisho, Phexiroosinne hankko tamaarey keyidi duufuwa bidosona.
Nam77ayka issife woxxidosona, shin hankko tamaarey Phexiroosappe aadhdhidi sinthattidi duufuwa gakkis.
He tamaarey hokkidi, moogo afilaa be7is, shin duufuwan wodhdhibeenna.
Simoon Phexiroosi iya kaalli yidi, duufuwan wodhdhidi moogo afilay yan de7eyssa be7is.
Qassi Yesuusa huu7en xaaxettida afilay xaaxettida mela dumma issi bessan de7eyssa be7is. He afilay dumma de7eesippe attin moogo afilaara issife deenna.
He wode sinthattidi duufuwa gakkida hankko tamaarey geli be7idi ammanis.
Yesuusi hayqoppe denddanaw besseyssa odiya Geeshsha maxaafaa qaala entti buroo akeekibookkona.
Hessafe guye, iya tamaareti bantta soo simmidi bidosona.
Shin Mayraama he duufuwa doonan eqqada yeekkashe hokkada duufuwa giddo xeellasu.
Bootha ma7o ma77ida nam77u kiitanchchoti Yesuusa ahay zin77idasuwan issoy huu7esoora hankkoy tohosoora uttidashin be7asu.
Entti ikko, “Maccasete, ays yeekkay?” yaagidi oychchidosona. Iya, “Entti ta Godaa efidosona; entti awun wothidaakko taani erikke” yaagasu.
Hessa gidaappe guye, iya guye simma xeelliya wode Yesuusi yan eqqidayssa be7asu. Shin I Yesuusa gididayssa erabuukku.
Yesuusi iikko, “Maccasete, ays yeekkay? Oona koyay?” yaagidi oychchis. Mayraama atakiltte oosanchchuwa daanin, “Godaw, ne ekkidabaa gidikko, iya awun wothidaakko taw odarkkii. Taani iya ekkana” yaagasu.
Yesuusi iikko, “Mayraame” yaagis. Iya iyaakko simmada, Ibraysxe doonan “Rebuuni” yaagasu. Hessas birshshethay “Asttamaariyaw” guussu.
Yesuusi iikko, “Taani buroo ta Aawakko boonna gisho tana oykkada ashshanaw koyoppa. Shin ta ishatakko bada, ‘Taani ta Aawakkonne hintte Aawakko, ta Xoossaakonne hintte Xoossaako, simmana gis’ gada enttaw oda” yaagis.
Magdela Mayraama Godaa be7idayssanne iw hessa I odididayssa bada iya tamaaretas odasu.
Wogga wode omarssi, iya tamaareti Ayhudetas yayyidi kariya gorddidi shiiqi uttidashin, Yesuusi yidi, entta giddon eqqidi, “Saroy hinttew gido” yaagis.
Hessa gidi simmidi ba kushiyanne ba miya entta bessis. Iya tamaareti Godaa be7ida wode daro ufayttidosona.
Yesuusi zaaridi enttako, “Saroy hinttew gido; ta Aaway tana kiittidayssada taanikka hinttena kiittays” yaagis.
Hessa gidaappe guye, entta bolla ufu gidi punnis. Qassi, “Geeshsha Ayyaana ekkite.
Hintte atto gida asaa nagaray atto geetettana. Hintte atto goonnayssata nagaray atto geetettenna” yaagis.
Shin tammanne nam77u tamaaretappe issoy, Didimoosa geetettiya Toomasi, Yesuusi yida wode enttara deenna.
Hessa gisho, hankko iya tamaareti Toomasakko, “Nuuni Godaa be7ida” yaagidosona. Shin Toomasi enttako, “Misimaren I cadettida iya kushiyan de7iya beeta be7onnanne he beeta ta biradhdhen bochchonna, qassi ta kushiya iya miyan yedda be7onna ammanikke” yaagis.
Saaminttafe guye, Yesuusa tamaareti qassika son shiiqidi uttidosona; Toomasikka enttara de7ees. Karey gorddettidi de7ishin Yesuusi yidi, entta giddon eqqidi, “Saroy hinttew gido” yaagis.
Hessafe guye, Yesuusi Toomasakko, “Ta kushiya ne biradhdhiyan bochchada be7a. Qassi ne kushiya ta miyan yeddada be7a; sidhoppa, ammana” yaagis.
Toomasi zaaridi, “Ta Godaw, ta Xoossaw” yaagis.
Yaatin Yesuusi, “Neeni tana be7ida gisho ammanadasa, shin tana be7onna ammanidayssati anjjettidayssata” yaagis.
Yesuusi ha maxaafan xaafettiboonna hara daro malaatata ba tamaareta sinthan oothis.
Shin Yesuusi I Kiristtoosa, Xoossaa Na7aa gideyssa hintte ammanana melanne ammanidi iya sunthan de7o demmana mela hessi xaafettis.
Hessafe guye, Yesuusi Xibaaryoosa Abbaa matan ba tamaaretas zaari qonccis. I enttaw hayssafe kaallidi de7iya hanotan qonccis.
Simoon Phexiroosi, Mentte geetettiya Toomasi, Qaana Galiilappe yida Natina7eeli, Zabdiyoosa naytinne Yesuusa tamaaretappe hara nam77ati issife de7oosona.
Simoon Phexiroosi enttako, “Taani molo oykkanaw bays” yaagis. Entti, “Nukka neera baana” yaagidi, wogoluwa giddo gelidosona. Shin entti he qamman aybi molokka oykkibookkona.
Wontta guura xalqey dolanaappe sinthe, Yesuusi abbaa gaxan eqqis, shin iya tamaareti Yesuusa gididayssa erbookkona.
Yesuusi enttako, “Ta laggeto, molo oykkibeekketii?” yaagis. Entti zaaridi, “Aykkoka oykkibookko” yaagidosona.
I zaaridi, “Hintte gitiya wogoluwappe ushachcha baggara yeggite; guutha molo hintte oykkana” yaagis. Hessa gisho, gitiya ushachcha baggara yeggidosona. Moloy darida gisho goochchidi kessanaw xoonettidosona.
Yesuusi dosiya tamaarey Phexiroosakko, “Hayssi Godaa!” yaagis. Simoon Phexiroosi I Godaa gidayssa si7ida wode kallo de7iya gisho ba ma7uwa ma77idi abbaa giddo guppi gelis.
Shin wogoluwan attida hankko tamaareti moloy kumida gitiya goochchidi, abbaafe gaxa keyidosona. Entti abbaafe nam77u xeetu wadha mela haakkoosona.
Entti abbaafe gaxa keyida wode xiifa bonqon moloy de7eyssanne uythi be7idosona.
Yesuusi enttako, “Ha77i hintte oykkida moluwappe guuthara hammite” yaagis.
Simoon Phexiroosi wogoluwan gelidi, xeetanne ishatammanne heedzu wogga moloti kumida gitiya goochchidi abbaafe gaxa kessis. Moloy hessa mela daro gidin gitey daakettibeenna.
Yesuusi enttako, “Haa yidi miite” yaagis. I Godaa gideyssa entti erida gisho iya tamaaretappe issoykka, “Neeni oonee?” gidi iya oychchanaw minniday baawa.
Yesuusi yidi, uythaa ekkidi enttaw immis; moluwakka hessada immis.
Yesuusi hayqoppe denddidi ba tamaaretas qonccishin hayssi heedzantho.
Entti midaappe guye, Yesuusi Simoon Phexiroosakko, “Yoona na7aw Simoona, tana hayssatappe aathada dosay?” yaagis. Simoon Phexiroosi, “Ee Godaw, taani nena doseyssa ne eraasa” yaagis. Yesuusi iyaakko, “Ta dorssa marata heemma” yaagis.
Yesuusi qassika, “Yoona na7aw Simoona, tana dosay?” yaagis. Simoon Phexiroosi, “Ee Godaw, taani nena doseyssa ne eraasa” yaagis. Yesuusi, “Ta dorssata heemma” yaagis.
Yesuusi heedzantho, “Yoona na7aw Simoona, tana dosay?” yaagis. Yesuusi heedzantho Simoon Phexiroosakko, “Tana dosay?” yaagidi oychchida gisho Phexiroosi azzanidi, “Godaw, neeni ubbabaa eraasa; taani nena doseyssa ne eraasa” yaagis. Yesuusi, “Ta dorssata heemma.
Taani new tuma odays; neeni na7atethan de7iya wode nerkka danccettada, ne koyida soo baasa. Shin ne cimida wode ne kushiya micca bessana. Hari danccisana; ne dosonna soo efana” yaagis.
Yesuusi hessa Phexiroosi ay mela hayqo hayqqidi, Xoossaa bonchchisaneekko erisanaw gis. Hessa gidaappe guye, Yesuusi Phexiroosakko, “Tana kaalla” yaagis.
Phexiroosi guye simmidi, Yesuusi dosiya tamaarey baappe guyera yeyssa be7is. He tamaarey, kaho miyason Yesuusakko shiiqidi, “Godaw, nena aathi immanay oonee?” gidayssa.
Phexiroosi he tamaariya be7idi, “Godaw, ha addey qassi waananee?” yaagidi Yesuusa oychchis.
Yesuusi iyaakko, “Taani yaana gakkanaw I daana mela taani koykko, hessi nena ay metidee? Neeni tana kaalla” yaagis.
Hessa gisho, he tamaarey hayqqenna giya oday ishata ubbaa gakkis. Shin Yesuusi, “Taani yaana gakkanaw, I daana mela taani koykko nena ay metidee?” yaagisippe attin “Hayqqenna” gibeenna.
Ha odabaa markkattidaynne hayssa xaafiday he tamaariya. Iya markkatethay tuma gideyssa nuuni eroos.
Yesuusi oothida hara darobay de7ees. Ta qoppin, ubbabay huu7en huu7en xaafettidaakko, xaafettiya maxaafatas kumetha alamey wothanw gidanabaa daanenna.
Tewofiloosa, Yesuusi ba oosuwa oykkida wodeppe salo bida gallasaa gakkanaw, oothidabaanne tamaarssidabaa ubbaa taani ta koyro maxaafan xaafas. Salo baanappe sinthe I ba doorida hawaareta Geeshsha Ayyaanan kiittis.
<range>
I ba waayappe guye hayqoppe denddidayssa sidhey baynna qonccisidi enttaw bana bessis. Oytamu gallas enttaw qonccidi Xoossaa kawotethaabaa entta tamaarssis.
Issi wode enttara issife mishe entta hayssada yaagidi kiittis: “Ta hinttew odida, ta Aaway immana gida ufayssaa qaala naagiteppe attin Yerusalaameppe keyoppite.
Ays giikko, Yohaannisi haathan xammaqis, shin guutha wodeppe guye Geeshsha Ayyaanan hintte xammaqettana” yaagis.
Hawaareti Yesuusara gahettida wode iyaakko, “Godaw, Isra7eeletas ne kawotethaa zaarana wodey hayssee?” yaagidi oychchidosona.
Yesuusi enttako, “Ta Aaway ba maatan oothiya wodiyanne laythaa hintte eranaw dandda7ekketa.
Shin Geeshsha Ayyaanay hintte bolla wodhdhiya wode hintte wolqqan kumana. Yaani simmidi, Yerusalaamen, Yihuda biitta ubban, Samaareninne sa7aa gaxa gakkanaw taw markkatta gidana” yaagis.
Hessa gidayssafe guye entti xeellishin, dhoqqu dhoqqu gidi, saluwa bin shaaraykka iya entta ayfiyaappe geenthis.
Yesuusi biya wode entti salo tishshi oothidi xeellishin, bootha ma7o ma77ida nam77u asati akeekonna entta matan eqqidi,
“Galiila asaw, salo xeellishe, hintte ays eqqideti? Ha hintte be7ishin salo bida Yesuusi hessadakka simmidi yaana” yaagidosona.
Hessafe guye, hawaareti Shamaho Deriyappe Yerusalaame simmidosona. Shamaho Derey Yerusalaames matan de7ees.
Entti Yerusalaame gelidi, bantta de7iya bessaa pooqiya bolla keyidosona. Enttika: Phexiroosa, Yohaannisa, Yayqooba, Inddiriyasa, Filphoosa, Toomasa, Bartolomiyoosa, Maatoosa, Ilfiyoosa na7aa Yayqooba, ba biittaas mishettiya Simoonanne Yayqooba na7aa Yihuda.
Hayssati ubbay maccasatara, Yesuusa aaye Mayraamiranne Yesuusa ishatara ubbay issi wozanan gididi minthidi woossosona.
He wode Phexiroosi xeetanne laatama gidiya ammaniyaa asay shiiqida bessan denddi eqqidi, hayssada yaagis:
“Asaw, Yesuusa oykkidayssata kaalethida Yihudabaa Geeshsha Ayyaanay kase Dawite doonan odida Xoossaa qaalay polettanaw bessees.
Yihudi nuura issife ha oosuwa oothanaw doorettida asi.”
Shin Yihudi ba iita oosuwan demmida miishen gade shammis. I gufannidi kunddin, iya uloy daakettis; iya maraacey ubbay kare keyis.
Yihuda bolla hanidabaa Yerusalaamen de7iya asa ubbay si7is. Hessa gisho, he gadiya bantta qaalan Akelddaama (Suutha gade) gidi xeegidosona.
“Hessika mazmure maxaafan, ‘Iya keethay kallo atto; oonikka iyan de7oppo. Qassi iya shuumatethaa hari ekko’ geetetti xaafettis.
“Hessa gisho, Godaa Yesuusi nu giddon simerettida wode ubban nuura de7eyssatappe,
qassi Xammaqiya Yohaannisa wodiyappe doomidi Godaa Yesuusi salo bida gallas gakkanaw nuura de7eyssatappe issi asi iya dendduwas nuura markka gidanaw bessees” yaagis.
Hessa gisho, asay dooruwas Yosxoosa giya Barssabaasa geetettiya Yoosefanne Maatiyasa nam77a shiishidosona.
Hessafe guye, Xoossaa woossishe, “Asa ubbaa wozana eriya Godaw, ha nam77atappe ne oona dooridaakko nuna bessa.
Yihudi ba bessaa bidi, aggida oosuwanne hawaaretetha oosuwa ekkana mela hayssatappe nuus qonccisa” yaagidosona.
Entta bolla saama yeggidosona. Saamay Maatiyasa bolla wodhdhin Maatiyasi tammanne issi hawaareta bolla guzhettis.
Phenxeqosxe giya gallasay gakkida wode ammaniyaa asa ubbay issife issi bessan shiiqidi de7oosona.
Qopponna wolqqaama goteda guummiya guunthay akeekonna saloppe yidi entti de7iya keethaa kumis.
Qassi tama laco daaniya inxarssati enttaw benttishe, shaaketti shaaketti entta ubbaa bolla wodhdhidosona.
Entti ubbay Geeshsha Ayyaanan kumidi dumma dumma doonan odettana mela Geeshsha Ayyaanay entta dandda7isin haasaya doomidosona.
He wode biitta ubbaafe yida Xoossaa yayyaa Ayhudeti Yerusalaamen de7oosona.
He guunthaa si7ida wode daro asay shiiqidosona. Ammaniya asay entta qaalan odettishin si7ida gisho
malaalettidi, “Ha odettiya asa ubbay Galiila ase gidokkonaayye?
Yaatin, nuuni, nu yelettida biittaa doonan entti odettishin waanidi si7anaw dandda7ido?
Nuuni Pharxen, Meedonan, Elaamen, nam77u shaafatappe giddon de7eyssati, Yihudan, Qaphadooqiyan, Phanxoosan, Iisiyan,
Phirggen, Phinfilen, Gibxxen, Qaarena matan de7iya Liibiyan de7eyssata. Nuuppe baggatikka Roomeppe yida asata.
Ayhudetinne Ayhudetetha ammano gelida asati, Qarxeesanne Arabe asati, Xoossay oothida gita oosuwa nu qaalan odettishin si7oos” yaagidosona.
Ubbay malaalettidi, gaanabaa dhayidi wolikko, “La hayssi ay guussee?” yaagidosona.
Shin harati, “Hayssati uyidi mathottidosona” yaagidi qelqisidosona.
Shin Phexiroosi, tammanne issi hawaaretara denddi eqqidi, ba qaala dhoqqu oothidi, enttaw hayssada yaagidi odis: “Ayhudetoo, Yerusalaamen de7iya ubbato, taani odeyssa si7ite.
Wonttafe heedzu saate gidiya gisho hintte qoppeyssada ha asati mathottibookkona; hessi hinttew eretto.
Shin hayssi haniday nabiya Iyyu7eeli odidayssi polettana melassa.
“ ‘Xoossay, wodiya wurssethan hayssada hanana yaagees: taani asa ubbaa bolla ta Ayyaana gussana. Hintte adde naytinne macca nayti, tinbbite odana. Hintte yalagati qonccethi be7ana; hintte cimati amuho amuhana.
He gallasatan tana ammaniyaa adde aylleta bollanne macca aylleta bolla taani ta Ayyaana gussana; entti tinbbite odana.
Qassi taani bolla saluwan oorathabaa, garssa sa7ankka malla bessana. Suuthi, taminne wolqqaama caagani benttana.
Gitanne bonchcho gidida Godaa gallasay gakkanaappe sinthe away dhumana; ageenaykka suuthi daanana.
He wode hessada hanana; Godaa sunthaa xeegiya oonikka attana’ yaagis.
“Isra7eele asaw, ha qaala si7ite. Naazirete Yesuusa oonatethay, Xoossay hintte giddon oothida wolqqaama oosuwaninne malaatatan hinttew qonccoyssa hinttee, hintte huu7en ereeta.
Xoossaa kase eraninne iya sheniyan Yesuusi hinttew aadhdhi imettis. Hintte iya nagaranchchoti masqaliya bolla kaqqidi wodhana mela aathi immideta.
Shin Xoossay hayqo wolqqaa diggidi iya denthis. Hessa gisho, hayqoy iya oykkanaw dandda7ibeenna.
Dawitey iyabaa odishe, ‘Taani yarkkonna mela, Goday ta ushachchan de7ees. Godaa ubba wode ta matan be7ays.
Hessa gisho, ta wozanay ufayttis; ta inxarssan ufayssi kumis; hayqqiya ta asatethay ufayssan daana.
Ays giikko, ta shemppuwa Si7oolen aggaka. Qassi ne Geeshsha Na7aa ahaa wooqisakka.
Neeni tana de7o ogiya erisadasa. Neeni taara de7eyssan ta ufayssay kumethi gidees’ yaagis.
“Asaw, nu aawa Dawitebaa ta hinttew geeshshada odana. Dawitey hayqqidi moogettis; iya duufoy hachchi gakkanaw nu matan de7ees.
Dawitey nabe gidida gisho Xoossay iya sheeshaappe issuwa iya kawotethaa araata bolla utisanaw iyaw caaqqida caaquwa erees.
Hessa gisho, Kiristtoosa dendduwa sinthe xeellidi, ‘Iya shemppoy Si7oolen attibeenna; iya asatethaykka wooqibeenna’ gidi odis.
“Xoossay, ha Yesuusa hayquwappe denthidayssas nuuni ubbay markka.
Hessa gisho, Xoossay baara haarana mela baappe ushachcha baggara iya dhoqqu dhoqqu oothidi, iyaw immana geetettida Geeshsha Ayyaana ekkidi, hayssa hintte ha77i be7eyssanne si7eyssa nu bolla gussis.
Gaasoykka, Dawitey ba huu7en salo bibeennashin yaagis: ‘Goday, ta Godaa, “Taani ne morkketa ne tohoy yedhdhiyaso oothana gakkanaw hayssan taappe ushachcha baggan utta” gis’ yaagis.
<range>
“Hessa gisho, ha hintte masqaliya bolla kaqqida Yesuusa, Xoossay Godanne Kiristtoosa oothidayssa Isra7eele asa ubbay tuma ero” yaagis.
Asay Phexiroosi gidayssa si7ida wode bantta wozanan boshettidi Phexiroosanne hankko hawaaretakko, “Ishato, yaatin nuuni ay oothinoo?” yaagidosona.
Phexiroosi enttako, “Hintte nagaray atto geetettana mela nagaraappe simmidi, hintte issoy issoy Yesuus Kiristtoosa sunthan xammaqetite. Xoossay immiya Geeshsha Ayyaana hintte ekkana.
Gaasoykka Xoossay immana gida ufayssa qaalay hinttes, hintte naytasinne Goday nu Xoossay baakko xeegiya haahon de7iya ubbaassa” yaagis.
Phexiroosi enttaw hara qaalakka gujji markkattidi, “Ha wodiya geella asaa bolla yaanaw de7iya pirddafe hintte huu7iya ashshite” yaagidi zoris.
Phexiroosi odidayssa ekkidayssati xammaqettidosona. He gallas heedzu mukulu gidiya asay ammanidosona.
Entti hawaareta timirttiyan, issifetethan, uythaa muusaninne Xoossaa woosan minnoosona.
Hawaareta kushen daro oorathabaynne malaati oosettiya gisho asa ubbay yayyidosona.
Ammanida ubbay issife de7oosona; banttaw de7iyaba ubbaa issife shaakettoosona.
Entti banttaw de7iyabaa bayzidi miishiya issuwas issuwas koshshida mela shaakkosona.
Ubba gallas issi wozanan gididi Xoossa Keethan shiiqoosona. Bantta keethan issoy issuwa xeegidi ufayssaninne ashkke wozanan kathaa moosona.
Xoossaa galatishe asa ubban sabettidosona. Goday atteyssata gallas gallas entta bolla gujjees.
Issi gallas Phexiroosinne Yohaannisi Xoossaa woossanaw uddufun saaten Xoossa Keethi bidosona.
Yelettoosoppe doomidi wobbe gidida issi addey Xoossa Keethi geliya asaappe miishe woossana mela ubba wode lo77o giya Xoossa Keethaa penggiyan ehidi wothoosona.
He wobbe addey Phexiroosinne Yohaannisi Xoossa Keethi gelana hanishin be7idi entta miishe woossis.
Enttika iya caddi xeellidi, “Nuukko haa xeella” yaagidosona.
Wobbe addey enttafe aykko ekkana daanin enttako xeellis.
Shin Phexiroosi iyaakko, “Taw miishey baawa, shin taw de7iyabaa taani new immana. Naazirete Yesuus Kiristtoosa sunthan denddada hamutta” yaagis.
Hessafe guye, wobbe addiya ushachcha kushiya oykkidi denthis. Ellesidi iya tohoynne qinccafiley minni aggis.
Addey guppidi denddi eqqis. Gedenne ha hamuthi doomis. Hessafe guye, hamuttishe, guppishenne Xoossaa galatishe enttara issife Xoossa Keethi gelis.
I hamuttishininne Xoossaa galatishin asa ubbay iya be7idosona.
Be7ida ubbay miishe woossanaw lo77o giya Xoossa Keetha penggen uttidayssi iya gididayssa eridosona; I hanidabaa be7idi malaalettidosona.
Addey Phexiroosappenne Yohaannisappe duuxike gidi oykkidi de7ishin asa ubbay malaalettidi, Solomone barandda giyason issife enttako woxxidosona.
Phexiroosi asaa be7ida wode asaakko, “Isra7eele asaw, ays hayssan malaaletteti? Woykko ays nuna caddi xeelletii? Nuuni nu wolqqan woykko nu xillotethan ha addiya hamuthidabaa hinttew daanii?
Abrahame, Yisaaqa, Yayqooba Xoossay, nu aawata Xoossay, ba na7aa Yesuusa bonchchis. Shin hintte hayqos aathi immidayssa Philaaxoosi billanaw koyinkka hintte iya sinthan, ‘Nuuni iya erokko’ yaagideta.
Hintte geeshshaanne xilluwaa, ‘Nuuni iya erokko’ gidi, shemppo wodhidayssa hinttew billana mela Philaaxoosa woossideta.
De7uwa immeyssa hintte wodhideta, shin Xoossay hayqoppe iya denthis. Hessas nuuni markka.
Ha hintte be7eysinne eriya addey paxidi minniday Yesuusa sunthan ammanidayssana. Ha hintte ubbaa sinthan iya hayssada pathiday I Yesuusa ammanida gishossa.
“Ha77ika ta ishato, hintteka hinttena kaaletheyssatada, eronna oothidayssa taani erays.
Shin Xoossay beni nabeta ubbaa doonan, ‘Kiristtoosi waaye ekkanaw bessees’ yaagidayssi hayssada polettana mela oothis.
Hiza, Xoossay hintte nagara atto gaana mela Godaakko simmite.
Godaa matappe minthetho wodey hinttew yaana. Xoossay Kiristtoosa gidana mela sinthattidi doorida Yesuusa hinttew yeddana.
Xoossay ba geeshsha nabeta doonan beni odidayssa mela ubbabay ooraxiya wodey gakkanaw Yesuusi salon gam77anaw bessees.
Musey, ‘Godaa Xoossay tana denthidayssa mela hintte giddofe hinttew nabe denthana. Hintte I geyssa ubbaa si7ite.
He nabey odeyssa si7onna asi oonikka asaa giddofe shaakettidi dhayo’ yaagis.
“Qassi Saamu7eelappe doomidi de7iya nabeti ubbay ha wodiyaba odidosona.
Hintte nabeta nayta; qassi Xoossay Abrahames, ‘Sa7an de7iya asa ubbaa taani ne sheeshaa baggara anjjana’ yaagidi nu aawatas gelida qaala laattiya nayta.
Xoossay hinttena ubbaa hintte iita ogiyappe zaaridi anjjana mela ba na7aa denthidi hinttew koyro yeddis” yaagis.
Phexiroosinne Yohaannisi asaas odishin kahine halaqati, Xoossa Keethaa naageyssata halaqaynne Saduqaaweti enttako yidosona.
Entti Yesuusi hayqoppe denddoyssanne iya gaason hayqoppe denddoy de7eyssa asaa tamaarssida gisho yilotidosona.
Hessa gisho, entta oykkidi sa7ay omarssida gisho wonttana gakkanaw qasho keethi gelssidosona.
Shin qaala si7idayssatappe daroti ammanidosona. Ammanida adde asaa tayboy ichchashu mukulukko bis.
Wonttetha gallas deriya haareyssati, cimatinne, higge asttamaareti Yerusalaamen shiiqidosona.
He asa giddon kahine halaqay Haanni, Qayyaafi, Yohaannisi, Iskkinddireynne kahine halaqaa soo asati ubbay de7oosona.
Hawaareta bantta sinthan essidi, “Aybi wolqqan woykko oodde sunthan hayssa hintte oothidetii?” yaagidi oychchidosona.
He wode Phexiroosi Geeshsha Ayyaanan kumidi, “Deriya haareyssato, cimatoo,
hachchi ha wobbe addiyaas oosettida lo77o oosuwasinne I waanidi paxidaakko hintte nuna oychchiko,
masqaliya bolla hintte kaqqin, Xoossay hayqoppe denthida Naazirete Yesuus Kiristtoosa sunthan ha addey paxidi hintte sinthan eqqidayssi hinttewunne Isra7eele asa ubbaas eretto.
‘Gimbbeyssati boridi ixxida shuchchay, godaa xaphuwa minthiya, ubbaafe aadhdhiya shuchchu gidis; he shuchchay Yesuusa.’
Hessa gisho, atotethi iya baggarappe attin hara oodde baggarakka baawa. Nuuni iya sunthan attana mela asa ubbaas Xoossay saloppe garssan immida hara sunthi baawa” yaagis.
Shiiqida asay Phexiroosinne Yohaannisi minnida minotethaa be7ida wode entti tamaariboonna coo asi gididayssa akeekidi malaalettidosona; entti Yesuusara de7eyssa eridosona.
Qassi paxida addey Phexiroosaranne Yohaannisara eqqidayssa asay be7idi giyabaa dhayidosona.
Shin Phexiroosanne Yohaannisa kare keyana mela oothidi bantta giddon,
“Ha asata nu ay oothinoo? Entta kushen oosettida gita malaatay Yerusalaamen de7iya ubbaas benttees. Nuuni hessa erokko gaanaw dandda7okko.
Shin ha oday asaa giddon laalettonna mela hizappe guye ha asati Yesuusa sunthan ooddeskka odonna mela minthidi naagisana” yaagidi zorettidosona.
Entta xeegidi, Yesuusa sunthan hizappe odonna mela woykko tamaarssonna mela kiittidosona.
Shin Phexiroosinne Yohaannisi enttako zaaridi, “Xoossas kiitettanayssafenne hinttew kiitetanayssafe Xoossaa sinthan awussi lo77oko ane hintte pirddite.
Nuuni be7idabaanne si7idabaa odonna agganaw dandda7okko” yaagidosona.
Biitta cimatinne deriya haareyssati kaseppe minthi naagisidi entta yeddi aggidosona. Asay hanidabaas Xoossaa galatiya gisho entta seeranaw dandda7ibookkona.
He malaatan harggiyafe pathida addiyaas laythay oytamappe aadhdhis.
Phexiroosinne Yohaannisi birshshettidi bantta dabbotakko bidi, kahine halaqatinne cimati banttako gidabaa ubbaa enttaw odidosona.
Entti hessa si7ida wode issi wozanan gididi Xoossaa hayssada yaagidi woossidosona: “Ubbaa Haariya Godaw, saluwa, sa7aa, abbaanne entta giddon de7iya ubbabaa medhdhidaysso,
Neeni ne aylliya, nu aawa Dawite doonan Geeshsha Ayyaanan, ‘Derey ays yilotidonaa? Asay ays coo maqettidonaa?
Sa7aa kawotinne deriya haareyssati issife Godaa bollanne Kiristtoosa bolla denddidosona’ yaagadasa.
“Tumakka, Heroodisinne Phenxe Philaaxoosi Ayhude gidonna asaaranne Isra7eele asaara ne doorida ne geeshsha Na7aa Yesuusa bolla denddanaw ha kataman shiiqidosona.
Qassi neeni ne wolqqaaninne ne sheniyan oothana gada qoppa uttidabaa ubbaa polidosona.
Ha77ika Godaw, entta manddethaa be7a; nuuni ne aylleti ne qaala kumetha wozanan odana mela nuna dandda7isa.
Ne geeshsha na7aa Yesuusa sunthan hargganchchota pathanaw, oorathabaynne malaatati oosettana mela ne kushiya micca” gidi woossidosona.
Entti Xoossaa woossidaappe guye he entti shiiqidasoy qaaxxis. Entta ubban Geeshsha Ayyaani kumin Xoossaa qaala minotethan odidosona.
Ammaneysati ubbay qofaninne wozanan issino gididosona. Entti banttaw de7iyabaa tabaa goonnashin issife shaakettoosona.
Hawaarti Godaa Yesuusi hayqoppe denddidayssa gita wolqqan markkattosona. Xoossay entta ubbaas aadho keehatethaa darssidi immis.
Biitti woykko keethi de7eyssati ubbay bayzi ekkida miishiya ehiya gisho ammaneyssata giddon metootanchchoy issoykka baawa.
Miishiya ehidi hawaaretas immoosona; he miishiya issuwas issuwas koshsheyssada shaakki shaakki immees.
Qoophiroosa giya bessan yelettida Yoosefa giya Leewe sheeshaappe gidida issoy de7ees. Iya sunthaa hawaareti Barnnabaasa (Minthetho na7a) gidosona.
Barnnabaasi baw de7iya biittaa bayzidi miishiya ehidi hawaaretas immis.
Issi Hananiya giya addey ba machche Saphphiirira gade bayzis.
He bayzida miishiyappe ba machchiya erishin baggaa ashshidi, attidayssa ehidi hawaaretas immis.
Shin Phexiroosi Hananiyakko, “Neeni Geeshsha Ayyaana cimmana melanne gadiya bayzida miishiyappe shaakkada ashshana mela Xalahey ne wozanan ays gelidee?
Neeni bayzanaappe kase gadey nebaa gidenneyye? Qassi neeni bayza simminkka miishey nebaa gidenneyye? Yaatin, hessa melabaa oothanaw ays ne wozanan qoppadii? Neeni Xoossaa bolla worddotadasappe attin asa bolla worddotabaakka” yaagis.
Hananey he qaala si7ida mela kunddidi hayqqis; hessa si7ida ubbay daro yayyis.
Na7atetha asati soo gelidi iya ahaa xaaxidi efidi moogidosona.
Heedzu saateppe guye Hananiya machchiya hessa eronna de7ashe Phexiroosi de7iyasuwa gelasu.
Phexiroosi iikko, “Hintte gadiya hayssa mela miishes bayzideti? Ane taw oda” yaagis. Iyakka, “Ee, hayssa mela miishes bayzida” yaagasu.
Phexiroosi maccasiw, “Neeranne ne azinaara Godaa Ayyaana paaccanaw ays zorettidetii? Hekko, ne azina moogida asati karen de7oosona; nenakka entti kare kessana” yaagis.
Maccasiya iirakka Phexiroosa tohuwa matan kunddada hayqqa aggasu; na7atethati geliya wode hayqqidaaro demmidi kare kessidi, I azina matan moogidosona.
Kumetha woosa keethaynne hessa si7ida hara asa ubbay daro yayyidosona.
Hawaareti daro malaatatanne oorathabata asaa giddon oothoosona. Ammaniya ubbay Solomone baaranddan issife shiiqosona.
Hara asappe enttara gahettanaw issi asikka minnibeenna, shin asay entta bonchchees.
Ammaniya addetanne maccasata tayboy kaseyssafe darishe bis.
Hessa gisho, asay hargganchchota halaninne alggan tookkidi Phexiroosi aadhdhiya wode iya kuyay enttafe issota issota bolla shemppana mela oge doonan kessidi wothoosona.
Qassi daro asay Yerusalaame matan de7iya katamatappe hargganchchotanne tuna ayyaani waaysiya asata ekkidi yoosona; ubbayka paxidosona.
Kahine halaqaynne iyara de7iya Saduqaaweti ubbay qanaaten kumidi hawaareta bolla denddidosona.
Hawaareta oykkidi deriya qasho keethan yeggidosona.
Shin Godaa kiitanchchoy qamma qasho keethaa penggiya dooyidi hawaareta kare kessidi,
“Bidi, Xoossa Keethan eqqidi ha ooratha de7o qaala asa ubbaas odite” yaagis.
Hawaareti hessa si7ida wode wontta guura Xoossa Keethi gelidi tamaarsso doomidosona. Kahineta halaqaynne iyara de7eyssati yidi, Isra7eele cimata ubbaa xeegi shiishidi hawaareta bantta sinthe ehana mela wotaaddareta qasho keethi kiittidosona.
Shin wotaaddareti qasho keethi bidi hawaareta demmibookkona. Guye simmi yidi deriyas,
“Nuuni biya wode qasho keetha penggey minthi gorddettin, naageyssati penggen eqqidayssata demmida. Shin nuuni kariya dooyaa wode giddon hari attoshin issi asikka baawa” yaagidosona.
Hessa gisho, Xoossa Keethaa wotaaddareta kiitteysinne kahine halaqati hessa si7ida wode “Hawaareta bolla aybi haanidee?” yaagidi hirggidosona.
He wode issi addey enttako yidi, “Hekko, qasho keethi hintte gelssida asati Xoossa Keethan eqqidi asaa tamaarssoosona” yaagidi enttaw odis.
Xoossa Keethaa wotaaddareta kiitteyssi ba wotaaddaretara bidi hawaareta ehis. Shin entti banttana asay shuchchan caddana gidi yayyida gisho entta aaddashidi ehidosona.
Entti hawaareta ehidi, shiiqida shangguwa sinthan essin kahine halaqay enttako,
“Hinttena nuuni he uraa sunthan tamaarssonna mela minthidi kiittibookko? Hekko, hintte timirttiya Yerusalaame katamaa ubbaa gathideta. He uraa shemppuwas nuna oythanaw qoppeeti?” yaagidi oychchis.
Phexiroosaranne hankko hawaaretara enttaw zaarishe, “Nuuni asas kiitettanaappe Xoossas kiitettanaw bessees.
Masqaliya bolla hintte kaqqidi wodhida Yesuusa nu aawata Xoossay hayqoppe denthis.
Isra7eeleti nagaraappe simmana melanne entta nagaray atto geetettana mela Xoossay Yesuusa haareyssanne ashsheyssa oothidi bonchchon baappe ushachcha baggan utisis.
Hessas nuuni markka; qassi Xoossay bana ammaneyssatas immida Geeshsha Ayyaanaykka markka” yaagidosona.
Shiiqida asay hessa si7ida wode daro yilottidi, hawaareta wodhanaw qoppidosona.
Shin asa ubban daro bonchchettida, higge asttamaarey, Gamaaliyale giya issi Farisaawey denddi eqqidi hawaareta guutha wodes kare kessana mela kiittis.
Hessafe guye, shiiqida asaakko, “Isra7eele asaw, ha asata bolla hintte oothanaw qoppiyabaappe naagettite.
Ays giikko, hayssafe kase Tewodaasi bana, ‘Taani gita’ gidi denddin, oyddu xeetu gidiya asati iyara issifidosona. Shin iya wodhin iya kaallida ubbay laalettin pathonna asi gididi attidosona.
Hessafe guye, asay taybettiya wode Galiila Yihudi denddidi daro asa panggayidi kaalethis, shin iyakka wodhin iya kaallida asa ubbay laalettis.
Ha77ika ta hinttew odays; ha asatappe shaakettite; entta bochchofite. Ays giikko, ha qofaanne ha oosuwa asi oothiyabaa gidikko dhayana.
Shin ha qofaynne ha oosoy Xoossafe yidabaa gidikko, hintte entta dhayssanaw dandda7ekketa. Geellada yaanishe hintte Xoossaara kaccettana” yaagidi odis. Hessa gisho, shiiqida asay Gamaaliyale zoriya ekkidosona.
Hawaareta soo xeegidi lisson garaafisis. Hessafe guye, enttako, “Yesuusa sunthaa nam77antho denthofite” gidi birshshi yeddidosona.
Yesuusa sunthaa gisho entti kawuyanayssi bessiyabaa gideyssa erida gisho shangguwa sinthafe ufayttishe keyidosona.
Entti ubba wode Xoossa keethaninne asaa son Yesuusi I Kiristtoosa gideyssa tamaarssonne sabbako aggibookona.
He wode kaalleyssata tayboy dari dari bishin, Girike doona odettiya Ayhudeti Yihudan yelettidi de7iya Ayhudeta bolla zuuzummidosona. Ays giikko, Girike doona odettiya Ayhudeti, “Gallas gallas imettiya kathan nu am77eti naaqettosona” yaagidosona.
Tammanne nam77u hawaareti woosa keethaa asa ubbaa xeegidi, “Nuuni Xoossaa qaala odeyssa aggidi kathi gishanaw nuus bessenna.
Hiza, ishato, lo77o asata, Geeshsha Ayyaananinne cinccatethan kumida laappun asata hintte giddofe doorite; nuuni entta ha oosuwas shuumana.
Shin nuuni, nu kumetha wodiya Xoossaa woosaninne qaala tamaarsson peeshshana” yaagidosona.
Hawaareti odida oday asa ubbaa ufayssis. Hessa gisho, ammanoynne Geeshsha Ayyaani kumida Isxifaanose, Filphoosa, Phirokoroosa, Niqaarone, Ximoona, Pharmmeenanne Ayhude ammano geli simmida Anxookiya Niqolawoosa dooridosona.
Entta hawaareta sinthan essin, hawaareti entta bolla kushe wothidi Xoossaa woossidosona.
Xoossaa qaalay dalggi dalggi bis. Yerusalaamen de7iya ammaneyssata tayboy dari dari bis; daro kahinetikka ammanidosona.
Isxifaanosey aadho keehatethaaninne wolqqan kumidi asaa giddon oorathabatanne malaatata oothees.
Aylletethafe keyida Ayhude Woosa Keetha asay Qereenappenne Iskkinddiriyappe Kilqiyafenne Iisiyappe yida issi issi asati denddidi Isxifaanosera palamidosona.
Shin Isxifaanosey Ayyaana wolqqan odettiya cinccatethaa entti eqettanaw dandda7ibookkona.
He wode entti, “Musenne Xoossaa I cayishin si7ida” giya worddo asata shammidosona.
Hessada oothidi biitta cimatanne higge asttamaareta iya bolla denthidosona. Isxifaanose oykkidi Shangguwa sinthe efidosona.
Iya bolla paydida worddo markkati, “Ha uray ha Xoossa Keethanne Muse higgiya zaari zaari cayees.
I, ‘Hayssi Naazirete Yesuusi, ha Xoossa Keethaa laallana; qassi Musey nuus immida higgiya laammana’ yaagishin nuuni si7ida” yaagidosona.
Shanggo shiiqon uttida asa ubbay Isxifaanose loythidi xeelliya wode iya som77oy kiitanchcho som77o daanees.
Kahineta halaqay Isxifaanosekko, “Hayssi tumee?” yaagidi oychchis.
Isxifaanosey, “Ta ishato, ta aawato, si7ite! Nu aawa Abrahamey Kaaranen daanaw baanappe sinthe Masephexoomiyan de7ishin, bonchcho Xoossay iyaw qonccidi,
‘Ne biittaafenne ne dabbotappe shaakettada taani nena bessiya biittaa ba’ yaagis.
He wode Abrahamey Kalddaaweta biittaafe keyidi Kaaranen daanaw bis. Iya aaway hayqqidaappe guye Xoossay iya ha biittaa ha77i hintte de7iya bessaa ehis.
I ha biittaafe hari attoshin tohoy yedhdhiya bessika Abrahames immibeenna. Shin na7i iyaw baynna wode Xoossay ha biittaa iyawunne iya sheeshaas laata oothidi immanayssa qaala gelis.
Xoossay Abrahamekko, ‘Ne sheeshay hara biittan imathatethan daana; yan oyddu xeetu laythi entti aylletethan haarettana.
Shin taani ne sheeshaa haariya deriya bolla pirddana. Hessafe guye, entti he biittaafe keyidi hayssan taw goynnana’ yaagis.
Xoossay Abrahame sheeshay qaxxarettana mela iyara caaqqin, Yisaaqi yelettida hosppuntha gallasan qaxxaris. Yisaaqi Yayqooba qaxxaris; qassi Yayqoobi tammanne nam77u ba nayta, nu aawata mayzata qaxxaris.
“Yayqooba nayti Yoosefa qanaattidi Gibxxe biittan aylletethas bayzidosona, shin Xoossay iyara de7ees.
Iya, iya waaye ubbaafe kessis. Gibxxe kawuwa sinthan sabanne cinccatethi iyaw immis. Gibxxe kawoy Yoosefas Gibxxe biittaanne ba keetha ubbaa aysanaada halaqatethi immis.
“Gibxxe biittaninne Kanaane biitta ubban koshi gelidi daro asaa un77ethis. He wode nu mayzati kathi demmanaw dandda7ibookkona.
Yayqoobi Gibxxe biittan kathi de7eyssa si7idi nu aawata koyro yaa yeddis.
Nam77antho buussan Yoosefi ba ishatas banatethaa erisis. Gibxxe kawoykka Yoosefa sheeshaa eris.
Yoosefi ba aawa Yayqoobanne ba dabbo ubbaa, laappun tammanne ichchashu asaa baakko yaana mela kiittidi ehisis.
Yayqoobi Gibxxe biittaa wodhdhis; inne iya nayti yan hayqqidosona.
Entta ahay he bessaafe Seekeme biittaa tookettidi bidi, yan Abrahamey Hamoore naytappe daro biran shammida duufon moogettis.
“Shin Xoossay Abrahames immana gidayssa poliya wodey gakkanaw matida wode Gibxxe biittan de7iya nu asay dari dari bis.
Hessafe guye, Yoosefa eronna hara kawoy Gibxxe biittan kawotis.
He kawoy nu zerethaa genidi guutha nayti hayqqana mela entta kare kessi yeggana mela nu aawata un77ethis.
“He wode Musey yelettis; I Xoossaa sinthan daro lo77o na7a. Ba aawa keethan heedzu ageena gakkanaw diccis.
Musey wora holettida wode Gibxxe kawuwa na7iya demma ekkada ba na7a oothada iya dichchasu.
Musey Gibxxeta cinccatetha ubbaa tamaaridi odaninne ooson mino asi gidis.
“Muses laythay oytama kumida wode ba ishata, Isra7eeleta be7anaw ba wozanan qoppis.
Isra7eelatappe issuwa Gibxxe issoy qohishin be7idi he Isra7eele uraa maaddidi, he qohida Gibxxe uraa wodhidi kushe zaaris.
Musey ba ishata ba baggara Xoossay ashshanaw haneyssa entti akeekana gidi qoppis, shin entti akeekibookkona.
“Wonttetha gallas nam77u Isra7eele asati issoy issuwara wadhettishin demmidi entta sigethanaw koyidi, ‘Asato, hintte ishantta; ays issoy issuwa qohetii?’ yaagis.
“Shin ba laggiya qoheyssi Musekko, ‘Nena nu bolla haareyssanne daynna oothiday oonee?
Neeni zine Gibxxe uraa wodhidayssada tana wodhanaw koyay?’ yaagidi Muse sugi yeddis.
Musey hessa si7ida wode Gibxxefe betidi Miidiyaame biittan bete asi gididi de7ishe nam77u adde nayta yelis.
“Godaa kiitanchchoy oytamu laythafe guye Siina Deriya matan de7iya bazzo tushiya giddon eexiya tama laco giddon Muses benttis.
Musey ba be7idayssan malaalettidi, loythi be7anaw tushiya mati shiiqidi de7ishin, Godaa qaalay,
‘Taani ne aawata, Abrahame Xoossaa, Yisaaqa Xoossaa, Yayqooba Xoossaa’ yaagishe Musekko yis. Musey yashshan kokkoridi xeellanaw dandda7ibeenna.
“Goday Musekko, ‘Neeni eqqida biittay geeshshi gidiya gisho ne tohuwan de7iya caammaa kessa.
Taani Gibxxen de7iya ta asaa un77etethaa be7as. Entta waasuwa si7ada entta ashshanaw wodhdhas. Ha77i haaya! Taani nena Gibxxe kiittana’ yaagis.
“Isra7eeleti Muse, ‘Nena nuna haareyssanne daynna oothiday oonee?’ yaagidi ixxidayssa tushiya giddon iyaw benttida kiitanchchuwa baggara haareyssanne ashsheyssa oothidi Xoossay kiittis.
Musey Isra7eeleta Gibxxefe kessidi malaalisiyabatanne oorathabata Gibxxe biittaninne Zo7o Abban oothidi entta oytamu laythi bazzo biittan kaalethis.
“Isra7eele asaakko, ‘Xoossay tana denthidayssada hintte sheeshaa giddofe ta mela nabe hinttew denthana’ yaagiday he Muse.
Bazzo biittan shiiqida Isra7eele asaara de7idayssi, nu aawataranne Siina Deriya bolla iyaw odida kiitanchchuwara de7ida Musey iya. Yaatidi, Xoossaa de7o qaala nuus immanaw ekkis.
“Shin nu mayzati Muses kiitettanaw dosibookkona; iya ixxidi guye Gibxxe simmanaw amottidosona.
Qassi Aaronakko, ‘Nuna kaalethiya xoossata nuus ootha. Ays giikko, hayssi nuna Gibxxefe ehida Musey, waanidaakko nuuni erokko’ yaagidosona.
He wode mari daanisidi eeqa oothidosona. He eeqaas yarshsho yarshshidi bantta kushen oothida oosuwan ufayttidosona.
Shin Xoossay enttaw zokko zaaris. Entti salo xoolinttota goynnana mela entta yeggi aggis. Nabeta maxaafan, ‘Isra7eele asaw, oytamu laythi kumethi bazzo biittan shukkida mehiyanne yarshshida yarshshuwa taw yarshshidetii?
Hinttee, hinttew goynnanaw kessida eeqaanne Moloke dunkkaaniya Refaana giya hintte xoossaa xoolintto misiliya tookkideta. Taani hinttena Baabilooneppe hini bagga yeddana’ geetettidi xaafettis.
“Nu aawatas bazzo biittan markka dunkkaaney de7ees. Iyakka Xoossay Muse kiittidayssadanne iya bessidayssada oothis.
Qassi nu aawati he dunkkaaniya bantta aawatappe ekkidi Xoossay kase yedethida Ayhude gidonna asaa biittaa oykkida wode Iyyaasura yaa ekkidi gelidosona. He dunkkaaney Dawite wode gakkanawukka he bessan de7is.
Dawitey Xoossan sabettis. Qassi Yayqooba Goday de7ana keethaa keexanaw Xoossaa woossis.
Shin iyaw keethaa keexiday Solomone.
“Hanoshin, Ubbaafe Bolla Xoossay asi keexida keethan deenna. Nabey gidayssa mela,
‘Saloy ta araata, sa7aykka ta tohoy yedhdhiyaso. Yaatin, taw hintte ay mela keethi keexanee? Woykko taani shemppiyasoy awunee?
Ha ubbaa ta kushiyan oothabiikkinaa?’ yaagees Goday.
“Hintte waanida si7onna asee? Hintte wozanay Xoossaa qaala ekkanaw ays ixxide? Hintte haythay ays tullidee? Hinttee, hintte aawatatho ubba wode Geeshsha Ayyaanaara eqetteeta.
Nabeta giddofe hintte aawati gooddonnay oonee? Xoossaa Na7ay, Xilloy yaanayssa kasetidi odidayssata wodhidosona. Ha77i hintte iya aathi immidi wodhideta.
Hintte kiitanchchuwa kusheppe Xoossaa higgiya ekkideta, shin kiitettibeekketa” yaagis.
Entti hessa si7ida wode bantta wozanan Isxifaanose bolla daro yilottidi, bantta mettershshaa saxxidi manddidosona.
Shin Isxifaanosey Geeshsha Ayyaanan kumidi, salo pude xeellidi, Xoossaa bonchchuwanne Yesuusa Xoossaa ushachcha baggan eqqidayssa be7is.
“Hekko, taani saloy dooyettin, Asa Na7ay, Xoossaa ushachcha baggan eqqidayssa be7ays” yaagis.
Qaalaa dhoqqu oothidi waassishe, bantta haythaa oykkidi issife iyaakko woxxidosona
Iya katamaappe gaxa kessidi, shuchchan caddidosona. Markkati bantta ma7uwa issi Saa7ola giya na7atethaa matan wothidosona.
Isxifaanosey, “Ta Godaa Yesuusaa, ta shemppuwa ekka” yaagidi xeegishin entti iya shuchchan caddoosona.
Gulbbatidi, ba qaala dhoqqu oothidi, “Ta Godaw, ha nagaraa enttaw atto ga” yaagis. Hessa yaagidi simmida mela hayqqi aggis.
Saa7oli Isxifaanose hayquwan ufayttis. He gallas Yerusalaamen de7iya woosa keethan gita goodi denddis. Hawaareti attin ammaneyssati ubbay Yihuda biittaninne Samaare biittan laalettidosona.
Issi issi Xoossaa asati Isxifaanose moogidosona; qassi iyaw daro yeekkidosona.
Shin Saa7oli woosa keethaa dhayssanaw koyees. Soo soo yuuyi gelidi, ammaniyaa addetanne maccasata goochchi goochchi kessidi qasho keethi gelssees.
Laalettida ammaneyssati bida bessa ubban qaala odidosona.
Filphoosi Samaare katamaa bidi Kiristtoosabaa asaas odis.
Daro asay Filphoosi gidayssa si7ida wodenne I oothiya malaatata be7ida wode iya akeekidi si7idosona.
Tuna ayyaanati waassidi daro asaappe keyidosona; qassi daro gunddatinne wobbeti bilettidosona.
He kataman de7iya asay daro ufayttidosona.
Shin Simoona giya issi uray he kataman de7ees. I, ‘Bana gita’ gidi Samaare asaa marotethan malaalisishe gam77is.
Guuthafe gita gakkanaw de7iya asa ubbay, “Gita Xoossaa wolqqay hayssa” gidi iyabaa si77oosona.
Daro wodeppe doomidi marotishe Samaare asaa malaalisida gisho asay iyabaa si7oosona.
Shin Filphoosi Xoossaa kawotethaabaanne Yesuus Kiristtoosa sunthabaa addetasinne maccatas odin, entti iyabaa ammanidi xammaqettidosona.
Qassi Simoonikka ba huu7en ammanidi xammaqettis. Filphoosara issife bida bessa ubban oosettiya gita malaatata be7idi malaalettis.
Yerusalaamen de7iya hawaareti Samaare asay Xoossaa qaala ekkidayssa si7ida wode Phexiroosanne Yohaannisa enttako yeddidosona.
Phexiroosinne Yohaannisi bidi, ammaneyssati Geeshsha Ayyaana ekkana mela enttaw Xoossaa woossidosona.
Ays giikko, Samaare asati Godaa Yesuusa sunthaa xalaalan xammaqettidosonappe attin enttafe issuwa bollaka Geeshsha Ayyaani wodhdhibeenna.
He wode Phexiroosinne Yohaannisi bantta kushiya entta bolla wothin, entti Geeshsha Ayyaana ekkidosona.
Hawaareti bantta kushiya entta bolla wothin, enttaw Geeshsha Ayyaanay imettidayssa Simooni be7ida wode Phexiroosasinne Yohaannisas miishe ehidi,
“Taanikka ta kushiya wothiya ubbay Geeshsha Ayyaana ekkana mela ha maata tawukka immerkketi” yaagis.
Shin Phexiroosi iyaakko, “Neeni Xoossaa imotaa miishen shammanaw qoppida gisho ne miishey neera dhayo.
Ne wozanay Xoossaa sinthan suure gidonna gisho new hayssan gishoy woykko qaadi baawa.
Hiza, ha ne wozanaa iitatethaa gisho nagaraappe simma. Ne wozanan de7iya iita qofaa Xoossay atto gaana mela Xoossaa woossa.
Gaasoykka, neeni iita qanaateninne nagara qashuwan de7eyssa taani be7ays” yaagis.
Simooni zaaridi, “Hintte gidayssafe issoykka tana gakkonna mela taw Xoossaa woossite” yaagis.
Phexiroosinne Yohaannisi markkattidaappenne Godaa qaala odidaappe guye Yerusalaame simmidosona. Samaaren de7iya daro gutatan Wonggelaa odidosona.
Godaa kiitanchchoy Filphoosakko, “Denddada Yerusalaameppe Gaaza efiya bazzo biitta ogiyakko ba. He ogey dugeha baggara de7ees” yaagis.
Filphoosi denddidi bis. Hinddeke giya Tophphiya kawees I miishe ubbaa naagiya Tophphiya asi de7ees. Ikka goynnanaw Yerusalaame bis.
Para gaariyan uttidi, Yerusalaameppe ba biittaa simmishe nabiya Isayaasa maxaafaa nabbabees.
Geeshsha Ayyaanay Filphoosakko, “He gaariyakko bada iya mati shiiqa” yaagis.
Yaatin Filphoosi woxxi bidi gakkiya wode moorinnay nabiya Isayaasa maxaafappe nabbabishin si7idi, “Ne nabbabeyassi new geli?” yaagis.
Moorinnay, “Taw odi gelssiya asi baynna waanidi gelanee?” yaagis. Baara gaariyan keyidi uttana mela Filphoosa woossis.
Moorinnay nabbabiya maxaafaa kifiley, “I dorssada shukettanaw laagettis; Dorssa mari ba ikisiya meedeyssata sinthan si77i geyssada, ikka ba doona dooyibeena.
I kawuyis; iyaw xillo pirddi dhays. iya de7oy ha sa7aappe qanxettida gisho iya sheeshaabaa oone odanay?” yaagees.
Moorinnay zaaridi Filphoosakko, “Nabey odebaa odi? Babaa odiyye woykko hara asabaa odi? Taw odarkkii” yaagis.
Filphoosi zaaridi, Xoossaa qaala he bessaafe doomidi, Yesuusabaa odiya Wonggelaa iyaw odis.
Entti bishe haathi de7iyaso gakkidosona. Moorinnay, “Haathe hayssa be7a; ta xammaqettonna mela aybi diggii?” yaagis.
Filphoosi iyaakko, “Neeni ne kumetha wozanaappe ammanikko dandda7aasa” yaagis. I zaaridi, “Yesuus Kiristtoosi Xoossaa Na7aa gideyssa taani ammanays” yaagis.
Gaarey eqqana mela moorinnay kiittin, nam77ay wodhdhidi haathan gelidosona; Filphoosi iya xammaqis.
Entti haathaafe gaxa keyida wode Godaa ayyaanay Filphoosa qopponna ekkis. Nam77antho moorinnay Filphoosa be7ibeenna, shin ba ogiya ufayttishe bis.
Filphoosi Azaaxonan bana demmis. Qassi Qisaariya yaana gakkanaw katamatan yuuyidi Wonggelaa markkattis.
He wode Saa7oli Godaa kaalleyssata wodhanaw manddidi kahine halaqaakko bis.
Godaa ogiya kaalliya addetanne maccata demmiko, qachchishe Yerusalaame ehanaw, Damasqqon de7iya Ayhude Woosa Keethatas dabddaabbey xaafettana mela iya woossis.
I bidi, Damasqqo katamaa gakkanaw matishin, qopponna saloppe wolqqaama poo7oy iya yuushuwan poo7is.
I sa7an kunddidashin, “Saa7olaa, Saa7olaa, ays tana goodday?” giya qaala si7is.
Saa7oli, “Godaw, neeni oonee?” yaagidi oychchis. “Taani, neeni gooddiya Yesuusa” yaagis.
Shin Saa7oli kokkorishenne malaalettishe, “Godaw, taani ay oothana mela koyay?” yaagis. Goday iyaakko, “Denddada katamaa gela; neeni oothanaw bessiyabay yan new odettana” yaagis.
Saa7olara ogiya biya asati aykkoka odettonna eqqi attidosona. Qaalaa si7oosona, shin oonakka be7ibookkona.
Saa7oli kunddida bessaafe denddidi xeelliya wode iya ayfey demmonna ixxis. Hessa gisho, entti iya kushiya oykkidi kaalethidi Damasqqo gelssidosona.
Heedzu gallas gakkanaw I xeellanaw dandda7ibeenna; aykkoka mibeenna; uyibeenna.
Damasqqon issi Hananiya giya Yesuusa tamaarey de7ees. Goday qonccethan, “Hananiya” yaagidi xeegis. Hananey zaaridi, “Ta Godaw, hayssan de7ays” yaagis.
Goday iyaakko, “Denddada Suure geetettiya ogiya bada, Yihuda son Saa7ola giya terseseppe yida uraa koya; Saa7oli woossees.
Qassi Hananey gelidi, Saa7oli nam77antho xeellana mela ba kushiya iya bolla wothishin qonccethan be7is” yaagis.
Hananey zaaridi, “Godaw, Yerusalaamen ne geeshsha asaa bolla he uray ay mela iitabaa oothidaakko taani daro asaappe si7as.
Qassi Damasqqon ne sunthaa xeegeyssata ubbaa qachchanaw, kahine halaqati iyaw maata immidosona” yaagis.
Shin Goday iyaakko, “Saa7oli Ayhude gidonna asaa sinthan, kawota sinthaninne Isra7eele asaa sinthan, ta sunthaa erisanawunne taw oothanaw doorettida miishe gidiya gisho neeni iyaakko ba.
Ays giikko, ta sunthaa gisho I ay mela waaye ekkanaw bessiyako taani iya bessana” yaagis.
Hananey bidi, soo gelidi, ba kushiya Saa7ola bolla wothidi, “Ta ishaa Saa7ola, neeni yaa ogiyan new benttida Godaa Yesuusi, neeni xeellana melanne Geeshsha Ayyaanan kumana mela tana kiittis” yaagis.
Ellesidi, Saa7ola ayfiyaappe issi poqo melabay wodhdhin, Saa7oli nam77antho xeellis. Qassi denddidi xammaqettis.
Kathi midi xaalidi, Damasqqon de7iya ammaneyssatara guutha gallas gam77is.
Ellesidi Saa7oli, “Yesuusi Xoossaa Na7a” yaagidi Damasqqon de7iya Ayhude Woosa Keethatan qaala tamaarssis.
Hessa si7ida ubbay malaalettidi, “Hayssi Yerusalaamen Yesuusa sunthaa xeegeyssata qachcheyssa gidenneyye? Qassi haa yiday entta qachchidi, kahine halaqata sinthe efanaassa gidennee?” yaagidosona.
Shin Saa7oli qaala odon minni minni bis. Yesuusi, I Kiristtoosa gideyssa qonccisidi odida gisho Damasqqon de7iya Ayhudeti iyaw zaariyaba dhayidosona.
Daro gallasappe guye Ayhudeti shiiqidi, Saa7ola wodhanaw zorettidosona.
Shin Ayhudeti bana wodhanaw qoppidayssa Saa7oli si7is. Entti iya wodhanaw qammanne gallas katamaa penggiyan naagoosona.
Shin iya tamaareti iya qamma efidi, gimbbe dirssaa maskkotiyara daachchora wodhisidosona.
Saa7oli Yerusalaame gakkida wode ammaneyssatara gahettanaw koyis. Shin I Kiristtoosa ammanidayssi enttaw tuma daanonna ixxin iyaw yayyidosona.
Shin Barnnabaasi Saa7ola hawaaretakko efis. Ogen Goday waanidi qonccidaakkonne haasayisidaakko, qassi Saa7oli Damasqqon Yesuusa sunthan yayyonna waattidi qaala odidaakko enttaw geeshshidi odis.
Saa7oli Yerusalaamen yuuyidi Godaa sunthan yayyonna qaala odishe, hawaaretara issife de7is.
Qassi Saa7oli Girike qaala haasayaa Ayhudetara odettishe palamees. Shin entti iya wodhanaw koyidosona.
Ammaniya asati hessa si7idi, Saa7ola Qisaariya efidi Terseese yeddidosona.
Yihudan, Galiilaninne Samaare ubban de7iya woosa keethati sarotethaan de7idosona. Qassi minnidosona; Godaas yayyishe Geeshsha Ayyaana minthethuwan dari dari bidosona.
Phexiroosi biitta ubbaa yuuyishe Liidan de7iya ammaniyaa asatakko gakkis.
Yan hosppun laythi kumethi gunddidi arssan zin77idi de7iya Eeniya giya addiya demmis.
Phexiroosi, “Eeniya, Yesuus Kiristtoosi nena pathana; denddada ne hiixa dentha” yaagis. Ikka ellesidi denddi eqqis.
Liidaninne Saaronan de7iya asa ubbay Eeniya be7idi, Godaakko simmidosona.
Yoophe kataman issi Xaabito giya ammaniyaara de7awusu. (Xaabito guussay gen77e guussu) Iya ba de7ida wode ubban lo77obaa oothashenne manqota maaddashe de7asu.
He wode iya harggada hayqqin, asay I ahaa meeccidi, pooqiya bolla kessidi zin77isidosona.
Liidi Yoophes mata. Ammaneyssati Phexiroosi Liidan de7eyssa si7idi, “Hayyana nuukko ellessada ya” yaagiya kiitaa nam77u asata bolla iyaakko kiittidosona.
Hessa gisho, Phexiroosi denddidi, enttara bis. Yaa gakkin, pooqiya bolla de7iya kifiliya iya gelssidosona. Am77eti Phexiroosa yuushuwan eqqidi yeekkishe Dorqqa enttara paxa de7ashe oothida qamisetanne afilata ubbaa Phexiroosa bessidosona.
Phexiroosi entta ubbaa kare kessidi, gulbbatidi Xoossaa woossis. Qassi ahaako simmidi, “Xaabite, dendda” yaagis. Xaabita ba ayfiyaa dooyada Phexiroosa be7ada, dendda uttasu.
Phexiroosi iyo ba kushiyan maaddidi denthi essis. Hessafe guye, ammaneyssatanne am77eta xeegidi, denddidaaro entta sinthe shiishis.
Ha oday Yoophe katama ubbaa gakkis. Daro asay Godaa ammanidosona.
Phexiroosi Yoophen Simoona giya galbba haasheyssa son daro gallas gam77is.
Qisaariyan, “Xaale ola asata” geetettiya olanchchota giddon issi Qornneliyoosa geetettiya mato halaqay de7ees.
Qornneliyoosi ba soo asaara Xoossaa minthi ammaniyaa asinne Xoossaa goynniya asi. Ayhude manqotakka daro maaddees, qassi Xoossaa ubba wode woossees.
Issi gallas uddufun saate heeran Xoossaa kiitanchchoy iyaakko yidi, “Qornneliyoosaa” gidi xeegishin I qonccethan geeshshidi be7is.
Qornneliyoosi dagammidi kiitanchchuwa tishshi oothi xeellidi, “Godaw, I aybee?” yaagis. Kiitanchchoy zaaridi, “Ne woosaynne manqota ne maaddeyssi Xoossaa sinthan hassayettis.
Ha77i Yoophe ase kiittada, Phexiroosa giya Simoona ehisa.
Phexiroosi abbaa doonan galbba haashiya Simoona son imathatethi siiratis” yaagis.
Qornneliyoosi baw odida kiitanchchoy bin, ba aylletappe nam77atanne Xoossaa goynniya ba mata wotaaddaretappe issuwa xeegidi,
enttaw ubbabaa odidi Yoophe kiittis.
Wonttetha gallas entti bidi, Yoophe katama matishin usuppun saate heeran Xoossaa woossanaw Phexiroosi pooqe bolla keys.
I koshattidi kathi maanaw koyis, shin kathi kaxishin I qonccethi be7is.
Saloy dooyettin, gita afila daaniyabay oyddu baggara oykettidi wodhdhishin I be7is.
Iyan oyddu tohora de7iya meheti, wora do7ati, ulora gooshettiya medhetethatinne salo kafoti ubbay de7ees.
He wode “Phexiroosaa, dendda eqqada shukkada ma” giya qaali iyaakko yis.
Shin Phexiroosi, “Godaw, akkay! Ta tunabaa ubbarakka ma erikke” yaagis.
Qassi, “Xoossay geeshshidayssa neeni tuna gooppa” giya qaali nam77antho iyaakko yis.
Hessika, heedzu toho hanidaappe guye he gita afila daaneyssi ellesidi pude salo ekettis.
Phexiroosi ba be7ida qonccethaa birshshethay, “Ay gidanddeshsha?” gidi ba wozanan qoppishin, Qornneliyoosi kiittida asati Simoona soo oychchi demmidi karen eqqidosona.
Bantta qaala dhoqqu oothidi, “Phexiroosa giya Simooni imathatethan de7ey hayssanee?” yaagidi oychchidosona.
Phexiroosi qonccethan be7idabaa qofa bolla de7ishin, Geeshsha Ayyaani iyaakko, “Hekko, heedzu asati nena koyoosona.
Denddada wodhdha, taani entta kiittida gisho sidhonna enttara ba” yaagis.
Phexiroosi asatakko wodhdhidi, “Hintte koyey tana; ays yidetii?” yaagis.
Entti zaaridi, “Nuna mato halaqay Qornneliyoosi kiittis. I xillo, Xoossaa goynniya asinne Ayhude asa ubban daro bonchchettida asi. Qornneliyoosi, nena ba soo ehisidi qaala neeppe si7ana mela geeshsha kiitanchchoy iyaw odis” yaagidosona.
Phexiroosi asata soo gelssidi mokkis. Wonttetha gallas, denddidi enttara bis. Yoophe kataman de7iya ammaneyssatappe issoti issoti iyara issife bidosona.
Wonttetha gallas, Qisaariya gakkidosona. Qornneliyoosi ba dabbotanne ba mata laggeta issife xeegi shiishidi, Phexiroosa naagees.
Phexiroosi soo gelana hanishin, Qornneliyoosi iyara gahettidi iya sinthan kunddidi iyaw goynnanaw koyis.
Shin Phexiroosi, “Dendda, takka ta huu7en ne mela ase” yaagidi iya denthis.
Phexiroosi Qornneliyoosara odettishe soo geliya wode daro asay shiiqidayssa demmis.
I asaakko, “Ayhude asi hara derera issifanaw woykko gahettanaw woga gidonnayssa hintte ereeta. Shin taani oonakka tuna woykko geeshshi gidenna goonna mela Xoossay tana bessis.
Hessa gisho, hintte taakko kiittin ixoy baynna yas. Ha77i tana ays xeegisidaakko taw odite” yaagis.
Qornneliyoosi, “Taani hachchi oyddu gallasappe kase hannoode uddufun saate woosa woossishin, phooliya ma7o ma77ida asi ta sinthan eqqis.
I taakko, ‘Qornneliyoosa, Xoossay ne woosaa si7is, neeni manqota maaddidayssaka hassays.
Hiza, ase Yoophe kiittada, Simoon Phexiroosa geyssa xeegisa. I, Simoona giya galbba haashiya uraa son abbaa doonan siiratis’ yaagis.
Hessa gisho, taani neekko ellesada kiittas; ne lo77o yadasa. Hiza, Xoossay nena Kiittidaba ubbaa si7anaw ha77i nuuni ubbay hayssan Godaa sinthan de7oos” yaagis.
Kaallidikka, Phexiroosi, “Xoossay asa som77o be7idi ase asappe shaakkenna.
Shin ase ubbaa oona gidikkoka baw yayyeyssanne xillo ooso ootheyssan Xoossay ufaytteyssa taani tuma akeekas.
Xoossay, ubbaa Goda gidida Yesuus Kiristtoosa baggara sarotethaa odishe ha Wonggelaa Isra7eele asaas kiittidayssa hintte ereeta.
Yohaannisi xinqqatebaa Galiilan sabbakida wodiyappe doomidi Yihuda biitta ubbaa gakkanaw hanidabaa hintte ereeta.
Xoossay Naazirete Yesuusas Geeshsha Ayyaananne wolqqaa immis. Xoossay iyara de7iya gisho lo77obaa I oothishe Xalahe kushen haarettida ubbaa pathishe yuuyis.
“Ayhude biittaninne Yerusalaamen I oothida ubbabaas nuuni markkatta. Entti masqaliya bolla kaqqidi iya wodhidosona.
Shin Xoossay heedzantho gallasan hayqoppe iya denthidi asaas qonccana mela oothis.
He qonccethay Xoossay koyro doorida markkatassafe attin asa ubbaas gidenna. I hayqoppe denddidaappe guye iyara midanne uyida.
Nuuni Wonggelaa asaas odana melanne paxa de7eyssata bollanne hayqqidayssata bolla pirddanaw Xoossay shuumiday Yesuusa gideyssa markkattana mela nuna kiittis.
Xoossay iya ammaniyaa ubbaa nagaray, iya sunthan atto geetetteyssa nabeti markkattoosona” yaagis.
Phexiroosi buroo he oda onggonnashin qaala si7iya ubbaa bolla Geeshsha Ayyaani wodhdhis.
Phexiroosara Yoophefe yida ammaniyaa qaxxarettida Ayhude ubbay, Ayhude gidonnayssata bolla Geeshsha Ayyaani gukkida gisho malaalettidosona.
Gaasoykka, entti dumma dumma doonan haasayishininne Xoossaa gitatethaa sabbishin si7idosona. He wode Phexiroosi zaaridi,
“Hayssati qassi nu mela Geeshsha Ayyaana ekkidayssati xammaqettonna mela haathe digganay oonee?” yaagis.
Entti Yesuus Kiristtoosa sunthan xammaqettana mela entta kiittis. Hessafe guye, entti banttara guutha gallas uttana mela Phexiroosa woossidosona.
Hawaaretinne Yihuda ubban de7iya ammaneyssati, Ayhude gidonnayssatikka Xoossaa qaala ekkidayssa si7idosona.
Phexiroosi Yerusalaame bida wode qaxxarettida ammaneyssati,
iyaakko, “Neeni qaxxarettiboonayssatakko gelada enttara kathi ays madii?” yaagidosona.
Shin Phexiroosi hanidabaa koyroppe doomidi maaran maaran odis:
“Taani Yoophe kataman Xoossaa woossashe qonccethi be7as. Gita afila daaniyabay oyddu baggara oykettidi saloppe wodhdhishe taakko yis.
Taani tishshi ootha iya giddo xeelliya wode oyddu tohora de7iya meheta, wora do7ata, ulora gooshettiya medhetethatanne salo kafota be7as.
‘Phexiroosaa, dendda, shukkada ma’ giya qaala si7as.
“Shin taani, ‘Godaw, akkay, tunabay woykko geeyonnabay ubbaka ta doonaakko shiiqi erenna’ yaagas.
“ ‘Xoossay geeshshidayssa neeni tuna gooppa’ yaagiya qaali nam77antho saloppe yis.
“Hessi heedzu toho hanin, wurssethan ubbabay salo pude ekettis.
He saatenkka heedzu asati Qisaariyappe taakko kiitettidi taani de7iya keetha gakki aggidosona.
Sidhonna enttara baana mela Ayyaanai taw odis. Qassi ha usuppun ishati Yoophefe taara Qisaariya bidayssatara Qornneliyoosa soo gelida.
Kiitanchchoy iya son eqqidi, ‘Yoophe kiittada Phexiroosa geetettiya Simoona xeegisa.
Nenanne ne soo asa ubbaa ashshiya qaala I new odana’ gidayssa Qornneliyoos nuus odis.
“Taani haasaya doomiya wode Geeshsha Ayyaanay koyro nu bolla wodhdhidayssada entta bollaka wodhdhi aggis.
He wode ‘Yohaannisi haathan xammaqis, shin hintte Geeshsha Ayyaanan xammaqettana’ yaagida Godaa qaalay taw qofettis.
Xoossay nuus Godaa Yesuus Kiristtoosa ammanidayssatas immida imotaa Ayhude gidonnayssataska immiko, yaatin Xoossaa digganaw taani oonee?” yaagis.
Entti hessa si7ida wode bantta palamaa aggidi, “Hesaa gidikko, Xoossay Ayhude gidonnayssatikka nagarappe simmidi de7on daanada qaada immis” yaagidi Xoossaa galatidosona.
Isxifaanose hayqos gathida gooda gaason laalettida ammaneyssati qaala Ayhudeta xalaalas odishe Siroofinqe, Qoophiroosanne Anxookiya gakkanaw yuuyidosona.
Shin Qoophiroosappenne Qereenaappe yida issi issi ammaniyaa asati Anxookiya bidi, Godaa Yesuusa Wonggelaa Girike asaaskka odidosona.
Godaa wolqqay enttara de7ees; qassi daro asay ammanidi Godaakko simmidosona.
He odaa Yerusalaamen de7iya woosa keethay si7ida gisho Barnnabaasa Anxookiya kiittis.
Barnnabaasi Anxookiya bida wode Xoossaa aadho keehatethaa oosuwa be7idi ufayttis. Entti ubbay bantta kumetha wozanan Godan minnidi daana mela entta zoris.
Barnnabaasi Geeshsha Ayyaanaynne ammanoy kumida lo77o asi gidiya gisho daro asay Godaa ammanidosona.
Hessafe guye, Barnnabaasi Saa7ola koyanaw Terseese bis.
Yan Saa7ola demmida wode Anxookiya ekkidi yis. Barnnabaasinne Saa7oli woosa keetha asaara laythi kumethi uttidi daro asaa tamaarssidosona. Ammaneyssati Anxookiyan “Kiristtaane” geetettidi koyro xeegettidosona.
He wode issi issi nabeti Yerusalaameppe Anxookiya wodhdhidosona.
Entta giddofe Agaboosa geyssi denddidi biitta ubban gita koshi keyanayssa Ayyaana wolqqan tinbbite odis. Hessi haniday Roome Kawuwa Qalawudiyoosa wodena.
Ammaneyssati huu7en huu7en bantta wolqqaa mela miishe kessidi Yihudan de7iya ammaneyssatas maade yeddanaw qofa qachchidosona.
Entti hessada oothidi, miishiya Barnnabaasa bollanne Saa7ola bolla woosa keethaa cimatas yeddidosona.
He wode Kawoy Heroodisi woosa keetha asaappe baggaa gooda doomis.
Yohaannisa ishaa Yayqooba mashshan wodhisis.
Hessi Ayhudeta ufayssidayssa be7idi, gujjidi Phexiroosakka oythis. Hessi haniday Paasika Baale bonchchiya gallasatana.
Phexiroosa oykkidi qachchis. Paasika bonchchiya gallasatappe guye deriya sinthe aathanaw qoppidi, oyddu oyddu wotaaddareti iya naagana mela tammanne usuppun wotaaddaretas aathi immis.
Hessa gisho, Phexiroosi qasho keethan naagettees. Shin woosa keetha asay iyaw minthidi Xoossaa woossosona.
Heroodisi Phexiroosa asaa sinthe shiishanaappe kase qamma Phexiroosi nam77u baggara nam77u wotaaddaretara santhalaatan qashettidi entta giddon dhiskkis. Naageyssati qasho keethaa penggetan eqqidi naagoosona.
Akeekonna de7ishin Godaa kiitanchchoy qonccis. Qasho keethan poo7oy poo7is. Kiitanchchoy Phexiroosa miyaa bochchi barkkisidi, “Elle dendda” yaagis. Iirakka santhalaatay iya kushiyappe wodhdhi aggis.
Kiitanchchoy iyaakko, “Ne ma7uwa ma77a, ne caammaaka aatha” yaagis. Phexiroosi hessada oothis; kiitanchchoy, “Ne laxana ma77ada tana kaalla” yaagis.
Phexiroosi qasho keethafe keyidi kiitanchchuwa kaallis. Iyaw qonccethi be7iyabaa daanisippe attin kiitanchchoy oothiyabay tuma daanibeenna.
Kiitanchchoynne Phexiroosi koyruwanne nam77antho wotaaddariya aadhdhidi katamaa efiya biraata penggiyako gakkidosona. Penggey enttaw barkka dooyetti aggis. Entti keyidi issi ogiyara bishin kiitanchchoy akeekonna Phexiroosappe shaaketti aggis.
Phexiroosas wozani simmin, “Tana Goday ba kiitanchchuwa kiittidi, Heroodisa kusheppenne naagidi uttida Ayhude asa ubbaafe ashshidayssa ha77i tuma eras” yaagis.
I hessa akeekida wode daro asay issife shiiqidi Xoossaa woossiya bessaa, Marqqoosa giya Yohaannisa aaye Mayraami soo bis.
Yan karen eqqidi xeegis. Issi Rooda giya oosanchchiya penggiya dooyanaw yasu.
Rooda Phexiroosa qaala gididayssa erida wode ufayssan kumada kariya dooyenna guye woxxa bada, “Phexiroosi karen eqqis” yaagada asaas odasu.
Asay iikko, “Neeni gooyay!” yaagidosona. Rooda Phexiroosa gididayssa geeshshada odasu. Entti, “Hessi iya naagiya kiitanchchuwa” yaagidosona.
Shin Phexiroosi karen eqqidi xeegidi aggonna ixxin asay kariya dooyidi iya be7idi malaalettidosona.
Shin entti si77i gaana mela Phexiroosi ba kushiyan mallidi Goday qasho keethafe iya waati kessidaakko enttaw qonccisi odidi, “Hayssa Yayqoobasinne ammaniyaa asatas odite” gidi yaappe keyidi harasoo bis.
Sa7i wonttiya wode “Phexiroosi aw bide” gidi wotaaddareti woli giddon daro kaccidosona.
Heroodisi Phexiroosa koyisin, I dhayida wode naageyssata qoridi, entta wodhana mela kiittis. Hessafe guye, Heroodisi Yihudappe Qisaariya wodhdhidi yan guutha wode uttis.
Heroodisi Xiroosa asaa bollanne Sidoona asaa bolla daro hanqettis. Entta biittay kathi Heroodisa biittaafe demmiya gisho entti issife gididi iya moorinnaa Bilasxoosa banttaw cima oothidi giiganaw Heroodisakko bidosona.
Heroodisi sunthida gallasan ba kawotethaa afilaa ma77idi, araata bolla uttidi asaas odis.
Asay, “Hessi Xoossaa qaala, asa qaala gidenna” yaagidi waassidosona.
Heroodisi Xoossaa bonchchiboonna gisho iirakka Godaa kiitanchchoy iya dechchin guxunen meetettidi hayqqis.
Shin Xoossaa qaalay diccishenne dalggishe bees.
Barnnabaasinne Saa7oli bantta oosuwa polidi Marqqoosa giya Yohaannisa banttara ekkidi Yerusalaameppe simmidosona.
Anxookiyan de7iya woosa keethan nabetinne asttamaareti de7oosona. Entti Barnnabaasa, Kareethi geetettiya Simoona, Qereenaappe yida Luukiyosa, Kawuwa Heroodisara diccida Minaahenne Saa7ola.
Entti Godaa goynnishininne xoomishin Geeshsha Ayyaanay, “Taani xeegida oosuwas Barnnabaasanne Saa7ola taw dummayite” yaagis.
Hessa gisho, entti xoomidaappenne woossidaappe guye bantta kushiya entta bolla wothidi yeddidosona.
Hessa gisho, Geeshsha Ayyaani entta kiittis. Selewuqe bidosona; yaappe markkaben gelidi Qoophiroosa haathan teqettida biitta bidosona.
Entti Silmmaana gakkidi Ayhude Woosa Keethatan Xoossaa qaala odidosona. Yohaannisi maaddishe enttara de7ees.
Entti Qoophiroosa haathan teqettida biittaa kanthidi Phaafu gakkiya wode issi worddanchcho nabiya Bar-Yesuusa giya Ayhude maruwa demmidosona.
He maroy deriya aysiya Sarggiyoos Phawuloosa giya akeekanchcho addiyara de7ees. Sarggiyoos Phawuloosi Barnnabaasanne Saa7ola baakko xeegidi Xoossaa qaala si7anaw koyis.
Shin Girike doonan maruwa sunthay “Elmmaasa” geetettees. I deriya haareyssi ammanonna mela digganaw koyidi Barnnabaasaranne Phawuloosara eqettis.
Shin Phawuloosa giya Saa7oli Geeshsha Ayyaanan kumidi maruwa caddi xeellidi,
“La, Xalahe na7aw, iitatethi ubbay kumidaysso, xillotetha ubbaas morkkiyaw, suure Godaa ogiya mirqeyssa aggikii?
Hekko, ha77i Godaa kushey ne bolla de7ees. Neeni qooqe gidana; guutha wodes awa poo7o be7akka” yaagis. Iira caaganaynne dhumay iya ayfiyaa goozin, ba kushiya oykkidi kaalethiya asi koyishe yuuyis.
Deriya haareyssi hessa be7ida wode Godaaba tamaarsseysan malaalettidi ammanis.
Phawuloosinne iyara de7eyssati Phaafuppe denddidi, Phinfiliyan de7iya Phergge markkabera bidosona. Yohaannisi enttafe shaakettidi Yerusalaame simmis.
Shin entti Pherggefe aadhdhidi Phisidiyan de7iya Anxookiya gakkidosona. Sambbaata gallas Ayhude Woosa Keethi gelidi uttidosona.
Muse higgeynne nabeta maxaafay nabbabettidaappe guye Ayhude Woosa Keetha halaqati, “Nu ishato, asaa minthethiya qaali hinttew de7iyakko asaas oderkketii” yaagidi enttako kiittidosona.
Phawuloosi denddi eqqidi ba kushe mallidi, “Isra7eele asataw, qassi Xoossaa goynniya Ayhude gidonna asaw, si7ite.
Ha Isra7eele asaa Xoossay, nu mayzata dooris. Gibxxe biittan imathatethan entti de7ishin, entta darssidi ba gita wolqqan Gibxxe biittaafe entta kessis.
Bazzo biittan oytamu laytha mela entta dandda7is.
Kanaane biittan Ayhude gidonna laappun kawotethata diggidi entta biittaa ba asaa laatisis.
Hessafe guye, nabiya Saamu7eela wode gakkanaw oyddu xeetanne ishatamu laytha mela aysiya daynnata enttaw immis.
Hessafe guye, entti banttaw kawo immana mela woossin, Xoossay Biniyame sheeshaappe Qiise na7aa, Saa7ola oytamu laythi kawotana mela enttaw immis.
Xoossay Saa7ola shaaridaappe guye entta bolla Dawite kawothis. Xoossay Dawitebaa markkattishe, ‘Taani koyaa ubbaa ta wozanaa mela oothiya Isseyye na7aa Dawite demmas’ yaagis.
“Xoossay, ‘Taani Dawite sheeshaappe Isra7eele deriya ashsheyssa ehana’ gidayssa mela Yesuusa ehis.
Yesuusi yaanappe sinthe Isra7eele asa ubbay bantta nagaraappe simmidi xammaqettana mela Yohaannisi qaala odis.
Qassi Yohaannisi ba oosuwa wurssana hanishe asaakko, ‘Tana oona gidi qoppeetii? Taani hintte naagiya Kiristtoosa gidikke, shin taani iya caammaa birshshanaw taw bessonnayssi taappe guyera yees’ yaagis.
“Ishato, Abrahame sheeshatoo, qassi hayssan Ayhude gidonnashin Xoossas yayyeyssato, ha atotethaa qaalay nuus kiitettis.
Ays giikko, Yerusalaamen de7iya asaynne entta halaqati Yesuusa eribookkona. Sambbaata ubban nabbabettiya nabeta qaala akeekiboonna gisho iya bolla pirddidi nabeti odida qaala polidosona.
Yesuusa wodhisanaw issi gaasoykka dhayin Philaaxoosi iya wodhana mela woossidosona.
Entti Yesuusabay Geeshsha Maxaafan xaafettidaba ubbaa polida wode masqaliyappe iya wodhisidi moogidosona.
Shin Xoossay hayqoppe Yesuusa denthis.
Hessafe guye, I baara Galiilappe Yerusalaame yidayssatas daro toho benttis. Entti ha77i iyabaa asaas markkattoosona.
“Xoossay nu aawatas immana gida Wonggelaa nuuni hinttew odoos.
Dawitey ba Mazmure Maxaafan nam77antho shemppuwan, ‘Neeni, ta Na7a, taani hachchi nena yelas’ geetettidi xaafettida Yesuusa, Xoossay hayqoppe denthidi nu mayzatas immana gidayssa nuus entta naytas polis.
I wooqonna mela Xoossay hayqoppe iya denthon erisanaw, ‘Taani Dawites immana gida ammanettida geeshsha anjjuwaa hinttew immana’ yaagidi odis.
Hessa gisho, Mazmure Maxaafan harason qassi, ‘Ne Geeshsha Na7aa ahaa wooqisakka’ yaagees.
“Dawitey ba wode Xoossaa qofaa polidaappe guye hayqqidi ba aawatara moogettidi wooqis.
Shin Xoossay hayqoppe denthidayssi wooqibeenna.
“Hessa gisho, ta ishato, nagara atotethay Yesuusa baggara kasetidi hinttew odettidayssa erite. Muse higgey nagarappe xillisanaw dandda7enna.
Shin Yesuusa ammaniyaa ubbay nagarappe xillees.
Hessa gisho, nabeti gidayssi hintte bolla gakkonna mela naagettite.
‘Xoossay gidabaa leeqiseyssato! Be7ite! Malaalettite! Dhayite! oonikka odin, hintte ammanonna oosuwa taani hintte wodiyan oothana’ ” yaagis.
Phawuloosinne Barnnabaasi Ayhude Woosa keethafe keyishin, kaalliya Sambbaatan hessa gujjidi odana mela asay enttana woossidosona.
Shiiqoy laalettidaappe guye daro Ayhudetinne Ayhudeta ammanuwan gelidi Xoossaa goynniya daroti Phawuloosanne Barnnabaasa kaallidosona. Ammanidayssati Xoossaa aadho keehatethan minnidi daana mela entta zoridosona.
Kaalliya Sambbaatan kataman de7iya asaappe daroti Xoossaa qaala si7anaw shiiqidosona.
Shin Ayhudeti daro asaa be7ida wode Phawuloosa qanaattidi iya haasaya ixxidi iya cayidosona.
Phawuloosinne Barnnabaasi yayyonna, “Xoossaa qaalay koyrottidi hinttew odettanaw koshshees. Shin hintte qaala ixxidi merinaa de7uwa ekkanaw nuus bessenna gidi hinttee, hintte huu7en pirddida gisho hiza nuuni Ayhude gidonnayssatakko simmos.
Gaasoykka Goday, ‘Alame kumethay ne baggara attana mela, taani nena Ayhude gidonna deriyas poo7o oothas’ yaagidi nuna kiittis” yaagidosona.
Ayhude gidonnayssati hessa si7ida wode ufayttidi Xoossaa qaala bonchchidosona. Qassi merinaa de7uwas doorettida ubbay ammanidosona.
Godaa qaalay he biitta ubbaa gakkis.
Shin Ayhudeti, Ayhude gidonna Xoosse goynniya dure maccasatanne kataman de7iya gita asata Phawuloosa bollanne Barnnabaasa bolla denthethidosona. He asati entta gooda doomidi bantta biittaafe kessidosona.
Shin Phawuloosaranne Barnnabaasara ixxeyssatas malla gidana mela bantta tohuwappe baana pittidi Iqooniyone katama bidosona.
Qassi Anxookiyan de7iya ammaneyssati Geeshsha Ayyaananinne ufayssan kumidosona.
Kaseyssadakka, Phawuloosinne Barnnabaasi Iqooniyonen Ayhudeta woosa keethi gelidi daro Ayhudetinne Ayhude gidonnayssati ammanana gakkanaw qaala odidosona.
Shin ammaniboonna Ayhudeti, Ayhude gidonnayssata wozanaa laammidi ishata bolla denthethidosona.
Hawaareti yan daro wode gam77idosona. Entti yayyonna Godaabaa odidosona. Goday malaatatanne oorathabaa entti oothana mela enttaw maata immidi ba aadho keehatethaa qaalay tuma gideyssa qonccisis.
Shin he katamaa asay shaakettidi, baggay Ayhudetara baggay qassi Hawaaretara gidis.
Ayhude gidonnayssatinne Ayhudeti bantta halaqatara issife gididi hawaareta qohanawunne shuchchan caddanaw koyidosona.
Hawaareti hessa eridi, Lisxiranne Darbbe giya Liqaa7oniya katamatanne entta heeran de7iya biittaa baqatidosona.
Yan Wonggelaa odidosona.
Yelettoosappe doomidi nam77u tohoy wobbin hamuti eronna issi addey Lisxiran de7ees.
He addey Phawuloosi odishin uttidi si7ees. Phawuloosi iya caddidi xeelliya wode paxanaw iyaw ammanoy de7eyssa be7idi,
ba qaala dhoqqu oothidi, “Sitti gada ne tohuwan eqqa” yaagis. Yaatin, guppi denddi eqqidi hamuthi doomis.
Phawuloosi oothidayssa asay be7idi bantta qaala dhoqqu oothidi Liqaa7oniya doonan, “Xoossati ase daanidi nuukko wodhdhidosona” yaagidosona.
Barnnabaasa, “Diya” gidi, Phawuloosi haasayan waannatiya gisho iya, “Hermmeesa” gidi sunthidosona.
Katamaappe gaxan de7iya eeqaa Diya keethaa kahineynne asay kormmatanne alleeqo ciishshata hawaaretas yarshshanaw koyidi katamaa pengge ehidosona.
Shin Barnnabaasinne Phawuloosi hessa si7ida wode entti oothanaw qoppidayssa ixxidi bantta ma7uwa peedhidosona. Asaa giddo woxxi gelidi,
bantta qaala dhoqqu oothidi, “Asaw, hayssa ays ootheetii? Nukka hintte mela ase. Ha pathonnabaappe saluwanne sa7aa, abbaanne entta giddon de7iya ubbabaa medhdhida de7o Xoossaakko hintte simmana mela hinttew nuuni Wonggelaa odoos.
I beni asaa bantta ogiya baana mela yeddi aggis.
Shin iraa saluwappe bukisis, kathaaka woden woden immis, kathi immidi hinttena daro ufayssis, yaatidi hinttew lo77obaa oothidi baw markka dhayssibeenna” yaagidosona.
Hawaareti hessa gidi banttaw asay yarshshonna mela waayidi diggidosona.
Anxookiyappenne Iqooniyoneppe yida Ayhudeti, asaa bantta bagga zaaridi shuchchan Phawuloosa caddidosona. Enttaw I hayqqidabaa daanin katamaappe gaxa goochchi efidi yeggidosona.
Shin ammaneysati yidi, iya yuushuwan eqqidashin I denddidi katamaa gelis. Wonttetha gallas Barnnabaasara issife Darbbe bis.
Entti Darbbe kataman Wonggelaa odidi darota ammanthidaappe guye Lisxira, Iqooniyonenne Phisidiya Anxookiya simmidosona.
Yan ammaneyssata minthethishenne entti ammanon minnidi de7ana mela zorishe, “Xoossaa kawotethaa gelanaw nuuni daro waaye ekkanaw bessees” yaagidi tamaarssidosona.
Qassi woosa keethatas huu7en huu7en cimata dooridosona. Xoomidaappenne woossidaappe guye entti ammanida Godaas entta hadara immidosona.
Phisidiya biittaa kanthidi aadhdhidi Phinfiliya bidosona.
Pherggen qaala odidaappe guye Axaaliya bidosona.
Yaappe entti bantta polida oosuwas Xoossaa aadho keehatethaas entta hadara immida Anxookiya markkabera simmidosona.
Anxookiya gakkida wode woosa keethaa asaa shiishidi Xoossay enttara oothida oosuwa ubbaanne Ayhude gidonna asay ammanana mela enttaw waati pengge dooyidaako odidosona.
Hessan ammaneyssatara daro wode gam77idosona.
Issi issi asati Yihudappe Anxookiya bidi, “Muse wogaatho hintte qaxxarettonna ixxiko attanaw dandda7ekketa” gidi ammaneyssata tamaarsso doomidosona.
