Nuuni biittafe medhettida addiya daaneyssa mela saloppe yida addiya daanana.
Ta ishato, ta geyssi hessa; ha77i nu ma77ida asatethay Xoossaa kawotethaa laattanaw dandda7enna. Wooqiya asatethay wooqonna asatethaa laattenna.
Ta hinttew issi xuura odana. Nu ubbay hayqqoko, shin wurssethan ubbay laamettana.
Moyzey punettiya wode ayfey qiphi xeellanaw hassayonna laamettana. Hayqqida asay wooqonna asi gididi denddana; nukka laamettana.
Hayssi wooqeyssi wooqonnayssa, hayssi hayqqeyssi hayqqonnayssa ma77anaw bessees.
Hayssi wooqeyssi wooqonnayssa, qassi hayssi hayqqeyssi hayqqonnayssa ma77iya wode Geeshsha Maxaafan, “Hayqoy xoonon mitettis” giya qaalay polettana.
Hessadakka, “Hayqo, ne xoonoy awun de7ii? Hayqo, ne qohiya wolqqay awun de7ii?” gida qaalay polettana.
Hayqoy dukkiya wolqqay nagara; qassi nagara wolqqay higge.
Shin nu Godaa Yesuus Kiristtoosa baggara nuus xoono immiya Xoossaa galati gakko.
Hessa gisho, ta siiqo ishato, qaaxxonna minnidi eqqite. Godaa oosuwan hintte daabureyssi coo gidonnayssa eridi ubba wode Godaa oosuwa azallonna oothite.
Ammaniya asaas miishe shiishobaa Galaatiya woosa keethatas taani kiittidayssada hintteka oothite.
Miishiya shiishoy ta hintteko biya wode gidonna mela issoy issoy saaminttafe koyro gallas, wogga wode wogga wode ba demmeyssafe kessidi ba son dagayo.
Taani yaa bida wode miishiya Yerusalaame gathana mela hintte dooriya asaas dabddaabbe immada entta Yerusalaame kiittana.
Enttara ta buussay koshshiyabaa gidikko entti taara baanaw dandda7osona.
Taani Maqedooniyara aadhdhanaw qoppida gisho yaa bada hintteko yaana.
Ta biyaso aw gidikkoka, ta buussan hintte tana maaddana mela hintte matan guutha wode gam77onna aggike. Balggo ageenata hintte matan aathonna waaya aggana.
Taani ogera aadhdhashe hinttena be7anaw koyikke. Goday giikko, hintte matan guutha wode takkanaw qoppays.
Shin taani Phenxeqosxe Baaley gakkanaw Efesoonan gam77ana.
Taw oosoy kumida dalgga penggey dooyettis, shin daro eqettiya morkketi de7oosona.
I ta mela Godaa ooso oothiya asi gidiya gisho Ximotiyoosi hintteko biikko, hintte matan I hirggonna daana mela oothite.
Oonikka iya kadhoppo. I taakko saro simmana mela iya maaddidi moyzite. Taani I hankko ammaneyssatara simmanayssa naagays.
Nu ishaa Aphiloosi hankko ammaneyssatara hintteko baana mela ta iya mintha woossas. Ha77i hintteko baanaw koyibeenna, shin iyaw injjetiya wode hintteko baana.
Barkkite; Ammanon eqqite; xaalite; minnite.
Ooso ubbaa siiqon oothite.
Ta ishato, Isxifaanoseynne iya soo asay Akkayan entti koyro ammanidayssata gideyssanne ammaneyssata maaddanaw banttana aathi immidayssa hintte ereeta.
Hintteka entta mela asaasinne, enttara ooson daaburiya ubbaas kiitettana mela ta hinttena woossays.
Isxifaanosey, Forchchunaasinne Akkayqoosi taakko yidayssi tana ufayssis. Hintte baynna bessan entti hinttena gididi ta pacaa kunthidosona.
Entti hinttena ufayssidayssada tanakka ufayssidosona. Hessa mela asata dogoppite.
Iisiya woosa keetha asay hinttena saro goosona. Aqiilinne Phirisqila bantta son shiiqiya woosa keethaa asaara issife hinttena Godaa sunthan wozanappe sarothoosona.
Ammaniya ishati ubbay hinttena saro yaagosona. Geeshsha yeeretethi yeerettishe issoy issuwa sarothite.
Taani, Phawuloosi, ha sarothuwa ta kushen xaafas.
Godaa dosonna asi de7ikko, qanggettidayssa gido. Nu Godaw, haaya!
Godaa Yesuus Kiristtoosa aadho keehatethay hinttera gido.
Ta siiqoy Kiristtoos Yesuusan de7iya hintte ubbaara gido. Amin77i.
Xoossaa shenen Yesuus Kiristtoosa hawaare gidida Phawuloosinne, nu ishaa Ximotiyoosi, Qoronttoosan de7iya Xoossaa woosa keethaasinne Akkaya biittan de7iya Xoossaa asa ubbaas xaafida kiitaa.
Xoossaa nu Aawappenne Godaa Yesuus Kiristtoosappe, aadho keehatethaynne sarotethay hinttew gido.
Maarotetha Aawas, ubba wode nuna minthethiya Xoossaas, nu Godaa Yesuus Kiristtoosa Aawas galati gido.
Xoossay nuus immida minthethuwan, meton de7eyssata nu minthethana mela Xoossay nuna nu meto ubban minthethees.
Nuuni Kiristtoosa daro waaya shaakettidayssada qassi nuuni iya daro minthethuwan minnana.
Nuuni waayettiko hessi hinttena minthethanaassanne hinttena ashshanaassa. Qassi nuuni minettiko nuuni genccida waaya mela hintteka genccidi, Xoossay hinttew immiya minthethuwan minnana.
Hintte nu ekkida metuwa mela ekkidi, nu minthethuwan shaakettanayssa nu eriya gisho nu ufayssay hinttenan mino.
Nu ishato, Iisiya biittan nuna gakkida metuwa hintte erana mela koyoos. He nuna gakkida metoy nu wolqqaafe darin, hayqqonna attoko gidi ufayssi qanxidashin.
Nuuni nu bolla hayqo pirddi pirddettida mela qoppida. Shin nuuni nu huu7en gidonnashin, hayqqidayssata denthiya Xoossan ammanettana mela hessi hanis.
Xoossay hessa mela iita hayqoppe nuna ashshis; ha77ika ashshana; sinthafekka I nuna ashshana gidi iyan ufayssi wothoos.
Woosan nuna maaddite. Daro woosa gaason Xoossaa maaduwa nu demmiya wode daro asay nu gisho Xoossaa galatoosona.
Nuuni nu geeshsha kahan ceeqettoos. Nuuni ha alamiyan de7ida de7uwan ubbarakka nu de7ida de7uwan tumatethaninne suuretethan hinttera de7ida. Hessika, ha alamiya cinccatethan gidonnashin Xoossaa aadho keehatethaana.
Nu hinttew xaafida dabddaabbey hintte nabbabanawunne akeekanaw dandda7iyabaappe attin haraa gidenna. Hintte iya akeekanaw dandda7eyssa ta ammanays.
Ha77i hintte nuna hanida keena ereeta, shin sinthafe kumethi eranayssa ta ammanettays. Nu Godaa Yesuusi simmiya wode nuuni hinttenan ceeqettidayssada hintteka nunan ceeqettana.
Hessa taani loytha erida gisho hintte nam77antho go7ettana mela kasetada hintteko baanaw qofa qachchas.
Taani Maqedooniya bashenne yaappe simmashe hinttena be7ana. Taani yaappe Yihuda biya wode hintte tana ta ogiyan maaddana gada qoppas.
Taani hessa gashe ay oothanaw bessiyako eronna asi daanaynaa? Woykko taani ta qofaa qachchiya wode asa qofada, issi toho “Ee” qassi issi toho “Akkay” giya asa meleyye?
Shin Xoossay ammanetteyssa gidiya gisho nu hinttew odiya qaalay “Ee” woykko “Akkay” geyssa gidenna.
Taani, Sillaaseynne Ximotiyoosi hinttew markkattida Xoossaa Na7ay, Yesuus Kiristtoosi ubba wode “Eeppe” attin “Ee” nne “Akkay” gidenna.
Xoossay immana gida ubbay Kiristtoosa baggara “Ee” gidees. Nuuni Kiristtoosa baggara Xoossaa bonchchoos, “Amin77i” gey hessa gishossa.
Nunne hintte Kiristtoosan minnidi eqqana mela oothidaynne ba oosuwas dooriday Xoossaa.
Nuuni iyabaa gideyssa erisanaw ba maatamiya nu bolla wothis; qassi ba Geeshsha Ayyaana oythi oothidi nu wozanan wothis.
Taani Qoronttoosa boonna aggiday hintte azanonna attana melassa; hessi worddo gidikko Xoossay ta shemppuwa taappe ekko.
Hinttee, hintte ammanuwan minnidi de7iya gisho nu hinttena ufayssanaw hinttera issife ootheyssatappe attin hinttena wolqqan ammantheyssata gidokko.
Taani nam77antho hintteko biikke gada qofa qachchiday hinttena azzanthonna agganaassa.
Taani hinttena azzanthikokka ta azzanthida hinttefe hari tana ufayssanaw de7ey oonee?
Taani hinttew he dabddaabbiya xaafiday, ta hinttena be7anaw biya wode tana ufayssanaw bessiya asan ta azzananaw koyonna gishossa. Ta ufayttiya wode hintte ubbayka ufayttanayssa ta ammanays.
Taani daro waayeninne un77an qassi daro afuthan xaafiday, hinttena azzanthanaassa gidonnashin taani hinttena ubbaa ay mela dosiyakko hinttena erisana melassa.
Ase azzanthida oonikka de7ikko ta iya balaa darssanaw koyikkefe attin tana gidonnashin hinttefe darota azzanthis.
Hinttefe dariya asay he uraa seerida seeray iyaw gidana.
Hessa gisho, he uray daro azzanidi, ufayssi qanxonna mela hintte iya maaranawunne minthethanaw bessees.
Hintte iya siiqeyssa zaari iyaw qonccisana mela ta hinttena woossays.
Ta he dabddaabbiya hinttew xaafiday, hintte paacettidi, ubbaban taw kiitetteyssa eranaw koyida gishossa.
Hintte maariya uraa takka maarana. Taani maaranabay aybi de7ikkoka, Kiristtoosa sinthan hintte gisho gada maaras.
Taani hessa oothiday Xalahiya cimo oosuwa nu eriya gisho xalahen cimettonna attana melassa.
Taani Kiristtoosa Wonggelaa sabbakanaw Xiro7aada bida wode Goday yan taw ooso oge giigisidi wothis.
Shin taani ta ishaa Tito yan demmaboonna gisho ta wozanay shemppibeenna. Hessa gisho, yan de7iya asaa sarothada iya koyanaw Maqedooniya bas.
Shin Kiristtoosa baggara ubba wode nuna xoonon kaalethiyanne shitto mela sawiya Kiristtoosabaa nu eriya timirttiya ubba bessi gathana mela oothiya Xoossaa galati gakko.
Nuuni attiyaa asaa giddoninne dhayaa asaa giddon Kiristtoosa baggara Xoossaas imettida sawiya shitto mela.
Dhayaa asaas hayqqoko efiya hayqo peeno; qassi attiyaa asaas de7okko efiya de7o sawo; yaatin, hessa mela oosuwas gidanay oonee?
Nuuni Xoossaa qaala wodhe demmanaw koyidi walakkidi zal77iya daro asaa mela gidokko. Shin Xoossay kiittida suure asata mela Kiristtoosan de7idi Xoossaa sinthan qaala odoos.
Nuuni zaaridi nuna sabbinooyye? Woykko hara asada, saba dabddaabbiya hinttew yeddanaw woykko hinttefe ekkanaw nuna koshshiyye?
Asi ubbay hinttena erana melanne nabbabana mela hintte nu wozanan xaafettidi de7iya nu dabddaabbe.
Hintte qalamen gidonnashin de7o Xoossaa Ayyaanan, shuchcha bolla gidonnashin asa wozanan xaafettidayssatanne nunan haggaazettida Kiristtoosa dabddaabbe gideyssa bessideta.
Nu hessa giday, Kiristtoosa baggara Xoossan ammanoy nuus de7iya gishossa.
Nu hessa oothanaw dandda7iday Xoossaa wolqqaanappe attin nuuni nu wolqqan aykkoka oothanaw dandda7okko.
Nu ooratha caaquwa oosanchchota gidana mela Xoossay nuna dandda7isis. He ooratha caaqoy Geeshsha Ayyaanan benttidayssafe attin xaafettida higgen gidenna. Higgey wodhees, shin Geeshsha Ayyaanay de7o immees.
Shuchcha bolla xaafettida higgey imettiya wode Xoossaa bonchchoy qonccis. Muse som77uwan de7iya bonchchoy dhayishe biyabaa gidikkoka, Isra7eele asay iya som77uwa tishshi oothidi xeellanaw dandda7ibookkona. Hiza, hayqo ehiya higgey hessa mela bonchchon qoncciko,
yaatin, Geeshsha Ayyaanan oosettiya oosuwa bonchchoy waanidi aadhdhenee?
Asa bolla pirdda ehiya higgey bonchcho gidikko yaatin, ase xillisiya ooratha ogey waanidi aadhdhidi bonchchettenne?
Kase bonchcho gididayssa ha77i aadhdhiya bonchchoy de7eyssara gathi be7iya wode bonchchoy baynnabaa gidis.
Guutha wodes qonccidi guyeppe dhaydayssi hayssada bonchchetiko, merinaw de7eyssi waanidi aadhdhidi bonchchettenne?
Nuus hayssa mela ufayssay de7iya gisho yeellatonna odettoos.
Nuuni, Isra7eele asay dhayishe biya bonchchuwa wurssethaa be7onna mela ba som77uwa kammida Muse mela gidokko.
Shin entta wozanay doccis. Hachchi gakkanaw entti gal77a caaquwa nabbabiya wode entta wozanay he kaman kameti de7ees. He kamay Kiristtoosa xalaalan qaarettees.
Shin hachchi gakkanawukka entti Muse maxaafaa nabbabiya wode ubban he kamay entta wozanaa kammees.
Shin oonikka Godaakko simmiya wode awudekka he kamay qaarettees.
Goday Ayyaana; Godaa Ayyaanay de7iya bessan la77atethi de7ees.
Nuuni ubbay kametiboonna som77on Godaa bonchchuwa be7ana. Nuuni Ayyaana gidida Godaa malaa daananaw bonchchofe bonchchon laamettana.
Hiza, Xoossay ba maarotethan ha oosuwa nuus immida gisho nuuni ufayssi qanxoko.
Nuuni yeellaya geema ooso ubbaa aggida; gene ooso oothoko; Xoossaa qaala worddora walakkoko. Tumaa qonccen haasayishe, asa ubbaa kahay nuna ekkana mela Xoossaa sinthan nuna shiishoos.
Nu odiya Wonggelay geemmidabaa gidikkoka, geemmiday dhayo ogen de7iya asaassa.
Ha alamiya haariya xoossay ammanonna asaa wozanaa goozis. Entti Xoossa malan qonccida Kiristtoosa bonchcho Wonggelaa poo7uwa be7onna mela diggis.
Nuuni, Yesuus Kiristtoosi Goda gideyssanne nu iya gisho hintte oosanchcho gideyssa odoosippe attin nubaa odokko.
“Dhuman poo7oy poo7o” gida Xoossay, Kiristtoosa som77uwan poo7iya Xoossaa bonchchuwa eraa poo7uwa immanaw ba poo7uwa nu wozanan poo7isis.
Shin ubbaafe aadhdhiya wolqqay nubaa gidonnashin Xoossabaa gideyssa bessanaw ha bonchcho shaloy meqqa miishe gidida nu asatethan de7ees.
Nu ubba baggarakka waayettida, shin meqerettibookko. Nuus haddirssi gidis, shin ufayssi qanxibookko.
Nu, morkketan goodettida, shin lagge dhayibookko. Nu morkketan shocettidi kunddida, shin dhayibookko.
Yesuusa de7oy nu asatethan qonccana mela iya hayquwa ubba wode nu asatethan tookkidi yuuyoos.
Yesuusa de7oy hayqqiya nu asatethan qonccana mela paxa de7iya nuuni iya gisho ubba wode hayqos aadhdhidi imettoos.
Hiza, hayqoy nunan oothiya wode de7oy hinttenan oothees.
Geeshsha Maxaafan, “Ta ammanas; hessa gisho haasayas” yaagettis. Hessa mela ammanoy nuus de7iya gisho haasayos.
Godaa Yesuusa hayqoppe denthida Xoossay, nunakka Yesuusara hayqoppe denthanayssanne hinttera issife ba sinthe shiishanayssa eroos.
Hessi ubbay haniday hintte gishossa. Xoossaa aadho keehatethay daro asaa gakkiya wode asay Xoossaa bonchchuwas daro galataa immana.
Hessa gisho, nuuni ufayssi qanxoko. Nu benttiya asatethay daaburishe biyabaa gidikkoka, nu ayyaana asatethay gallas gallas ooraxees.
Ha77is nuuni waayettiya ha kawushsha waayey, ubbaafe keehi gitatiya merinaa bonchchuwa nuus immisana.
Nuuni benttiyabaa gidonnashin benttonnabaa xeellos. Benttiyabay ha77issa, shin benttonnabay merinaassa.
Ha77i nu de7iya dunkkaane daaniya ha sa7a asatethay laalettikokka, asi keexiboonna, Xoossay keexida merinaa keethay nuus salon de7eyssa eroos.
Salo asatethaa ma77anaw amottishe ha77i ha sa7an de7ishe oolos.
Nuuni hessa ma77iya wode kallottoko.
Dunkkaane daaniya ha sa7a asatethan nu de7ishe deexettidi oolos. Hayqqiya nu asatethay de7on laamettana mela salo asatethaa ma77anaw koyoosippe attin ashuwappe shaakettanaw koyidi gidenna.
Nuna hayssas giigisiday Xoossaa. Qassi sinthafe yaanabaas oythi oothidi ba Ayyaana nuus immis.
Hessa gisho, nuuni ha sa7a asatethan de7iya wode ubban Godaappe haakkidi de7eyssa erikkoka ubba wode ammanettidi de7oos.
Nuuni de7ey ammanonnappe attin be7iyaban gidenna.
Nu ha sa7a asatethaafe shaakettidi, nu soo bidi Godaara issife daanaw amottiya gisho ammanettidi de7oos.
Hessa gisho, nu ha asatethan de7in woykko ha asatethaafe shaakettin, nu amoy iya ufayssanayssa.
Nuuni issoy issoy ha sa7an de7ishe lo77o gidin woykko iita gidin, oothida oosuwas bessiya pirddaa ekkanaw Kiristtoosa pirdda araata sinthan shiiqana.
Hiza, nuuni Godaa bonchcheyssi ay guussekko eriya gisho asay nu odeyssa ekkana mela zoroos. Xoossay, nuuni ooneekko nuna erees; qassi hintteka hintte kahan nu ooneekko ereeta yaagada qoppays.
Wozanan gidonnashin malan ceeqettiya asaa doona oythanaw hintte nunan ceeqettana mela hinttew gaaso gidanaw koyoosippe attin nu nuna zaaridi nashshanaw koyokko.
Nu gooshshi gidikko Xoossaa bonchchossa; wozanaama gidikko hinttessa.
Issoy ubbaas hayqqidayssanne ubbay qassi iyara hayqqidayssa nu eriya gisho Kiristtoosa siiqoy nuna haarees.
De7on de7eyssati hizappe guye banttaw gidonnashin enttaw hayqqidayssasinne hayqoppe denddidayssas daana mela Kiristtoosi asa ubbaa gisho hayqqis.
Hizappe guye, nuuni oonakka asa qofan pirddoko. Hayssafe kase nuuni Kiristtoosakka asa qofan pirddidabaa gidikkoka, hizappe hessada pirddoko.
Hessa gisho, oonikka Kiristtoosan de7ikko ooratha medhetethi; gal77a medhetethay aadhdhis; ubbayka oorathi gidis.
Hessa ubbaa Xoossay oothis. I Kiristtoosa baggara nuna baara sigethis. Qassi harata baara sigethana mela nuus sigetho ooso immis.
Xoossay Kiristtoosa baggara asa ubbaa baara sigethees. Entta nagaraa taybibeenna; qassi asaa baara sigethiya qaala nuus immis.
Xoossay asaa nu baggara xeegiya gisho nu Kiristtoosan kiitettidi asaa Xoossaara sigettite gidi Kiristtoosa gisho woossos.
Nuuni Xoossaa xillotethaa Kiristtoosa baggara ekkana mela, nagara eronna Kiristtoosa nu gisho nagaranchcho asada oothis.
Nuuni Xoossaara issife oothiya asi gideyssada, hintte ekkida aadho keehatethaa hada oothonna mela nu hinttena woossos.
Xoossay, “Ta nena si7ana woden si7as; atotetha gallasan nena maaddas” yaagees. Hekko, ta si7iya wodey ha77i; atotetha gallasay hachchi.
Oonikka nu oosuwa borana melanne nunan dhubettana mela koyokko.
Gidoshin, nu tuma Xoossaa oosanchchota gideyssa nu oothiya ubbaban bessida. Daro genccan, waayen, meton, un77an,
garaafetethan, qashon, ixon kumida wocaman, daaburan, dhiskko dhayon, xooman,
geeshshatethan, eratethan, dandda7an, keehatethan, Geeshsha Ayyaanan, tuma siiqon,
tumaa haasayaninne Xoossaa wolqqan nuuni iya oosanchchota gideyssa bessida. Qassi xillotethay nuus tooranne gonddalle.
Nuuni bonchchettidanne tooshettida; cayettidanne galatettida. Tumaa haasayos, shin asay nuna worddanchcho gidosona.
Nu asan erettida asi, shin erettonna asa mela gidida. Hayqqidosona yaagettida, shin paxa de7oos; shocettida, shin hayqqibookko.
Nuuni azzanikkoka ubba wode ufayttoos. Nu manqo daanos, shin daro asaa dureyoos. Qassi aykkoyka baynna asi daanos, shin ubbay nubaa.
Qoronttoosa asaw, nu hinttew qonccen odida; nu uluwaa hinttena bessida.
Hintte nuna hintte siiquwa bessonna diggidetappe attin nu nu siiquwa hinttena diggibookko.
Aawu ba naytas odeyssada ta hinttew odays; nu hinttena nu uluwaa bessidayssada, hintteka hintte uluwaa nuna bessite.
Ammanonna asaara bessonna ogen waaxettofite. Xillotethasinne nagaras aybi gahetethi de7ii? Poo7osinne dhumas aybi issifetethi de7ii?
Kiristtoosanne Xalahe issife gathiyabay aybe? Qassi ammaneysinne ammanonnayssi issife koxiyabay aybe?
Xoossaa Keethas eeqatara aybi issifetethi de7ii? Xoossay, “Taani entta giddon de7ana, entta giddon hamuttana. Taani entta Xoossaa gidana; enttika ta ase gidana” gidayssada, nuuni de7o Xoossaa keethi.
Hessadakka, Goday, “Entta giddofe shaakettidi keyite; tuna gididabaa bochchofite; ta hinttena ekkana.
Ta hinttew aawa gidana; hintte taw adde naytanne macca nayta gidana; yaagees Ubbaafe Wolqqaama Goday” yaagis.
Hiza, ta siiqoto, ha ufayssay nuus de7iya gisho nu ashuwanne nu shemppuwa tunisiyabaa ubbaafe nuna geeshshoos. Xoossaas yayyidi nu geeshshatethaa polo oothoos.
Hintte uluwaa nuna bessite. Nuuni oonakka naaqqibookko; oonakka qohibookko; oonakka cimmibookko.
Taani hessa hintte bolla pirddanaw giikke. Hayssafe kase ta hinttew odidayssada, hintte nu wozanan de7eeta; nu paxa de7inkka hayqqinkka hinttefe shaakettoko.
Ta odiyabaa hinttefe qottike; ta hinttenan ceeqettays; nu waaye ubban minettays; qassi gita ufayssi ufayttays.
Nuuni Maqedooniya bida wode ubba baggara waayettidappe attin shemppibookko. Karera morkketan, nu gaathan yashshan un77ettida.
Shin azzanidayssata minthethiya Xoossay, Tito yuussan nuna minthethis.
Nuna minthethiday Tito yuussaa xalaala gidonnashin hintteka iya minthethidayssana. Hintte tana laamoteyssa, taw azzaneyssanne taw qoppeyssa ta si7ida wode tana daro ufayssis.
Ta dabddaabbey hinttena azzanthikokka ays xaafadinaashsha gada qiirottike. Ta qiirottiday ta xaafida dabddaabbey hinttena guutha wodes azzanthida gishossa.
Ha77i taani ufayttiday, ta hinttena azzanthida gisho gidonnashin hintte azzanoy hinttena hintte nagaraappe zaarida gishossa. Xoossay ba sheniyada hinttena azzanthisippe attin nu hinttena aybinkka qohibookko.
Xoossay koyaa azzanoy, atotethaakko gathiya nagaraappe simo ehees; iyan qiiroyabay baawa. Shin ha sa7aa azzanoy hayqo ehees.
Hintte azzanoy hinttenan ayfisida ayfiyaa be7ite. He azzanoy hinttena ay mela denthethidaakko, ay mela zaaro immanaada giigisidaakko, he uraa bolla ay mela hanqisidaakko, ay mela taw yayyana mela oothidaakko, ay mela amoyidaakko, he uraa seeranaw ay mela giigidaakko be7ite. Ha ubbaban hintte geeshshi gideyssa markkayideta.
Hessa gisho, taani ha dabddaabbiya hinttew xaafiday, naaqqida uraa woykko naaqettida uraa gisho gidenna. Shin hintte nuus ay mela qoppiyako Xoossaa sinthan hinttee, hinttena be7ana mela xaafas.
Nuuni ufayttiday hessa gishossa. Nu ufayssaafe aadhdhidi nuna daro ufayssiday, hintte Tito ufayssidayssanne iya wozanaa shemppisidayssa.
Taani hinttena nashshada iyaw odin hintte tana yeellayibeekketa. Shin nuuni ubba wode hinttew tumaa odida; hessadakka nuuni Tito sinthan hinttena nashshidayssi tuma gidis.
Hintte iyaw yashshan kokkoridi, iya mokkidayssa qassi iyaw ay mela kiitettidaakko I qoppiya wode hinttew de7iya siiqoy minnishe bis.
Taani ubbaban hinttenan ammanettiya gisho ufayttays.
Nu ishato, Xoossay Maqedooniyan de7iya woosa keethatas immida aadho keehatethaa hintte erana mela nu koyoos.
Entti gita meton paacettidosona, shin entta ufayssay wolqqaama. Entta manqotethaas zawi baawa, shin bantta imuwan daro keehidosona.
Entti bantta wolqqaa melanne bantta wolqqaafe aadhdheyssa dosidi immidayssas ta markka.
Entti Xoossaa asaa maaddiya lo77o ooso nuura oothanaw koyidi nuna daro woossidosona.
Entti nuuni qoppidayssafe aathidi oothidosona. Koyrottidi banttana Godaas immidosona; kaallidi, Xoossaa sheniyada banttana nuus immidosona.
Ha lo77o oosuwa doommida Titoy gujji oothanaadanne hinttena maaddidi, he oosuwa polisanaada iya woossida.
Shin hintte ubbaban, ammanon, haasayan, eratethan, gita amon, nuna siiqoninne ubbaban durettidayssada ha lo77o oosuwankka hintte keeha gidana mela nu koyoos.
Taani hessa kiittanaw giikke. Shin harata gita amuwaa hintte siiquwara gatha be7ada hintte ay keena tumeekko eranaw gays.
Hintte nu Godaa Yesuus Kiristtoosa aadho keehatethaa ereeta. Kiristtoosi dure gidi uttidi, hintte iya manqotethan duretanaada hintte gisho manqis.
Taani ha odan hinttena maaddiya zore zoranaw koyays. Hintte zillaythi immanaw xalaala gidonnashin hessa oothanaw amotethankka hintte koyro.
Hintte oothanaw doomida oosuwa ha77i polite. Hintte hinttew de7eyssa keena immiko, hessi hintte immanaw daro amotteyssa qonccisees.
Issi asi immanaw amottiko, iya imoy Xoossaa sinthan ekettey, I baw de7idayssa keena imminappe attin baynnabaappe immanaw un77ettin gidenna.
Taani hessa gey, hintte ubbay issi gina gidana melassafe attin harati waayappe shemppin hintte waayettana melassa gidenna.
Wode entta palahay hintte pacaa kunthana mela ha77i hintte palahay entta pacaa kuntho. Hessan hintte gina gidana.
Geeshsha Maxaafan, “Daro shiishidayssas palahibeenna; guutha shiishidayssas paccibeenna” geetetti xaafettidayssa mela.
Nu hinttew qoppeyssada Titoykka hinttew qoppana mela oothida Xoossay galatetto.
Titoy hintteko biday, nu iya denthethida gisho xalaala gidonnashin I ba shenen baanaw amottida gishossa.
Wonggelaa markkatethan woosa keetha ubban daro erettida ishaa, nuuni Titora issife kiittoos.
Hessa bolla nuuni ha keeha imotaa efiya wode nuura baana mela ha lo77o oosuwan Godaa bonchchanawunne harata maaddanaw de7iya amuwa bessanaw I woosa keethatan doorettis.
Ha imettida keeha imuwa, nu ooso bolla peeshshiya wode borettonna mela naagettoos.
Nuuni Godaa sinthan xalaala gidonnashin asa sinthankka lo77o gididabaa oothoos.
Qassi daro wode paacen minnidi aadhdhida nu ishaa, enttara hintteko kiittida. I hinttenan keehi ammanettiya gisho ha77i hinttena maaddanaw daro amottees.
Titobaa eranaw koykko, I hinttena maaddanaw taara oothiya ta ooso laggiya. Hankko ishatabaa gidikko woosa keethati kiittidayssata; qassi asay entta duussaa be7idi Kiristtoosa bonchchosona.
Hessa gisho, woosa keethati hintte siiquwanne nu hinttena nashsheyssi tuma gideyssa qonccisanaw hintte siiquwa ha asata bessite.
Ammaniya asaas kessiya miishiyabaa ta hinttew xaafanaw koshshenna.
Hintte maaddanaw keehi amotteyssa ta erays. Hintte Akkaya asay, zillaythafe doomidi maaddanaw giigettidayssa taani Maqedooniya asaas doona kunthada odas. Hintte gita amoykka enttafe darota denthethis.
Ha oosuwan hinttenan nu ceeqettiya ceeqoy hada gidonna mela koyro hinttebaa ta odidayssada hintte giigettidi naagana mela ha ishata hintteko kiittas.
Maqedooniya asay taara bidi, hintte giigettonna de7ishin, demmiko, nu hinttenan yeellatana; qassi hintte nuuppe aadho yeellatana.
Hessa gisho, ha ishati taappe sinthattidi hintteko bidi, hintte immana gida imuwa kasetidi giigisana mela ta enttana kiittas. Taani gakkiya wode he imoy giigi uttees. He wode he keehatetha imoy wolqqan gidonnashin dosan gideyssa erisees.
Hayssa akeekite; guuthu zeriday guuthu cakkana; daro zeriday daro cakkana.
Xoossay ufayssan immiya uraa dosiya gisho wolqqan woykko dosi baynna gidonnashin issi issi asi ba wozanan qoppidayssada dosan immanaw bessees.
Ubba wode ubbaban koshshiyaba ubbaa demmidi lo77o ooso ubbaa oothanaw dandda7ana mela Xoossay hinttew ba anjjuwaa darssana.
Geeshsha Maxaafan, “I ba shaluwa manqotas laallis; iya xillotethay merinaw de7ana” yaagees.
Zereyssas zerethi, maanaw kathi immiya Goday, hintte zeriya zerethaa darssidi immana. Hintte xillotethaa ayfiyaakka darssana.
Daro asay hintte immiya imuwa nuuppe ekkidi, Xoossaa galatanaada, hintte ubba wode darssidi immeyssata gidana mela Xoossay hinttena ubba baggara dureyana.
Ha hintte immiya imoy ammaniyaa asaa pacaa kuntho xalaala gidonnashin asay Xoossaa galatanaw gaaso gidees.
Ha hintte oosoy hintte ammanuwa ersidi Kiristtoosa Wonggelaa hintte ammanidinne iyaw kiitettidi hinttew de7iyabaa enttaranne haratara shaakettida gisho ubbay Xoossaa bonchchana.
Xoossay hinttew immida aadho keehatethaa gisho entti hinttew Xoossaa woossishe hinttena be7anaw laamotosona.
Zawi baynna Xoossaa imuwas Xoossay galatetto.
Ta hinttera de7iya wode shugo, qassi hinttefe haakkiya wode nu bolla minnees yaagettida, Phawuloosi, keehanne ashkke gidida Kiristtoosa sunthan hinttena woossays.
Taani hintteko biya wode nu asho qofara simerettiya asi oothidi qoppiya asaa bolla mino qaalan odettanaw qofa qachchas. Hintte bolla hessada odettana mela hintte tana oothonnaada hinttena woossays.
Nuuni ha sa7an de7ikkoka ha sa7aa asada olettoko.
Nu ola miishey ha sa7ayssa gidenna. Shin miixa laallanaw wolqqara de7iya Xoossaa toora. Tumaara eqettiya palamaanne,
Xoossaa eronna mela diggiya otoro qofa ubbaa laalloos. Asa qofa ubbaa di77idi Kiristtoosas kiitettana mela oothoos.
Hintte kiitettethay polo gidiya wode nuuni kiitetetha ixo ubbaa seeranaw giigettana.
Hintte ayfey be7ida mela pirddeeta. Oonikka bana Kiristtoosabaa gidi qoppiyabaa gidikko, nukka Kiristtoosabaa gideyssa ero.
Goday taw immida maatan ceeqetikokka hessan yeellatikke. He maatay taw imettiday hinttena dichchanaassafe attin qohanaassa gidenna.
Taani ta dabddaabbiyan hinttena yashisanaw koyada xaafidabaa daanoppo.
Issi issi asay, “Phawuloosa dabddaabbey deexonne wolqqaama, shin iya som77on be7iya wode I daaburanchcho; iya odaykka pathenna” yaagosona.
He asati nu haahon de7ishe xaafiya dabddaabbiyaninne matan hinttera de7ishe oothiya oosuwa giddon dummatethi baynnayssa akeeko.
Nuuni banttana nashshiya asatara nuna ginayanaw woykko gaaddeyanaw koyokko. Shin entti banttana banttara ginayidi woykko gaaddeyidi be7ishe eeya.
Shin nuuni Xoossay nuus immida dhassan ceeqettoosippe attin zawaa pinnidi ceeqettoko; he zaway hinttekokka gakkees.
Nuuni besseyssafe aathidi ceeqettoko, shin Kiristtoosa Wonggelaa hintteko gathidayssan ceeqettoos.
Nuuni Xoossay essida zawappe pinnidi, harati oothida ooson ceeqettoko. Gidoshin, hintte ammanoy diccana mela Xoossay immida zawan hintte giddon nu oothiya oosoy dalggana gidi qoppoos.
Nuuni hara asi ba zawan oothida ooson gelidi ceeqettoko, shin hinttefe pinnidi haratas Wonggelaa markkattanaw dandda7os.
Shin, Geeshsha Maxaafan, “Ceeqqiya ubbay Godaa lo77otethan ceeqqo” yaagidi xaafettis.
Goday nashshiya uraappe attin bana baw nashshiya uray nashettenna.
Ta guutha eeyatethaa hintte ha77ika dandda7ana gada qoppays; hayyana dandda7ite.
Xoossay hinttew qoppidaysssada, takka hinttew qoppays. Taani hinttena geeshsha geela7ida issi addiya, Kiristtoosas immanaw oychcha wothas.
Shin shooshay ba geniyan Hewaanno balethidayssada ooni eri hintte wozanay iitidi Kiristtoosas de7iya hintte suuretethaanne geeshshatethaa agganddetii gada hirggays.
Issi asi yidi, nuuni hinttew markkattida Yesuusappe hara Yesuusa hinttew markkatiko, woykko hintte ekkida Ayyaanaappenne Wonggelaappe hara ayyaananne Wonggelaa hinttew odikko, si77i gidi ekkeeta.
Shin taani Yesuus kiittida “Gita hawaaretappe” guuxays gada qoppike.
Taani oda eronna asi gidikkoka, eratethi taw de7ees. Hessa ta hinttew daro ogen qonccisas.
Taani miishe oychchonna Xoossaa Wonggelaa hinttew coo odidaysinne hinttena dhoqqu oothada tana toochchidayssi taw nagara gidi?
Taani hinttew oothanaw hara woosa keethatappe miishe bonqqa ekkas.
Ta hinttera de7iya wode tana metinkka hinttefe issi asikka waaysabiikke. Maqedooniyappe yida ammaneyssati tana koshshiyaba ubban maaddidosona. Hachchi gakkanaw ta hinttew tooho gidabiikke sinthaskka tooho gidikke.
Kiristtoosa tumatethay tanan de7ishin, ta ceequwa Akkaya biittan tana oonikka diggenna.
Ta hayssa ays gaynaa? Hinttena dosonna gishosseyye? Taani hinttena doseyssa Xoossay erees.
“Nukka hintte mela oothoos” yaagidi ceeqqiya hankko hawaareta ceequwa gaasuwa dhayssanaw ha77i ta ootheyssa sinthaskka oothana.
Hayssa mela asati Kiristtoosa hawaare daananaw banttana laammiya worddanchcho hawaaretanne cimmiya oosanchchota.
Hessi malaalisiyabaa gidenna; ays giikko, Xalahey poo7o kiitanchcho daananaw bana laammees.
Hessa gisho, Xalahe oosanchchoti xillotethaa oosanchchota daananaw banttana laammiko hessi gitabaa gidenna. Entti wurssethan bantta oosuwada ekkana.
Oonikka tana eeya gidi qopponna mela zaaradakka odays. Ta hinttew eeya daanikkoka ta guuthara ceeqettana mela tana eeya oothidi ekkite.
Taani hayssada ceeqettada odettey, Goday koyeyssada gidonnashin eeyatethan odays.
Daro asay ha sa7aaban ceeqettiya gisho takka ceeqettana.
Hintte wozanaama gidiya gisho eeya asabaa ufayssan dandda7eeta.
Oonikka hinttena aylleykko woykko hinttena bonqiko woykko baw maadettanaw hintteko shiiqikko woykko hintte bolla otortiko woykko hinttena baqqiko hintte dandda7eeta.
Nuuni hessa oothanaw daro daaburanchcho gideyssa yeellatashe ta odays. Shin oonikka minnidi ceeqqettiko, takka ceeqqettanaw minnays. Taani hessa eeya asada odettays.
Entti Ibraawe? Takka Ibraawe. Entti Isra7eele? Takka Isra7eele. Entti Abrahame sheeshee? Takka Abrahame sheeshi.
Entti Kiristtoosa oosanachcho? Taani gooshsha asada odays, enttafe aadhdhiya Kiristtoosa oosanchcho. Taani ooson daro daaburas; daro wode qashettas; garaafettas; daro wode hayqoppe attas.
Ayhudeti tana hasttamanne uddufuna ichchashu toho garaafidosona.
Heedzu toho xam77an shocettas; issi toho shuchchan cadettas; markkabey heedzu toho me77is; abbaa giddon issi qamma kumethi aqada pee7as.
Taani daro ogiya daaburan hamuttas. Kixa haathafenne panggafe attas. Ayhudetinne Ayhude gidonna asay ta bolla meto gathidosona. Katamay, bazzoy, abbay, tana yashshis; ammaniyaa daaniya asati tana waaysidosona.
Taani ooson daaburasinne cawattas, daro toho dhiskko dhayas, koshattas, saamottas, daro toho xoomas, meegettas, kallottas.
Haraba ubbaa taybonna ubba wode tana qofisey woosa keethatabaa.
Issi asi daaburiya wode iyara ta daaburabiikinna? Issi asi nagaran dhubettiya wode ta awude qiirottonna aggadina?
Ta ceeqettanaw koshshiyabaa gidikko taani daaburanchcho gideyssa erisiyaban ceeqettana.
Merinaw bonchchettida Xoossay, nu Godaa Yesuus Kiristtoosa Aaway, ta worddotonnayssa erees.
Damasqqo kataman Aretaasa giya kawuwappe garssara haareyssi tana oythanaw koyidi Damasqqo katamaa penggiya naagisis.
Shin asay tana daachchon yeggidi, katamaa dirssaa maskkootiyara wodhisin taani iya kushiyappe attas.
Ceeqetethas go77i baynnayssa erays. Shin ceeqettanaw koshshiko, Godaappe ekkida qonccethan ceeqqana.
Tammanne oyddu laythafe kase, Kiristtoosa ammaniyaa issi uray heedzantho saluwa bidayssa ta erays. He uray ashon woykko ashoppe karera bidaakko ta erikke; Xoossay erees.
He uray heedzantho saluwa ekettidayssa erays. Shin I ashon woykko ashoppe karera ekettidaakko ta erikke; Xoossay erees.
He uray gannate ekettidi asi qonccisanawunne asi odanaw dandda7onnabaa si7is.
Taani he addiyaban ceeqettana, shin taani ta daaburaappe attin tanan ceeqettiyabay baawa.
Taani tumaa odettiya gisho ceeqettanaw koykkoka eeya gidikke. Shin asi ta ootheyssa be7eyssafenne si7eyssafe aathidi qoppona mela gada ceeqetethi aggays.
Taw qonccida gita qonccethan ta otorttonna mela tana waaysanaw ta ashuwan caddiya Xalahiya kiitanchchoy taw imettis.
Ha waaysiyaba taappe diggana mela taani Godaa heedzu toho woossas.
Shin Goday, “Ta wolqqay ne daaburan qoncciya gisho ta aadho keehatethay new gidana” yaagis. Kiristtoosa wolqqay tanan qonccana mela ta daaburan ufayttashe ceeqettays.
Taani Kiristtoosa gisho daaburiya wode cayettiya wode waayettiya wode goodettiya wode metootiya wode ta daaburan ufayttays. Ays giikko, ta daaburiya wode he wode minnays.
Taani eeya asada ceeqettas. Hessada ta ceeqettana mela oothiday hinttena. Ta, ta huu7en erettonna asi gidikkoka, “Gita hawaareta” geetetteyssatappe guuxike. Hessa taw markkattanaw bessey hinttenashin.
Ta hintte giddon de7ashe dandda7an oothida malaatatinne mallati ta tuma hawaare gideyssa bessosona.
Ta hinttew tooho gidonnayssafe attin hara woosa keethatappe hintte aybin guuxidetii? Hessi bala gidikko tana maarite.
Taani hintteko baanaw giigettishin hayssi taw heedzantho. Ta hinttenappe attin hinttew de7iyabaa koyonna gisho hinttena waaysanaw koyikke. Yelidayssati bantta naytas shalo minjjoosonappe attin nayti banttana yelidayssatas shalo minjjokona.
Ta hintte gisho taw de7iyabaanne tana aatha imminkka tana ufayssees. Yaatin, taani hinttena hessada keeha siiqiya wode hintte tana guuthara siiqetii?
Gidikkoka, ta hinttew tooho gidikke; waaysabiikke; shin hinttena cimoninne genen oykkidabaa hinttew daanonna aggenna.
Hari attoshin, ta hintteko kiittida asatappe hinttena cimmida asi de7ii?
Titoy hintteko baana mela taani woossas; qassi ammaniyaa ishaakka iyara yeddas. Yaatin, Titoy hinttena cimmide? Nuuni nu oosuwa issi ayyaanan oothibookko? Qassi nu hanoykka issino gidennee?
Nu ubba wode hintte sinthan nuna xillisanaw mootettiyabaa hinttew daanii? Nu Kiristtoosan de7idi Xoossaa sinthan ha77i gakkanaw odoos. Nu siiqo ishato, nu ha ubbaa oothey hinttena dichchanaassa.
Ta hintteko biya wode ooni eri hintte ta koyeyssada hanonna, qassi takka hintte koyeyssada hanonna gahettonna aggoko gada yayyays. Qassi ooni eri hintte giddon palami, qanaatey, hanqoy, yiiqey, zigirssi, asa sunthu iisoy, otoroynne kachchi doonna aggenna gada yayyays.
Taani nam77antho hintteko biya wode Xoossay hintte sinthan tana kawushshana gada yayyays. Kase nagara oothidi he bantta oothida tunatethaafe, laymatethafenne yeellayaa oosuwappe simmiboonna asata be7ada azzanonna aggike gada yayyays.
Ta hintteko bishin hayssi heedzantho. Ay mootoykka nam77u woykko heedzu markkan minnees.
Taani nam77antho hinttera gahettida wode hintte giddon kase nagara oothida uraanne harata ubbaa seeronna aggike gada oda wothas. Ha77i ta haakkada de7ikkoka simmada hintteko biya wode ooddeskka qadhettike.
Tanan de7idi odey Kiristtoosa gideyssa hintte eranaw koyeeta. I hinttera haasayaa wode wolqqaamappe attin hintte giddon daaburanchcho gidenna.
Kiristtoosi masqaliya bolla daaburan kaqettis, shin Xoossaa wolqqan de7on de7ees. I daaburanchcho gididayssada, nukka daaburanchcho. Shin hinttena haggaazanaw Xoossaa wolqqan iyara de7on daana.
Ammanon minnidi de7iyakko hinttena hinttew paaci be7ite. Paacen hintte kunddonna attiko, Kiristtoosi hinttenan de7eyssa hintte ereeta. Shin Kiristtoosi hinttenan doonna ixxiko hintte kunddeeta.
Nuuni paacen kunddonayssa hintte ereeta gada ammanays.
Hintte iitabaa oothonna mela nuuni Xoossaa woossos. Nuuni mino gideyssa asay be7ana mela gidonnashin nuuni mino gidonna ixxikokka, hintte lo77o oothana mela nuuni woossos.
Nuuni tumaas oothoosippe attin tumaara eqettiyabaa aybaakka oothoko.
Nu daaburiya wode hintte qassi minniya wode nuna ufayssees. Hintte borey baynnayssata gidana mela nu hinttew Xoossaa woossos.
Taani hinttefe haakkada de7ashe xaafiday hessa gishossa. Taani hintteko biya wode Goday taw immida maatan zemppada hintte bolla godattanaw koyikke. Goday taw maata immiday, hinttena maaddanaassafe attin qohanaassa gidenna.
Wurssethan ta ishato, saro de7ite. Borey baynna de7ite; ta zoriya si7ite. Issi wozanan gididi de7ite; sarotethan de7ite. Siiqonne saro immiya Xoossay hinttera gido.
Geeshsha yeeretethi yeerettishe, issoy issuwa sarothite.
Xoossaa asa ubbay hinttena saro saro yaagosona.
Asappe woykko asa baggara gidonnashin Yesuus Kiristtoosappenne iya hayqoppe denthida Xoossaa Aawappe hawaare gidana mela kiitettida ta Phawuloosi,
taara de7iya ammaniyaa ishati ubbay, Galaatiyan de7iya woosa keethatas kiittida kiitaa.
Xoossay nu Aawaynne nu Godaa Yesuus Kiristtoosi hinttew aadho keehatethaanne sarotethaa immo.
Ha iita wodiyappe nuna ashshanaw, nu Xoossaa, nu Aawa shenen Kiristtoosi nu nagara gisho bana aathi immis.
Xoossaas Merinaappe merinaa gakkanaw bonchchoy gido. Amin77i.
Kiristtoosa aadho keehatethan hinttena xeegida Xoossaa aggidi, hara Wonggelaakko, hintte ellesidi, waanidi simmidaakko tana malaalisees.
Hinttena balethanawunne Kiristtoosa Wonggelaa wobbisanw koyaa guutha asati de7oosonappe attin tuma Wonggelay issino.
Shin nuna gidin woykko salo kiitanchcho gidin nuuni hinttew koyro odida Wonggelaappe dummattiya hara Wonggelaa hinttew odiyabaa gidikko, I qanggettidabaa gido.
Hayssafe sinthe nuuni gidayssada ha77ika zaarada gays. Hintte ekkida Wonggelaappe dummattiya Wonggelaa oonikka hinttew odikko he uray qanggettidabaa gido.
Yaatin, tana asi nashshana mela koyaynayye? Woykko Xoossi nashshana mela koyaynaa? Woykko ta ase ufayssanaw koyaynaa? Ta ase ufayssanaw koyabaa gidikko, Kiristtoosa aylle gidikke.
Ta ishato, ta hinttew odida Wonggelay asappe gidonnayssa hintte erana mela ta koyays.
Taw ha Wonggelaa Yesuusi Kiristtoosi qonccisisippe attin asappe ekkabiikke woykko asi tana tamaarssibeenna.
Ta kase Ayhude ammanon de7iya wode waana de7idaakko, hintte si7ideta. Ta woosa keethaa qadhey baynna gooddanawunne dhayssanaw baaxetas.
Ayhude ammano naagon, ta woden de7iya Ayhude ishatappe aadhdhays. Nu aawata wogaaskka aadhdhada mishettays.
Shin ta buroo ta aaye ulon de7ishin Xoossay tana dooris; ba aadho keehatethan tana xeegis.
Ayhude gidonna asaas Wonggelaa odana mela Xoossay ba Na7aa taw qonccisida wode ta oodderakka zorettabiikke.
Woykko taappe sinthe hawaare gididayssatara gahettanaw Yerusalaame babiikke. Shin ta kasetada Arabe biittaa bas; hessafe simmada Damasqqo katamaa yas.
Heedzu laythafe guye, Phexiroosara gahettanaw Yerusalaame bada iyara tammanne ichchashu gallas uttas.
Shin Godaa ishaa Yayqoobappe attin hankko hawaareta be7abiikke.
Ta hinttew xaafiydayssi worddo gidonnayssa Xoossaa sinthan hinttew qonccisays.
Hessafe guye, taani Sooriya biittaanne Kilqiya biittaa bas.
Yihudan de7iya woosa keethaa asay tana be7idi eribookkona.
Shin entti, “Kase nuna gooddiya uray, ha77i he I dhayssanaw koyaa ammanuwabaa sabbakees” yaageyssa si7idosona.
Si7ida ubbay ta gaason Xoossaa galatidosona.
Tammanne oyddu laythafe guye, Barnnabaasara zaarada Yerusalaame bas. He wode Tito taara ekkada bas.
Xoossay taw qonccisida qonccethan yaa bada Ayhude gidonna asaa giddon ta sabbakiya Wonggelaa enttaw qonccisas. Kase ta woxxida wothaynne ha77ika ta woxxiya wothay hada gidonna mela gada kaaletheyssata dumma shiishada enttaw odas.
Hari attoshin, taara de7iya Titoy Girike asi gidikkoka, qaxxaretto gidi un77ethibookkona.
Gidoshin, ammaniyaa ishata daanidi nu giddo gelida issoti issoti I qaxxarettana mela koyidosona. He asati Kiristtoos Yesuusan nuus de7iya la77atethaa wochchidi be7anaw geeman nu giddo gelidi zaaridi nuna aylle oothanaw koyoosona.
Shin tuma Wonggelay hinttenan minnidi daana mela nuuni hari attoshin, guutha wodeskka enttaw kushe immibookko.
Shin halaqa daaniya asata oonatethay taw aykkoka gidenna. Xoossay asa som77o be7idi pirddenna. Ha asati ta markkattiya Wonggelaa bolla gujjidabay baawa.
Shin Phexiroosi, Ayhudetas Wonggelaa odana mela Xoossay iyaw hadara immidayssada tawukka Ayhude gidonna asaas Wonggelaa odiya hadaraa immidayssa entti guyeppe be7idosona.
Hiza, Phexiroosi Ayhudeta hawaare gidana mela oothida Xoossay, takka Ayhude gidonna asaas hawaare gidana mela oothis.
Qassi tuussu daanidi benttiya Yayqoobi, Phexiroosinne Yohaannisi, taw imettida aadho keehatethaa be7ida wode nuura issifidayssa qonccisanaw ta kushiyanne Barnnabaasa kushiya oykkidosona. Nuuni Ayhude gidonna asaakko, qassi entti Ayhude asaakko baanaw giigidosona.
Entti nuna minthidi hadara giday, nuuni manqotas qoppanayssa. Kasekka ta hessa oothanaw amotteys.
Phexiroosi Anxookiya katamaa yida wode I balida gisho taani iya som77on “Neeni baladasa” gas.
Yayqoobi kiittida guutha asay yaanappe sinthe I Ayhude gidonna asaara mees, shin entti yidaappe guye, “Ayhude gidonna asaappe ammanidayssati qaxxarettanaw bessees” giya asaas yayyidi enttafe shaakettis.
Qassi hankko ammanida Ayhudeti Phexiroosa hanuwa kaallidosona. Hari attoshin, Barnnabaasikka iya qofan gooshettis.
Shin entti Wonggelaa tumatethan suure hamuttonnayssa be7ada, Phexiroosa asa ubbaa sinthan, “Neeni Ayhude gidashe, Ayhude wogaatho gidonnashin Ayhude gidonna asada de7aasa; yaatin, waanada Ayhude gidonnayssata, ‘Ayhude wogan de7ite gada wolqqatay?’ ” yaagas.
Nuuni yeletan Ayhude, shin nagaranchcho gidida Ayhude gidonna asaa mela gidokko.
Shin asi Yesuus Kiristtoosa ammanidi xilleesippe attin higge naagidi xillonnayssa eroos. Oonikka higge naagidi xillonna gisho nukka higge naagidi gidonnashin Kiristtoosan ammanidi xillana mela Kiristtoos Yesuusa ammanida.
Nu Ayhudetikka Kiristtoosa baggara xillanaw koshshees. Hessa gidikko nukka hara asada nagaranchcho gideyssa be7oos. Yaatin, nu nagara oothana mela denthethey Kiristtoosa guusseyye? Ubbaka gidenna!
Hiza, ta laallidayssa zaarada keexiyabaa gidikko taani ta huu7en higge mentheyssa gideyssa qonccisays.
Taani Xoossaas daana mela higge baggara higges hayqqas.
Taani Kiristtoosara masqaliya bolla kaqettas. Taani hizappe taw de7ikke, shin Kiristtoosi tanan de7ees. Ta ha77i de7iya de7uwa, tana dosidi ta gisho bana aathi immida Xoossaa Na7aa ammanada de7ays.
Taani Xoossaa aadho keehatethaa hada oothike. Xillotethi asas higge baggara benttiyabaa gidiyakko, Kiristtoosi coo hayqqis guussu.
Hinttenoo, akeeki baynna Galaatiya asaw, hintte ayfiyaa sinthan Kiristtoosi masqale bolla kaqettida misileda qonccidi benttees. Yaatin, tumaas hintte kiitettonna mela hinttena bitiday oonee?
Ta issibaa eranaw koyays; hintte Geeshsha Ayyaana ekkiday higge naagidiyye woykko hintte si7ida Wonggelaa ammanidi ekkideti?
Hintte hessa mela eeye? Hintte Xoossaa Ayyaanan doomidi, ha77i wolqqan polanaw koyeetii?
Hintte Wonggelaa gaason daro waayettiday melee? He waaye ubbay coo gididee?
Xoossay hinttew Geeshsha Ayyaana immeynne hintte giddon malaatata oothey, hintte higge naagida gishoyye woykko Wonggelaa si7idi ammanida gisho?
Ane Abrahame be7ite, “I Xoossaa ammanis; Xoossay iyaw hessa xillotethi oothidi ekkis” geetettidi xaafettis.
Hiza, ammaneyssati Abrahame nayta gideyssa erite.
Xoossay Ayhude gidonna asaa ammanon xillisanayssa Geeshsha Maxaafay be7idi, “Kawotetha ubbay nenan anjjettana” yaagidi, Wonggelaa Abrahames kasetidi odis.
Hessa gisho, ammaniyaa ubbay ammanida Abrahamera issife anjjettidosona.
Higge naagidi xillana giya oonikka qanggettidayssa. Ays giikko, Geeshsha Maxaafan, “Higge maxaafan xaafettida ubbaa naagonna oonikka qanggettidayssa gido” geetettidi xaafettis.
“Xilloy ammanon daana” geetettidi xaafettida gisho oonikka Xoossaa sinthan higge naagidi xillonnayssi erettidabaa.
Higgey ammanon zemppenna. Shin, “Higgiya naagiya oonikka higgiyan de7on daana” yaagees.
“Mitha bolla kaqettidi hayqqiya oonikka qanggettidayssa” geetetti xaafettida gisho Kiristtoosi nu gisho qanggettidayssa gididi, nuna higge qanggethafe wozis.
Xoossay Abrahames immida anjjoy, Yesuus Kiristtoosa baggara Ayhude gidonna asaa gakkana melanne Xoossay immana gida Geeshsha Ayyaana nuuni ammanon ekkana mela hessa oothis.
Ta ishato, ta hinttew asa de7on meeze gididi de7iyabaa leemiso oothada odays. Asi caaqqida caaqoy minnidaappe guye, oonikka he caaquwa shaaranaw woykko iya bolla haraa gujjanaw dandda7enna.
Xoossay he keeke qaalaa Abrahamesinne iya zerethaas immis. Geeshsha Maxaafay, daro asas odiyada, “Ne zerethatas” geenna. Shin issi asas odiyada, “Ne zerethaas” yaagees; ikka Kiristtoosa.
Taani gey hayssa; oyddu xeetanne hasttamu laythafe guye imettida higgey, koyro Xoossay minthida caaquwa shaaridi ufayssa qaala dhayssanaw dandda7enna.
Xoossay immiya laatay higgen ekettiyabaa gidiyakko Xoossay immida ufayssaa baggara gideyssi attees. Shin Xoossay ba aadho keehatethan laata Abrahames ufayssa qaala baggara immis.
Yaatin, higgey ays imettidee? Higgey imettiday, Abrahames ufayssa qaali imettida zerethay yaana gakkanaw iita oosoy aybeekko erisanaassa. Higgey kiitanchchota baggara imettidi, giddo gididi sigethiya issi asa baggara ooso bolla pee7is.
Giddo gididi sigethiya uray issi asa xalaalas gidenna, shin Xoossay issino.
Yaatin, higgey Xoossaa ufayssa qaalara eqettiyye? Akkay, gidenna! Higgey imettiday asas de7o immanaw gidiyakko, xillotethi higge baggara benttanashin.
Shin Yesuus Kiristtoosa ammanin benttiya ufayssa qaalay ammaneyssatas imettana mela kumetha alamey nagaras haarettidi de7eyssa Geeshsha Maxaafay odees.
Shin ammanoy yaanappe kase higgey nuna qachchi wothis. He ammanoy qonccana gakkanaw higgey nu bolla gorddi wothis.
Hessa gisho, nuuni ammanon xillana mela Kiristtoosi yaana gakkanaw higgey na7a naagiya asa mela nuna naageyssa gidis.
Shin ha77i ammanoy yida gisho higgey hizappe guye na7a naagiya asa mela nuna naageyssi attis.
Hintte ubbay Yesuus Kiristtoosa ammanidi Xoossaa nayta gidideta.
Kiristtoosara issino gidanaw xammaqettida ubbay Kiristtoosa ma7oda ma77ideta.
Hintte ubbay Kiristtoosan issino gidiya gisho Ayhude asaa giddoninne Girike asaa giddon, aylle giddoninne womaanno giddon, adde giddoninne maccasa giddon dummatethi baawa.
Hiza, hintte Kiristtoosabaa gidikko hintte Abrahame zare. Xoossaa ufayssa qaalada hintte laatteyssata.
Ta geyssi hayssa. Laattey na7aa gidi de7ishe, shalo ubbay iyabaa gidikkoka, I ayllefe aykkoka dummatenna.
Shin iya aaway gida wodey gakkanaw I hadara ekkidayssata kusheninne naageyssata kushen de7ees.
Hessadakka, nuuni na7atethan de7iya wode alamiya wogaas ayllettidi de7ida.
Shin wodey gakkida wode Xoossay higgefe garssan, maccasappe yelettida ba na7aa kiittis.
I hessa oothiday, higges haarettidi de7eyssata wozanawunne nuna ba nayta oothanaassa.
Nu Xoossaa nayta gidiya gisho “Abbaa, Aawaw” gidi xeegiya ba Na7aa Ayyaana nu wozanaa giddo kiittis.
Hessa gisho, hizappe neeni Xoossaa na7appe attin aylle gidakka. Neeni iya na7a gidikko, Xoossaa laatteyssa gidadasa.
Hintte kase Xoossaa eronna wode xoosse gidonnayssatas aylle gididi haarettideta.
Shin ha77i hintte Xoossaa erideta; ubbarakka Xoossan erettideta. Yaatin pathonnanne go77onna alame wogatakko guye waanidi simmeetii? Wodhdhi eqqidi, waanidi enttaw aylle gidanaw koyeetii?
Dumma gidida gallasata, ageenata, wodetanne laythata hintte loythi bonchcheta.
Tana hinttebay yashshees; ta hinttew coo daaburadinaashsha?
Ta ishato, ta hintteda hanida gisho hintteka taada hanite gada hinttena woossays. Hintte tana aybinkka qohibeekketa.
Taani koyro harggettashe hinttew Wonggelaa odidayssa hintte ereeta.
Ta harggey hinttew paace gidikkoka, tana saletibekketa; ixxibeeketa. Shin tana Xoossaa kiitanchcho woykko Kiristtoos Yesuusa mokkeyssada mokkideta.
Yaatin, he hinttew de7iya ufayssay ubbay aw bidee? Hinttew dandda7ettidaakko, hintte taw, hintte ayfiyaa kessidi immiyako ixxonnayssa ta markkattays.
Yaatin, ta hinttew tuma odida gisho hinttew morkke gidadinaayye?
He asati hinttena banttako zaaranaw koyoosona, shin entta qofay lo77ossa gidenna. Entta qofay hinttena shaakkanaassanne hintte enttaw qoppana mela oothanaassa.
Lo77obaa oothanaw amottiko lo77o, shin hessi ta hinttera de7iya wode xalaala gidonnashin ubba wode gido.
Ta siiqo nayto, Kiristtoosi hinttenan misilettana gakkanaw yelos maccasi miixotteyssada ta hintte gisho miixottays.
Hinttebay taw haddirssi gidin ta un77ettas; ha77i hintte giddon ta benttada shenetada odiyakko ay mela dosaynashin.
Muse higgen haarettidi daanaw koyeyssato, ane taw odite; higgey ay giyakko erekketii?
Geeshsha Maxaafay, “Abrahames ayllefenne godattefe yelettida nam77u nayti de7oosona” yaagees.
Aylle na7ay asi na7a yeliya maaran yelettis, shin godatte na7ay Xoossaa ufayssa qaalan yelettis.
Ha maccasati nam77u caaqotas leemiso gididi ekettoosona. Enttafe issinniya, Siina Deriyappe yidaara, ba nayta aylletethas yelasu; iyakka Aggaaro.
Aggaara Arabe biittan de7iya Siina Deriyan leemisettada ha77i de7iya Yerusalaame daanawusu. Ays giikko, iya ba naytara aylletethan de7awusu.
Shin salon de7iya Yerusalaamey aylletethan de7ukku; iya nu ubbaas aayo.
Geeshsha Maxaafay, “Naatte, yelonna maynthete ufaytta; naatte miixotta eronnaree ilila. Azinara de7iya maccaseeppe, azini baynna maccasees nayti daro” yaagees.
Ta ishato, hintte Yisaaqada Xoossaa ufayssa qaalan yelettida nayta.
Shin he wode asa maarada yelettidayssi, Ayyaana wolqqan yelettidayssa goodis. Hachchika hessa mela.
Shin Geeshsha Maxaafay woygi? “Aylle na7ay godatte na7aara issife laattonna gisho aylliw I na7aara wolla kessa yedda” yaagees.
Hessa gisho, ta ishato, nuuni godattee naytappe attin ayllee nayta gidokko.
Nuuni la77atethan daana mela Kiristtoosi nuna aylletethaafe kessis. Hiza, minnidi eqqite; zaaridi aylletetha qambbaran geloppite.
Ta, Phawuloosi, geyssa si7ite. Hintte qaxxarettanaw koykko, Kiristtoosi hinttena aykkoka maaddenna.
Qaxxarettiya oonikka higgey kiittiya ubbaa polanaw besseyssa gujjada ta odays.
Higge naagidi xillanaw koyeyssato, Kiristtoosappe shaakettideta; Xoossaa aadho keehatethaafe kunddideta.
Shin nuuni Xoossaa Ayyaana baggara ammanon xillanaw ufayssan naagoos.
Hiza, Kiristtoos Yesuusan de7ikko, siiqon qoncciya ammanoppe attin qaxxarettin, qaxxarettonna aggin nuna aykkoka maaddenna.
Kase hintte lo77o woxxeeta, shin ha77i tumaas kiitettonna mela hinttena diggiday oonee?
Hayssa mela iita cimoy hinttena xeegida Xoossaafe yibeenna.
Hessika, “Guutha irshshoy munuqa ubbaa denthees.” geetettidi xaafettidayssa mela.
Hinttew hara qofi baynnayssas ta Godan ammanettays. Shin hinttena buqiya oonikka Xoossafe ba pirddaa ekkana.
Ta ishato, ta ha77i gakkanaw qaxxaro sabbakkiyabaa gidikko, yaatin tana ays gooddonaa? Hessi tuma gidiyakko Kiristtoosa masqaliyabaa tamaarssoy asaas dhube gidennashin.
Hinttena buqeyssati qaxxaretetha xalaala gidonnashin banttana qaaratiyakkoka ta dosays.
Ta ishato, hintte la77a daanaw xeegettideta. Gidoshin, hintte la77atethay asho amo polanaw hinttew gaaso gidoppo; hessafe aathidi issoy issuwa siiqon maaddite.
Higge ubbay, “Ase needa dosa” yaagiya issi qaalan qashettis.
Shin hintte issoy issuwara saxetiyabaanne meetettiyabaa gidikko, hintte woli wurssonna mela naagettite.
Hiza, ta hinttew odays; Ayyaanan de7ite; hintte asho amuwaa poloppite.
Asho amoy Ayyaana amuwaara morkke; qassi Ayyaana amoykka asho amuwaara morkke. Entti issoy issuwara ixettiya gisho hintte dosiyabaa oothanaw dandda7ekketa.
Shin Ayyaanay hinttena kaalethiyabaa gidikko higgey hinttena haarenna.
Asho oosoti erettidayssata; enttika, laymatethi, tunatethi, qayxe,
eeqa goynno, bita, morkketethi, kachchi, qanaate, hanqo, bana doso, shaaketethi, iita tobbe
gene, matho, yethinne hessa hessa melata. Kase ta hinttew odidayssada ha77ika ta hinttew odays. Hayssa melabata ootheyssati Xoossaa kawotethaa laattokona.
Shin Ayyaana ayfey, siiqo, ufayssi, sarotethi, dandda7a, keehatethi, lo77otethi, ammano,
ashkketethi, bana haaro. Hayssa melabata ixxiya higgey baawa.
Kiristtoos Yesuusabaa gididayssati bantta ashuwa iya iita qofaranne iya amuwaara issife masqaliya bolla kaqqidosona.
Nu Ayyaanan de7iyabaa gidikko, nuna Ayyaanay kaaletho.
Ane issoy issuwa yiloyishenne qanaatishe coo ceeqetteyssa aggoos.
Ta ishato, issi asi nagaran kunddiko, Ayyaanan de7iya hintte he uraa ashkketethan suurisite. Shin neeni hessa melaban paacettonna mela nena naaga.
Issoy issuwa deexo toohuwa tookkite. Yaatikko Kiristtoosa higgiya poleeta.
Issi asi aykkoyka baawashin, bana haratappe lo77o gidi qoppiko, I bana cimmees.
Shin issi issi asi ba oosuwa paacco. Hessafe guye, haratara bana gaaddeyeyssa aggidi baw ceeqettiyabaa demmees.
Issi issi asi ba toohuwa baw tookkanaw bessees.
Xoossaa qaala tamaariya oonikka lo77obaa ubbaa ba asttamaariyara shaakettees.
Hinttee, hinttena cimmofite. Asi ba zeridabaa zaaridi cakkiya gisho Xoossaa bolla qelqisoppite.
Ba asho amuwaa kunthanaw zeriya oonikka, ba asho amuwaappe hayqo buuccana. Shin Ayyaanaa ufayssanaw zeriya oonikka Ayyaanaappe merinaa de7o cakkana.
Ane lo77o ooso oothanaw azalleyssa aggoos. Nuuni azallonna ixxiko wodey gakkiya wode nu zeridayssa cakkana.
Nu injje wode demmiko, asa ubbaas, aathidikka ammaniyaa asaas lo77obaa oothoos.
Taani ta kushen, ay mela gita pidaalen hinttew xaafidaakko be7ite.
Asa sinthan lo77o gididi benttanaw koyaa asati hintte qaxxarettana mela koyoosona. Shin hessa entti oothey, Kiristtoosa masqaliya gisho enttana goodi gakkonna melassa.
Entti hintte qaxxaretethan ceeqettanaw koyidi hinttena qaxxaretto goosonappe attin qaxxarettidayssatikka bantta huu7en higgiya naagokkona.
Shin alamey taw kaqettidayssafenne taanikka alamiyas kaqettida, Godaa Yesuus Kiristtoosa masqaliyappe attin hara ceeqetethi taappe haakko.
Hiza, qaxxarettin qaxxarettonna aggin aykkoka maaddenna. Maaddey ooratha medhetethi gido.
Ha wogaa kaalliya ubbaasinne Xoossaa dere gidida Isra7eeles sarotethaynne maarotethay gido.
Taani Yesuusas madunxida beeta ta asatethan tookkida gisho hizappe tana oonikka waaysoppo.
Ta ishato, nu Godaa Yesuus Kiristtoosa aadho keehatethay hinttera gido. Amin77i.
Xoossaa shenen Kiristtoos Yesuusa hawaare gidida Phawuloosappe, Efesoonan de7iya geeshshatasinne Kiristtoos Yesuusa ammaneyssatas xaafettida kiitaa.
Xoossaa nu Aawappenne Godaa Yesuus Kiristtoosappe aadho keehatethaynne sarotethay hinttew gido.
Salon de7iya ayyaana anjjo ubban Kiristtoosa baggara nuna anjjida, nu Godaa Yesuus Kiristtoosa Aaway, Xoossay galatetto.
Nuuni iya sinthan geeshshatanne borey baynnayssata gidana mela Xoossay alamey medhettanaappe kase Kiristtoosa baggara ba siiquwan nuna dooris.
Xoossay ba sheniyan ba dosidayssada Yesuus Kiristtoosa baggara nuna ba nayta oothanaw kasetidi qoppi wothis.
Xoossay ba siiqiya Na7aa baggara nuus coo immida aadho keehatethay bonchchettana mela hessa oothis.
Xoossaa aadho keehatethaa duretethaada Kiristtoosa suuthan wozettidi nagara atotethaa demmida.
Ba aadho keehatethaa cinccatethaninne eratethan kunthidi nuus immis.
Xoossay ba dosidayssada Kiristtoosa baggara iya sheniya xuuraa nu erana mela oothis.
Wodey gakkiya wode Xoossay polanaw qoppida qofay, saloninne sa7an de7iya medhetetha ubbay Kiristtoosappe garssan gidana melassa.
Ubbabaa ba sheniyada oothiya Xoossay, kasetidi ba qoppi wothidayssada Kiristtoosa baggara nuuni iyabaa gidana mela nuna dooris.
Hessa I oothiday, Kiristtoosan ufayssi wothidi naagon koyro gidida nuuni Xoossaa bonchchuwa galatan qonccisana melassa.
Hintteka hintte atotethaa Wonggelaa, hessika tuma qaala si7ida wode Kiristtoosa ammanideta. Xoossay hinttew immana gida Geeshsha Ayyaanan hintte attamettideta.
Xoossaa bonchchoy galatettana mela Xoossay ba asaa wozana gakkanaw Geeshsha Ayyaana nuus oythu oothidi immis.
Hessa gisho, Godaa Yesuusa hintte ammaneyssanne geeshshata ubbaa hintte siiqeyssa ta si7ida wode
ta woosan hinttena qoppashe hintte gisho Xoossaa galateyssa aggabikke.
Godaa Yesuus Kiristtoosa Xoossay, bonchcho Aaway, Xoossaa hintte aathi eranaada cinccatethaanne qonccetha ayyaana hinttew immanaada taani Xoossaa woossays.
Xoossay hinttena xeegida ufayssaynne geeshshati laattiya bonchcho laatay ay mela darookko hintte erana mela Xoossay hintte wozana ayfiyaa dooyana mela taani Xoossaa woossays.
Qassi iya ammaniyaa nunan oothiya iya wolqqay ay mela aadhdhida giteekko hintte erana mela woossays. He wolqqay xoonettonanne daaburonna wolqqaa. Ha nunan de7idi oothiya wolqqaynne,
Kiristtoosa hayqoppe denthidi, salon Xoossaafe ushachcha baggara utisida gita wolqqay issino.
Iya sunthay, ayseyssatappenne maata aawatappe, haareyssatappenne godatappe, bolla gididi ha alamiya xalaalan gidonnashin sinthafe yaana alamiyankka hara sunthata ubbaafe dhoqqa.
Xoossay ubbaa Kiristtoosa tohuwappe garssan haarisis; qassi woosa keethan ubbaban Goda gidana mela iya shuumis.
Woosa keethay Kiristtoosa kumethi oothiya iya asatethaa. Medhetethay de7iya bessa ubban Kiristtoosi ba huu7en ubbabaa kuntheyssa.
Hayssafe kase hinttee, hintte nagaraanne hintte qohuwa gaason hayqqidayssata.
He wode hintte ha alamiya iita ogiya kaallideta. Carkkuwa bolla de7iya ayyaana wolqqata halaqaasinne ha77ika Xoossaas kiitettonna asaa haariya ayyaanas kiitettideta.
Nu ubbayka kase he asata giddon nu asho amuwaanne nu wozanaa sheniya kaallidi de7ida. Nukka harata mela nu medhetethan Xoossaa hanquwa ekkanaw de7eyssata.
Shin Xoossaa gita maarotethaafenne nuus de7iya gita siiquwappe denddidayssan,
hari attoshin nuuni nu qohuwan hayqqidi de7ishin Kiristtoosa baggara nuus de7o immis. Hintteka attiday Xoossaa aadho keehatethaana.
Xoossay nuna Kiristtoosara issife hayqoppe denthidi salo sohuwan iyara issife wothis.
I hessa oothiday, Kiristtoos Yesuusa baggara nuus qonccisida ba keehatethaanne zawi baynna ba aadho keehatetha duretethaa yaana laythan nuna bessanaassa.
Hintte aadho keehatethan ammanon attideta. Hessika, Xoossaa imotappe attin hintte ooson benttidabaa gidenna.
Oonikka ceeqettonna mela atotethay benttiday ooson gidenna.
Nuuni Xoossaa medhetethi; I nuus kasetidi giigisi wothida lo77o oosota oothana mela Kiristtoos Yesuusa baggara oorathi medhettida.
Hessa gisho, hinttenoo yeletan Ayhude gidonnayssato, Ayhudeti banttaw asa kushen qaxxarettidi, hinttena qassi qaxxarettiboonayssata gidi xeegeyssa akeekite.
He wode hintte Kiristtoosappe shaaketti de7idayssa, Isra7eele asaas allaga gididi de7idayssa, Xoossaa ufayssa qaalappe haakkidi de7idayssanne ha alamiyan ufayssinne Xoossi baynna de7idayssa akeekite.
Shin hintte kase haakkidi de7idayssati, ha77i Kiristtoos Yesuusan de7idi Kiristtoosa suuthan mata shiiqideta.
Kiristtoosi nu sarotethaa; I Ayhudenne Ayhude gidonna asaa timidi, nam77aa shaakki wothida morkketetha godaa laallis.
I banan ha nam77u zaretappe issi ooratha ase medhdhidi, higgiya iya kiitaranne wogatara issife ba asatethan dhayssidi sarotethi immis.
Kiristtoosi masqaliya bolla hayqqidi morkketethaa dhayssis; qassi nam77u zareta issi asatethi oothidi Xoossaara sigethis.
Kiristtoosi yidi, Xoossaafe haakkidi de7iya hinttew, qassi matidi de7iya enttaw sarotetha Wonggelaa odis.
Nu ubbay iya baggara issi Ayyaanan Aawa sinthe shiiqanaw dandda7os.
Hizappe hintte allaga woykko imathe gidekketa, shin hintte ha77i geeshshata biittaa asinne Xoossaa soo asi.
Hintte hawaaretinne nabeti baasida baasuwa bolla keexettideta. Godaa xaphuwa minthiya shuchchay Kiristtoos Yesuusa.
Iyan keetha ubbay issife oykettidi Godan geeshsha Xoossa keethi gidanaw diccees.
Hintte qassi Xoossay ba Ayyaanan de7iya keethi gidanaw Kiristtoosan issife keexetteta.
Hessa gisho, taani, Phawuloosi, Ayhude gidonna hintte gisho Kiristtoos Yesuusan qasho asi gidas.
Ta hinttena maaddana mela Xoossay ba aadho keehatethan taw immida ha oosuwabaa hintte loythi si7ideta.
Ta hinttew kase qanthan xaafidayssada Xoossay ba xuuraa qonccethan taw qonccisis.
Ta xaafidayssa hintte nabbabiya wode Kiristtoosa xuuraa ta ay mela eridaakko hintte akeekanaw dandda7eeta.
Ha xuuray geeshsha hawaaretasinne nabetas ha77i Ayyaana baggara qonccidayssada beni wode asaas hessada qonccisibeenna.
Xuuray hayssa: Ayhude gidonna asay Wonggelaa baggara Isra7eeletara issife Xoossaa anjjuwaa laattoosona. Isra7eeletara issi keetha asi gidoosona; Kiristtoos Yesuusa baggaara Xoossaa ufayssa qaala ekkoosona.
Xoossay ba oothiya wolqqaa baggara taw immida aadho keehatethan ha Wonggelas oosanchcho gidas.
Taani geeshshata ubbaafe laafa gidikkoka Ayhude gidonna asaas zawi baynna Kiristtoosa duretethaa Wonggelaa odana mela ha aadho keehatethay taw imettis.
Qassi kase wodiyan ubbaa medhdhida Xoossan qosettidi de7iya xuuras, Xoossaa qofay aybeekko qonccisanaw aadho keehatethay taw imettis.
Xoossay hessa oothiday ha77i wodiyan woosa keetha baggara salo sohuwan de7iya halaqatasinne haareyssatas ba dumma dumma qonccethaa erisanaassa.
Xoossay ba merinaa qofaa nu Godaa Kiristtoos Yesuusa baggara polanaw hessa oothis.
Nu ammanon yashshi baynna Xoossako shiiqana mela Kiristtoosi nuus minotethinne la77atethi immis.
Taani hintte gisho waaye ekkiya gisho hintte ta waayan yeellatonnaada hinttena woossays; taani hintte bonchchuwas waayettays.
Taani aawa sinthan gulbbatada woossey hessa gishossa.
Saloninne sa7an de7iya issi issi soo asay iyan sunthettees.
Xoossay ba bonchcho duretethaafe hintte garssa asatethaa minthiya wolqqaa ba Ayyaana baggara immana mela hinttew woossays.
Qassi ammanon Kiristtoosi hintte wozanan daana melanne hintte siiqon xapho yeddidi minnidi daana mela woossays.
Hessadakka, Kiristtoosa siiqoy ay mela dalggeko, adusseeko, dhoqqekonne ciimmooko geeshshata ubbaara eriya wolqqaa hintte akeekana mela woossays.
Eratethaafe aadhdhiya Kiristtoosa siiquwa hintte erana mela qassi de7o immiya Xoossaa wolqqan hintte kumana mela ta woossays.
Hiza, nu giddon oothiya ba wolqqaa baggara nuuni woosseyssafe woykko qoppeyssafe aathidi oothanaw dandda7iya Xoossaas,
woosa keethaninne Kiristtoos Yesuusan wode ubban merinaappe merinaa gakkanaw bonchchoy gido. Amin77i.
Hiza, Godaa gisho qashettida taani, hintte xeegettida xeessas bessiya de7o daana mela hinttena woossays.
Hintte ubba wode aadanne hayo gidite; issoy issuwa dandda7itenne siiqon de7ite.
Sarotethan qashettidi Ayyaanay immiya issifetethaa naaganaw minnite.
Xoossay hinttena xeegida wode issi ufayssas xeegidayssada issi asatethinne issi Ayyaani de7ees.
Issi Goday, issi ammanoynne issi xinqqatey de7ees.
Ubbaafe bolla gidida, ubbaa baggara oothiyanne ubbaa giddon de7iya issi Xoossay, ubbaa Aaway de7ees.
Shin Kiristtoosi immanaw koyidayssada nu issoy issoy dumma dumma imota ekkida.
Hessa gisho, Xoossaa qaalay, “I pude keyida wode di7ettida darota baara ekkidi bis; asaaskka imotaa immis” yaagees.
Yaatin, “Pude keyis” guussay woy guussee? I koyro duge, sa7aa ziqqa bessaa wodhdhis guussu gidonna ixxiko ay gussee?
Ha duge wodhdhidayssi, ubba bessan benttanaw ubbaafe dhoqqa saluwa keyidayssi iya.
I issota issota hawaareta, issota issota nabeta, issota issota Wonggela sabaaketa, issota issota woosa keethi heemmeyssata, issota issota asttamaareta oothidi immis.
I hessa oothiday Kiristtoosa asatethi gidida woosa keethi dichchanawunne ammaniyaa asaa Xoossaa oosos giigisanaassa.
Hessadakka, nu ubbay Xoossaa Na7aa eridi ammanon benttiya issifetethaakko gakkidi, Kiristtoosa ayyaana de7uwa kumethaa gakkidi diccana melassa.
Hizappe guye, asaa gene cimon giigida balethiya worddo timirtte carkkoninne hobben gedenne haa kuullo kaa7iya nayta mela gidanaw bessenna.
Shin nuuni tumaa siiqon odishe asatethaas huu7e gidiya Kiristtoosara de7iya issifetethaa gujji gujji dichchoos.
Kumetha asatethay Kiristtoosa bolla zemppees qassi dumma dumma asatetha billiteti issoy issuwara oykettidi uttis. Issi issi asatetha kifiley ba oosuwa oothiya wode kumetha asatethay siiqon diccees.
Hessa gisho, taani hayssa hinttew Godaa sunthan odaysinne markkattays. Go77i baynna qofaa qoppiya Ayhude gidonna asatada de7oppite.
Entta qofay dhumis; bantta wozanaa muumisidosona. Entti eratetha dhayoninne ixxas gidi Xoossay immiya de7uwappe haakkidosona.
Entti yeella giyabaa erokkonna; entti laymatethas banttana aathi immidosona; qassi tunabaa ubbaa guye goonna oothoosona.
Shin hintte Kiristtoosa eriday hessa mela ogen gidenna.
Iyabaa tuma si7ideta. Qassi Yesuusan de7iya tumaa mela iyappe tamaarideta.
Hintte kase de7iya de7o ogiya aggite. Qassi ba cimmiya amon dhaya hintte ceega asatethaa diggite.
Hintte wozanaa qofan ooraxite.
Tuma xillotethaninne geeshshatethan Xoossaa leemison medhettida ooratha asatethaa ma77ite.
Hiza, worddo odettofite. Nuuni ubbay Kiristtoosa asatethaa billiteta gidiya gisho asa ubbaara tuma odettite.
Hanqettite, shin hintte hanquwan nagara oothofite. Hintte hanqeti de7ishin awi wullofo.
Xalahes besse immofite.
Kaysiya uray hizappe guye kaysotoppo. Shin manqota maaddiyabay iyaw daana mela ba kushen lo77obaa ootho.
Hintte doonappe iita qaali keyoppo. Shin si7eyssata go77ana melanne harata minthethiya koshshiya lo77o qaali hintte doonappe keyo.
Xoossay hinttena woziya gallasaas hinttena attamidi wothida Xoossaa Ayyaana azzanthofite.
Cametethi, yilo, hanqo, waaso, cashshenne iita ubbaa hinttefe haassite.
Aathidi issoy issuwas keehanne qadhetteyssata gidite. Xoossay Kiristtoosa baggara hinttew atto gidayssada hintteka wolis atto giite.
Hiza, Xoossay dosiya naytada iya daanite.
Kiristtoosi nuna dosidi bana nu gisho Xoossaas sawiya imonne yarshsho oothidi immidayssada hintteka siiqon de7ite.
Shin laymatethi, tunatethinne uuzetethi ammaniyaa asaas bessonna gisho hintte giddon ubbaraka si7ettofo.
Xoossaa galatiteppe attin yeellayabaynne eeya odi woykko qidhey hinttew bessonna gisho hintte giddon ubbaka de7oppo.
Hayssa erite; oonikka laymatey woykko tunabaa oothey woykko uuzettey Kiristtoosa kawotethaanne Xoossaa kawotethaa laattanaw dandda7enna. Uuzetethi eeqa goynno mela.
Hayssata gaason Xoossaa hanqoy kiitettonna asaa bolla yaana gisho oonikka hinttena pathonna odan cimmofo.
Hessa mela asaara issifetethi oothofite.
Kase hintte dhuman de7ideta, shin ha77i Godaa baggara poo7on de7eeta. Hiza, poo7o asada poo7on simerettite.
Poo7oy lo77otethi, xillotethinne tumatethi ayfees.
Godaa ufayssiyabaa oothanaw koyite.
Go77i baynna dhuma ooso qonccisiteppe attin iyara issifoppite.
Entti geeman oothiya oosuwa hari attoshin odanawukka yeellayees.
Shin ubbabay poo7on keyaa wode qonccen benttees.
Poo7oy ubbabaa qonccen bessees. Hessa gisho, “Neno dhiskkeysso barkka; hayqoppe dendda; Kiristtoosi ne bolla poo7ana” yaagettis.
Hiza, hintte waanidi de7iyakko akeeki be7ite. Cinccata giditeppe attin eeyata gidoppite.
Laythay iita gidiya gisho injjetiya wode ubbaa go7ettite.
Hessa gisho, Godaa sheney aybeekko akeekiteppe attin eeyoppite.
Geeshsha Ayyaanan gallas gallas kumiteppe attin dhayokko hinttena kaalethiya gisho woyne ushshan mathottofite.
Mazmuren, sabaninne ayyaana yethan, issoy issuwara odetite. Qassi hintte wozanan zammarishenne sabbishe Godaa galatite.
Nu Godaa Yesuus Kiristtoosa sunthan ubba wode Xoossaa Aawa ubbabaas galatite.
Kiristtoosa bonchchuwas gidi issoy issuwas haarettite.
Machcheto, Godaas haaretteyssada hintte azinatas haarettite.
Kiristtoosi woosa keethaas huu7e gideyssada azinikka ba machchees huu7e. Qassi Kiristtoosi ba asatethi gidida woosa keethaa ashsheyssa.
Shin woosa keethay Kiristtoosas haaretteyssada machcheti bantta azinatas ubbaban haarettanaw bessees.
Azinatoo, Kiristtoosi woosa keethaa dosidi bana iw immidayssada hintteka hintte machcheta dosite.
I woosa keethaa ba qaala baggara haathan meeccidi geeshshis.
Kiristtoosi woosa keethaa qiti woykko som77o tuussi woykko hessa melabay baynna I kumetha bonchchuwara geeshshinne borettonnaaro oothidi baakko shiishanaw koyidi hessa oothis.
Hessadakka, azinati banttana doseyssada bantta machcheta dosanaw bessees. Ba machchiw doseyssi bana dosees.
Bana ixxiya asi oonikka baawa, shin Kiristtoosi woosa keethaas ootheyssada ba asatethaa muzeesinne naagees.
Nuuni Kiristtoosa asatethaa billiteta.
Xoossaa qaalay, “Hessa gisho, asi ba aawanne ba aayiw aggidi, ba machcheera issife daana; entti nam77ayka issi asho gidana” yaagees.
Hayssi gita xuura, shin taani hessa Kiristtoosabaanne woosa keethabaa leemiso oothada odays.
Gidoshin, hintte issoy issoy hintte machcheta hinttee, hinttena doseyssada dosite. Issi issi machcha ba azinaa bonchchanaw bessees.
Nayto, hintte Godaaba gidiya gisho hinttena yelidayssatas kiitettite. Hessi hinttew bessiyabaa.
“Ne aayiwunne ne aawa bonchcha.” Hessi ufayssa qaali de7iya koyro kiitaa.
“Ne hessa poliyabaa gidikko ubbay new injjetana; ne laythay sa7a bolla aduqqana.”
Aawato, hintte nayta Godaa qaala tamaarssoninne entta kaaleson dichchiteppe attin enttana caamisoppite.
Aylleto, Kiristtoosas kiitetteyssada hintte sa7a godatas yashshan, bonchchoninne suure wozanan kiitettite.
Entta sinthan saba demmanaw entti be7iya wode xalaala oothofite. Shin Kiristtoosa aylletada Xoossaa sheniya wozanappe polite.
Asas gidonnashin Godaas gidi hintte kumetha wozanaappe oothite.
Aylle gidin woykko goda gidin issoy issoy ba oothida lo77o oosuwas Godaappe woyto ekkanayssa ereeta.
Godato, asa som77o be7idi maaddonna Goday, saluwan de7eyssaa ereeta. Hessa gisho, hintte aylleta manddeyssa aggidi entti hinttew bonchchon kiitetteyssa mela hintte enttaw lo77obaa oothite.
Wurssethan, Godaaninne iya gita wolqqan minnite.
Xalahe cimuwa eqettanaw dandda7ana mela Xoossay hinttew immida ola miishiya ubbaa ma77ite.
Nu olay asara gidonnashin salon de7iya tuna ayyaana olanchchotara, maata aawatara, haareyssataranne ha dhuma alamiya wolqqatara.
Hessa gisho, iita gallasaa teqqanawunne ubbaa polidi, minnidi eqqanaw hintte dandda7ana mela Xoossaa ola miisheta ubbaa ma77ite.
Tumaa xeessan danccoda danccidi, xillotethaa xurureda tiran wothidi, sarotethaa Wonggelaa hintte tohuwan caammada aathidi minnidi eqqite.
