Shin ne sheneda oothanaw koyasippe attin neera zorettonna wolqqan aykkoka oothanaw koyikke.
Anasmoosi guutha wode neeppe shaakettidayssi, ooni eri simmidi ubba wode neera de7onna aggenna.
Hiza, hayssafe guye Anasmoosi aylle gidonnashin ayllefe I daro aadhdhees. I taw ay mela siiqo ishee! Qassi I new asa baggarakka Godaa baggarakka aadhdhida isha.
Hiza, neeni tana ne lagge giyabaa gidikko tana mokkeyssada iya mokka.
I nena qohidabay woykko I acottidabay de7ikko taappe ekka.
He acuwa taani qanxana gada taani, Phawuloosi, ta kushen xaafays. Neeni taw ne shemppuwa acota uttidayssa taani nena akeekisanaw koshshenna.
Ta ishaw, Godaa baggara neeppe maade demmanaw koyays. Kiristtoosa baggara tana minthetha.
Taani gidayssafe daro neeni oothanayssa erada qassi ne taw kiitettanayssa ammanada hayssa xaafays.
Xoossay hintte woosa si7idi tana hintteko guye zaarana gada qoppiya gisho taw imathi shemppiya keethi giigisa.
Kiristtoos Yesuusa gisho taara qashon de7iya Ephafiri nena saro saro gees.
Qassi taara issife oothiya Marqqoosi, Arsxirokoosi, Deemasinne Luuqaasi nena saro saro goosona.
Godaa Yesuus Kiristtoosa aadho keehatethay hintte ayyaanaara gido.
Kase Xoossay, nu aawatas nabeta baggara dumma dumma ogen daro wode odis.
Shin ha wurssetha wodiyan ubbaa iya laatisida qassi alamiya iya baggara medhdhida ba Na7aa baggara nuus odis.
Na7ay Xoossaa bonchchuwa phoolethaanne kumetha Xoossaa Xoossatethaa ekkidi, ba wolqqaama qaalan ha alamiya katisidi oykkis. Asaa entta nagaraappe geeshshidaappe guye Ubbaafe Bolla Xoossaa ushachcha baggan saluwan uttis.
Iyaw imettida sunthay kiitanchchota sunthaafe bolla gideyssada I enttafe bolla.
Hiza, Xoossay kiitanchchotappe ooddeko, “Neeni ta Na7a; ta hachchi new aawa gidas” gidee? Woykko qassi ooddeko, “Taani iyaw aawa gidana; ikka taw na7a gidana” gidee?
Qassi Xoossay ba bayra Na7aa ha alamiya kiittishe, “Xoossaa kiitanchchoti ubbay iyaw goynno” yaagis.
Xoossay kiitanchchotabaa odishe, “Xoossay ba Kiitanchchota carkko, ba aylleta tama laco oothees” yaagees.
Shin ba Na7abaa odishe, “Xoossaw, ne kawotethay merinaw de7ees. Ne kawotethaa ne xillotethan ayssasa.
Neeni xillotethi dosadasa; iita ixxadasa. Xoossay, ne Goday, nena ne laggetappe aathidi dooris, ufayssa zayte nena tiyis” yaagees.
Xoossay Zaaridi, “Godaw, koyro neeni sa7aa medhdhadasa; saloti ne kushe ooso.
Hessati ubbay dhayana; shin neeni daana. Entti ubbay afilada wurana.
Neeni entta salenaada xaaxana; qassi entti afilada laamettana. Shin neeni ubba wode nena; ne laythayka wurenna” yaagees.
Shin Xoossay kiitanchchotappe ooddeko, “Taani ne morkketa ne tohoy yedhdhiyaso oothana gakkanaw, hayssan taappe ushachcha baggan utta” gidee?
Kiitanchchoti ubbay atotethi demmanaw de7iya asata maaddanaw Xoossay kiittida ayyaanata gidokkonaayye?
Hessa gisho, nuuni si7ida tumaappe harasoo ekettonna mela he si7idayssa minthidi naaganaw bessees.
Hiza, kiitanchchota baggara odettida qaalay tuma gidikko, iya naaqoynne kiitettonna ixxoy pirdda ehiyabaa gidikko,
yaatin, nuuni hayssa mela gita atotethaa ixxas giikko, waanidi attanee? Koyro Goday ba huu7en he atotethaa odis; qassi iyappe si7idayssati nuus geeshshidi markkattidosona.
Qassi Xoossay malaatatan, oorathabatan, dumma dumma mallataninne ba sheniyada immida Geeshsha Ayyaana imotatan markkatethaa minthis.
Xoossay ha nuuni odiya sinthafe yaana alamiya, kiitanchchotas haarisibeenna.
Geeshsha Maxaafay issi bessan hayssada yaagees: “Neeni asas qoppanaw asi aybe? Woykko neeni iya naaganaw I aybe?
Ne iya kiitanchchotappe guutha wodes guuthadasa; Iya huu7en bonchchonne saba kallachcha wothadasa.
Qassi ubbabaa iya tohuwappe garssan wothadasa” yaagees. Xoossay ubbabaa iyaw haarisiya wode iyaw haarettiboonnabay aybikka baawa. Shin ha77i ubbabay iyaw haarettishin nuuni be7ibookko.
Shin nuuni kiitanchchotappe guuthara guuxida Yesuusa be7oos. Xoossaa aadho keehatethaa gaason Yesuusi asa ubbaas hayqqis. I waaye hayqo hayqqida gisho bonchchonne saba kallachcha iya huu7en wothis.
Ubbabay iyawunne iya gaason medhettida Xoossay, daro nayta baara bonchchisanaw entta atotethaa huu7iya, Yesuusa waayen polo oothanaw iyaw bessees.
Yesuusinne he I geeshshida asa ubbay issi aawa nayta. Yesuusi entta, “Ta ishata” gidi xeeganaw yeellatonnay hessassa.
Yesuusi, “Taani ne sunthaa ta ishatas awaajjana; deriya shiiquwan nena galatana” yaagees.
Qassi I, “Taani ta ammanuwa iya bolla wothana” Qassika, “Xoossay taw immida naytara ta hayssan de7ays” yaagees.
Nayti ashoynne suuthi de7eyssata gidiya gisho Yesuusikka enttada ase gidis. I hessa oothiday, hayqo bolla wolqqi de7iya Xalahiya ba hayquwan dhayssanaassa.
Qassi bantta de7o laytha ubban hayqo yashshan ayllettidi de7eyssata aylletethaafe wozanaassa.
Tuma Yesuusi yiday Abrahame zerethi maaddanaassafe attin kiitanchchota maaddanaassa gidenna.
Asaa nagaray atto geetettana mela Xoossaa sinthan maariyanne ammanettida kahine halaqa gidis. Hessa gisho, I ubbaban ba ishata daananaw bessees.
I ba huu7en paacen waayettida gisho paacetteyssata maaddanaw dandda7ees.
Hessa gisho, Xoossay xeegida geeshsha ishato, nu ammanon Godaa gidi xeegiya hawaariyanne kahine halaqaa Yesuusa be7ite.
Musey Xoossaa Keetha ubban ammanettidayssada Yesuusikka bana doorida Xoossaas ammanettidayssa.
Keethe keexeyssi keethafe aadhdhidi bonchchetteyssada Yesuusi Museppe aadhdhiya bonchcho ekkanaw bessees.
Issi issi keethaa keexida asi de7ees, shin ubbaa giigisiday Xoossaa.
Musey Xoossaa Keetha ubban ammanettida aylle gididi, Xoossay sinthafe gaanabaas markka gidis.
Shin Kiristtoosi Xoossa Keethan na7ada ammanettidayssa. Nuuni ekkana gidi naagiya ufayssaa minthidi naagikko Xoossaa keethi gidoos.
Hessa gisho, Geeshsha Ayyaanay geyssada, “Hachchi hintte Xoossay geyssa si7iya wode
bazzo biittan paaciya gallas, hintte aawati makkalidayssada, hintte wozanaa minthofite.
Hintte aawati tana paaccidosona; oytamu laythi ta oosuwa be7idosona.
Hessa gisho, ta he yeletethaa hanqettada, ‘Entti ubba wode bantta wozanan baloosona; ta ogiya eribookkona’ yaagas.
Hessa gisho, taani ta hanquwan caaqqada, ‘Ta shemppo bessaa ubbaka gelokkona’ yaagas” yaagees.
Ta ishato, hinttefe ooddenkka, de7o Xoossaafe hinttena shaakkiya iitanne ammanonna wozani doonna mela naagettite.
Hinttefe oonakka nagari balethin, ba wozanaa minthonna mela “Hachchi” yaagettidi xeegettishin gallas gallas issoy issuwara zorettite.
Nu koyro ammanuwa nuuni wurssethi gakkanaw minthidi naagikko, Kiristtoosara issife laattana.
Geeshsha Maxaafan, “Hachchi Xoossay geyssa hintte si7iya wode he wode entti makkalatethan hanidayssada, hintte wozanaa minthofite” yaagis.
Xoossay giyabaa si7idi makkaliday oonee? Musey Gibxxefe kaalethi kessida ubbaa gidokkonaayye?
Xoossay oytamu laythi oona hanqettidee? Nagara oothidayssatanne entta ahay bazzo biittan wodhdhi attida asata gidokkonaayye?
Qassi Xoossay, “Ta shemppo bessaa gelekketa” yaagidi caaqqiday, iyaw kiitettonna ixxida asaappe attin ooddesse?
Hiza, entti he shemppo bessaa gelonna attiday ammaniboonna gisho gideyssa nu be7oos.
Hiza, Xoossay nuna ba shemppo bessaa gelssana gida qaalay buroo sinthafe de7iya gisho hinttefe oonikka he shemppo bessaa gelonna attonna mela naagettoos.
Enttaw Wonggelay sabbakettidayssada, nuuskka sabbakettis. Shin entti si7idabaa ammanidi ekkiboonna gisho entta go77ibeenna.
Gidoshin, alamey medhettosappe doomidi Xoossaa oosoy polettidayssa gidikkoka, Xoossay, “Taani ta hanquwan caaqqada, ta shemppo bessaa ubbaka gelokkona” gidayssada, nuuni ammanidayssati iya shemppo bessaa gelana.
Laappuntha gallasaaba issi bessan, “Xoossay laappuntha gallasan ba ooso ubbaafe shemppis” yaagis.
Qassika he bessan, “Entti ta shemppo bessaa ubbarakka gelokkona” yaagis.
Koyro Wonggelaa si7idayssati kiitettonna ixxidi shemppo bessaa gelibookkona. Yaaniya gisho, ha77ika he shemppo bessaa gelana issi issi asati de7oosona.
Hessa gisho, Xoossay, “Hachchi” gidi xeegishe issi gallas nuus qanxis. Daro wodeppe guye Xoossay Dawite baggara, “Xoossay giyabaa hachchi hintte si7iya wode hintte wozanaa minthofite” yaagidi odis.
Iyyaasuy enttaw shemppuwa immidabaa gidiyakko, Xoossay hara gallasabaa guyeppe odennashin.
Hiza, Xoossaa asaas Sambbaata shemppoy naagettidi de7ees.
Xoossaa shemppo bessaa geliya oonikka, Xoossay ba oosuwappe shemppidayssada ikka ba oosuwappe shemppana.
Hessa gisho, oonikka he asaa kiitetetha ixxuwa kaallidi, kunddonaada Xoossaa shemppo bessaa gelanaw minnoos.
Xoossaa qaalay de7onne ootheyssa. Nam77u baggara qarattida mashshafe aadhdhidi oco. I shemppo, ayyaana, xaphonne kolize gakkanaw kanthidi caddees. Qassi asa wozanan de7iya geemmida qofaanne amuwaa shaakkidi pirddees.
Xoossaa sinthafe qosettiyabay ayba medhetethika baawa. Iya ayfe sinthan ubbabay qonccenne kallo de7ees. Nuuni zaaro immanaw bessey iya sinthana.
Hiza, salo keyida gita kahine halaqay, Xoossaa na7ay Yesuusi, nuus de7iya gisho nu ammanuwa minthidi naagoos.
Nu kahine halaqay nu daaburiya wode nuus qadhettanaw dandda7eyssa. I nagara oothibeenna, shin nuuda ubbaban paacettis.
Hiza, maarotethaa ekkanawunne maade koshshiya wode aadho keehatethaa demmanaw aadho keehatethay de7iyasuwa Xoossaa araatakko yayyonna shiiqoos.
Issi issi kahine halaqi asaa giddofe doorettidi, Xoossaara gathiyaban asaa gisho imotanne nagara yarshsho yarshshanaw shuumettees.
I ba huu7en daaburanchcho gidiya gisho eronnayssatasinne baleyssatas qadhettanaw dandda7ees.
I ba nagara gishonne asa ubbaa nagara gisho yarshsho yarshshanaw bessey hessassa.
Oonikka ha bonchchuwa baw ekkanaw dandda7enna, shin Aaroni kahine halaqa gidanaw xeegettidayssada Xoossan xeegettanaw bessees.
Hessadakka, Kiristtoosi kahine halaqa gidiya bonchchuwa baw ekkibeenna. Shin Xoossay iya, “Neeni ta Na7aa. hachchi ta new Aawa gidas” yaagees.
Qassi harason, “Malkkexaadiqey kahine gididayssada, neeni merinaw kahine gidana” yaagees.
Yesuusi ase gididi ha alamiyan de7iya wode bana hayqoppe ashshanaw dandda7iya Xoossaa daro yeehoninne afuthan woossis. I, iya bonchchidi kiitettida gisho Xoossay iya woosaa si7is.
Yesuusi Xoossaa Na7a gidikkoka ba waayettida waayan kiitetethi tamaaris.
Hessankka, Yesuusi ba oosuwa polidaappe guye baw kiitettiya ubbay merinaa atotethaa demmana mela gaaso gidis.
Xoossay Malkkexaadiqe shuumidayssada kahine halaqa oothidi iya shuumis.
Ha nu oda bolla gujji haasayanabay darobay de7ees, shin hintte akeekay guutha gidiya gisho hinttew odi gelssanaw waayses.
Hintte hannoode asttamaare gidanaw bessees, shin Xoossaa qaalaa koyro timirttiya hinttena zaari tamaarssiya hara asi koshshees. Hintte mino kathi maanaw dandda7onna gisho maathi koshshees.
Maathi paahettiya oonikka yooga na7a gidiya gisho lo77onne iita shaakki erenna.
Shin mino kathi lo77onne iita shaakkidi eriya kahaama asaassa.
Hiza, Kiristtoosabaa tamaarssiya koyro timirttiya aggidi Kiristtoosan kahaamatethako boos. Hayqo oosoppe simobaanne Xoossaa ammanobaa koyro timirttiyako guye simmoko.
Hessadakka, xinqqatetabaa, kushe wosobaa, hayqoppe denddobaanne merinaa pirddabaa zaari tamaarokko.
Xoossay giikko nu hessa oothana.
Issi toho poo7oy poo7idayssata, salo imota ekkidayssata, Geeshsha Ayyaanan shaakettidayssata,
lo77o Xoossaa qaalanne sinthafe yaana alamiya wolqqaa be7idayssata,
guyeppe kaddidayssata nagaraappe nam77antho zaaranaw dandda7ettenna. Ays giikko, entti bantta dhayuwas Xoossaa Na7aa zaari kaqqiya mela masqaliya bolla iya kaqqosonanne asa sinthan kawushshosona.
Ubba wode I bolla bukkiya iraa uyada, goyida uraa maaddiya kathi immiya biittiya Xoossan anjjettidaaro.
Shin agunthunne kinchchote doliya biittiya aybibaakka maadduku; iw qanggethay matattis; wurssethan xuugettana.
Nu siiqo ishato, nuuni hayssada odiyabaa gidikkoka, hinttena atotethaako kaalethiya lo77obay hinttew de7eyssa eroos.
Xoossay suure pirddeyssa. Xoossay, hintte oothida oosuwanne kase gidin ha77ika ammaneyssata maaddidi, iyaw de7iya siiquwa bessidayssa dogenna.
Hintte ubbay ufayssan naageyssa demmana gakkanaw ha minotethaa wurssethi gakkanaw bessana mela nu amottoos.
Hintte ammanoninne dandda7an naagiya ufayssaa laattiya asaa daanana melappe attin azalla gidana mela koyokko.
Xoossay Abrahames immana gidi caaqqida wode baappe aadhdhiya hari giti baynna gisho ba huu7en caaqqis.
Iyaakko, “Taani nena anjjana; ne zerethaaka darssana” yaagis.
Abrahamey dandda7an naagidi Xoossay immana gida ufayssaa ekkis.
Asi caaqqishe baappe gitatiya uran caaqqees; he caaqoy geetettidabaa minthidi, palama ubbaa teqqees.
Hessa gisho, Xoossay ba laamettonna qofaa ufayssa qaala laatteyssatas qonccisanaw koyida gisho caaqon minthis.
Xoossay worddotenna. Iya ufayssa qaalaynne caaqoy, nam77ayka laamettokona. Ha nam77ubatan nu sinthan de7iya ufayssaa oykkanaw danadda7ana mela geshe demmanaw iyaakko baqatida nuuni, wolqqaama minthetho demmana.
Ha ufayssay nu shemppuwas, markkabey qaaxxonnaada minthidi oykkiya biraata mela. He ufayssay magaraajjuwafe guye baggan de7iya geeshsha bessaa gelis.
Yesuusi Malkkexaadiqe shuumatethaada merinaw kahine halaqa gididi, nu gisho nuuppe sinthattidi he bessaa gelis.
Malkkexaadiqey, Saaleme Kawoy, Ubbaafe Bolla Xoossaa kahine. He Malkkexaadiqey Abrahamey kawota oli xoonidi simmishin iyara gahettidi iya anjjis.
Abrahamey ba di77idabaa ubbaafe iyaw asraata kessidi immis. Malkkexaadiqe sunthay koyro “Xillotethaa kawo”, nam77antho, “Saaleme kawo” birshshethay, “Sarotethaa kawuwa” guussu.
Malkkexaadiqes aaya woykko aawu woykko zare paydoy baawa. Iya yeletethaas doomethi woykko iya de7uwas wurssethi baawa, shin Xoossaa Na7a daanidi merinaw kahine gidis.
Malkkexaadiqey ay mela giteekko be7ite. Nu aawata mayzay, Abrahamey, ba de77idabaappe iyaw asraata immis.
Kahine gidiya Leewe zarey Isra7eele asappe, hessika Abrahame zerethi gidida bantta ishatappe asraata ekkana mela higgey kiittees.
Malkkexaadiqey Leewe zare gidonna ixxikokka Abrahameppe asraata ekkis; ufayssa qaali de7iya Abrahame anjjis.
Guuthay gitan anjjetteyssi palanthenna.
Issi baggara, asraata ekkeyssati hayqqiya asata, shin hara baggara asraata ekkeyssi de7on de7ees yaagidi odettidayssa.
Hiza, asraata ekkiya Leewey, Abrahame baggara asraata immis gaanaw dandda7ettees.
Ays giikko, Malkkexaadiqey Abrahamera gahettiya wode Leewey yelettiboonnabaa gidikkoka, ba mayzaa Abrahame gulbbatan de7ees.
Isra7eele asaas higgey Leewe kahinetethaa baggara imettis. Ha Leewe kahinetethay polo gididabaa gidiyakko Aaronayssa mela gidonnashin, Malkkexaadiqe mela hara kahine shuumanaw ays koshshidee?
Hiza, kahineti laamettiya wode higgeykka qassi laamettanaw bessees.
Ha nu iyabaa odiya uray hara zare; iya sheeshaappe oonikka yarshsho bessan kahinetethan oothibeenna.
Nu Goday Yihuda sheeshaappe yidayssi erettidayssa. Gidoshin, Musey kahintebaa odishe Yihuda zariyaba aybaakka odibeenna.
Malkkexaadiqe mela hara kahiney yidabaa gidiyakko ha nu odiyabay aadhdhi qonccana.
I kahine gididay dhayonna de7uwa wolqqaanappe attin iya mayzaa higgeninne wogan gidenna.
Geeshsha Maxaafay, “Malkkexaadiqe kahinetethaa mela, neeni merinaw kahine” yaagidi markkattees.
Koyro higgey daaburanchchonne maaddonabaa gidiya gisho shaarettis.
Muse higgey aybinkka polo oothanaw dandda7ibeenna. Shin nuuni iya baggara Xoossaakko shiiqiya ubbaafe aadhdhiya ufayssa qaalay nuus imettis.
Kiristtoosi kahine gidiya wode Xoossay caaqqis, shin harati kahine gidida wode hessa mela caaqoy baawa.
Shin Yesuusi caaqon kahine gidis. Xoossay yaagidi caaqqis; “Goday caaqqis; I ba qofaa laammenna; ‘Neeni merinaa kahine’ ” yaagis.
Ha caaquwa gaason Yesuusi nuus ubbaafe aadhdhiya qaala caaquwas waase gidis.
Kahinetethan oothonna mela hayqoy entta diggida gisho koyro kahineta tayboy daro.
Shin Yesuusi merinaw de7iya gisho iya kahinetethaa hari laattenna.
Hessa gisho, I ubba wode entta gisho gaannatanaw merinaw de7iya gisho Xoossaakko iya baggara yeyssata polo ashshanaw dandda7ees.
Hiza, nuus koshshiyabaa immiya, geeshshay, boreynne tuni baynnayssi, nagaranchchotappe shaakettidaysinne saluwappe aadhdhidi dhoqqida kahine halaqay nuus koshshees.
I hankko kahine halaqata mela koyro ba nagara gisho kaallidi asaa nagaraa gisho gallas gallas yarshsho yarshshanaw koshshenna. I bana yarshshida wode zaarethonna ogen issi toho bana yarshshis.
Muse higgey daaburanchcho asaa kahine halaqa oothidi shuumees. Shin higgiyafe guye yida caaqo qaalay merinaw polo gidida Xoossaa Na7aa shuumis.
Nuuni haasayaa gitabay hessa. Saluwan Ubbaafe Bolla Xoossaa araatappe ushachcha baggan uttida hayssa mela kahine halaqay nuus de7ees.
I asan gidonnashin Godan eqqida tuma dunkkaaniyan Xoossa Keethan oothees.
Kahine halaqa ubbay imonne yarshsho yarshshanaw shuumettees. Hessa gisho, ha kahiney yarshshanaw issibay daanaw koshshees.
Higgey kiiteyssada yarshshiya kahineti de7iya gisho Kiristtoosi sa7an de7iyabaa gidiyakko kahine gidenna.
Entti kahinetethan oothiya dunkkaaney salon de7eyssas leemisonne kuya. Musey dunkkaaniya essiya wode Xoossay iyaakko, “Taani nena deriya bolla bessida leemisuwa kaallada ootha” yaagis.
Shin Yesuusi giddo gididi sigethiya caaqoy, koyro caaquwappe aadhdheyssada I ekkida oosoy enttayssafe aadhdhees. Hessi eqqiday aadhdhiya caaqo qaalana.
Koyro caaquwan bali baynaba gidiyakko nam77antho caaqo koshshenna.
Shin Goday iya boridi, hayssada yaagis: “Taani Isra7eele asaaranne Yihuda asaara ooratha caaqo caaqqiya wodey yaana.
He caaqoy ta entta aawata Gibxxe biittaafe kushiya oykkada, goochcha kessida wode enttara caaqqida caaquwa mela gidenna. Entti ta caaquwan ammanettiboonna gisho taani entta yegga aggas yaagees Goday.
Shin hizappe guye Isra7eele asaara ta caaqqana caaqoy hayssa yaagees Goday. Taani ta higgiya entta guugiyan wothana; entta wozanan xaafana. Taani entta Xoossaa gidana; enttika ta ase gidana.
Enttafe oonikka ba shooruwa woykko ba ishaa, ‘Godaa era’ yaagidi tamaarssenna. Entti guuthafe gita gakkanaw ubbay tana erana.
Taani entta naaquwa atto gaana; entta nagaraa zaara qoppike” yaagees.
Xoossay ha caaquwa “Oorathi” gidi xeegishe koyroyssa gal77isis. Hiza, gal77aynne ceegay dhayaa wodey gakkis.
Koyro caaquwas Xoossaa goynniya wogaynne sa7a Xoossa Keethay de7ees.
Dunkkaaney eqqis. Iyan xomppe wothiya kocay, xarpheezaynne Godaa sinthan wothiya uythay de7ees; he bessay Geeshsha Bessaa geetettees.
Nam77antho magaraajjuwafe guye baggara de7iya bessay Ubbaafe Geeshsha Bessaa geetettees.
Iya giddon ixaane cuyisiya worqqa saaxineynne worqqan meeshettida caaqo Taabotey de7ees. He caaqo Taabotiyan mannay de7iya worqqa xaaroy, aacida Aarona xam77aynne Muse higgey xaafettida nam77u lochche shuchchati de7oosona.
He Taabotiyappe bolla baggara atotetha kamaa bantta qefiyan genthiya bonchcho kiruubeti de7oosona. Shin ha77i he ubbaa qonccisidi odanaw dandda7okko.
Ha ubbay hayssada giigidaappe guye, kahineti ubba wode bantta oosuwa oothanaw dunkkaaniyas koyro kifiliya geloosona.
Shin kahine halaqaa xalaali dunkkaaniyas nam77antho kifiliya laythafe issi toho gelees. I yaa gelishe ba nagaraa gishonne asay eronna oothida nagaraa gisho suutha yarshsho ekkonna gelenna.
Koyro dunkkaaney eqqidi de7ishin, Ubbaafe Geeshsha Bessaa efiya ogey buroo dooyettiboonnayssa Geeshsha Ayyaanay hessan erisees.
Hessi ha wodiyas leemiso; Xoossas immetiya imoynne yarshshoy goynniya uraa kaha geeshshanaw dandda7onayssa hayssi bessees.
Hessati muussabaa, ushshabaanne dumma dumma meechcha wogata odeyssata. Entti ooratha wogay yaana gakkanaw oosettiya kare bagga wogata.
Shin Kiristtoosi ha77i nu demmida lo77obaatas kahine halaqa gididi yis. I gelida dunkkaaney gitanne polo gididayssa. He dunkkaaney asa kushen oosettibeenna qassi ha alamiyabaa gidenna.
Kiristtoosi Ubbaafe Geeshsha Bessaa geliya wode deesha suuthinne mara suuthi ekkidi gelibeenna. Shin merinaa atotethaa immanaw ba suuthaa ekkidi zaarethonna ogen issi toho gelis.
Deesha suuthaynne kormma suuthay, xuugettida ussa bidoy, tunida asaa bolla dharccettidi enttana geeshshiyabaa gidikko,
merinaa Geeshsha Ayyaana baggara borey baynna yarshsho oothidi, Xoossaas bana immida Kiristtoosa suuthay, de7o Xoossaa goynnana mela hayqo kaalethiya oosuwappe nu kaha waati aathi geeshshennee?
Hessa gisho, xeegettidayssati Xoossay immida merinaa laata ekkana mela Kiristtoosi ooratha caaquwas giddo gididi sigetheyssa gidis. Hessi haniday asay koyro caaquwappe garssan de7iya wode oothida nagaraappe enttana wozanaw I hayqqidayssana.
Hiza, keekey de7ikko, he keekida uraa hayqoy erettanaw koshshees.
Keekida uray hayqqiko iya keekey minnees. Keekida uray hayqqonna attiko iya keekey oothenna.
Hari attoshin, koyro caaqoykka suuthi baynna minnibeenna.
Musey higge kiita ubbaa asaas odidaappe guye mara suuthinne deesha suuthi haathara walakkidi, zo7o dorssa ikisenne hisophe boncco ekkidi, maxaafaa bollanne asaa bolla wurxxis.
Musey asaakko, “Hintte naagana mela Xoossay kiittida suutha caaqoy hayssa” yaagis.
Hessadakka, dunkkaaniya bollanne oothiya miishe ubbaa bolla suuthaa wurxxis.
Tumakka higgey geyssada guuthabatappe attin ubbabay suuthan geeyees. Suuthi gukkonnashin atotethi baawa.
Saluwabaas leemiso gididayssati ubbay mehe yarshshon geeyanaw koshshees. Shin salobati bantta huu7en hessafe aadhdhiya yarshshuwan geeyanaw koshshees.
Kiristtoosi tuma Xoossa Keethas leemiso gidida, asa kushen oosettida Ubbaafe Geeshsha Bessaa gelibeenna. Shin I ha77i nu gisho Xoossaa sinthan benttanaw saluwa gelis.
Kahine halaqay laythan laythan ba suuthi gidonnayssa ekkidi, Ubbaafe Geeshsha Bessa gelees. Shin Kiristtoosi daro toho bana yarshshanaw salo gelibeenna.
Hessada hanidabaa gidiyakko, Kiristtoosi alamey medhettosappe doomidi daro toho waayettanaw koshshees. Shin ha77i wodiya wurssethan nagara digganaw bana yarshshidi zaarethonna ogen issi toho benttis.
Asi ubbay issi toho hayqqanaw hessafe guye pirddettanaw bessees.
Hessadakka, Kiristtoosi daro asaa nagara digganaw issi toho yarshshettis. Shin I nagara tookkanaw gidonnashin bana naageyssata ashshanaw nam77antho qonccana.
Muse higgey yaanaw de7iya lo77obatas kuyappe attin ba huu7en waanna gidenna. Hessa gisho, laythan laythan pacey baynna yarshshettiya yarshshoy goynnanaw shiiqiya asaa polo oothanaw dandda7enna.
Higgey entta polo oothanaw dandda7idabaa gidiyakko entti yarshsho yarshsheyssa agganashin. Qassi goynnanaw shiiqiya asay bantta nagaraappe geeyana; entta kahaykka enttana bala gidi mootenna.
Shin he yarshshoti laythan laythan nagara qofisoosona.
Ays giikko, kormma suuthinne deesha suuthi nagara digganaw dandda7enna.
Hessa gisho, Kiristtoosi ha alamiya yida wode hayssada yaagis: “Neeni yarshshonne imo koyabaakka; shin taw asho giigisadasa.
Neeni xuugettiya yarshshoninne nagara yarshshuwan ufayttabaakka.
He wode ‘Ta gisho maxaafan xaafettidayssada, Godaw, taani ne sheniya oothanaw yas’ yaagas” yaagis.
Yarshshoy yarshshettana mela higgey kiittiyabaa gidikkoka, Kiristtoosi koyro, “Neeni yarshshonne imo, xuugettiya yarshshonne nagara yarshsho koyabaakka; enttan ufayttabaakka” yaagis.
Kaallidikka I, “Godaw, hekko taani ne sheniya oothanaw yas” yaagis. Hessa gisho, Kiristtoosi nam77anthuwa essanaw koyroyssa shaaris.
Yesuus Kiristtoosi Xoossaa sheniya oothidi, zaarethonna ogen issi toho ba ashuwa yarshshida gisho nuuni geeyida.
Kahine ubbay, nagara digganaw dandda7onna he yarshshota gallas gallas yarshshishe eqqidi ba oosuwa oothees.
Shin Kiristtoosi ubba wodes gidiya issi nagara yarshshuwa yarshshidi, Xoossaafe ushachcha baggan uttis.
He wodiyappe doomidi iya morkketi iya tohoy yedhdhiyabaa oothana gakkanaw naagees.
I zaarethonna ogen issi toho bana yarshshida yarshshuwan geeshshata merinaw polo oothis.
Qassi Geeshsha Ayyaanay nuus hayssa markkattees. Koyro hayssada yaagis:
“He gallasatappe guye, taani enttara caaqqiya caaqoy hayssa: Taani ta higgiya entta qofan wothana; entta wozanan xaafana” yaagees.
Kaallidikka, “Taani entta nagaraanne entta iita oosuwa zaara qoppike” yaagees.
Hiza, nagari atto geetettidaappe guye nagaras yarshshettiya yarshsho koshshenna.
Hiza, ta ishato, nuuni Yesuusa suuthaa baggara Ubbaafe Geeshsha Bessaa gelanaw nuus minotethi de7ees.
Nu gelanay Kiristtoosi ba magaraajjuwa, hessika ba ashuwa baggara nuus dooyida oorathinne de7o gidida ogiyana.
Nuus Xoossa Keetha bolla shuumettida gita kahine halaqay de7ees.
Nuuni iita kahappe geeyanaw nu wozanaa wurxettidi, nu asatethaa xillo haathan meecettidi, suure wozananinne polo ammanon Xoossaako shiiqoos.
Nuus ufayssa qaala immida Xoossay ammanttidayssa gidiya gisho nu markkattiya ufayssaa ushachchi haddirssi goonna minthidi oykkoos.
Issoy issuwa siiqosinne lo77o oosos waati denthethaneekko ane qoppoos.
Issoti issoti meeze oothidi shiiqeyssa aggidayssada nuuni issife shiiqeyssa aggoko. Shin Godaa gallasay matattidayssa hintte be7iya gisho hessa kaseyssafe aathidi oothite.
Nuuni tumaa eratethaa ekkidaappe guye erishe nagara oothiko, hizappe nu nagaraa gisho yarshshettana yarshshoy baawa.
Shin hiza attiday yashshiya pirddaanne Xoossaa morkketa xuugganaw giigida wolqqaama tamaa.
Muse higgiya kiitettonna ixxida oonikka nam77u woykko heedzu asi iya bolla markkatiko qadhey baynnashin hayqqees.
Yaatin, Xoossaa Na7aa kadhida uray, bana geeshshida Xoossaa caaqo suuthaa tunabaada qoppida uray, qassi aadho keehatetha Ayyaanaa cayida uray, ay mela iita pirddaa ekkanaw bessiyako ane qoppite.
Hiza, “Halo kesoy tabaa, ta kushe zaarana” gidayssa nu eroos. Qassika, “Goday ba asaa pirddana” yaagis.
De7o Xoossaa kushen kunddethi daro yashshees.
Hinttew Xoossaa poo7oy poo7idaappe guye hintte daro waayen, gita baaxen genccida beni wodiya qoppite.
Issi issi toho hintte asa sinthan cayettideta; goodettideta; issi issi toho hessa mela waayey gakkida asaara issife waayideta.
Qashon de7iya asaaskka qadhettideta. Hinttew lo77onne dhayonna shaloy salon de7eyssa hintte erida gisho hintte shaloy bonqettiya wode ufayssan dandda7ideta.
Hessa gisho, gita woytoy de7iya hintte minotethaa yeggofite.
Xoossaa sheniya polidi, I hinttew immana gida ufayssaa ekkana gakkanaw genccanaw koshshees.
Hiza, Geeshsha Maxaafan, “I, yaana gidayssi yaana; gam77enna.
Shin ta xilloy, tanan ammanettidi daana; oonikka guye simmiko tana ufayssenna” yaagees.
Nuuni ammanettidi attiyaa asaa baggafe attin guye simmidi dhaya asaa bagga gidokko.
Ammanoy guussay, demmana gidi ufayssan ammanettidi naagiyabaanne nu be7onnabaa be7iyada oothidi ekkiyabaa.
Beni aawati ammanon Xoossaafe markkatethi ekkidosona.
Alamey Xoossaa qaalan medhettidayssa nu ammanon eroos. Qassi benttiyabay benttonnabaappe medhettis.
Aabeli Qaa7elayssafe aadhdhiya yarshsho Xoossaas yarshshiday ammanona. Xoossay Aabela imuwa ufayttidi ekkida wode I xillo gididayssa markkattis. Aabeli hari attoshin, hayqqidikka ba ammanuwan ha77i gakkanaw odees.
Heenokey hayqqonna salo biday ammanona. Xoossay iya ekkida gisho oonikka iya be7anaw dandda7ibeenna. Heenokey salo ekettanaappe sinthe I Xoossaa ufayssida asi gideyssi odettis.
Ammanoy baynna oonikka Xoossaa ufayssanaw dandda7enna. Xoossaakko yaa oonikka Xoossay de7eyssanne bana koyeyssatas woyto immeyssa ammananaw koshshees.
Nohey buroo benttonnabaas Xoossay iyaw odida wode Xoossaas yayyidi, bananne ba soo asaa ashshanaw ammanon markkabe keexxis. Yaatidi ba ammanuwan alamiya pirddidi, ammanon benttiya xillotethaa Xoossaafe ekkis.
Abrahamey laata oothidi ekkana biittaa baana mela Xoossay iya xeegida wode hari attoshin, I aw biyakko eronna ixxikokka kiitettiday ammanona.
Abrahamey Xoossay iyaw immana gida biittan bete asada de7iday ammanona. Xoossay he immana gidayssa iyara issife laattanaw de7iya Yisaaqaranne Yayqoobara wolla dunkkaanen de7is.
I, Xoossay qoppidi keexida xaala baasoy de7iya katamaa naagees.
Saara ba huu7en cimidabaa gidikkoka ufayssi immida Xoossay ammanettidayssa gideyssa erida gisho qanthatanaw wolqqa demmiday ammanona.
Hessa gisho, hayqqida asi daaniya issi addiyafe salo xoolintto melanne abbaa gaxan de7iya tayboy baynna shafe mela zerethay yelettidosona.
He asa ubbay banttaw geetettida ufayssaa qaala ekkonna ammanon hayqqidosona. Shin haahora hessa be7idi, demmidaada oothidi, ufayssan ekkidosona. Qassi entti sa7an imathenne bete asi gideyssa eridosona.
Hessada giya asay bantta biittaa naageyssa qonccen bessees.
Entti he aggidi keyida biittaa guye qoppidabaa gidiyakko guye simmanaw dandda7osona.
Shin ha77i aadhdhi lo77iya salo biittaa laamotosona. Hessa gisho, Xoossay enttaw katama giigisida gisho “Entta Xoossaa” geetettidi xeegettanaw yeellatenna.
Abrahamey paacettida wode Yisaaqa yarshshiday ammanonna. He ufayssa qaala ekkida Abrahamey ba issi na7aa yarshshanaw giigis.
Xoossay Abrahamekko, “Ne zerethay Yisaaqa baggara xeegettana” yaagidi odis.
Xoossay hayqoppe denthanaw dandda7eyssa Abrahamey ammanida gisho Yisaaqa hayqoppe paxi denddidaada oothidi zaari ekkis.
Yisaaqi wodeppe hananabaa eridi Yayqoobanne Eesawe anjjiday ammanona.
Yayqoobi hayqqana hanishe, issi issi Yoosefa nayta anjjidaynne guufe bolla katidi goynniday ammanonna.
Yoosefi hayqqanaw matida wode Isra7eele asay Gibxxefe keyanayssa odidaynne ba meqethaa oothanabaa entta kiittiday ammanona.
Musey yelettidaappe guye iya aayanne iya aaway mala lo77o na7a gididayssa be7idi heedzu ageena qottiday ammanona; entti kawuwa awaajjuwa yayyibookkona.
Musey diccidaappe guye Gibxxe kawuwa na7ee na7a geetettanayssa ixxiday ammanona.
Musey nagaran guutha wodes ufayttanaappe, Xoossaa asaara waaye ekkanayssa dooris.
I wodeppe demmana woytuwa tishshi oothidi xeellida gisho Gibxxe shaluwappe aathidi Kiristtoosa gisho borettanayssi daro aadhdhiya duretethi gididayssa eris.
Musey Kawuwa hanquwa yayyonna, Gibxxefe keyiday ammanona. Benttonna Xoossaa be7ida asada hanidi ba qofan genccis.
Hayqo ehiya kiitanchchoy Isra7eele asaa bayra nayta wodhonna mela Musey Faasikanne suutha wurxetha wogaa oothiday ammanona.
Isra7eele asay mela biittara hamuttiyada hamuttidi, Zo7o Abbaa pinniday ammanona. Shin Gibxxe asay gelanaw paaci be7ishin haathay entta mittis.
Isra7eele asay Iyaarkko katamaa shuchcha dirssaa laappun gallas yuuyidi, kunddisiday ammanona.
Laymiya Ra7aaba biittaa wochcheyssata mokkida gisho kiitettonna asaara hayqqonna attiday ammanona.
Hiza, haraa ta ay go? Gediyoonabaa, Baaraqabaa, Samsoonabaa, Yofttaahebaa, Dawitebaa, Saamu7eelabaa, qassi nabetabaa odanaw taw wodey gidenna.
Entti ammanon kawotethata xoonidosona; xillotethan aysidosona; Xoossay immana gida ufayssaa ekkidosona; gaammota doona gorddidosona;
tama wolqqaa toysidosona; morkkata mashshaafe attidosona; bantta daaburan minnidosona; olan wolqqaama gididosona; allaga toora goodidosona.
Maccasati bantta hayqqidayssati hayqoppe paxin ekkidosona. Qassi harati aadhdhiya hayqoppe dendduwa ekkanaw koyidi qashuwappe bilettanayssa ixxidosona.
Harati asan borettidi lisson garaafettidosona; harati santhalaatan qashettidi qasho keethan yegettidosona.
Entti suchchan cadettidosona; magaazen nam77a keyidi phalqqettidosona; paacettidosona; mashshan hayqqidosona; enttaw ubbabay dhayin metootidosona. Dorssa itenne deesha ite ma77idi yuuyidosona.
Enttaw ha alamey giigonna ixxin bazzo biittan, dere bolla, gonggoloninne olla giddon yuuyidosona.
Xoossay entta ammanuwabaa markkattikokka, he ubbay geetettida ufayssa qaala ekkibookkona.
Xoossay nuus lo77obaa qoppi wothida gisho entti nuuni baynna polo gidokkona.
Hiza, shaarada nu yuushuwan darida hayssa mela markkatti nu matan de7iya gisho nuna dhubbiya ubbaanne oykkidi haariya nagaraa diggidi, nu sinthan de7iya gaadde wothaa genccan woxxoos.
Nu ammanuwas oge dooyidayssanne nu wurssetha poluwakko nuna gathiya Yesuusa bolla nu ayfiyaa wothoos. Yesuusi wodeppe de7iya ufayssaa gisho masqaliya waaya dandda7idi, yeella hayquwa kadhidi, Xoossaafe ushachcha baggan uttis.
Hiza, hintte doccidi ufayssi qanxonna mela nagaranchchota ixuwa dandda7ida Yesuusa qoppite.
Nagarara de7iya baaxiyan buroo suuthu gussana gakkanaw eqettibeekketa.
Xoossay ba qaalan, ba naytada hinttena zoridayssa dogideta. “Ta na7aw, Xoossaa seera leqqofa; i nena seeriya wode ufayssi qanxofa.
Goday ba dosiya uraa seeres; qassi ba na7ada ekkiya ubbaa garaafees” yaagees.
Xoossay hinttena ba naytada seeriya wode genccite; Aaway seeronna na7i oonee?
Xoossay ba nayta ubbaa seeres; hintte seerettonna ixxiko tuma iya nayta gidonnashin balakko nayta.
Qassi nuna yelida nu aawati nuna seerosona; nukka enttana bonchchoos. Yaatin, nuuni nu ayyaana Aawas waanidi aathi haarettoko?
Hiza, nu aawati banttaw lo77o daanida mela guutha wodes nuna seeridosona. Shin Xoossay nu go77aas, nu iya geeshshatethan shaakettana mela seeres.
Nuuni seerettiya wode yiloyeesippe attin ufayssenna. Shin guyeppe seeretethaa meezetida asaas seeray, saroy kumida xillotethaa ayfe ayfisees.
Hiza, hintte arggaacida qesiyanne hintte daaburida gulbbata minthite.
Wobbey paxana melappe attin aathi meqqonna mela hintte tohuwas suure oge giigisite.
Asa ubbaara saro daanawunne geeshshatethan daanaw minnite; geeshshatethi baynna oonikka Godaa be7anaw dandda7enna.
Hinttefe ooddeskka Xoossaa aadho keehatethay pacconnaada, qassi camo ayfe ayfidi daro asaa tunisiyanne dhayssiya zerethada gidonna mela naagettite.
Hintte giddon laymatiya asi woykko issi toho miya kathas ba bayratethaa toochchidi bayzida Eesawe mela asi doonna mela naagettite.
Guyeppe Eesawey he anjjuwaa ekkanaw koyida wode digettidayssa ereeta. I he anjjuwaa afuthan minnidi koykkoka, demmanaw dandda7ibeenna; I nagaraappe simmanaw qaada demmibeenna.
Hintte kushen boshettiya Siina deriyakko, eexiya tamaakko, dhumaakko, caaganaakko, gotiyakko,
moyziya waasuwako woykko qaalay si7ettiya bessaako yibeekketa. He qaala si7ida asay hara guzha qaala si7onna mela woossidosona.
Ays giikko, “Hari attoshin, do7i he deriya bochchiko, shuchchan cadettidi hayqo” yaagida kiitaa entti tookkanaw dandda7ibookkona.
He haniyabay daro daganthiyaba gidida gisho Musey, “Taani yashshan kokkoras” yaagis.
Shin hintte Xiyoone Deriyakko, de7o Xoossay de7iya Yerusalaame katamaakko, issife shiiqidi ufayttiya daro mukulu kiitanchchotakko saluwa yideta.
Entta sunthay salon xaafettida woosa keethaa bayra naytakko, asa ubbaa pirddiya Xoossaakko, polo gidida xillo asaa ayyaanatakko yideta.
Ooratha caaquwas giddo gididi sigethiya Yesuusakko, Aabela suuthaafe aadhdhiyabaa odiya wurxettida suuthaakko yideta.
Hinttew odiya uraa qaala ixxas goonna mela naagettite. Kaseyssati sa7an gididi odida kiitaa si7onna ixxidi attiboonnabaa gidikko yaatin, salon gididi odiya qaala nuuni ixxas giikko waanidi attanee?
He wode iya qaalay sa7a qaathis. Shin ha77i taani, “Sa7a xalaala gidonnashin issi toho zaarada saluwakka qaathana” yaagis.
“Issi toho zaarada” giya qaalay qaaxxonnobay minnidi daana mela qaaxxiya medhettidabati dhayanayssa bessees.
Nuuni qaaxxanaw dandda7onna kawotethaa ekkiya gisho Xoossaa galatoos; Xoossaa ufayssiya ogen bonchchoninne yashshatethan iya goynnos.
Hiza, nu Xoossay tuma xuuggiya tama.
Ammaniya asada issoy issuwara polo siiqetite.
Imathe mokkeyssa dogoppite. Issi issi asati hessada oothishe eronna kiitanchchota mokkidosona.
Qashon de7eyssata hintteka enttara issife qashon de7iyada oothidi enttana qoppite. Waaye ekkiya asaara issife hintteka waaye ekkiyada oothidi enttana qoppite.
Ekoynne geloy asa ubbaa matan bonchchettidabaa gido. Qassi Xoossay laymateyssatanne laammeyssata pirddanaw de7iya gisho azinaynne machchiya issoy issuwas ammanettanaw bessees.
Miishe siiqoppe hinttena naagite; hinttew de7iyaban alite. Xoossay, “Taani nena ubbarakka yeggike woykko aggike” yaagis.
Hessa gisho, nuuni ammanettidi, “Goday tana maaddeyssa; ta yayyike; asi tana ay oothanee?” yaagos.
Xoossaa qaala koyro hinttew odida hinttena kaaletheyssata qoppite. Entti waanidi de7idaakko entta duussaa be7idi entta ammanuwa kaallite.
Yesuus Kiristtoosi zinekka hachchika merinawukka laamettenna.
Dumma dumma ooratha timirtten harasoo bidi dhayoppite; booppite. Nu wozanay Xoossaa aadho keehatethan minnanaw besseesppe attin min go77onna kathan wogaa polon gidoppo.
Shin dunkkaaniya giddon oothiya kahineti he yarshsho kathaafe maanaw enttaw maati baynna yarshsho bessay nuus de7ees.
Kahine halaqay nagara yarshshos mehe suuthi ekkidi yarshshanaw Ubbaafe Geeshsha Bessaa gelees. Shin he mehiya ashuwa dirssaafe karen xuuggees.
Hessadakka, Yesuusi deriya nagaraappe ba suuthan geeshshanaw katamaa penggiyafe karen waayettis.
Hiza, nuuni boriya tookkidi dirssaafe kare iyakko keyoos.
Hiza, nuus hayssan merinaw de7iya katami baawa, shin nuuni yaana katamaa naagoos.
Hiza, Yesuusa baggara ubba wode iya sunthaas markkattiya mettershsha galata yarshsho Xoossaas immoos.
Lo77obaa oosonne hinttew de7iyabaappe metootida asaas imo dogoppite. Hiza, hessa mela yarshshoy Xoossaa ufayssees.
Hinttena kaaletheyssatas kiitettite; entti giyabaa oothite. Entti bantta oothiyabas Xoossaa sinthan oyshettanaw de7iya gisho hinttena heemmoosona. Hintte enttaw kiitettiko, bantta oosuwa ufayttidi oothana; hessi hanonna ixxiko, entti azzanishe oothana; hessi hinttena aybibaakka maaddenna.
Nuus Xoossaa woossite. Nu kahay geeshshi; nu ubba wode lo77obaa oothanaw koyoos.
Taani hintteko ellesada yaana mela hintte taw minthidi Xoossaa woossana mela ta hinttena hadara gays.
Sarotethaa Xoossay, dorssa heemmiya nu Godaa Yesuusa, ba merinaa caaqo suuthan hayqoppe denthidayssi,
iya sheniya oothana mela lo77obaa ubban I hinttena dancciso. Iya ufayssiyabaa Yesuus Kiristtoosa baggara nunan Xoossay ootho. Yesuus Kiristtoosa baggara Xoossaas merinaappe merinaa gakkanaw bonchchoy gido. Amin77i.
Ta ishato, ta ha dabddaabbiya hinttew qanthan xaafida gisho hintte ta zoriya salettonna ekkana mela ta hinttena woossays.
Nu ishay, Ximotiyoosi qashoppe bilettidayssa erite. I ellesidi taakko yiikko ta iyara hinttena bada be7ana.
Hinttena kaaletheyssatanne ammaniyaa ubbaa saro giite. Xaaleppe yida ammaniyaa asay hinttena saro yaagoosona.
Xoossaa aadho keehatethay hintte ubbaara gido. Amin77i.
Xoossaanne Godaa Yesuus Kiristtoosa aylley, Yayqoobi, biitta ubban laalettida tammanne nam77u sheeshatas kiittida kiita. Saro, ay mela de7eetii?
Ta ishato, hinttena dumma dumma paacey gakkiya wode hintte lo77obaa demmidaada kumetha ufayssan ekkite.
Hintte ammanuwa paacetethay dandda7a hinttew immeyssa ereeta.
Hintte wurssethi gakkanaw dandda7ikko aybi pacey baynna polonne kumethi gideta.
Hinttefe ooddeskka cinccatethi dhayikko Xoossaa woosso. Iyaw imettana. Xoossay oonakka boronna ubbaas keehatethan immiya Xoosse.
Shin I woossiya wode sidhonna ammanon Xoossaa woosso. Sidhiya oonikka carkkoy sugin qaaxxiya abbaa zule mela.
Nam77u qofi de7eynne ba ogiyan eqqonna oonikka Godaappe aykkoka demmana gidi qoppofo.

Ammaniya manqo asati, Xoossay enttana dhoqqu oothiya wode ufaytto.
Qassi ammaniyaa dure asati Xoossay enttana ziqqi oothiya wode ufaytto. Dure asati ciishshada dhayana.
Away ba mishaara keyidi maataa melisin, ciishshay qolettees; iya lo77otethayka dhayees. Hessadakka, dure asati bantta oosuwan daaburishe dhayana.
Metuwa xoonidi aadhdhidaappe guye, Xoossay bana siiqeyssatas immana gidi qaala gelida de7o kallachchaa ekkana gisho meton gencciya asi anjjettidayssa.
Oonikka paacettiya wode “Tana Xoossay paaces” gooppo. Xoossay iitan paacettenna; qassi I oonakka paaccenna.
Shin issi issi asi ba iita amuwaan gooshettiya wodenne cimettiya wode paacettees.
Hessafe guye, amotethi qanthattidi nagara yelees; qassi nagari diccidi hayqo yelees.
Ta siiqo ishato, cimettofite.
Lo77o imoynne kumetha anjjo ubbay saloppenne saluwa poo7uwa medhdhida Xoossaa aawappe yees. Xoossay kuyada ubba wode laamettenna.
Nuuni, iya medhetethaas koyro gidana mela nuna tuma qaalan ba shenen yelis.
Ta siiqo ishato, hayssa akeekite. Asi ubbay si7anaw elleso, shin odettanawunne hanqettanaw ellesoppo.
Asa hanqoy Xoossay koyaa xillotethaa ehenna.
Hessa gisho, tuna hanotanne iitatetha ubbaa diggidi, Xoossay hintte wozanan tokkida hintte shemppuwa ashshanaw dandda7iya qaala aadatethan ekkite.
Shin Xoossaa qaala ooson peeshshiteppe attin sissa xalaalan hinttena cimmofite.
Qaalaa si7idi oothonna asi, I ba som77uwa masttoten be7iya asa mela.
I ba som77uwa be7idi bees, shin I ay daaniyakko ellesi dogees.
Shin oonikka aylletethafe kessiya polo higgiya akeekan be7idi, kaallidi naagey, si7idayssa dogonna ooson peeshshiya uray, ba ooso ubban anjjettana.
Ba inxarssaa naagonna ammanays giya uray bana cimmees; iya ammanoy hada.
Xoossaa Aawa sinthan borey baynna geeshsha ammanoy hayssa: aaya aawu baynna naytanne am77eta maadonne alamiya tunaappe bana naago.
Ta ishato, hintte nu bonchcho Godaa Yesuus Kiristtoosa ammaniyabaa gidikko, asa som77o xeellidi ase bonchchofite.
Leemisos, worqqa migiddo aathidi, lo77o ma7o ma77ida dure asi hintte shiiquwa yis. Qassi curqqa ma7o ma77ida manqo asikka yis.
Lo77o ma7o ma77ida addiya hintte aathi bonchchidi, “Ne hayssan lo77iya oydiyan utta” gidi, qassi manqo addiya, “Ne yan eqqa woykko hayssan ta tohuwa matan sa7an utta” geeta.
Yaatin, hinttee, hintte giddon shaaketethi medhdheyssatanne iita qofara de7iya daynnata mela gidekketiyye?
Ta siiqo ishato, si7ite. Ammanon dure gidana melanne bana siiqeyssatas immana gida salo kawotethaa laattana mela ha sa7an de7iya manqota Xoossay dooribeenneyye?
Shin hintte manqota toochcheeta. Hinttena un77etheyssati dureta gidokkonaayye? Hinttena daynna sinthi goochcheyssati entta gidokkonaayye?
Hintte xeegettida lo77o Godaa sunthaa cayeyssati entta gidokkonaayye?
Shin Geeshsha Maxaafan, “Ase ubbaa nena ne doseyssada dosa” geetettidi xaafettida Xoossaa kawotethaa higgiya hintte polikko lo77o ootheeta.
Shin hintte asa som77o xeellidi bonchchiko, nagara ootheeta qassi higgey hinttena higge menthida asada pirddana.
Oonikka higge ubbaafe issuwa menthidi, attida ubbaa naagikko ubbaa menthidaada taybettees.
“Laammofa” gida Goday, qassi “Wodhoppa” gis. Shin neeni laammonna aggada wodhidabaa gidikko, higgiya menthadasa.
Aylletethafe kessiya higgiya sinthan pirdda ekkanaw de7iya asada odetitenne oothite.
Ase maaronna oonakka Xoossay maaronna pirddana. Shin maarotethay pirddaa xoonees.
Ta ishato, hinttefe issi asi taw ammanoy de7ees gidi, ba ammanuwa ooson bessonna ixxiko iya ay maaddanee? Iya ammanoy iya ashshanaw dandda7ii?
Leemisos issi ishay woykko issi michchiya kallotikonne enttaw miyabay dhayikko,
hinttefe issi asi enttako, “Saro biite! Tama kayite! Kallidi miite!” gidi, koshshiyabaa enttaw immonna ixxiko entta ay maaddii?
Hessa gisho, oosoy baynna ammanoy barkka hayqqidayssa.
Shin issi asi, “New ammanoy de7ees; qassi taw oosoy de7ees. Neeni ne ammanuwa ne oosuwappe shaakkada tana bessa; takka ta ammanuwa ta oosuwan nena bessana” gaana.
Neeni, issi Xoossay de7eyssa ammanaasa; hessi lo77o. Tuna ayyaanatikka ammanoosona; yashshan kokkorosona.
Neno eeyaw! Ammanoy oosoppe shaakettidi maaddonnayssa eranaw koyay?
Nu aawa Abrahamey, ba na7aa Yisaaqa yarshsho bessaa bolla wothida wode ba oosuwan xillibeenne?
Iya ammanoynne iya oosoy issife oothidayssa be7ikki? Iya ammanoy iya oosuwan polettis.
Geeshsha Maxaafay, “Abrahamey Xoossaa ammanis. Xoossay hessa iyaw xillotethi oothidi taybis” gidayssi polettis. Qassi I Xoossaa dabbo geetettidi xeegettis.
Asi ammano xalaalan gidonnashin ooson xilleyssa be7aasa.
Hessadakka, laymiya Ra7aaba Isra7eeleppe kiitettidayssata mokkada hara ogera entta moyzida wode ba oosuwan xillabeekke?
Shemppoy shaakettida asatethay hayqo gideyssada, oosoy shaakettida ammanoykka hayqqidayssa.
Ta ishato, hinttefe daroti asttamaare gidoppo. Nu, asttamaareti haratappe aadhdhiya pirddaa ekkanayssa hintte ereeta.
Nu ubbay daroban balettoos. Ba odan balettonna oonikka banatethaa naaganaw dandda7iya polo asi.
Parati nuus kiitettana mela bixaala barssidi nuuni koyaa bessi ubbaa efoos.
Markkabey hessa mela gita gidishe wolqqaama carkkuwan sugettikokka, iya laaggeyssi ba koyaa bessi zaaridi laaggiya guutha mithan laagettidi bees.
Hessada inxarssi asatethaa giddon guutha gidikkoka daro gitaban ceeqettees. Guutha tami daro gita woraa xuuggees.
Inxarssi tama mela. Inxarssi nu asatethaa giddon iitan kumida alame; asatetha ubbaa tunisees. Gaannameppe keyaa tamada nu de7uwa wotha ubbaa xuuggees.
Do7atanne kafota, ulora gooshetteyssatanne abban de7iya medhetethata ubbaa asi haarees; enttika haarettidosona.
Shin oonikka inxarssi haaranaw dandda7ibeenna. Inxarssi wodhiya marzey kumida haarettonna iita medhetethi.
Nu inxarssan, nu, Godaanne Xoossaa galatoos. Qassi iyara Xoossaa leemison Medhettida asaa qanggoos.
Issi doonappe galatinne qanggethi keyees. Ta ishato, hessada hananaw bessenna.
Pulttoy issi ollafe mal77iya haathinne cammiya haathi pulttanaw dandda7ii?
Ta ishato, balase mithi shamaho ayfanaw dandda7ii? Woykko woyne mithi balase mitha ayfe ayfanaw dandda7ii? Camo haathafe mal77o haathi keyanaw dandda7enna.
Hintte giddon cinccinne akeekanchchoy oonee? Ba lo77o de7uwa, ashkketethaninne cinccatethan oosettida ooson besso.
Shin hintte wozanan cammiya qanaateynne bana dosoy de7ikko ceeqettofite; tumaa bolla worddotoppite.
Hessa mela cinccatethay saloppe yidabaa gidonnashin hessi asabaa, alamebaa, xalahebaa.
Qanaateynne bana dosoy de7iya son ooshshinne iita ooso ubbay de7oosona.
Shin bollafe yaa cinccatethay ubbaafe sinthe geeshshi. Qassi sarotethi, aadatethi, si7idi ekkeyssa, qadhetteyssa, lo77o ayfey kumidayssa, ase shaakkonnayssanne cubbotethi baynnayssa.
Sarotethaa doseyssati sarotethi zeridi xillotethi buuccosona.
Ooshshinne oli hintte giddo awuppe yii? Entti yey hintte asatethaa haaranaw olettiya hintte asho amuwaappe gidenneyye?
Hintte amotteeta, shin demmeketa; hessa gisho, wodheeta. Minthi koyeeta, shin demmanaw dandda7ekketa; hessa gisho, ooyetteetanne oletteeta. Hintte Xoossaa woossonna gisho koyabaa demmeketa.
Hintte woosseta, shin demmeketa. Hintte asho amuwaa polanaw wobbe ogen woossiya gisho demmeketa.
Hinttenoo, laymateyssato! Ha alamiya dosey Xoossara morkke gideyssa erekketii? Ha alamiyara dabbotanaw koyey oonikka Xoossaara morkke.
Geeshsha Maxaafay, “Xoossay nunan daana mela oothida Ayyaanay, nuuni iyaw buzo gidana mela amottees” gidayssa coo gidabaa daanii?
Shin Geeshsha Maxaafay, “Xoossay otoranchchota ixxees, shin banttana kawushsheyssatas maarotethaa immees” yaagiya gisho Xoossay maarotethaa darssidi immees.
Hessa gisho, Xoossaas haarettite; Xalahiyara eqettite; I hinttefe haakkana.
Xoossaakko shiiqite; I hintteko shiiqana. Hinttenoo, nagaranchchoto, hintte kushiya meecettite; nam77u qofi de7eyssato, hintte wozanaa geeshshite.
Kayottite, yeekkitenne afuxite. Hintte miichchay yeehon, hintte ufayssay azzanon laameto.
Godaa sinthan hinttenatethaa kawushshite; I hinttena dhoqqu dhoqqu oothana.
Ta ishato, issoy issuwa zigiroppite. Ba ishaa zigireynne iya bolla pirddey higge zigireesinne higge bolla pirddees. Neeni higge bolla pirddiko higge bolla pirddeyssa gidaasappe attin higge poleyssa gidakka.
Higge immeynne pirddey Xoossaa xalaala. Ashshanawunne dhayssanaw dandda7ey iya. Yaatin, asa bolla pirddiya neeni oonee?
Hintte, “Nuuni hachchi woykko wontto ya katamaa woykko ha katamaa baana; yan laythi uttana; zal77idi wodhisana” yaageyssato, si7ite.
Wontto aybi hananeekko hintte erekketa. Hintte de7oy waananekko erey oonee? Hintte guutha wode benttidi dhayaa akka mela.
Hessa aggidi, “Goday giikko nuuni daana; hayssa woykko hessa oothana” yaaganaw bessees.
Shin hintte ha77i otortteetanne ceeqetteeta. Hessa mela ceeqo ubbay iita.
Hessa gisho, lo77obaa oothanaw erishe oothonna uraas hessi nagara.
Hinttenoo, dureto, hintte bolla iita metoy yaa gisho yeekkitenne zeleelite.
Hintte shaloy buuqqis; hintte afilaykka bilan meetettis.
Hintte worqqaynne hintte biray shi7is. He shi7ay hintte bolla markka gidana. I hintte asatethaa tamada maana. Hintte ha wurida qammatan hinttew shalo dagayeeta.
Hintte gaden oothi pee7ida asaa kera miishiya qanxibeekketa. Hessi hintte bolla waasses. He asata waasoy wolqqaama Godaa haythan si7ettis.
Ha sa7an hintte ulo xalaalas qoppidi, injjen de7ideta. Shukas giigettida meheda hinttena dhiikkideta.
Hinttera eqettanaw dandda7onna xillo asa bolla pirddideta; iya wodhideta.
Ta ishato, Goday yaana gakkanaw genccite. Goshshanchchoy torchche iraynne sila iray yaana gakkanaw genccidi al77o kathaa naagidi waati gathi ekkiyako qoppite.
He goshshanchchuwada hintteka genccite. Godaa yuussay matattida gisho ufayssan naagite.
Ta ishato, Xoossay hintte bolla pirddonna mela issoy issuwa bolla zuuzummofite. Pirddeyssi penggen eqqis.
Ta ishato, waayan genccida, Godaa sunthan odida nabeta leemiso oothidi ekkite.
Dandda7an genccidayssata nuuni anjjettidayssata goos. Iyyoobey waanidi genccidaako hintte si7ideta. Goday wurssethan iya waati maaddidaakko be7ideta. I maarotinne qadhey kumida Godaa gidiya gisho hessa oothis.
Shin ubbaafe sinthe, ta ishato, saluwan gidin woykko sa7an gidin woykko hara aybinkka caaqqofite. Xoossaa pirddan hintte gelonnaada hintte oday ee gidikko, “Ee” giite; akkay gidikko, “Akkay” giite.
Hintte giddon meto ekkiya oonikka de7ikko Xoossaa woosso. Ufayttiya oonikka de7ikko galatan yexxo.
Hinttefe harggettiya oonikka de7ikko woosa keetha cimata xeego. Entti Godaa sunthan shamaho zayte tiyidi iyaw Xoossaa woosso.
Ammanon woossida woosay hargganchchuwa pathana. Goday iya, harggiyafe denthana; I nagara oothidabaa gidikkoka Goday iya maarana.
Hessa gisho, hintte paxana mela hintte nagara issoy issuwas paaxitenne issoy issuwas woossite. Xillo asa woosay wolqqaama ooso oothees.
Eliyaasi nu mela ase. Iri sa7an bukkonna mela minthidi Xoossaa woossin heedzu laythinne usuppun ageena sa7an iri bukkibeenna.
Zaaridi I Xoossaa woossin saloppe iri bukkis; sa7aykka kathi mokkis.
Ta ishato, hinttefe oonikka tuma ogiyappe buutikko, haray iya tumaakko zaarikko,
nagaranchchuwa iya bala ogiyappe zaariya oonikka, iya shemppuwa hayqoppe ashsheyssanne iya daro nagaraas maarota immeyssa ero.
Taani, Yesuus Kiristtoosa hawaarey Phexiroosi; Phanxoosan, Galaatiyan, Qaphadooqiyan, Iisiyaninne Bitiiniyan betanchchoda laalettidi de7iya Xoossay doorida, asaas ha dabddaabbiya xaafas.
Yesuus Kiristtoosas hintte kiitettana melanne iya suuthan geeyana mela, Xoossaa Aaway ba kase eran dooridayssatasinne Geeshsha Ayyaanan geeyida, hinttew aadho keehatethaynne sarotethay gido.
Yesuus Kiristtoosa hayqoppe denthidi ba gita maarotethan nam77antho yeletethaanne dhayonna ufayssaa immida nu Godaa Yesuus Kiristtoosa Aaway, Xoossay galatetto.
Qassi Xoossay hinttew dhayonna, iitonnanne buuqqonna laata salon giigisis.
He laatay wode wurssethan qonccanaw de7iya atotethaas Xoossaa wolqqan ammanon hinttew naagettidi de7ees.
Ha77i guutha wodes hintte dumma dumma paacen un77ettikokka hessan ufayttite.
He paacey hinttena gakkiday, taman yeggin dhayaa worqqafe hintte ammanoy aadhonne tuma gideyssa bessanaassa. He paacettida ammanuwan Yesuus Kiristtoosi qoncciya wode galataa, bonchchonne saba hintte ekkana.
Hintte Yesuusa be7ibeekketa, shin iya siiqeta. Hintte ha77i iya be7iboonnabaa gidikkoka, iya ammaneeta. Qassi odan qonccisanaw dandda7ettona ufayssaninne bonchchon kumideta.
Hintte ammanon naagiya hintte shemppuwa atotethaa ekkana.
Aadho keehatethaa baggara hinttew giigida ha atotethaabaa nabeti eranaw gita koshshaninne naagon koyidosona.
Enttan de7iya Kiristtoosa Ayyaanay iya waayabanne hessafe guye yaana bonchchuwabaa kasetidi markkattishe, awude woykko waanidi hananeekko akeekan pilggidosona.
Nabeti odida tinbbitey banttaw gidonnashin hinttew gideyssa Xoossay hinttew qonccisis. Ha77i asay hinttew odida Wonggelaa saloppe kiitettida Geeshsha Ayyaana wolqqan hinttew odidosona. Kiitanchchotika hessa be7anaw amottidosona.
Hessa gisho, oosos hinttena giigisite; hinttena haarite. Yesuus Kiristtoosi qoncciya wode hintte ekkana aadho keehatethaa ufayssan naagite.
Xoossaa naytada iyaw kiitettite; hintte kase eronna oothida iita amuwaa kaallofite.
Shin hinttena xeegida Xoossay geeshshi gididayssada hintteka hintte duussa ubban geeshshi gidite.
Geeshsha Maxaafan, “Taani geeshshi gidida gisho hintteka geeshshi gidite” geetetti xaafettis.
Asa som77o be7onna iya oosuwada pirddiya Xoossaa, “Nu Aawaw” gidi xeegiyabaa gidikko, ha sa7aa imathatetha duussaa yashshan de7ite.
Hinttee, hintte aawatappe laattida pathonna de7uwappe wozettidayssi, dhaya biran woykko worqqan gidonnayssa ereeta.
Borey woykko borssoy baynna dorssa suuthada al77o gidida Kiristtoosa suuthan wozettideta.
Xoossay alamey medhettanaappe kase Kiristtoosa dooris, shin ha wurssetha wodiyan Kiristtoosi hintte gisho qonccis.
Hintte ammanoynne hintte ufayssay Xoossan gidana mela iya hayqoppe denthidi, bonchchida Kiristtoosa baggara Xoossan ammaneeta.
Hintte tumatethaas kiitettidi hinttenatethaa geeshshideta. Hintte issoy issuwa wozanappe siiqeta, shin ha77ika tuma wozanappe minthidi siiqite.
Hintte nam77antho yelettiday dhayaa zerethafe gidonnashin merinaw de7iya Xoossaa qaalan dhayonna zerethaafe yelettideta.
Xoossaa qaalay, “Asi ubbay maata mela; iya bonchcho ubbay ciishsha mela. Maatay melees, ciishshaykka qolettees.
Shin Godaa qaalay merinaw de7ees” yaagees. Hinttew odettida Wonggelaa qaalay hayssa.
Hiza, iitatethi ubbaa, cimo ubbaa, cubbotethi qanaatenne zigirssi ubbaa hinttefe diggite.
Goday keeha gideyssa hintte eridi meezetidayssada ha77i yelettida guutha naytada hintte atotethan diccishe baanaw Xoossaa geeshsha qaala maathaa ubba wode amottite.

Asan borettidi Xoossan doorettida al77o gidida de7o shuchchaa, Godaa Yesuusakko shiiqite.
Hintte Ayyaana keethi keexettiya de7o shuchchata. Hintte Yesuus Kiristtoosa baggara Xoossaa ufayssiya ayyaana yarshsho yarshshiya geeshsha kahineta.
Geeshsha Maxaafan, “Hekko, taani Xiyoone kataman godaa xaphuwa minthiya, doorettida, al77o shuchchaa wothas; iyan ammaniyaa oonikka yeellatenna” yaagees.
Ha shuchchay hinttew ammaneyssatas al77o, shin ammanonnayssatas, “Gimbbeyssati kadhidi ixxida shuchchay godaa xaphuwa minthiya, ubbaafe aadhdhiya shuchchu gidis.”
Qassika, “Ha shuchchay ase dhubbiya shuchchunne ase kunddisiya zaalla” yaagees. Entti hessas qaadettida gisho Xoossaa qaalaa kiitettonna ixxidi dhubettidosona.
Shin Xoossay dhumappe malaalisiya ba poo7uwakko hinttena xeegiday, hintte iya lo77otethaa haratas odanaw doorettida zare, kawo kahine, geeshsha derenne Xoossaa dumma dere.
Hintte kase Xoossaa dere gidekketa, shin ha77i hintte iya dere. Hintte kase maarotethi demmibeekketa, shin ha77i maarotethi demmideta.
Ta ishato, hintte ha sa7an imathenne betanchcho gididayssada hintte shemppuwa oliya asho amoppe haakkana mela taani hinttena woossays.
Ammanonna asay hinttena iita oothiya asada zigiryaa wode Xoossay nuna be7anaw yaa gallas, entti hintte lo77o oosuwa be7idi Xoossaa galatana mela hinttew lo77o de7oy de7o.
Godaa gisho gidi maatara de7iya asatas haarettite; ubbaafe bolla gidiya gisho kawuwaskka haarettite.
Entti iita ootheyssata seeranawunne lo77o ootheyssata sabbanaw kawuwappe kiitettida gisho deriya ayseyssatas haarettite.
Hinttee, hintte lo77o oosuwan eronna eeya asaa doona oythanayssi Xoossaa shene.
Xoossaa aylle gididi la77atethan de7iteppe attin hintte la77atethaa iita oosos kama oothofite.
Asa ubbaa bonchchite; ammaniyaa asaa siiqite; Xoossaa yayyite; kawo bonchchite.
Aylleto, lo77o godatasinne keeha godata xalaalas gidonnashin iitaataskka bonchchon haarettite.
Asi Xoossaa gisho gidi bessonna waaye waayettiko Xoossay iya anjjana.
Shin hintte nagara oothin hinttena dechchiya wode hintte dandda7ikko hinttew ay galati de7ii? Shin lo77obaa oothidi waaye dandda7ikko Xoossay hinttena hessas anjjana.
Xoossay hinttena xeegiday hessa gishossa; Kiristtoosi hinttew waayettis; hintte iya kaallana mela, hinttew leemiso gidis.
I nagara oothibeenna; iya doonankka worddoy benttibeenna.
Entti iya cayaa wode zaaridi cayibeenna. Shin waaye ekkishe xillo pirddiya Xoossaas ba pirdda aggaagisppe attin manddibeenna.
Nuuni nagaras hayqqidi xillotethas daana mela Kiristtoosi ba ashuwan nu nagaraa masqaliya bolla tookkis; hintte iya madunthan paxideta.
Kase hintte oge balidi dhayida dorssa mela, shin ha77i hintte shemppuwa heemmeyssakkonne naageyssakko simmideta.
Hessadakka, machcheto, hintte azinatappe Xoossaa qaalas kiitettonayssati de7ikkoka aykkoka odettonashin, hintte yashshatethaanne hintte geeshsha de7uwa be7idi ammanana mela enttaw haarettite.
